UNokwayiyo Deyizana (95), ophakathi, ekunye nabantwana bakhe eshiya indlu yodaka esiya kwayakhelwe ngurhulumente UMFANEKISO: SITHANDIWE VELAPHI
Omnye oxhamlileyo nguNokwayiyo Deyizana (95) waseCenyu Lands. “Ndiziva kamnandi kakhulu, kuba xa kusina imvula besingalali kuba indlu ibisiwa.
Ndibulela ubaw’ uMaphosa (Ramaphosa) othe wasakhela izindlu. Ndibulela nonokontraka othe wasakhela le ndlu kwakunye neekomiti zasekuhlaleni.”
UDeyizana noMvuyo abakhange bakwazi ukuzibamba, bakhala ngethuba benikwa ithuba lokuphosa amazwi malunga nenkonzo abayinikwe ngumbuso.
UMphathiswa weSebe, uNonceba Kontsiwe, uthi kulo nyakamali isebe lizimisele ukuqwalasela nangakumbi abantu abahlelelekileyo – abaquka abantu abadala kakhulu, abantwana abangenabazali, abantu abaphila nenkubazeko kwakunye namagqala omkhosi.
UNokwayiyo Deyizana (95) ekunye namagosa karhulumente kwindlu entsha ayanikwe kwiveki ephelileyo UMFANEKISO: SITHANDIWE VELAPHI
“Iinyembezi zovuyo zabantu abafumana ezi zindlu zihlaba ngaphakathi. Abantu abakholelwa, bebesele bencamile bengenathemba ukuba ubomi babo bungatshintsha. 
Iyavuyisa eyokubona isebe likwazi ukutshintsha ubomi babantu. 
Umntu nokuba mdala, xa kufika iintsuku zokugqibela, ziza kufika enendawo yakhe elungileyo.
“Sihlola umsebenzi owenziweyo inyanga nenyanga, ukujonga ukuba yinto eyenziwayo ukunqanda ukujika kwemali ngenxa yokungachithwa ngokwezicwangciso.
Oku kuza kwenza ukuba sibone ukuba kungalungiswa njani.
Siyawakhuthaza amagosa ukuba mabamise kuba umntu kuza kufuneka aphendule ukuba kutheni kungenzekanga ngokwezicwangciso zesebe,” utshilo uKontsiwe.
Kulo mmandla waseCenyu iyaqhuba iprojekthi yokwakhiwa kwezindlu.
Kuza kwakhiwa izindlu ezingamakhulu amane anamashumi amahlanu (450) eCenyu Village logama ziza kuba ngamakhulu amathandathu anamashumi alithoba anesibini (692) eCenyu Lands.

XA ungakuthathel’ ingqalelo ukunikela ngomongo wethambo lakho, yazi ukuba isizalwane sakho singasemngciphekweni ombi xa singanesigulo esinokubangela ukuba sifune ukufakelwa umongo omtsha.
Oku kungenxa yokuba ubani uncedakala lula ngomongo wesizalwane sakhe xa enesigulo esifana neLeukaemia (umhlaza oongcambu zawo zisemongweni wethambo) okanye ezinye izifo ezinxulumene negazi.
Unyaka nonyaka, amakhulu abantu baseMzantsi Afrika abaneempawu ezibonisa ukunqongophala kwamajoni omzimba okuzikhusela kwizifo kwakunye nezifo ezisegazini, afikelela kwinqanaba elibi kakhulu apho iye ibe kukufakelwa umongo omtsha kuphela eyona ndlela abanokunyangeka ngayo.
Xa ufikelele kweso sigaba sokugula, ukufakelwa umongo omtsha ngempumelelo kubangela ukuba abantu abangaphezu kwe60% banyangeke.
Ngelishwa, kwinkoliso yezigulane ezingenawo amalungu osapho angabanikeli abafanelekayo (malunga nesigulane esinye kwezithathu ezinamalungu osapho angabanikezeli), umntu ofanelana nabo abanokufumana umongo wakhe ingangumntu omnye ebantwini abayi100 000.
Kutheni bembalwa nje abantu abantsundu ababhalisayo ukuze banikele ngomongo?
Kukho ingcinga engeyonyaniso nexhaphakileyo yokuba ukunikela ngomongo yinkqubo ebuhlungu, kukuhlaselwa, yaye kukuthathwa kwento umntu onikelayo angafuni kunikela ngayo. 
Yaye njengoko kwamhla mnene ibiyindaba yakwamkhozi ukuthetha ngomhlaza (cancer) nokungabikho kwemithombo yolwazi kwiikliniki zasekuhlaleni ngokuphathelele imibutho esindisa ubomi efana ne-South African Bone Marrow Registry (SABMR), kulula ukubona ukuba kutheni zixhaphake kangaka nje ezi ngcinga zingeyonyaniso.
UNonhlanhla Mtshali, ongumongikazi waseRhawutini, ngomnye wabo bathe bafakelwa umongo, nto leyo eyamsindisayo.
“Olu tyando lwenze okukhulu kum. 
Lundinike ithuba lesibini ebomini. 
Sisoloko sikhona isisombululo [engxakini] mna ndasifumana eSABMR, kuba balikhonkco phakathi kwabantu abakhangela ubomi kwanabo banikela ngabo,” utshilo uMtshali.Nonhlanhla Mtshali

Abahlali belinde phandle kwikliniki yasePaballong eMatatiele.
Kwimpelaveki edlulileyo abahlali basePaballong bebebhinqe omfutshane becheba ingca yekliniki yale ndawo.
“Ingca siyichebela ukuba kubekho indawo yokuhamba kule kliniki. Singqubanisene iintloko sathenga ipetroli ze abanoomatshini bokucheba ingca beza noomatshini babo,” utshilo umhlali wale wadi.
“Asiboni nkqubela phambili kule ndawo yethu kwaWadi 15 phantsi komasipala waseMatatiele. 
Kule ndawo sikuyo sinekliniki ejongene nale wadi yonke kodwa imeko yayo ayintlanga konke konke,” kutsho umhlali.
Omnye umhlali uxelele I’solezwe ukuba bagqibe kwelokucheba kule kliniki emva kokuba beqaphele ukwena kwengca.
“Ayikho indawo yokulinda ngaphakathi kule kliniki. Xa kubanda abantu bahlala phandle engceni. Amagumbi ekliniki mathathu ngaphakathi. 
Sigqibe kwelokuba masivule indawo yabo yokulinda ngokuthi sichebe ingca.
“Siye saphinda sacheba nakwindawo eneholo loluntu, ekhritshi, ukuze sibambe iindibano kakuhle,” kutsho lo mhlali.

UMandela ukhule esenza izifundo zomculo ebuncinaneni bakhe de waya eNatal Technikon apho enze izifundo zomculo weJazz, ze waphuma waya eUnivesity of Cape Town esenza iiMasters zakhe emculweni.

Olitshantliziyo kula mmandla uThino Mankayi uthi busesichengeni ubomi babo babhinqileyo kuba zininzi iziganeko zokuxhatshazwa kwamanina kwaye amatyala angahambeli ndawo.
Uthi ukukhululwa ngebheyile komrhanelwa akungomzekelo mhle kwenza ekubeni nezinye izaphulimthetho zidakase kuba zisazi zakukhutshwa ngebheyile.
“Ukuba lalingazange lishicilele efowunini ixhoba ngelingazange likholelwe luluntu nangumthetho xa lisithi lidlwengulwe ngenxa yohlobo olu lihamba ngalo eli tyala.
Siyaphoxeka, siyadaniswa zinkundla zamatyala ngokohlobo eziqhuba ngalo kweli tyala. 
Siza kulwa de kube kanti utshintsho lukhona kweli tyala,” utshilo uMankayi.
Omnye olilungu lokuhlala othethe neli phephandaba uthi uyabona naye ukuba ingalo yomthetho iliyekele ixhoba. 
Uthi bekufanele umrhanelwa usengaphakathi eziseleni ingakumbi ubungqina bukhona kwaye bucace gca.
Uthi uziva okungathi amatyala odlwengulo awathathelwa ngqalelo.
Olu shicilelo lwathi saa kumakhasi onxibelelwano.
Lwenziwa lixhoba ubude ziiyure ezingapha kwesibhozo nalapho acenga umrhanelwa ekubeni angamlimazi, kwaye emcenga ekubeni makangayenzi le nto ayenzayo kodwa waphela eyenza.
Umrhanelwa uvelile enkundleni ngomhla weshumi elinesithathu kwinyanga ephelileyo lachithwa ityala kuba ummangali engekho ngaphakathi enkundleni, kanti ummangali ulinde ngaphandle elindele ukubizwa njengoko wakhutshwa kusithwa kuphungulwa inani njengoko kulandelwa imiqathango yeCovid-19.
Umrhanelwa ubuyele kwakhona ngomhla wesine kule nyanga ze ityala lamiselwa umhla wamashumi amabini anesibini kwinyanga yeKhala (July). 
Umrhanelwa ulinde ngaphandle apho agilana nexhoba.
INKWENKWE yaseQonce uAxola May (16) ebezibona esiya eYunivesithi emva kokugqiba amabanga wakhe aphezulu, ekwanephupha lokuba ngumdlali wombhoxo.
Kodwa ilanga litshone emini amathemba aphela kuAxola emva kweendaba ezibuhlungu zokuhlaselwa kukungahambi kwegazi ngendlela efanelekileyo emathanjeni akhe omzimba (bone marrow).
Ngokudizwe lusapho lukaAxola, ungumntwana onothando kwaye okhululekileyo obonwabelayo ubom nosapho lwakhe kwakunye noontanga bakhe. 
Ikwanguye nomthandi kwanomdlali webhola yombhoxo.
Esona sisombululo esinokuthi sihlangule uAxola kule ngxaki kwaye afumane obunye ubomi kukuba enziwe utyando lokujongwa kwencindi phakathi emathanjeni (A stem cell transplant).
Ingxaki kuAxola, iqale ngokumane ephuma igazi ezimpumlweni, ulusu lwajika, kwamane kuqaqamba iindlebe kwaye kumane ukuphuma igazi kwiintsini.
Iindaba zokuba uAxolea uhlaselwa sisigulo esibeka ubomi bakhe emngciphekweni, khange zimphathe kakuhle umakhulu wakhe kwakunye nomakazi wakhe nabamkhulisayo emva kokubhubha kukamama kaAxola eseneminyaka emibini kuphela.
“UAxola ebekungxamele ukugqiba esikolweni kwaye aye eyunivesithi. Phambi kokuba agule, ebezixelele ngokudlalela iqela lebhola yombhoxo laseKapa iWestern Province Rugby.
Ebesoloko ejonge kuSiya Kolisi kwaye iliqhawe lakhe,” kutsho usapho.
Ngokokutsho kukaJames Alana onguMlawuli kwiDKMS Africa Country, uthi imeko kaAxola imbi kakhulu kwaye izigulana ezininzi zaseAfrika zisemngciphekweni kakhulu ngenxa yokunqaba kwenani labantu abanikeza ngegazi.
IDKMS, ibongoza uluntu ekubeni lubhalise ukuze kukhule inani akwazi uAxola afumane umntu anokuchanana ngqo naye ngegazi.
“Ndiyacela ndidomboza kuye nabani na onokunikela ngegazi ancede unyana wam aphile, azotsho akwazi enze konke ebekunqwenela ukwenza ebomini,” woleke ngelo umakazi wakhe.
Ungabatyelela abakwaDKMS xa ufuna ukunceda kumnatha wonxibelelwano.
IZIKO lemfundo yoonomngqushwana eAdelaide, iPhakamisani Educare Centre, livuliwe kwakhona emva komsebenzi wokuliphucula nokulixandisa oshiye oomanejala bechulumancile futhi nabantwana beyekile ukufundela kwingxinano.
Oku kuza emva kokuba eli ziko lixhamle kwinkqubo yeNkquleqhu yokuPhuculwa kweZiseko eyenziwa yiFama yoPhehlo-mbane ngoMoya yaseCookhouse (Cookhouse Wind Farm).
IPhakamisani Educare Centre yaseAdelaide iphuculwe futhi yaxandiswa.
Lo msebenzi wokuphuculwa kweli ziko ubuquka ukuphuculwa kwenkqubo yogutyulo lwelindle, ukohlulwahlulwa kwamaziko okufundela nokwakhiwa kwegumbi lokufundela elitsha, phakathi kweminye imisebenzi. 
Balishumi elinesine abantu basekuhlaleni abathe baqashwa kumsebenzi wokuphuculwa nokuxandiswa kweli ziko.
INqununu yeli ziko, uQaqamba Ndunyana, uthi phambi kwalo msebenzi, iziko labo belakhelwe ukwamkela abantwana abangamashumi amane, kodwa bebeye bamkele abangamashumi amahlanu.
“Ikomiti yolawulo kweli ziko ichulumancile malunga nolu phuhliso, nolubangele ukuba eli ziko likwazi ukwamkela ngokukhuselekileyo abantwana abangamashumi amathandathu,” kutsho uNdunyana.
IGosa loNxibelelwano noLuntu kwiFama yoPhehlo-mbane ngoMoya yaseCookhouse, uLifa Baskiti, ucacise ngelithi le projekthi ichaza ingqibelelo malunga nokumelwa xa kuthethwa ngokuxhanyulwa,nanjengoko amaziko aseAdelaide engakhange axhamle kwisigaba sokuqala sale projekthi.
UBaskiti woleke ngelithi, “IFama yoPhehlo-mbane ngoMoya yaseCookhouse iyavuya ngokunceda la maziko ukuze athobele imimiselo nemigangatho ebekwe ngurhulumente,neza kubangela ukuxhamla okuthe xhaxhe kula maziko mayelana nezibonelelo zikarhulumente”.
Noxa nje eli ziko liphuculwe ze laxandiswa ngenkxasomali yeFama yoPhehlo-mbane ngoMoya yaseCookhouse,lo msebenzi ubandakanye uqhogelwano apho kuquka indima edlalwe liSebe loPhuhliso loLuntu, uMasipala waseRaymond Mhlaba,iEarly Inspiration, engabaqeqeshi abancede ekuqulunqeni ingxelo yohlolo lomsebenzi, kwakunye namagosa empilo yokusingqongileyo.
UManejala weMisebenzi yoLuntu kwiFama yoPhehlo-mbane ngoMoya yaseCookhouse, uTshepo Kgoloane, uthi iinjongo zale Nkqubo yoPhuhliso lweZiseko kwiMfundo yooNomngqushwana kukwenza amaziko alungele ukufunda futhi axhase uphuhliso lwabantwana abancinane kuluntu lwaseSomerset East, Cookhouse, Bedford naseAdelaide.

Imbethimanqindi yaseMpuma Koloni ezenzele igama ezizweni, u-Azinga Fuzile, ibuyele ekhaya ekuqaleni kwale veki inyathelela phezulu emva kokuzuza impumelelo ebalulekileyo eMelika. 
UFuzile, 24, ubethe uMartin Ward waseNgilane wemkelwa yingqondo okomzuzwa emlweni obuseLas Vegas ekuseni ngeCawe ephelileyo.
Nangona uWard eye emlweni we-IBF junior lightweight ezithembile neqela lakhe –kodwa bagoduke imisila iphakathi kwamathanga emva kokwiswa kabini ngamanqindi ayingozi yimbethimanqindi yelokishi yaseDuncan Village, eMonti,emjikelweni wesine nakowesixhenxe phambi kokuchithwa kwawo umlo.
Nangona uWard ekwazile ukuhamba umgama obonakalayo emlweni – kodwa uFuzile ebenkqenkqeza phambili ngamanqaku.
Ibikokokuqala uFuzile esilwela eMelika kwaye umsebenze omhle awenzile kungenzeka kumvulele amanye amathuba amanhle anokuthi amkhulise njengembethimanqindi esakhulayo.
Emva komlo, uFuzile uthe akwenze eqongene yinto ebesoloko eyenza xa ezilolonga. 
“Indlela endilwe ngayo, yindlela endizilungiselele ngayo,” utshilo uFuzile emva komlo eMelika. 
“Size apha sisazi ukuba uza kundixhola ngamanqindi. Besinayo indlela yokuphindisa ngayo xa esenza lo nto.
Isicwangciso sethu sisenze kakuhle kakhulu,” utshilo uFuzile, obengakwazi nokuthetha ngenxa yemincili.
Emva komsebenzi ocwengileyo awenze eMelika, ngoku uFuzile ugxeleshe ukudibana nendoda eyakuthi iphumelele phakathi kukaRakhimov noKenechi 
Ogawa emlweni wentshinga ye-IBF engenamntu obekelwe inyanga yeKhala.
UFuzile ufuna uRakhimov kuba efuna ukuziphindezela. URakhimov waseRussia wambetha uFuzile kumjikelo wesibhozo ngo-2019. 
“Ndinqwela kuphumelele uRakhimov ngoba ikhona into ekufuneka siyilungise. Nokuba kuphumelele bani, kodwa ndikulungele ukudibana naye,” utshilo uFuzile.
Impumelelo yakhe iqhwatyelwe izandla nguMphathiswa uFezeka Nkomonye neNkulumbuso uLubabalo Mabuyane.
UZandile Rubushe yimbaleki yemigama emide ehlala eMdantsane, eMonti.
Emva kokupaneka kunyaka ophelileyo ngenxa yeKhorona exikixe ihlabathi lonke, kulo nyaka izinto azifani. 
Nangona umngcipheko wokosulelana kwabantu ngeKhorona usephezulu kwilizwe loMzantsi Afrika – kodwa abakwicandelo lezemidlalo bakwazile ukubuyela kwiindawo zabo zemidlalo ngokwahlukana kwemidlalo abakuyo. 
Iimbaleki zephondo leMpuma Koloni bezidibene kwidolophi yase-Ugie – apho bezikhuphisana kugqatso lweembaleki ekuthiwa yi-Elundini 10km Road Race kwiveki ephelileyo.
Ngenxa yothando nokuzibophelela kwazo ekubalekeni, iimbaleki zizincamile zabaleka engqeleni ebiqhaqhazelisa amazinyo.
UZandile Rubushe, 36, ngomnye weembaleki ezithathe inxaxheba kugqatso obeluse-Ugie kwinqanaba leembaleki ezingaphezulu kwamashumi amathathu anesihlanu eminyaka.
Nangona iimbaleki zaseMpuma Koloni zihamba kwiindawo ngeendawo ekukho kuzo iitumente zeembaleki –kodwa ukuswela nokungafumani kwazo inkxaso zezinye zezinto ezenza ubomi bazo bubenzima kakhulu.
“Ndibaleke kakuhle e-Ugie qha bekubanda kakhulu. Kuyanyanzeleka sibaleke ngoba sifuna ukuphucula amaxesha esiwenze ngaphambili.
Kodwa enye into kukuba sifuna imali ukuze sikwazi ukuzithengela iitenese zokubaleka ngoba asinabo abaxhasi thina,” utshilo uRubushe oqeqeshwa nguLuthando Hejana.
Emva kokungabaleki kunyaka ophelileyo, iimbaleki ziya kwiitumente ezahlukeneyo ngoba zifuna ukunyusa umgangatho phambi kokuya kwimidyarho yeembaleki emikhulu.
“Eyona nto ebendiyifuna kukunyusa isantya endibaleka ngaso ngoba ndilungiselela imidyarho efana neSanlam Marathon neSoweto Marathon,” 
utshilo uRubushe, obuyele eMdantsane nembasa emva kokubamba indawo yesithathu kwi-Elundini 10km Road Race.
“Kumnandi kakhulu kum, ndinamandla kwaye ndingatsho ndithi ndiwulungele umdyarho omkhulu onokuvela ngoku,” utshilo uRubushe, ocela inkxaso koosomashishini nakubo bonke abantu abanokunceda iimbaleki ezidinga izinto zokubaleka.
Lusikisiki – 28 May 2021- UYonela Sompepho waseMasobhuza Primiray School, eLusikisiki, ngomnye wabathathe inxaxheba emidlalweni yeqakamba yabezikolo ekuthiwa yiKFC Mini-Cricket Activation Programme. 
Emva kokunqumama kunyaka ophelileyo ngenxa yeKhorona esagqugqisa ihlabathi, inkqubo yophuhliso yeqakamba ekuthiwa yiKFC Mini-Cricket Activation ibuyile kulo nyaka.
Kwiveki ephelileyo, abantwana bezikolo zaseMpuma Koloni bafumene ithuba lokufunda nokudlala iqakamba namagqala aziwayo afana noMfuneko Ngam noZintle Mali.
Izikolo ezifumene inyhweba yokutyelelwa yiCricket South Africa ibambisene noKFC ziquka i-Old Bunting Junior Secondary School yaseNgqeleni, 
iTiyo Soga Primary School yakuCentane, iMasobhuza Primary School yaseLusikisiki ne-Esitofini Primary School yaseBizana.
Injongo yotyelelo lweCricket South Africa ibikukunika abantwana ithuba lokudlala iqakamba phantsi kweliso elibukhali leencutshwe eziyidlala kwinqanaba eliphezulu.
Konke oko bekusenziwa kubekwe phambili imiqathango yokhuseleko njengokuba ilizwe lisaphethwe mbengane yiKhorona.
Zonke izikolo bezifumene izinto zokuzikhusela kwaye isikolo ngasinye besinomntu oqinisekisa ukuba imithetho iyathotyelwa.
Umququzeleli weCricket SA, uBuhle Motshegoa, uyishiye iMpuma Koloni engawuvali umlomo ngenxa yetalente ayibonileyo.
IMpuma Koloni yenye yeendawo ezivelise abadlali abaphambili kwiqakamba eMzantsi nabazibonakalise kwihlabathi lonke abafana noMakhaya Ntini noMark Boucher.
“Siyavuya ngoba sikwazile ukuqhubela phambili neenkqubo zethu zokudlalisa abantwana ezikolweni.
Kuhle ukubabona bencumile. Siyibone sisafika lo nto apha eNgqeleni.
Wonke umntu ukuvuyele ukubandakanyeka emdlalweni weqakamba esebenzisa izixhobo ezikhoyo. 
Nangona sibadlalisile abantwana – kodwa eyona nto esemqoka kuthi kukuqinisekisa ukuba bayonwaba sibone netalente yabo, emakhwenkweni nasemantombazaneni,” utshilo uMotshegoa.
Injongo yeKFC Mini-Cricket kukukhulisa umdlalo weqakamba ngokuwutyala ebantwaneni bezikolo besebancinane, bawudlale, bawuqhele ukuze bawubone njengowona mdlalo ophambili onokubanika ikamva eliqaqambileyo.
ULebogang Manyama ubuye namagowuli amathathu emdlalweni weDStv Premiership, iKaizer Chiefs ebethe kuwo iGolden Arrows ngo’3-2 eFNB Stadium.
Isekhona intlantsi yethemba kwiKaizer Chiefs emva kokuba ibuye ngasemva yabetha iGolden Arrows ngamagowuli amathathu kwamabini (3-2) emdlalweni obutshisa eFNB Stadium ngolu rhatya. 
ULebogang Manyama liqhawe leChiefs emva lokufaka amagowuli amathathu eyedwa emdlalweni wanamhlanje. 
Le yimpumelelo yokuqala yeChiefs emva kokuba igxothe umqeqeshi wayo, uGavin Hunt, kwiveki ephelileyo okulandele ukubethwa kwayo yiBlack 
Leopards ethotyiselwe kwiGladAfrica Championship emva kokubethwa namhlanje. 
UBruce Bvuma wenze umsebenzi omhle zisuka emdlalweni ngethuba evala ibhola embi ebikhatywe nguKnox Mutizwa.
Ibhalise ebhodini kuqala iGolden Arrows ngebhola efakwe nguMichael Gumede kwisigaba sokuqala. 
Ilinganisile iChiefs ngebhola efakwe nguManyama onikelwe ibhola nguWillard Katsande – obengasadlaliswa kakhulu kusekho uHunt. 
Amaqela omabini aye kwixesha lokuphumla ebambene ngo’1-1 nangona iChiefs ibikhe yanalo ithuba lokufaka elinye igowuli. 
Iphinde yakhokela iGolden Arrows emva kwebhola efakwe ngu-Eric Mathoho ezipalini zakhe. 
UManyama ufake ugowuli lakhe lesibini emva kokunikelwa ibhola entle nguNkosingiphile Ngcobo ongene kwisigaba sesibini somdlalo.
Kuthe xa kushiyeke imizuzu engaphezulu kancinci kweshumi kuphele umdlalo, uManyama ubhakuzelise umnatha okwesithathu atsho Amakhosi anyukela kwindawo yethoba.

iBaroka FC ibethwe yi-Orlando Pirates ngo’2-1, iSuperSport United ibethe iMaritzburg United ngo’2-0, iStellenbosch ibambenge ngeqanda neTS Galaxy kanti yona iChippa United ibambene ngeqanda neTshakhuma FC.Kaizer Chiefs: Bvuma, Zulu, Cardoso, Mathoho, Frosler, Katsande, Baccus, Parker, Manyama, Nurkovic, Castro.

Umdlali weChippa United, u-Oupa Manyisa, uwiswe phantsi emdlalweni weDStv Premiership izolo. Umfanekiso:Sydney Mahlangu/BackpagePix
Amathuba weChippa United okusinda ezembeni xa kuphela isizini ambalwa – kodwa nangani kunjalo, lisekhona elinye ithuba lokubuyela kwiDStv Premiership. 
Iqela likaMnu. Siviwe Mpengesi lizibhaqa lisengxakini emva kokungakwazi kwalo ukuqokelela amanqaku awoneleyo emidlalweni yesizini ephela ngoMgqibelo wale veki. 
Nangona iChippa United izenzele imbali kwiNedbank Cup ebethwe kuyo yiTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila – kodwa ayikwazanga ukuqhuba kakuhle emidlalweni ebalulekileyo yeDStv Premiership. 
Ayikho sengxakini ngenxa yokungabikho kwabadlali, mhlawumbi ingakukungena nokuphuma kwabaqeqeshi eqeleni okwenze abadlali bangakwazi ukwenzaumsebenzi ngendlela eyiyo.
Yathembisa iChippa ekuqaleni kwesini isaphethwe nguLehlohonolo Seema. Wagxothwa emva kwemidlalo emihlanu, kwangena uDan Malesela owayesuka kwiTS Galaxy. 
Wazama naye, kodwa emva kokungabikho kweziphumo ezincumisayo, wakhonjwa emnyango. 
Wafika uVladislav Heric, naye wazama – kodwa wagxothwa kushiyeke imidlalo emibini. 
UPeter Maloisane uxelele iintatheli ukuba iChippa isazimisele ukulwa emidlalweni emibini kule veki. 
Akukho nto enokuyena engako, ngaphandle kokuba amaqela angentla kuyo angabethwa.
UMaloisane uvumile ukuba iChippa incwase ukulwela ukuhlala kwiDStv Premiership ngokulwa emidlalweni yokuxabangela (PSL Playoffs) eza kudlalwa emva kokusongwa kwesizini. 
Ambalwa amathuba weChippa okubetha iSuperSport United emdlalweni wokugqibela eGqeberha ngoba nayo ifuna ukuvala isizini kakuhle. 
Yonke imidlalo yokugqibela iza kuqala ngaxeshanye ngentsimbi yesithathu. 
Akukacaci kekambe ukuba imidlalo yokuxabangela iza kuqala nini ngoba amaqela eGladAfrica asenkundleni emva kokuba iPSL yalile ukunika indebe iRoyal AM kuba iSekhukhune United, ekwindawo yesibini ingazange inikwe amanqaku wayo amathathu.
Imidlalo yeDStv Premiership:Mgqibelo: Mamelodi Sundowns vs Cape Town City @Loftus Stadium; TS Galaxy vs Kaizer Chiefs @Mbombela Stadium; Golden Arrows vs Stellenbosch @Sugar Ray Xulu Stadium, Swallows vs Baroka @Dobsonville Stadium; 
Chippa United vs SuperSport United @Nelson Mandela Bay Stadium; Orlando Pirates vs Tshakhuma FC; Black Leopards vs Bloemfontein Celtic @Thohoyandou Stadium; Maritzburg United vs AmaZulu @Harry Gwala Stadium.
Yiminyaka engaphaya kwesihlanu izinto zingahambi kakuhle kwiKaizer Chiefs. 
Lo nto ayibaphathanga kakuhle abaphathi beChiefs, ingakumbi usihlalo wayo uKaizer Motaung. 
Amakhosi agqibela ukuphakamisa indebe kusekho uStuart Baxter. 
Emva koko kwaqeshwa uSteve Komphela, uGiovanni Solinas, uErnst Middendorp noGavin Hunt – bonke boyisiwa kukunceda iChiefs. 
Aboyiswanga kukubuyisela ubunganga bayo kuphela, boyiswe nakukuyidlalisa umdlalo ocacileyo ebaleni. 
UMotaung watyala imali kwinkqubo yophuhliso kuba efuna kuveliswe abadlali abanokudlalela iChiefs ngendlela yayo. 
Ngenxa yokungaqhubi kakuhle kweChiefs, abadlali abancinane abalifumananga ithuba.
Kwanyanzeleka basasazwe kwamanye amaqela. Izinto ziguqukile ngoku. 
UMotaung uqeshe uMolefi Ntseki njengentloko yenkqubo yophuhliso (Kaizer Chiefs Youth Development Academy) ngoMvulo kule veki. 
Umsebenzi wakhe kukuvelisa abadlali bangomso abaza kubiyisa ubunganga beChiefs. 
UNtseki ufika eNaturena emva kokulaxazwa kwakhe yiSafa ngenxa yokungakwazi kwaBafana Bafana ukuya kwi-Afcon eza kusingathwa yiCameroon kunyaka ozayo.
“Siza kuvelisa abadlali abaza kubeka iKaizer Chiefs endaweni yayo ebholeni. 
Lo nto iza kuqala kubadlali abasakhulayo nabadlali kwiMultiChoice Diski Challenge. 
Abadlali esibavelisileyo baza kunyuselwa kwiqela elikhulu. Kodwa eyona nto ibaluleke kakhulu kum ngumdlali esiza naye kwiChiefs. 
Kufuneka siyazi indlela esebenza ngayo iChiefs ukuze sibe nabadlali abaqaqambileyo kwiChiefs endala,” utshilo uNtseki, ethetha eNaturena. 
Nangona izinto zingamhambelanga kakuhle kwiqela lesizwe uNtseki – kodwa ungomnye wabaqeqeshi abambalwa abafunde kakhulu ngebhola eMzantsi Afrika.
Akuphelelanga apho, usebenze nabadlali abatsha kumaqela esizwe onke. 
Ukunikwa kwakhe umsebenzi wokuvelisa abadlali yiChiefs kumfanele ngokupheleleyo. 
Ethetha ngethuba esamkela uNtseki, uMotaung uthe: “UNtseki ufike ngexesha elihle sisenza iinguqu. 
Siqinisekile ukuba siqeshe umntu olungileyo. Ungumntu osebenze kuzo zonke izigaba zebhola ekhatywayo. 
Njengokuba iChiefs igxothe uHunt kwiveki ephelileyo ngenxa yeziphumo ezibi, kukho into ethi kubuya uBaxter ebekuthiwa ufuna ukuncediswa 
nguNtseki akhe wasebenza naye kwiqela lesizwe. 
Akukacaci ke ngoku kwakwenzeka ntoni njengokuba uNtseki sele enikwe esinye isikhundla.
Namhlanje usihlalo weKaizer Chiefs, uKaizer Motaung, wamkelwe uMolefi Ntseki njengentloko yeYouth Development Academy.
Ezingena ngokuhlwa kwanamhlanje zithi iKaizer Chiefs ibhengeze igama likaMnu. 
uMolefi Ntseki ngengendoda eza kuba yintloko yeYouth Development Academy. 
OkaNtseki utyikitye isivumelwano sengqesho seminyaka emithathu yonke neChiefs. 
Ukuqeshwa kukaNtseki kuza emva kwamahum-hum abethe ndiii kwiveki ephelileyo athi uza kuba ngumncedisi kaStuart Baxter ekuthiwa uza kungena endaweni kaGavin Hunt – ogxothwe kwiveki ephelileyo emva kokuba iChiefs ibethwe yiBlack Leopards ngo’2-1 esemsileni weDStv Premiership nangona (iChiefs) ibiqale yakhokela ngegowuli. 
Iinguqu ezenziwa ngabaphathi beChiefs ngamalungiselelo wesizini ezayo emva kokuba iqhube kakubi kule sizini esongwa ngempelaveki.
“Sivuyiswa kukufika kukaMolefi Ntseki apha kwiKaizer Chiefs. Ufika ngexesha elilungileyo ngoba sizama ukwenza iinguqu ezinyanzelekileyo. 
Sicinga ukuba siqeshe umntu ofanelekileyo ngoba uzihambe zonke izigaba zebhola; ukusukela esikolweni, kwiinkqubo zophuhliso nakumaqela wesizwe,” utshilo uKaizer Motaung.
Sekulithuba elide iChiefs izingela umntu onokuphatha inkqubo yophuhliso equka amaqela wayo wabadlali abasakhulayo nelidlala kwiMultiChoice Diski Challenge. 
UMnu. Ntseki, 51, uyaziwa jiekelele ebholeni yaseMzantsi. Kutshanje uchithwe yiSafa njengomqeqeshi waBafana Bafana emva kokungakwazi ukuya kwi-Afcon ezayo. 
Kulindeleke asebenzisane nomqeqeshi ozayo futhi ibe nguye okhangela abadlali abanokudlalela iChiefs ngokokutsho kukaMotaung.
“Sizimisele ukwenza umsebenzi obonakalayo kwiinkqubo zethu zonke zophuhliso. 
Asizimiselanga ukuphulukana nabadlali abaveliswe yinkqubo yethu yophuhliso. 
Abaqeqeshi bethu bamaqela amancinci benza umsebenzi omhle kakhulu kwaye sifuna ukuyibona iqhubela phambili lo nto. 
Sifuna ukubona abadlali abasakhulayo benyuselwa kwiqela elikhulu ukuze indlela edlala ngayo iChiefs ingaguquki. 
Umfanele lo msebenzi uNtseki ngoba uyazi kakuhle ibhola yale mihla. Sinethemba lokuba uza kusebenzisana nabo bonke abaqeqeshi ukuze iqela libuyele kwindawo yalo ebholeni yaseMzantsi Afrika nakwi-Afrika yonke,” 
utshilo uMotaung, ongakhange ayiphathe ekaStuart Baxter – osenokubhengezwa njengomqeqeshi weChiefs ingaphelanga le veki.
UGavin Hunt ugxothiwe yiKaizer Chiefs. 
Ezingenayo ngorhatywa lwanamhlanje zithi Amakhosi amkhombise umnyango uGavin Hunt, ngoko nangoko! 
Isibhengezo senziwe yiKaizer Chiefs kwikhasi lonzibelelwano, uFacebook, emizuzwini embalwa egqithileyo. 
Oku kwenzeka emva kokungadlali kakuhle kweChiefs phantse yonke isizini ka-2020/21. 
Izizathu zokuchithwa kwakhe azikaziwa – kodwa Amakhosi athe akubuya enze ingxelo egcweleyo ngelinye ixesha. 
“IKaizer Chiefs isiqhawule isivumelwano sengqesho sikaGavin Hunt,” itshilo ingxelo. Izolo elinye, Amakhosi aguqiswe phantsi ngo’2-1 yiBlack Leopards esemsileni.
Phantse yonke isizini esongwayo, iChiefs yoyisakele ukuphumelela imidlalo – ingakumbi xa idlala namaqela amancinci. 
Phantsi kwegama lakhe uHunt, uqeqeshe emidlalweni engamashumi amane anesine. 
Uphumelele ishumi elinambini qha, uphulukene neshumi elinesihlanu waze wadlala ntanganye kwelishumi elinesixhenxe. 
UHunt waqeshwa yiChiefs ekuqaleni kwesini emva kokugxotha uErnst Middendorp – kodwa zange ikwazi ukuthenga abadlali ngenxa yesigwebo seFifa. 
Nangona egxothiwe, uHunt ukwazi ukuyibeka endaweni entle kakhulu iChiefs emidlalweni yeCAF Campions League.
Indebe yeGladAfrica Championship.
Nangona iRoyal AM ivale isizini ikwindawo yokuqala kwiGladAfrica Champions – kodwa ayithwaliswanga isithsaba njengeentshatsheli futhi 
akukabikho nesiqinisekiso esithi iza kunyukela kwiDStv Premiership kwisizini ezayo. 
Emdlalweni wokugqibela, iRoyal AM ibambene ngo’1-1 neCape Town All Stars. 
Kanti yona iSekhukhune United ekwindawo yesibini ingombe iJDR Stars ngo’3-1. 
Emva kwemidlalo yokugqibela, omabini amaqela abange ngelithi aziintshatsheli. 
Yalile iPremier Soccer League ukunika iRoyal AM indebe kuba isithi kusekho umba weSekhukhune ongekasonjululwa. 
Ingxaki yaqala emdlalweni owawuphakathi kwePolokwane City neSekhukhune kwinyanga yoMqungu kulo nyaka.
Ingxelo ithi iPolokwane yophula umthetho wePSL onyanzelisa inani elithile labadlali abangaphantsi kwamashumi amabini anesithathu emdlalweni. 
Ikomiti yoluleko yoxutha amanqaku amathathu kwiPolokwane – kodwa isimanga, loo manqaku zange anikwe iSekhukhune eyabethwa ngo’1-0 kula mdlalo. 
Yabhena iSekhukhune. Saphumelela isibheno sayo – kodwa isimanga esenzekayo, iPSL zange iwabale amanqaku wayo amathathu. Kukho loo 
ngxubakaxaka ekulindeleke ukuba isonjululwe yinkundla emva kokuba iPSL ingazithobelanga iziphumo zenkqubo yesibheno.
Noxa iSekhukhune ikwindawo yesibini – kodwa ithi yiyo efanele ukuya kwiDStv Premiership ngoba inamanqaku amathathu iPSL esawankonyileyo. 
Asicaci esona sizathu esibangele iPSL ingayiniki amanqaku wayo iSekhukhune. 
Oku kunyanzele iSekhukhune ibhenele enkundleni ukuze inikwe amanqaku wayo amathathu. 
Ingqonyela yeSouth African Football Association (Safa), uTebogo Motlanthe, uthe iPSL kufanele isithobele isigqibo esathathwa kwinkqubo yezibheno ngoba esa sigqibo ngeke siguqulwe. 
“Isigqeba esiphethe iPSL asikwazi ukuguqula isigqibo senkqubo yoluleko. Yinkundla enokuyenza lo nto,” utshilo uMotlanthe.

Imbethimanqindi yaseMpuma Koloni ephambili, uAzinga “Golden Boy” Fuzile, intingele eMelika – apho iyokulungiselela umlo obalulekileyo. 
UFuzile, 24, uzimisele ukumbetha anxile anxile uMartin Ward aza kulwa naye eLas Vegas ekuseni ngeCawe. 
Le mbethimanqindi yaseDuncanvillage ifulathele uMzantsi Afrika iphelekwa nguTeris Ntuthu – umthelekisi ophethe iRumble Boxing Africa Promotions. 
Uhambe kakuhle kekambe uFuzile ngoba unikwe amazwi enkuthazo yiNkulumbuso yaseMpuma Koloni, uMnu. 
Oscar Lubabalo Mabuyane, emnqwenelele okuhle kodwa eluhambeni lwakhe.
Umlo ophakathi kukaFuzile noWard ungokufumana ilungelo lokulwela intshinga ye-IBF junior-lightweight. 
Ngaphandle kwamathandabuzo, uFuzile zimvuyisile iindaba zokunikwa kukaMnu. Mzamo Njekanye amaphephamvume okungena eMelika. 
Ebeshiyekile yena ngoba enganikwanga ilungelo lokungena eMelika enemiqathango engqingqwa ngelixesha leKhorona.
UNjekanye uza kuqinisekisa ukuba imbethimanqindi yakhe iya emfazweni ngeCawe ikwisimo esiyilungeleyo. 
“Ndivuye kakhulu emva kokufumana imvume yokuya eMelika. 
Nayo inkwenkwe yam yonwabile ngoba iyazi ukuba ndiza kuba secaleni kwayo xa isilwa. 
Amalungiselelo sawagqiba kudala. Kudala sazilungiselela kwaye ndisatsho, umlo siwulungele. 
Siyokulwela impumelelo eMelika,” utshilo kumajelo eendaba uNjekanye phambi kokufulathela uMzantsi Afrika.
Nangona uFuzile esabethwe kanye nguShavkat Rakhimov – kodwa kwakufuneka azimisele ngoba uWard akalilo ifokofoko. 
Phantsi kwegama lakhe uWard, 29, uwise amadoda alishumi elinanye emilweni engamashumi amabini anesine, ubethwe komnye waze wadlala ntanganye kwemibini. 
Yena uFuzile uwise amadoda asibhozo emidlalweni yakhe elishumi elinanye. 
“Uyimbethimanqindi enenqindi elihle, ephephayo futhi ekwaziyo ukuzikhusela – kodwa ndiza kuba ngaphezulu kuye,” utshilo uWard kwiNation phambi komlo.
Ubuyele kwiCape Town City kwakhona uEric Tinkler njengomqeqeshi wayo omtsha.
Emva kokushiya iCape Town City kwisizini ka-2016-17, uEric Tinkler ubuyele kuyo ekuqaleni kwale veki. 
UTinkler, 50, uzibophelele kwiqela laseKapa emva kokugxothwa kukaJan Olde Riekerink ngenxa yeziphumo ezingancumisiyo. 
Yena uTinkler ubuyela ebholeni emva kokudinga umsebenzi iinyanga eziliqela ukuseka oko wagxothwa yiMaritzburg United ebiyiqeqesha ekuqaleni kwesizini eqhubekayo. 
Akothusanga ukubuyela kwakhe kwiqela likaJohn Comitis ngoba kulapho uTinkler waphumelela indebe yeTelkom Knockout okokuqala njengomqeqeshi. Uthembise ngokuphumelela ezinye iindebe kwiCity.
“Kundichulumancise kakhulu ukubuyela kwiCape Town City. 
Ndaqhuba kakuhle kakhulu apha ngo-2016 kwaye ndiseneenkumbulo zezinto esazenzayo. 
Liqhube kakuhle iqela naphantsi kukaBenni McCarthy ngoba liphumelele indebe yeMTN8. 
Kodwa ke ngoku, ndibuyile kwaye ndifuna ukuphumelela ezinye iindebe. Inawo amandla okuyenza lo nto iCape Town City,” utshilo uTinkler.
Njengokuba uTinkler efike isizini seyisongwa, akulindelekanga nto kakhulu kuye emidlalweni eshiyekileyo ngaphandle kokuqinisekisa ukuba iCape Town City ibethelela indawo yayo kwiTop 8. 
Nangani kunjalo, umqeqeshi unezinto afuna ukuzibethelela ebadlalini bakhe abaza kufika phambi kokuqala kwesizini elandelayo. 
“Sifuna ukuguqula indlela abacinga ngayo abadlali abaza kwiCape Town City. Kufuneka baqonde ukuba iCape Town City ayoleli yokuya kumaqela abhetele ngoba liqela elifuna ukuphumelela iindebe. 
Abadlali kufuneka beze kuyo benalo nto ezingqondweni zabo,” utshilo uTinkler.
Izinto zamhambela kakubi umqeqeshi ogxothiweyo mhla iCape Town City yabethelwa ekhaya ngo’5-1 ngaMaZulu aqeqeshwa nguMcCarthy – enye yezinto ezabhenca ukungalawuleki kakuhle kwabadlali. 
Emva kokushiya iCape Town City, uTinkler waphumelela indebe yeMTN8 kwiSuperSport United awayisa kwisigaba sokugqibela seConfederation Cup kwangonyaka omnye.
Umqeqeshi weqela lesizwe loMzantsi Afrika labadlali abaselula, uDavid Notoane, uwabizile amagama wabadlali abangamashumi amabini anesihlanu aza kuya nabo emidlalweni ye-Olimpiki. 
Kwiveki ezayo, uMzantsi Afrika (Under-23) kulindeleke ube yinxalenye yetumente yamazwe afana neBrazil, iArgentina neKorea eza kubanjelwa eDubai ukusukela ngomhla wesihlanu ukuya ngoweshumi elinanye kwinyanga yeSilimela. 
UNotoane uya kusebenzisa itumente eqala kwiveki ezayo njengesixhobo sakhe sokulola amakhwenkwe wakhe phambi kokuya eJapan eza kusingatha imidlalo ye-Olimpiki kulo nyaka.
Abadlali abachongiweyo ngumxube wabadlali abadlalela amaqela alapha eMzantsi Afrika namanye aseYurophu. 
“Itumente esiya kuyo eDubai iza kuba sisiqalo samalungiselelo wethu wemidlalo ye-Olimpiki,” utshilo uNotoane, emva kokubhengeza amagama wabadlali azimisele ukulwa ngabo eJapan kwindibano ebiseGoli ngoLwesibini. 
Okusemqoka kumqeqeshi kukuzama ukudibanisa abadlali bakhe abadlala eMzantsi Afrika nabo badlala kumazwe ohlukeneyo eYurophu ixesha lisamvumela. 
Abadlali boMzantsi Afrika baza kufumana uvavanyo lokwenyani njengokuba beza kudibana neBrazil, iKorea ne-Argentina ngoba loo mazwe anabadlali abasemgangathweni ophezulu.
“Siza kuzama ukusebenzisa itumente esiya kuyo njengeqonga lokudibanisa abadlali abasuka phesheya nabalapha ukuze siqinisekise ukuba sihamba sineqela elomeleleyo. 
Sinethemba lokuba sakubafumana bonke abadlali abachongiweyo ngoba lo nto iza kusinika ithuba lokujonga ukulungelwa kwethu imidlalo ye-Olimpiki,” utshilo uNotoane. 
Amazwe ehlabathi aza kudibana eJapan emidlalweni ye-Olimpiki ekulindeleke iqale ngomhla wamashumi amabini anesithathu kwinyanga yeKhala ukuya ngomhla wesibhozo kweyeThupha nangona kukho abantu abathi mayimiswe ngenxa yeKhorona.
Umdlali webhola ekhatywayo, uEsam Ngqumshe, nomqeqeshi wakhe omtsha we-Ayakha Stars. 
Ngethuba iqala ukudlala ibhola ezitalatweni intwazana yaseMandela, eMthatha, zange icinga ukuba ngenye imini iza kudlala ibhola kwinqanaba eliphezulu. 
Oku kwenzeke kuEsam Ngqumshe, 12, odlalela iqela elikwiSafa Sasol Women’s League ekudlala kuyo amaqela ephondo leMpuma Koloni.

kwiJubase Academy – eyasungulwa nguHoseya Jubase kwiminyaka egqithileyo eMandela. 
Yifolosi eza kunceda uMzantsi Afrika ngenye imini uNgqumshe ukuba uqhubela phambili nendlela adlala ngayo. 
“Kumnandi ukudlala ibhola ekhatywayo,” utshilo uNgqumshe, ngokukhulu ukuzithemba ethetha neli phephandaba.
“Ndiqale ukudlala ibhola esitalatweni apha eMandela phambi kokuya kwiJubase Academy. 
Kundivuyise kakhulu ukuthathwa yi-Ayakha Stars ngoba bendingazazi ukuba ndakude ndifike kwinqanaba endikulo. 
Ndamkelwe kakuhle kuyo kwaye nomqeqeshi uthi ufuna ukundibona ndiphumelele,” utshilo uNgqumshe. 
Kule sizini, uNgqumshe uthi sele efake amagowuli amane emidlalweni emihlanu. 
Ngumsebenzi omhle kakhulu lowo kwaye uyamkhuthaza ngoba ufuna ukudlalela iqela lesizwe. 
“Ndifuna ukudlalela aBanyana Banyana ebomini bam,” utshilo uNgqumshe, owothuse abantu abaninzi kuquka nomama wakhe. 
Inkqubela eyenziwe yile ntwazana efunda uGrade 6, eSiyalakha Christian School, izise uvuyo emzini wakwaNgqumshe.
“Ewe, umntana wam uyayidlala ibhola. Abantu abaninzi bathi uyidlala ngathi yinkwenkwe. 
Le yokuba uyintombazana abayithembi ncam. Kuyandivuyisa ukudlala kwakhe ibhola ngoba bendikade ndisithi yinto nje yasesitalatweni. 
Sothukile xa enyukela kwizinga eliphezulu,” utshilo umama wakhe, uNosipho Ngqumshe.

Nangona efuna impumelelo eSandton Convention Centre – kodwa uMbumbulwana uyakwazi ukubaluleka kokuzilungiselela.

Umqeqeshi we-Al Ahly, uPitso “Jingles” Mosimane, ubuyele kwilizwe lakwaFaro ekhathazekile ngenxa yabalandeli beMamelodi Sundowns abamthuke ngonina. 
Oku kwenzeke phambi komdlalo weCAF Champions League obuphakathi kweSundowns ne-Al Ahly ophele ingu’1-1 eLucas Moripe Stadium elanga phezolo. 
Iqela likaPitso liye ladlulela phambili ngoba liyibethe ngo’2-0 iSundowns emdlalweni obuseCairo kwiveki ephelileyo. 
Abalandeli beSundowns bashicelelwe ngomnxeba ophathwayo betherhe phambi kweBhasi ebikhwelise abadlali be-Al Ahly bebephethe amaphekepheke amakhalibhothi abhalwe izithuzo ezijoliswe kuPitso. 
Emva komdlalo, uPitso uvakalise ukukhathazeka kwakhe yindlela aphatheke ngayo elizweni lakhe. 
Ukusukela oko wathatha iintambo njengomqeqeshi we-Al Ahly, uPitso ebeqala ukubuyela eMzantsi Afrika.
“Ndiye ndaphazamiseka kakhulu emoyeni wam xa ndibona abantu bephakamise amakhalibhothi andithuka ngomama. 
Ndizibuze umbuzo: Yintoni endingayenzanga (kwiSundowns) ukuze ndingahlonipheki ngolu hlobo? 
Kodwa ke ndiyazazi izinto zebhola. 
Ndiyamazi umntu owenza le nto kwiSundowns. Kuninzi endingakuthetha kodwa ke sobe ndithethe,” utshilo uPitso, obenxubile noxa iAl Ahly iyifumene into ebiyifuna eMzantsi Afrika. 
Emva kokushiya iSundowns kunyaka ophelileyo, kwabakho iingxelo ezithi bekukho ukungaboni ngasonye phakathi kwakhe nabantu abathile. 
“Ndifumene imiyalezo emibi kakhulu ukusukela oko ndifikile eMzantsi Afrika. Lo miyalezo ibisuka emntwini okwiSundowns – hayi abalandeli bayo. 
Kukhe kwakho nezinto ezibhaliweyo ezisuka emagqwetheni ezimalunga nendlela endahamba ngayo. 
Ezo izinto ndizibekele incwadi yam kwaye zakubaliswa ngenye imini,” utshilo uPitso.
Ngentsasa yanamhlanje, iSundowns isixolisele isenzo esibi esenziwe ngabalandeli bayo kuPitso Mosimane. 
“Sifumene izikhalazo ezingokuziphatha kakubi nezithukho ezikhutshwe ngabalandeli beSundowns. 
Abalandeli beSundowns akufanelanga bageze okanye bathuke nokuba ngubani ngendlela abenze ngayo ngoba oko kuyakhabana nendlela yokuziphatha kwethu. 
Siyaxolisa kwi-Al Ahly nakubo bonke abachaphazelekileyo,” itshilo igxelo ebhaliweyo, elebele ngelithi iSundowns iza kuba khangela bonke abathuke uPitso futhi iza kubathathela amanyathelo. 
Eminyakeni esibhozo, uPitso uncede iSundowns yaphumelela iindebe ze-Absa Premiership, iTelkom Knockout, iNedbank Cup, iCAF Champions League neSuper Cup.

SOUTH AFRICA -Lusikisiki – 28 May 2021- UYonela Sompepho waseMasobhuza Primiray School, eLusikisiki, ngomnye wabathathe inxaxheba emidlalweni yeqakamba yabezikolo ekuthiwa yiKFC Mini-Cricket Activation Programme. 
Emva kokunqumama kunyaka ophelileyo ngenxa yeKhorona esagqugqisa ihlabathi, inkqubo yophuhliso yeqakamba ekuthiwa yiKFC Mini-Cricket Activation ibuyile kulo nyaka. 
Kwiveki ephelileyo, abantwana bezikolo zaseMpuma Koloni bafumene ithuba lokufunda nokudlala iqakamba namagqala aziwayo afana noMfuneko Ngam noZintle Mali. 
Izikolo ezifumene inyhweba yokutyelelwa yiCricket South Africa ibambisene noKFC ziquka i-Old Bunting Junior Secondary School yaseNgqeleni, iTiyo Soga Primary School yakuCentane, iMasobhuza Primary School yaseLusikisiki ne-Esitofini Primary School yaseBizana.
Injongo yotyelelo lweCricket South Africa ibikukunika abantwana ithuba lokudlala iqakamba phantsi kweliso elibukhali leencutshwe eziyidlala kwinqanaba eliphezulu. 
Konke oko bekusenziwa kubekwe phambili imiqathango yokhuseleko njengokuba ilizwe lisaphethwe mbengane yiKhorona. 
Zonke izikolo bezifumene izinto zokuzikhusela kwaye isikolo ngasinye besinomntu oqinisekisa ukuba imithetho iyathotyelwa. 
Umququzeleli weCricket SA, uBuhle Motshegoa, uyishiye iMpuma Koloni engawuvali umlomo ngenxa yetalente ayibonileyo. 
IMpuma Koloni yenye yeendawo ezivelise abadlali abaphambili kwiqakamba eMzantsi nabazibonakalise kwihlabathi lonke abafana noMakhaya Ntini noMark Boucher.
“Siyavuya ngoba sikwazile ukuqhubela phambili neenkqubo zethu zokudlalisa abantwana ezikolweni. 
Kuhle ukubabona bencumile.

NOXA nje phantse omnye kwabo balishumi abafikisayo eMzantsi Afrika ebhubha ngenxa yokuzibulala, umngcipheko ungaphaya kokuqonda kulutsha oluguquke ngokwesini (transgender), noluye lungafumani nkxaso oluyifunayo.
Ukuguquka ngokwesini (transgender) kuxa ubani eziva engakhululekanga ngokwesini sakhe sokuzalwa, ze aguqukele kwesi angazalwanga esiso.
Ukungcikivwa kwabantu ngenxa yesini sabo akwamkelekanga, batsho abasemagunyeni UMFANEKISO: USELUGCINWENI
Ingxelo ithi abantu abaguquke ngokwesini bakumngcipheko omandla weemeko zokuphazamiseka kwengqondo ezifana nomvandedwa okanye ukusebenzisa gwenxa iziyobisi, apho isiqingatha sabantu abadala abaguquke ngokwesini baye babeneengcinga zokuzibulala ze abanye babo (1/3) bazame ukuzibulala.
“Kubalulekile ukwazi ukuba ukuzichaza njengoguquke ngokwesini, ayikokugula ngengqondo,” kutsho uNjingalwazi Gerhard Grobler, ugqirha wengqondo obesakuba nguMongameli weSouth African Society of Psychiatrists (SASOP).
“Ulutsha oluzichaza njengoluguquke ngokwesini lungagagana nomvandedwa, ukonyuka komngcipheko wokuzonzakalisa ngenxa yokubekwa ibala, ukungamkeleki, ingcinga yokuba bafihla eyona nyaniso ngendlela abayiyo, ukuzijongela phantsi, ukuzikhetha bucala, ukungcikivwa nokuxhatshazwa,” utshilo uGrobler.
Le mingcipheko, ngokokutsho kukaGrobler, iyehla xa ulutsha oluguquke ngokwesini lufumana inkxaso ekuhlaleni nangokothuthuzelo lomphefumlo.
UGrobler uthi ukuguquka ngokwesini “asiyonto entsha” kuba kudala abantu bakwenza oko kwiintlanga zonke ehlabathini kuquka naseAfrika.
Lo Njingalwazi ukugxininisile ukuba ukuzichaza ngesini esithile kwanendlela ozikhethela ngayo indlela yokwabelana ngesondo, zizinto ezahlukeneyo.
“Ukuzichaza ngokwesini yindlela ubani asiva ngayo ngaphakathi isini sakhe, sokuba uyindoda okanye umfazi okanye ongenanto yakwenza nezozini zibini (indoda nomfazi). 
Ukuzikhethela indlela yokwabelana ngokwesondo kuchaza indlela ubani atsaleka ngayo ngokomzimba, uthando kwanomphefumlo, kwaye oko akuphehlwa ngasini somnye umntu. 
Abantu abaguquke ngokwesini (transgender), ingangabantu abasitreyithi, abaziigeyi, abanomdla kwizini ezahlukeneyo (bisexual) okanye abantu abangenamdla kwezesondo (asexual),” utshilo uGrobler.
UGrobler ugqabaze izinto ezibalulekileyo kubazali, iintsapho kwanabahlobo bolutsha oluguquke ngokwesini.
La magqabaza aquka: ukwazi inguquko ngokwesini yomntu nendlela azikhethela ukuphila ngayo ngokwesini; thetha nesikolo okanye iziko ngemeko neemfuno zomntwana wakho, kodwa imvume iphume emntwaneni; hlonipha ubomi babucala bomntwana wakho; sukunyanzelisa umntwana ukuba enze izinto ngendlela ethile okanye anxibe ngendlela ethile; funa inkxaso kwingcaphephe ejongene nezengqondo ingakumbi lowo ujongene ncakasana nabantwana kuquka nabo bafikisayo; sukumcingela umntwana wakho malunga nemidla yakhe kwezesondo; zifundise malunga nemiba kwanamalungelo wabo baguquke ngokwesini (transgender).
Ethetha eBotshabelo eFreyistata ngoLwesibini, uSuku lweNkululeko, uMongameli Cyril Ramaphosa uthe: 
“Njengelizwe kufuneka sikuheshe ukungcikivwa nokungamkelwa koluntu lweLGBTQI+ (Lesbian, Gay, Bisexual, Transgender, Queer and Intersex +). 
Kwezi nyanga zidlulileyo, kubekho izehlo zolwaphulomthetho ezibini ngakumalungu olu luntu, kuquka nokubulawa. 
Le yinto ekufanele ukuba siziva sinentloni ngayo sisisizwe.”
“Ndifuna ukuthumela umyalezo ongqongqo wokuba ulwaphulomthetho olujoliswe kwintiyo alusokuze lunyanyezelwe kuluntu lwethu kwaye abo benza olu lwaphulomthetho baza kufunyanwa futhi bajongane nengalo yomthetho,” utshilo uRamaphosa.

I-Inkululeko isebenza noluntu lwaseMakhanda ekuchongeni imiceli mngeni kunye namathuba kwezemfundo kwaye isebenza ngaphakathi kwezakhelo ezikhoyo kunye neenkqubo zokujongana nale mingeni nokuxhamla kuloo mathuba.

I-Inkululeko uyakonwabela ukusebenzisana ne-Rhodes University Office ye-Community Engagement kunye noPhuhliso lwezeNtlalontle ukufumana abafundisi abakumgangatho ophezulu bokusebenza nomntu ngamnye wolutsha lwe-Inkululeko. 
Ikwasebenzisana namanye amaziko angenzi nzuzo eMakhanda asebenza nabantwana ekwabelaneni ngezimvo, izibonelelo kunye nokuqonda.
Inkululeko isebenzisene kakhulu neYunivesithi yaseSyracuse eSyracuse, eNew York, kwiDyunivesithi yaseMichigan, eAnn Arbor eMichigan, kwiKholeji yaseBloomfield eBloomfield, eNew Jersey, kwiYunivesithi yaseOxford e-United Kingdom kunye nabafundi  namavolontiya  efakhalthi abasebenza eMakhanda.
Ixabiso lethu kunye nemigaqo ekhokelayo.
I-Inkululeko iyayiqonda into yokuba wonke umntu unelungelo lokuqhuba imfundo ekumgangatho ophezulu ebalungiselela ukuya eyunivesithi okanye ukungena kwicandelo lomsebenzi awuthandayo.
I-Inkululeko iyaqonda ukuba iyantlukwano kwezentlalo nezoqoqosho imile ngenxa yesiphumo socalucalulo. 
Oku kungafaniyo kwezoqoqosho nakwezentlalo kungaliwa nemfundo kunye nethuba elikuzisayo ngokuvumela ulutsha-oluzelwe kuMzantsi Afrika omtsha, olawulwa ngentando yesininzi-ukuba alandele amaphupha abo emfundo ephakamileyo kwaye azibonelele kunye neentsapho zabo.
I-Inkululeko ikholelwa ukuba abantu abahluphekileyo bahluphekile-kodwa bayakwazi ukuphumelela. 
Ukubonelela ngamathuba, inkxaso kunye nokudumisa abantu ukuba baqhubeke nemfundo yabo kunokuba nefuthe elikhulu kwindlela abantu abazijonga ngayo, kwaye, nakwindlela abajonga ngayo oko kunokwenzeka ebomini babo.
Iyunithi yeshishini lase-Inkululeko eMakhanda, eMzantsi Afrika isungule ekuqaleni kuka-2016, ngenxa yenkxaso-mali yembewu evela kwiJohn Ben Snow Memorial Trust.

Ukusukela ngelo xesha, iyunithi ixhaswe yi-The Learning Trust kunye neDewan Family Foundation.
Uluvo lweli shishini lwentlalo luphume kwikhosi yentsebenziswano kunye neWhiteman School of Management kwiYunivesithi yaseSyrause.

Phambi kokuvulwa kweCommon Ground, bekukho amathuba amancinci kakhulu kubantu abancinci ukuba bazibandakanye ngokuqinisekileyo, kwimeko abahlala kuyo.
Ngelixa kukho iindawo ezininzi zentselo, akukho mabala okudlala. 
Ngelixa kukho iivenkile ezininzi ezithengisa utywala, zimbalwa iikhefi.
Uluntu lwaselokishini esisebenza kulo luxineke kakhulu. 
Ukuba nendawo ekhuselekileyo, emema abantu abancinci- kwaye eyilelwe ngabantu abancinci- ukuba beze, (bengaselanga tywala kwaye bengasebenzisanga ziyobisi) xa bedlala umdlalo webhodi, ukuthatha inxaxheba kwitumente yebhola ekhatywayo, okanye ukuya kwi-intanethi zifuneka kakubi kuluntu esisebenza Phakathi kulo.
Wenze kakuhle ukufumana isixhobo sakho sokuncedisa ukuva. 
Eli linyathelo lokuqala ekuncedeni ukuba uve ngcono.
Kwiiveki ezintandathu ezizayo sizakuthumela imifanekiso, amanqaku elizwi, imiyalezo kwaye sikutsalele umnxeba ukuze sikuncede uqhelane nokusebenzisa isixhobo sakho sokuva. 
Ezi ngcebiso zizakunceda ukuba usebenzise isixhobo sakho sokuva ngendlela eyiyo.
Awukho wedwa! Ngaphazu kwezigidi ezingama-466 zabantu jikelele ezweni banengxaki yongeva kwaye ngumntu omnye kubantu abathathu, abakwiminyaka engaphezu ku65. 
Ukufumana izixhobo zokuncedisa linyathelo lokuqala ukuze ukwazi ukuva ngcono. 
Kwiveki yokuqala, lindela umyalezo ntsuku zonke. 
Izakunceda lo nto noqhelana nezixhobo zakho zokuva.
Namhlanje sizaku cacisela ukuba zinxitywa njani izixhobo zokuva. 
Sebenzisa isipili ukuze ubone uzinxiba kakuhle na izixhobo zakho zokuva.
Inqanaba 1: Phambi kokuba siqale- jonga izixhobo zakho zokuva indawo (apho ufaka khona ibhetri) nethumbu. 
Ekugqibeleni kwe thumbu kukho iplastiki engqukuva. 
Ibizwa ngokuba yi-dome. Ukuba unezixhobo ezibini, jonga le plastiki ingaphambili ibizwa ngokuba yi-tip/incam yethumbu. 
Ekhohlo iphawulwe ngombala ohlaza okwesibhakabhaka, kwaye eyasekunene iphawulwe ngombala obomvu.
Inqanaba 2: Beka umzimba wesixhobo emva kwendlebe yakho. 
Yifake ngocoselelo i-dome phakathi endlebeni yakho uqinisekise ukuba ingene phakathi ukuze ingataki, iphume.
Inqanaba 3: Kukho icingo leplastiki elongezelelweyo elinceda ithumbu lihlale endaweni yalo. 
Kufuneka ifakwe kwibhakethi eliyinxalenye lelungu lendlebe. 
Jonga kumfanekiso esikuthumelele wona. 
Ukuba isixhobo sakho sokuva awusinxibanga kakuhle, awuzokuziva kakuhle iizandi. 
Cela uncedo kwizihlobo zakho okanye utsalele thina ukuba unemibuzo.
Xa ufumana isixhobo sokuva, kuza kuvakala ngokwa hlukileyo xa uqala. 
Kungoba ingqondo yakho ngoku iva iizandi eyazigqibela kudala ukuziva. 
Qala ngokunxiba izixhobo zakho zokuva kwi yure ezimbalwa ngosuku ngalinye, ude uqhelane nazo uzinxibe usuku lonke.
Namhlanje siza kuthetha ngoku nakekela izixhobo zokuva.  
Ezi zixhobo ziyabiza kakhulu kungoko kufanele uzinakekele ngamaxesha onke. 
Zigcine zomile ngamaxesha onke izixhobo zakho zokuva. 
Amanzi okanye imiphula ingazo nakalisa izixhobo zakho zokuva.  
Zikhuphe izixhobo zakho zokuva xa usemvuleni uzifake entweni eyomileyo. 
Khupha ibhetri ufake izixhobo zakho zokuva kwi nkonxa eyomileyo. 
Shiya amacango ezixhobo zakho evulekile. Gcina izixhobo zakho kwindawo ekhuselekileyo uzibeke kude ebantwaneni, okanye kwindawo ezinobiwa kuyo. 
Ukuba wenze yonke le nto, izixhobo zakho ziyakuhlala ixesha elide kwaye zisebenze ngcono.
Ekuseni faka ibhetri kwisixhobo sokuva usivale ukugqiba kwakho. 
Vala isandla sakho entla kwesixhobo sakho sokuva usibambe usisondeze entla kwendlebe yakho. 
Ukuba isixhobo sakho senza ingxolo, ibhetri iyaphela kuyanyanzeleka ufake entsha. 
Ufaka ibhetri entsha:  Vula isiciko sebhetri, thatha endala uyikhuphe. 
Susa iphepha kwibhetri entsha. 
Icala elisicwecwe lingu (+) icala. 
Faka ibhetri entsha kwisivalo. 
Qinisekisa (+) ubuso bujonge phezulu. 
Vala ucango lwebhetri. 
Isixhobo sokuva sizakwenza ingxolo xa ucango lebhetri luvaliwe nebhetri entsha ifakiwe.
Namhlanje siza kufunda ukuba sisebenza njani isixhobo sokuva. 
Isixhobo sokuncedisa ukuva singumatshini osebenza njenge TV okanye imfonomfono. 
Ifuna ukugcinwa ikhuselekile. Kufuneka ibekwe kude kwindawo etshisayo efana nelanga, nakwi ndawo ebandayo njenge sikhencezisi. 
Isixhobo esi sisebenza ngokutsala ingxolo iyenze ivakale ikhwaze. 
Isixhobo esi asizubuyisa indlela ubusiva ngayo kuqala kodwa sizakwenza uve ngcono.
Ingoma kaLefa Mosea ethi Naha ya rona, yingoma ethetha ngokumanyana singama-Afrika kwaye sibuke ubuhle bezwekazi lethu.
UMosea, 34, owenza isidanga somculo iBmus(ed) eNelson Mandela University, eGqeberha, wazalelwa eSebokeng eVaal, waze kamva wafudukela ePitoli nekulapho akhulele khona.
Encokolela I’solezwe, uMosea uthi ePitoli kulapho italente yakhe yomculo yaqala khona, waze wazifundisa ukubetha isiginci ngo2003.
Phantsi kweliso elibukhali lomhlohli wakhe wezomculo, uMosea waye wadlala le katali ngelixa efunda amabanga akhe aphakamileyo esikolweni, de wabe kanti ufikelela kwimatriki ngo2005.
Ngenxa yothando lwakhe lomculo, uye wazibhaqa ephakathi eVusi Mahlasela Music Development Foundation eState Theatre ePitoli. 
Apho udibene nesixhobo sesaksofoni asithanda kunene kodwa ekwakunzima ukuba abe naso ngaphambili ngenxa yokuswela imali.
“Ukufika kwam eGqeberha eMpuma Koloni ndidibene neemvumi eziselula saze senza iqela elibizwa iTake Note. 
Ngo2011 iTake Note yatyikitywa phantsi kweNative Rhythms kaSipho Sithole,” kubalisa uMosea.
Ekunye neTake Note, uMosea unyathele kumaqonga amakhulu, esingabalula kuwo iStandard Bank Joy of Jazz, iUgu Jazz Festival, iEbubeleni, iNational Arts Festival neBuyelekhaya.
Emva kokusebenza ithuba elide neTake Note besabelana ngeqonga neemvumi ezinkulu zoMzantsi Afrika, uMosea uye wakhupha ingoma ebizwa Mabele ngo2017, walandelisa ngethi Naha ya rona ngo2020.
UNaha ya rona uthetha “ilizwe lethu” ngolwimi lwesiXhosa. 
Ezi ibe zingoma zakhe zokuqala njengemvumi ezimeleyo.
Iingoma zikaMosea zohlobo lweAfro-Jazz nazicula ngolwimi lwesiSotho ubukhulu becala, zithetha ngemanyano, ubuAfrika nobuntu.
“Ndikwathetha nangeemeko zobomi, ingakumbi izinto endinamava wazo,” kutsho uMosea.
Kutshanje ukhuphe icwecwe lakhe elineengoma ezilishumi. Kweli cwecwe, elibizwa Double Standards, usebenze neemvumi ezinjengoZim Ngqawana 
Jnr, uDongadala Bemdiliza noSiyabulela Mdebele.
“[Kweli cwecwe] ndithetha ngohlobo emasizixhobise ngalo singama-Afrika. Ngokuzixhobisa andithethi ngokuya esikolweni kuphela, kodwa sifumane okulele kumhlaba weAfrika,” kutsho uMosea okwangutata wabantwana ababini.
Uthi ngokusebenzisa ulwimi lwakokwabo lwesiSotho ezingomeni zakhe uzama ukugcina olu lwimi luphila.
Simbuza ngokuthethwa luSuku lweAfrika kuye, uthe: “Usuku lweAfrika lusuku lokuzikhangela ukuba singoobani njengama-Afrika kwaye sakuzifumana siqale apho ukuzakha.
Ikopi yecwecwe iyafumaneka kuMosea okanye uzithengele kwiivenkile zomculo kwi-intanethi.

NGOMSO, uLwesihlanu umhla we7 kuCanzibe 2021, yeyokuqala iEbubeleni Fashion Show eGqeberha.
IEbubeleni Fashion Show yokuqala kulo nyaka iyinxalenye yokubhiyozela iminyaka elishumi eqhuba umnyhadala womculo weEbubeleni eMpuma Koloni.
Umnyhadala we-Ebubeleni khange uqhutywe phambi komndilili kunyaka ophelileyo ngenxa yentsholongwane yekhorona. 
Lo mnyhadala uye waqhutywa kumabonakude.
Abaququzeleli balo mnyhadala bathi kulindeleke nangomso kube kuhle kwiqonga leFashoni yeEbubeleni.
“Ngethuba kuvalwe zonke iingcango zolonwabo kunyaka ophelileyo, iEbubeleni yeza nomnyhadala womculo owaboniswa ngobuxhakaxhaka bale mihla nakumabonakude, waze watsala ababukeli abangaphaya kwe400 000. 
Eli qondo kulindeleke libuye nakwiFashion Show ngomso,” kutsho abaququzeleli.
IEbubeleni Fashion Show iza kubanjelwa kwisakhiwo iTramways, eGqeberha.
Lo mnyhadala weFashoni wenziwe wayimpumelelo yiPresidential Employment Stimulus Programme yeNational Arts Council of South Africa.
“Sinqwenela ukubanegalelo ekukhuthazeni iyantlukwano ngokobuchule eNelson Mandela Bay ngokukhulisa icandelo lezefashoni kulo mmandla; ukudala ibango lentengiso ngokunika abayili beempahla bendawo yethu ithuba lokuvezwa kubathengi belizwe nakwabeendaba, senze ingxolo yefashoni kulo mmandla, kuvuse umdla wabakhenkethi bangaphandle ukuba bandwendwele isixeko sethu kwaye sibekwe kwinqanaba leWorld Fashion Capital, ” kutsho uMarc Mahambehlala onguSihlalo weEbubeleni Festival Projects NPC (Non-Profit Company).
Yena uNamhla Fihla ongumyili weempahla nokwalilungu lebhodi Ebubeleni Festival Projects NPC uthe: 
“IMpuma Koloni inabayili abaninzi abaselula abanetalente, ingakumbi abo baphumelela kwiiyunivesithi kodwa bayakhathazeka kukungafiki ndawo ukubonisa izinto zabo, baphele beshiya amakhaya abo besiya kwiidolophu ezinkulu. ”
Abayili bempahla baye bamenywa ukuba bangenise umsebenzi wabo wakutsha nje, iiprofayili zabo nokukhuthaze olo yilo lwabo.
UMahambehlala uthi bafumene malunga nabayili abanomdla abangama89 abafake izicelo zokubonisa ngemisebenzi yabo.
“Abagwebi abaphuma kwicandelo lefashoni baye baqwalasela ezo zicelo baze bakhetha abayili abalishumi kuphela, ngabo abaza kubonisa ngomsebenzi wabo. 
Bonke abayili baza kuxhamla kwitasi yeEmployment Stimulus Programme,“ kutsho uMahambehlala.

Mhlawumbi kudala uzibuza ukuba ngubani lo Ben 10 kaMam’ uMadlala othetha isiXhosa kuZalo, ngethamsanqa I’solezwe lesiXhosa limkhangele lamfumana esaxakekile kwezo zitalato zakwaMashu.
Eli tyendyana nguOthembele Nomgca, inzalelwane yaseBhungeni, eFlagstaff eMpuma Koloni.
UNomgca, ominyaka engama20 ubudala, udlala indima kaBongz kulo mdlalo oboniswa rhoqo ngokuhlwa phakathi evekini kwiSABC 1.
UBongz lo, owaqala ukubonakala kuZalo kunyaka ophelileyo, nguBen 10 omtsha kaMam’ uMadlala kulo mdlalo othandwa kunene eMzantsi Afrika.
UBongz ligatyana lomfana ovela emakhaya eMpuma Koloni, ebaleka impathombi yabazali bakhe, ugaleleka kwelaseThekwini ngelifuna ukuzibophela amaxonya ukuze naye abe ngumntu ebantwini.
Akukho nto ubomi basesitalatweni obungamfundisanga yona.
UNomgca, oqale kunyaka ophelileyo ukubonisa isakhono sakhe kuZalo, udlala indima yakhe yokuqala ngqa kumabonakude.
Akuphumelela iMatriki ngo2017 eKokstad eminyaka ilishumi elinesithandathu, uNomgca wakhetha ukuyokwenza izifundo zeDrama and Production eDurban University of Technology (DUT), apho wayesabela kubizo olwamfikela ekuGrade 11. 
Kulapho aye wadibana nabanye abadlali bakamabonakude abaziwayo abafana noWiseman Mncube (Sibonelo kuZalo) noThobani Nzuza ( owayenguKhehla kuZalo).
Ubalisa athi ukhule engenamnqweno wokuba ngumdlali kamabonakude.
“Bendizithandela umculo nombhoxo. Kodwa phaya kuGrade 11 ndanento ethanda ukubukela Ityala lamawele, ndilinganise umlinganiswa onguPhekeza esikolweni, lwaqala apho ke uthando lwalo msebenzi ndiwenzayo ngoku,” kutsho uNomgca.

Le ngoma kaMbidana, esandul’ ukuphuma ekhasini, yenzelwe abathandi bomculo ukuba balibale kancinane ngoxinizelelo abanalo olubangelwe kukufika kweCovid-19.
Le ngoma inendawo ethi [Wakhomenta, ndakhomenta, wareact(a) ndareact(a), zam’ eyokuza ikhona eyokubuya].
Ebalisela I’solezwe lesiXhosa ngale ngoma, uMbidana uthi umculo wakhe ukhuthazwa bubomi bemihla ngemihla, izinto ahlangabezana nazo kwanamabali abantu abamngqongileyo.
“Yingoma eyonwabisayo kakhulu ebantwini abatsha. Iza kubenza balibale okomzuzwana ngekhorona,” kutsho uMbidana.
Igama elisetyenziswe nguMbidana kule ngoma yakhe elithi ‘Ematrasini’ lisetyenziswa ngabantu abatsha kumakhasi onxibelelwano xa bethetha ngokuwela iziko.
“Kuba [ngeli xesha leCovid-19] bechitha ixesha elininzi kumakhasi onxibelelwano, kuphinde kubekho amagama abaye badlale ngawo, ’ematrasini’ ibe lelinye lamagama atsale umdla kum,” kutsho le mvumi.
Kule ngoma uthi usebenze neAfro-Victimz.
UMbidana, waseLuphilisweni eMbizana, ucula umculo wohlobo lweAfro-House neAfro-Soul.
Enye yeengoma zakhe ethi ‘Abalali’ akunye kuyo noFusion Tone, yaphumelela imbasa yeBest Dance Song kumawonga iSouth African Upcoming Musicians Awards.
Ukanti enye ingoma adume ngayo ithi ‘Ndibambe’ nayenze noDJ Soso.
Umculo kaMbidana uyafumaneka kuzo zonke iivenkile zeintanethi.
Inkosikazi yaseRhawutini ibeleke abantwana abalishumi, ngaxeshanye, yatsho isophula irekhodi lehlabathi leGuiness likaHalima Cissé obeleke abantwana abalithoba eMorocco kwinyanga ephelileyo.
UGosiame Thamara Sithole, 37, ubeleke aba bantwana balishumi (decuplets ngesiNgesi) kwisibhedlele sasePitoli ngokuhlwa kwangoMvulo, utshilo umyeni wakhe uTeboho Tsotetsi.
UGosiame Thamara Sithole nomyeni wakhe uTeboho Tsotetsi UMFANEKISO: Thobile Mathonsi/African News Agency (ANA)
UTsotetsi uthi uSithole, osuka kwilokishi yaseTembisa Ekurhuleni, ubeleke amakhwenkwe asixhenxe namantombazana amathathu emva kokusetyenziswa kwesikere.
“Ebeneenyanga ezisixhenxe neentsuku ezisixhenxe ekhulelwe. 
Ndineemvakalelo,” utshilo uTsotetsi, ongaphangeliyo.
USithole, okwanamawele aneminyaka emithandathu, uxelele iPretoria News kwinyanga ephelileyo ukuba wayengayikholelwa ekuqaleni kwalo nyaka xa wayexelelwa ngoogqirha ukuba ukhulelwe abantwana abathandathu (sextuplets), phambi kokuba olunye upopolo luveze ukuba unabantwana abasibhozo (octuplets).
Abanye ababini zange babhaqwe ekuqaleni kuba babekumbhobho ongalunganga, ngokokutsho kukaSithole.
USithole, ongumanejala evenkileni, uthi kwakumothusile ukukhulelwa olu hlobo. Uthi kwakunzima ekuqaleni, egula. 
Ukwathe khange akunyangele ukukhulelwa.
UNjingalwazi Dini Mawela, isekela ntloko kwisikolo sezobugqirha eSefako Makgatho Health Sciences University, uthi imeko kaSithole inqabile kwaye ivame ukubangelwa lunyango lokufuna ukukhulelwa.
Aba bantwana baza kugqiba ezi nyanga zizayo kwizixhobo zokukhulisa abantwana ngenxa yokuba bebekhulelwe “ngomngcipheko ophezulu”, utshilo uMawela.
Ndenza isiqinisekiso sokuba olu phando nalo msebenzi ujongene nendlela apho abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo abathi bazotywa ngayo kwincwadi zedrama ngokubhekisele kwisini sabo sabosobufazi, wenziwe ndim. 
Apho ndisokusebenziso aphando lwabanye ababhali, ndizokucaphula ukuba ndisebenzisa amagama omnye umbhali.
Kolu phando bekujongwane nendlela apho ababhali abasini sobuduna kwakunye nabo babhinqileyo abathi babazobe ngayo abalinganiswa abayintloko, abangamabhiqa kwiincwadi zabo zedrama zolwimi lwesiXhosa. 
Umphandi ukhokelwe yinto yokuba kukho ingxaki kwindlela amabali ethu edrama esiXhosa athi abhalwe ngayo. Kuye kwabonakalo ukuba umxholo wala mabali uyafana awuyelelenanga. 
Umphandi ubonile ukuba ababhali bathetha into enye, kwaye bethetha into enye nje, umphandi akangqinelani nabo. 
Oku kungangqinelani kuye kwazalwa kukutshintsha kwamaxesha. 
Ezi zinto aba babhali bezi ncwadi zedrama ababhala ngazo zizinto ezazisenzeka kude kudala. 
Ngenxa yokutshintsha kwamaxesha, akukho mntu ulindeleleke ukuba aphile ngale ndlela ezi ncwadi zisikhokelela ngayo. 
Incwadi nganye ephononongiweyo ibijongwa phantsi kweenkalo ezithile, ezithe zangqinelana nolu phando, ukuze umphandi afike apho ebesiya nolu phando. 
Apha kolu phando umphandi ude wafika apho kufel’ithole khona nolu phando, yonke imibuzo ebaqale enayo yaphanduleka ekuhambeni kophando. 
Sibabonile ababhali beencwadi zedrama bezibhala iincwadi zabo, kunye nendlela leyo bathi bazibhala ngayo. 
Siwubonile umohluko phakathi kwababhali besini sobuduna kunye nababhali ababhinqileyo nendlela ababazoba ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo. 
Ababhali besini sobuduna bababzoba abalinganiswa abangamabhinqa njengabantu ekumele bexhomekeke kwabo besini soduna, hayi abantu abazimeleyo, abaziphandelayo. 
Umfundi umbonile umbali webali leqonga xa ezoba abalinganiswa uFuneka kunye noZanele phaya kula ncwadi u-Ndiyekeni njengabantu abaxhwitha amadoda ade ome nko, bawashiye engenanto, bakugqiba bawalahlele ngaphandle. 
Khumbula indlela yena umbhali ka-‘Inene nasi Isibhozo’, esizobela umlinganiswa 
uMasukude njengomfazi okhohlakeleyo, ongcolileyo, othakathayo, kwaye oligqwirha. 
Sithe sisakhuza oko kubunjwa kuMasukude, saze sadibana nomlinganiswa uNojenti, phaya ku-‘Ndixoleleni’, ekhohlakele yena kuqala efana nje noMasukude, naye engumbulali othakathayo. 
Umphandi usebenzise yanye jwi incwadi ebhalwe libhinqa, oku akwenzekanga ngampazamo, kwenziwe ukubonisa ukunqongaphala kweencwadi zedrama ezibhalwa ngmabhinqa, abe ezama ukunyusa isidima samabhinqa, esiwiswe ngezi ncwadi zininzi zibhalwa ngababhali besini sobuduna. 
Le meko ikwayiyo ekhuthaze umphandi ukuba enze uphando olunje ngolu, ukuze amehlo abo babhalayo avuleke babone ukuba ingxaki ikho, kwaye ifuna bona ukuba bancede kwangoku ithuba lisekhona. 
Kumabali edrama amane athe axoxwa apha kolu phando u-‘Inene nasi Isibhozo’, ‘Ndiyekeni’, ‘Ndixoleleni’ kunye no-‘Iinkunzi Ezimbini,’ siwabonile ke amabhinqa ecinezelwa kwaye ephathwa kakubi ngabantu besini sobuduna. 
Uqaphele ukuba amabhinqa awaphili phantsi kwengcinezelo kusini na ngoba ngelinye ixesha umntu lo uphila phantsi kwengcinezelo, akayiqondi naloo nto, de yolathwe ngomnye umntu. 
Iba ngulo mncedi ke nawe. Ukuba wena apha ebomini bakho uyaqonda ukuba uyacinezelwa ngumntu othandana naye, ophangela naye okanye ofunda naye, zama ukuba uphume kolo manyano, nokuba ulibhinqa okanaye uyindoda. 
Kaloku namabhinqa anaso isakhona sokucinezela amadoda, ingakumbi emitshatweni. 
Umfazi ayiphathe indoda yakhe caba indoda ayinakukwazi ukwenza nto ngaphandle kokuba icele imvume emfazini, njengokuba sibonile phaya kwibali lethu u-‘Iinkunzi Ezimbini’ isenziwa nguSibonda loo nto emfazini wakhe uNolasti. 
Yinto apha le eyimoshayo imitshato, nayo nayiphi na indibano phakathi kwabantu ababini, ngoba kaloku omnye umntu ngoku uza koyika ukuphila ubomi bakhe, kufuneka aphilele omnye umntu ngenxa yoloyika analo. 
Umphandi angacebisa ukuba abo bathi bawafunde amabali anje, bawafunde ngamehlo kunye neendlebe ezibukhali ngoba bangakhawuleza babhidakala kwinto amabayithathe okanye bayizuze xa begqibile ukuzifunda ezi zifundo zedrama. 
Umphandi uphinde acebise ababhali abasafundayo ukuba basuke baphele kumba wokuzoba amabhinqa njengabantu ababuthathaka abaxhomekeke kuphela kumadoda, ngoba amaxesha atshintshile ngoku, azisekho njalo izinto. 
Ukuba kukho ingcamango abafuna ukuyizoba, mabayizobe ngokupheleleyo, bayibeke phambili ingxaki, bakugqiba baze nesisombululo. 
Umzekelo, ukuba umbhali utshiswa yinto afuna ukuyibhala ngamabhinqa emhluphayo, efana nokungazihloniphi kwamabhinqa, uvumelekile ukuba akubhale oko, kodwa makangapheleli apho. 
Makagqithele aze neengcebiso apho amabhinqa angathi aziphucule ngayo, ukuze ibhinqa elisakhulayo elifunda loo ncwadi libe nenkuthazo nokuba belisalahleka ebomini balo. 
Ingcebiso yomphandi yokugqibela yeyokuba ababhali besini sobuduna bakhe babhale iidrama ezinyusa isikhundla samabhinqa, ngoba kuninzi okwenziwa ngamabhinqa, kodwa okungabhalwayo ezincwadini. 
Singabantu abaphangela kweli bakala lezezibhalo sinokukhuthazana, sinyusane ukuze wonke umntu aphumelele, hayi into yokuba abanye banyuke ngokucinezela abanye. 
Umphandi uthanda ukukhuthaza abo basakhulayo, bathe banomdla ekubhaleni ukuba bayibone le ntlekela yenzeka kwizibhalo zethu zolwimi lwesiXhosa, ze bakhuthazeke ukuba nabo babhale iincwadi ezifana nezi, nto nje bona bazame ukunyusa isidima samabhinqa, baphelise le nto yokucinezela esinye esini maxa benyusa esinye. 
USibonda naye unale ngxaki inye, naye uphakamile wathetha, engqinelana nesi sithethi, ngokuba yena ukhala ngento yokuba, umfazi wakhe 
uNolasti akanayo intlonipho kwaye uziphethe emtshatweni wabo ngenxa yale mfundo anayo. 
Imfundo emfazini ibonwa njengokuba yingxaki ngokuba umfazi ofundileyo unento yokufuna ukwenza izigqibo zekhaya. 
Iqalele apho ingxabano phakathi kukaSibonda kunye nomfazi wakhe omcinci uNolasti. 
Abanye abafazi bakaSibonda, uNifinishi kunye noNokhaya bona bathobekile. 
Kaloku bona ngabafazi abadala kwaye abanayo kwaphela imfundo. 
Ukutshata komfazi wesithathu kukaSibonda yabangela utshintsho emzini wabo ngokuba uNolasti akafani nabo tu. 
Izinto zekhaya ezifana nokucoca, ukupheka okanye ukwenza iti, uNolasti uziyekela kubo, ngelithi yena uyaphangela, kwaye uyabondla ngemali ayibhatalwayo ekhitshini, ngoko ke bona mabenze imisebenzi yaphakathi kwekhaya. 
Oku kubangela ukuba abafazi bakaSibonda bangamthandi lo Nolasti. 
Le ngxwabangxwaba yile yabangela ukuba uNolasti awushiye umzi wakhe, agoduke ngokuba yena akazibona ephila ndlelanye naba bafazi bakaSibonda ngoba yena uphucukile kwaye ufundile, ngoko ufuna ukuphathwa njengomntu okwelo nqanaba hayi nje ngathi akabalulekanga. 
Mve kule ngxoxo ingezantsi: Nolimithi: Ndinqanda ndinganqandi ubonanje. 
Iyakhubekisa okunene into yokuba abafazi benziwe amakhoboka amadoda olu hlobo, ukuze kube kukho izinto ezifana nooNofinishi aba, kuba enjenje nje umyeni wakho woniwa ngabo. 
Ukuba bebengengabo abathoba-sikutyele bangabo ngengenje uSibonda. 
Ibe ke iculo alihlabelayo livunywa yiyo yonke le lali, akakhathaliseki nokuba uyiloza kangakanani na. 
Nawethu amadoda kufuneka asiphathe njengokuba esitsho. 
Inene yinto ngobunto bayo le yobubonda, ndakuyicel’ivuthiwe ndifung’amaKhwemnte. 
Nolasti: Masingazikhathazi kakhulu wethu Mfazi. 
Kaloku yonke into ilunga ngokulungiswa. 
Mna ndicinga ukuba xa sinokubashumayeza abanye abafazi aba, sibabonise ingxaki esikuyo thina bafazi, bangasebenzisana nathi ekuthuleni le dyokhwe siyithwaliswe ngumendo. 
Isengenzeka ubonanje into yokuba baninzi abacinga njengathi qha bayoyika ukuzidandalazisa izimvo zabo kuba bacinga ukuba mhlawumbi kuza kuthiwa baphokele. 
Kuyaqapheleka ke ukuba umlinginiswa oyintloko apha kule ncwadi yedrama nguNolasti. 
Lo mlinganiswa zininzi izinto ezimvelelayo, ezithi zibe yingxaki ebomini bakhe ngenxa yokuba elibhinqa. 
Apha ngentla sibona ethetha nesihlobo sakhe esikhuthaza ukuba sinyamezele emzini waso nokuba sekunzima kangakanani na ngoba uyayazi into yokuba emendweni kuyanyanyezelwa. 
Le ntetho iphakathi kukaNolasti kunye noNolimithi, uNolimithi ekhalaza ngempatho mbi abayifumana ebayenini babo, beziva behleli phantsi kwengcinezelo emizini yabo. 
Oku kuthethwa ngaba bafazi ngoku kanye kuza kuthethwa ngako apha kwesi sahluko. 
Apha kweli bali ingcingane yesini sobukhomokazi igqame kakhulu ukogqitha le ifumaneka pha kwela bali u-‘Inene nasi Isibhoza’. 
Xa sijonge umlinganiswa oyintloko uNolasti, siyambona lo mlinganiswa ukuba uyangena phantsi kwebhinqa elithi lilwele inkululeko namalungelo amabhinqa. 
Sikubona oku ngokwezenzo zakhe, kuqala, udaba lokuba kanti ufundile luyakuxhasa oku, udaba lwesibini lelokuba, lo mfazi uyakwazi ukuzimela endodeni yakhe, akenzi nantoni na ayixelelwayo okungathi ulusana. 
Umyeni kaNolasti onguSibonda, yindoda apha esinokuthi yindoda eqotho yomXhosa, othi apha alihloniphe kakhulu isiko lakhe. 
Ngoko ke unendlela azilindele ukuba abafazi bakhe baziphathe ngayo, kwaye kunezinto alindelele ukuba bazenze njengoko bengamakhosikazi akhe. 
Funda incoko phakathi kukaNolasti nendoda yakhe uSibonda xa bebuya emngcwabeni: 
Sibonda: Kanene akukho nto niyenzayo ngaphandle kokuthetha nina bafazi. 
Iphi ikofu Nolasti? Ndidiniwe ndingumfi ndilapha nje.  
Nolasti: Ndidinwe oku kwam ubonanje. 
Ubungenakuyenza ngokwakho namhlanje ikofu? 
Sibonda:Uthi mna mandenze ikofu? Uyaziva kakuhle le nto uyithethayo? 
Le ncoko ingentla phakathi kwesi sibini sitshatileyo isibonisa indlela isini sesiduna esisibona ngayo isini sobukhomokazi. 
Apha sibona ngokucacileyo ukuba le ndonda inala ngcamango yokuba umsebenzi womfazi kukukhathelela indoda yakhe maxesha onke. 
Kaloku qwalasela ukuba bobabini badiniwe bavela esingcwabeni, umfazi yena uvela ukuya kupheka nokuhlamba izitya emngcwabeni, kucacile ukuba soze ithi kanti akadinwanga, kodwa kuyo yonke loo nto kunyanzelekile ukuba afike emzini wakhe aphinde enze imisebenzi yakhe yobufazi. 
Aba bafazi apha kweli bali bayayibona le mpatho, abanye bayayikhaba, babe abanye beyivuma ngoba abazi ngcono, nabo banala ngcamango yento yokuba umsebenzi wabo njengabafazi kukunakekela indoda yabo, ukucoca indlu, ukupheka nokukhulisa abantwana. 
Le yantlukwano ikho phakathi kwaba bafundileyo kunye nabo bangakhange bawabona amasango esikolo. 
Nantsi incoko phakathi kukaNolasti kunye nomhlobo wakhe uNolimithi ekubeni uNolasti embalisela ngendlela umyeni wakhe uSibonda athi wamkweka ngayo emngcwabeni, xeshikweni esithi amadoda abhubha esemancinci ngenxa yabafazi babo abaphucikileyo kwaye abangenandlela yokuyiphatha indoda, bona bantu noko baqiqileyo, kwaye bafundileyo, kwaye bayiqwalaselayo le mpatho mbi: 
Nolimithi:Ndinqanda ndinganqandi ubonanje. 
Iyakhubekisa okunene into yokuba abafazi benziwe amakhoboka amadoda olu hlobo, ukuze kube kukho izinto ezifana nooNofinishi aba, kuba enjenje umnyeni wakho woniwa ngabo. 
Ukuba bebengabo aba thobasikutyele bangabo ngengenje uSibonda…  
Nolasti:Masingazikhathazi kakhulu wethu Mfazi. 
Kaloku yonke into ilunga ngokulungiswa.
Mna ndicinga ukuba xa sinokubashumayeza abanye abafazi aba, sibabonise ingxaki esikuyo thina bafazi, bangasebenzisana nathi ekothuleni le dyokhwe siyithweliswe ngumendo. 
Ukuba uyakhumbula xa bekuchazwa ukuba yintoni ingcingane yesini sobukhomokazi, bekuxhentsiwe phezu kwento yokuba, le ngcingane ithetha ngamabhinqa athi adibana alwela inkululeko yabo kunye namanye amabhinqa. 
Le nto kanye yenziwa nguNolasti kunye nesihlobo sakhe uNolimithi. 
Jonga pha kwezi ndawu bathi “Iyakhubekisa okunene into yokuba abafazi benziwe amakhoboka amadoda olu hlobo” baze baphinde bathi 
“Mna ndicinga ukuba xa sinokubashumayeza abanye abafazi aba”. 
Aba bafazi babini yimizekelo emihle yamabhinqa afuna ukuncedisana namanye amabhinqa ukuze bakhululeke phantsi kwengcinezelo yamadoda. 
Abayenzi lento ukukhulula iziqu zabo kuphela, bafuna ukunceda nabanye bababone ukuba le mpatho baphantsi kwayo, ayiyiyo. 
Akulula ke ukubonisa wonke umntu ukuba bahleli phantsi kwengcinezelo xa bona bengayiboni loo nto. 
UNolasti uthe xa ezama ukubabonisa abanye abafazi aba atshate nabo apha kuSibonda into yokuba le ndlela uSibonda abaphatha ngayo asiyondlela yokuphatha abafazi. 
Uthe akuzimela lo mfazi, abanye abafazi aba babini bambona njengomntu oziphakamisileyo kwaye ophucukileyo. 
Bave bezithethela uNofinishi kwakunye nomfazi wesibini uNokhaya: 
Nokhaya: Ndixakiwe nam Nofinishi, kudala ndiyijika-jika ingqondo yam kodwa andiphumi nasiphumo. 
Kucace gca okwekat’emhlophe ehlungwini khona ukuba asisobe sonwabe sonke kweliya khaya lethu belifudula liseluxolweni ngenxa yokusa nokuswela imbeko kukaNolasti.  
Nofinishi: Usimele ngempucuko yokuba yena akanakuphathwa yincentsa. 
Ndixakwa kukuba wayeze kuthini apha kanti ufuna ukuziphatha. Inzima le mfundo yabo, ibaphambanisa ingqondo. 
Bayafuna ukuba ngabafazi kodwa abakwazi tu ukwenda! Lo Nolasti ungafika engqayiza, ezibiza ukuba yena uyinkosikazi kaJwarha uqobo, ezingomba isifuba kuba etshate ezi-ofisini zeemantyi, inqaba kukuziphatha okwenkosikazi. 
Kucacile ukuba aba bafazi babini abavani kwaphela noNolasti kwaye le nto yakhe yokuba abe kanti ufundile nabo bayibona nje ngokuba yingxaki ngoba bathi yiyo le imenza ukuba acinge uphucukile kunabo. 
Bayalibala into yokuba ukutya oku bakutyayo, nempahla le bayinxibisa abantwana babo ithethwa nguNolasti, ngenxa yale mfundo yakhe bangayiboneli ntweni. 
Indaweni yokuba banyamane bebo bathathu, bencedisane kwaye bakhuthazane ukuze kuhlaleke kamnandi emzini wabo, wayalwana, kwaye abahloniphani, nto le iliwa yile ngcingane yesini sobukhomokazi. 
Ngoba ngoku- bhekisele kule ngcingane, amabhinqa kumele ukuba amanyane ancedisane ukulwa ingcinezelo yamadoda. Bona aba bafazi bayayikhuthaza. 
Kweli bali likaMothlabane umbhali usizobele umlinganiswa oyintloko ukuba abe ngumntu obhinqileyo, kwaye ofunde ngaphezu kwendoda yakhe, ngoko ke ukungalingani ngokwesini sekubonakele ngokupheleleyo. 
Indaba yokufunda kukaNolasti nokuphangela kwakhe yingxaki kakhulu apha kweli bali, ingakumbi emnyenini wakhe uSibonda. 
Kaloku le meko ibhalwe phantsi kwayo le ncwadi, yokuba nomfazi ofundileyo yinto apha engaqhelekanga kula maxesha ngoba imfundo asiyonto apha ibonwa ibalulekile ngoba, indoda yiyo ekumele ukuba iphangele ibuye nemali endlini, xeshikweni umfazi esenza imisebenzi yasendlini, ngoba kaloku indoda yiyo intloko yekhaya. 
UMfazi kaSibonda omncinci ufundile kwaye uphangela emakhitshini, ngokoke naye ungena nemali endlini ethi isetyenziswe ukuthenga ukutya, impahla yabantwana njalo njalo. 
Oku kubangela ukuba uSibonda azive eyindoda engaphelelenga ngoba abafazi bakhe abadala bondliwa ngumfazi wakhe omncinci. 
Yena uNolasti uyibona le nto nje- ngokuba uncedisana nomnyeni wakhe kwizinto zasekhaya. 
Oku kwenzeka phakathi kwesi sisbini kuko okubangela kuthiwa ukuba kukho ukungalingani ngokwesini. 
UNolasti wenza ngandlela zonke ukuqinisekisa ukuba uncedisana nomnyeni wakhe apha endlini, kodwa yena uSibonda lo uqinisekile ekubeni yena 
akasoze aphathwe ngumfazi kwaye angahlonitshwa ngenxa yokuba lo mfazi ephangela. 
Funda into ethethwa nguSibonda xa uNolasti ethe wavuma ukugcina abantwana baka- Nkosikazi White, umqeshi wakhe, ebusuku xeshikweni bona besaphumile, abe phofu uNolasti engacelanga mvume kumnyeni wakhe: 
Nolasti: Kaloku baza kuya entlanganisweni nomnyeni wakhe, babuye ebusuku kakhulu. 
Mna ndiza kugcina abantwana lo gama bona besentlanganisweni… 
Sibonda: Ingaba iindlebe zam zinomphula okanye ndicothelwa bubuthulu? 
Uyandixelela yonke le nto okanye ufuna uluvo ngokugcina abantwana babeLungu ebusuku? 
Nolasti:Hayi wethu ndiyacela ungabi sathetha enye into. Sendivumile kuMedem. 
Sibonda:Uvume njani Nolasti? Uyivuma njani into elelo hlobo ungakhange ugqithe kum? 
Uthetha ukuba uza kusuka uzigqibele ukuba unokubuya nanini na xa uthanda apha emzini wam 
Kucacile into yokuba uSibonda yindoda apha ethanda ukuphatha. 
Ufuna ukuba izinto zihambe ngendlela yakhe. 
Nengcingane yokungalingani ngesini isixelela loo nto ke ukuba isini sesiduna sizibona sibaluleke ngaphezu kweso sobukhomakazi, yiyo loo nto uSibonda elindele uNolasti ukuba acele imvume kuye kuqala phambi kokuba enze izigqibo, okungathi uNolasti ngumntwana ongayaziyo into ayenzayo. 
Amaxesha esiphila kuwo ngoku awasafani namaxesha ootatomkhulu noomakhulu bethu ababephila kuwo. 
Nto leyo ethetha into yokuba amasiko nezithethe zethu zakwaXhosa zitshintsha nokutshintsha kwamaxesha. 
Kakade ayikho into ehleli ihleli, zonke izinto ziyatshintsha. 
Xa sijongane nendawo amabhinqa akuyo ngoku size sithelekise nendawo awayekuyo ngoko, utshintsho luyabonakala. 
Kuninzi okwakulindeleke kumabhinqa kwixesha lakudala, ingakumbi emitshatweni. 
Amabhinqa ayelindeleke ukuba kanti atshatile phambi kokuba afike kwiminyaka ethile, ukuba kanti kufika loo minyaka bengatshatanga, babejongwa njengabantu abangaphelelanga. 
Bona ke abo batshatileyo banezabo izinto ekulindeleke bezenzile. Zonke ke ezi zinto bese zikhankanyiwe kumancandelo angaphambili, xa bekuthenthwa ngeendidi zamabhinqa alwela ukungalingani ngokwesini. 
Apha kweli candelo umphandi ufuna ukuchopha kumba wezikhundla ezibakho emtshatweni. Xa abantu betshata, sube kutshatha ibhinqa kunye nomntu wesilisa. 
Ekubeni oko kwenzekile, utata wekhaya uye abonwe njengentloko yekhaya, apho kulindeleke ukuba ondle umfazi wakhe, akhusele umzi wabo. 
Ukanti lona ibhinqa lilindeleke ukuba linakekele umnyeni walo ngokuqinisekisa ukuba ukutya kuhleli kukho etafileni, indlu icocekile kwaye konke akufunayo kukhona endlini, ze amzalele abantwana lande usapho.  
Kodwa konke oko kwatshintsha nokutshintsha kwamaxesha. 
Kula maxesha kukho amabhinqa aphangela mihla yonke, de baphangele ezinzulwini zasebusuku, nto leyo ethetha ukuba, ixesha lokuba apheke, acoce indlu, anakekele umyeni wakhe liyancipha, kunyanzelekile ukuba umnyeni anyuse iikawusi, angene esikhundleni sobufazi. 
Nto le ibingasoze ingcamleke kumaxesha akudala. 
Masikhe siqaphele apha kweli bali likaMothlane, apho umlinganiswa uNolasti athi athathe umsebenzi wasebusuku kuba acingela imali azakuyizuza kulo msebenzi, ezakuthi incedisane nabo emzini wakhe nomnyeni wakhe uSibonda, masikhe siphonononge le ncoko yabo: 
Nolasti: Nisebenze njani namhlanje Jwarha? 
Sibonda: Sizamile Nkosikazi, ibe njani eyakho imini? 
Nolasti: Hayi kube kuhle kakhulu nakum. Loo nto ke ndifumene nesithembiso sokubhaselwa ngeR20 yonke ngomso. 
Hayi sendibona ukuba ndiza kusebenzisa kakuhle neMedem wam. 
Sibonda: iR20 yonke? Yeyantoni? 
Nolasti: Kaloku baza kuya entlanganisweni nomyeni wakhe, babuye ebusuku kakhulu. 
Mna ke ndiza kugcina abantwana lo gama bona basentlanganisweni. 
Emva kwentlanganiso baza kukhe badanise nje kancinci bazikhumbuze iimini zobutsha babo. 
Sibonda: Ingaba iindlebe zam zinomphula okanye ndicothelwa bubuthulu bethu? 
Uyandixelela yonke le nto okanye ufuna uluvo lwam ngokugcina abantwana babeLungu ebusuku? 
Nolasti: Hayi wethu ndiyacela ungabi sathetha enye into. 
Sendivumile kuMedem.  
Sibonda: Uvume njani Nolasti? Uyivuma njani into elolo hlobo ungakhange ugqithe kum? 
Uthetha ukuba uza kusuka uzigqibele ukuba unokubuya nanini na xa uthanda apha emzini wam? 
Nolasti: Andikhange ndicinge njalo, eyona nto isuke yaphambili kum leli themba lale mali ingaka ndiza kuyifumana ekubeni ndisazi ukuba 
sixakeke sinje kweli khaya. 
Ndiqonde ukuba xa sinokuyifumana le R20 ungatsho ukwazi ukurhafela laa ntsimi isemmangweni, sibe nakho nokuthengela abantwana iimpahla zobusika. 
Sibonda: Ngubani obethe andikwazi kuzenza ezo zinto ngokwam? Sekutheni sendicingelwa nguwe njengoku indlela yokwenza izinto emzini wam? 
Nolasti: Besekukade. He wethu Sigqibo! Yintoni le nto uthi uzazi ukuba utsala nzima ube uzenza ngathi unekratshi? Uyazi ukuba kule mbalela asisavuni nto iyiyo, siyalamba. 
Ukuba ibingeyiyo le mali ndiza nayo kwaba beLungu ngesekukudala abantwana bethu bengasahlawuli esikolweni. Ngesingesakwazi nokumondla uMama wakho, andisathethi ngemali yoogqirha bakhe. 
Kutheni le nto usuka undenze umoni ngokuza nemali yokukuncedisa ekwenzeni ukuba intlalo yekhaya ibe lula? 
Sibonda: Unayo le nto yokuthi ndibeka isheleni ubeke indaliso. Yiyeke usayithanda kunjalonje loo nto ukuba akufuni kuvana negwangqa! 
Nolasti: Yeyiphi ecaphukisayo ke ngoku? Andithi ndithetha inyani xa ndi… 
Sibonda: (Egragrama) ndithe kuwe sukuthetha ndithetha. 
Bathi cwaka ke bade bafika ekhaya. 
Aye endlwini alala kuyo uNolasti, ajikeleze phandle uSibonda ehlola izinto-yinto, emana ukuzithethela.
Ewe utheth’inyaniso lo mfazi. 
Kodwa ke loo nyaniso ithi makandiphathe emzini wam, le mali yakhe imnika igunya lokwenza unothanda? 
Angaske ayeke noko kuphangela kuba andizange ndaxhomekeka mfazini kakade. 
Ukuphangela kwakhe akufanele kumnika gunya lakubuya ngonothanda akugqiba ukuba ngumendi. 
Loo nto ingabonakalisa nabanye aba.
