Yena ke ade asukele phezulu njekungokuba loo Mlungu wakhe yena akayazi into yokuba kufuneka acele emzini wakhe? 
Ingathi iza kuzal’amathokazana le nto yaba beLungu ndifung’ udadethu! 
Aphazanyiswe kuloo ntlanganiso yakhe kukubizelwa isidlo sangokuhlwa. 
Apha ngentla siyakubona oku kungquzulana phakathi kwesi sibini uNolasti kunye noSibonda, xa sibona uNolasti exelela umyeni wakhe into yokuba uceliwe nguMedem wakhe ukuba asebenze ebusuku, agade abantwana xa bona nomyeni wakhe besephumile. 
Apha umbhali usibonisa imeko apho lowo uyintloko yekhaya ilibhinqa hayi indoda, ngoba umyeni akaphangeli ngumfazi ophangelayo. 
Ingcambu yale ngxabona siyibona apha ngentla izalwa yile nto. 
uNolasti nguye ophangelayo, nguye oza nemali kweli khaya, nguye oncedana nomama womyeni wakhe ukubhatala amaxabiso kagqirha xa engaphilanga, ikwanguye ondla umyeni wakhe kunye nabafazi bakhe ababini. 
USibonda akayithandi nakancinci le nto. Akafuni ukuba umfazi wakhe aphangele ebusuku, kodwa le mali aza kube eyiphangelela yile iza kuphinda incedisane nabo apha endlini. 
Ude unendawo ezifuna ukucebisa umfazi wakhe ukuba awuyeke lo msebenzi, kuba lo mfazi akakhange aqale kuye kuqala phambi kokuba avume ukuwuthatha lo msebenzi, kodwa lo mfazi, ukuvuma kwakhe ukuthatha lo msebenzi uwuthathe enenjongo yokunceda, hayi ukudala ingxabano phakathi kwakhe nomyeni wakhe. 
USibonda uthi xa sele esukile kuNolasti, avume ukuba lo mfazi unyanisile ukuba le mali iza kunceda apha phakathi kwekhaya, kodwa into enzima kukukuvuma oku apha emfazini wakhe. 
Eyona nto iqaphelekayo apha kule ncoko yabo, yinto yokuba, uSibonda uzibona ingathi isikhundla sakhe sobudoda siyadodobala ngenxa yala mandla alo mfazi okuzimele apha kweli khaya. 
Akayithandi indaba yokuba uNolasti engaaxhomekekanga kuye, kanti iguqukile, nguSibonda oxhomekeke kuNolasti. 
Kodwa yena uNolasti akayiboni njalo, uyibona ngendlela yokuba uncedisana nomyeni wakhe, ngoba ude athi, 
“Ndiqonde ukuba xa sinokuyifumana le R20 ungatsho ukwazi ukurhafela laa ntsimi isemmangweni, sibe nakho nokuthengela abantwana iimpahla zobusika,” ukubonisa ukuba yena ebezama ukunceda, hayi ukumosha. 
Kweli xesha siphila kulo, amabhinqa angaphangela naphina apho afuna ukuphangela khona, ayisekho laa nto ithi, le yimisebenzi yobudoda, le yeyobubhinqa, imisebenzi ivulekile kuluNtu lonke. 
Oku ke kuthetha ukuba uyakwazi ukufika kusapho oluthile apho ibhinqa lisamkela imali engaphaya kunaleyo yomyeni wakhe, okanye ibe kanti lo myeni akaphangeli kwa ukuphangeli. 
Loo nto ithethe ukuba, eli bhinqa lilo elibeka isonka etafileni. 
Ingxaki ke iqale apho, ngoba ngoku lo myeni akasenalo ilungelo lokungxola ngokuba yintloko yekhaya, ngoba konke okulindeleke ukuba ekwenzile 
njengentloko yekhaya akasakwazi ukwenza. 
Yiyo loo nto uza kubona imitshato emininzi ingasebenzi, ngoba abantu besilisa abafuni kuyamkela yonke le nguqu, ade athi omnye, 
“ Andisoze nditshate umntu owamkela ngaphezulu kunam, ndim indoda kufuneka kucace.” 
Kanti ke akunyanzelekanga ukuba kube njalo, kuba kaloku wonke umntu kufuneka atshintshe nokutshintsha kwamaxesha. 
Ithuba lokuba amabhinqa abonelwe entweni nabo lifikile. 
Ixesha lokuba amabhinqa athathelwe ingqalelo kwigalelo abanalo eluntwini sele lifikile. 
Bantu bakuthi amaxesha esiphila kuwo namhla awafani nalawo amandulo, kwaye awasoze aphinde abuyele.  
Siyayibona le nto isenzeka apha kule ncwadi kaMothlabane pha kula mzi kaSibonda. 
uNolasti nguye ophangelayo, uSibonda akayithandi kuyaphi le nto yokuphangela komfazi wakhe, ngoba uyabona ukuba umfazi wakhe akaxhomekekanga kuye nganto,into ekunayo ngulo mfazi obeka ukutya etafileni, esondla uSibonda nabafazi bakhe ababini. 
Le nto imhlalisa kakubi uNolasti, de uSibonda ambethe, avalelwe ngamapolisa, ze amgxothe uNolasti emzini wakhe ngenxa yoko. 
Omnye umntu angacinga ukuba uSibonda uza kuvuya axhentse enomfazi ophangelayo, obeka ukutya etafileni, encedisana naye apha phakathi kwekhaya. 
Kodwa hayi, yena ubona indima yakhe phakathi kwekhaya ithathwa ngumfazi wakhe. 
Esi sahluko sahluke mpela kwisahluko esiphambi kwaso ngoba esi siphambi kwaso besijongenene nendlela ababhali besini sobuduna ababazoba ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqile, sabe esi sona sijonga indlela umbhali olibhinqa athi abazobe ngayo abalinganiswa abangamabhinqa. 
Umohluko ke ukho kwaye mkhulu. 
Simbonile umbhali wale ncwadi yedrama isetyenziswe apha, emzoba umlinganiswa wakhe oyintloko obhinqileyo njengomfazi owomeleleyo, ozimeleyo kwaye okwaziyo ukuzenzela izigqibo zakhe. 
Nangona umyeni wakhe lo mfazi ebesilwa naye lonke ithuba alifumanayo, oku akukhange kume endleleni yeli bhinqa, uqhubekekile ephangela, esondla usapho lwakhe, wathi xa egxothwa emzini wakhe ngumyeni wakhe ngenxa yokungquzulana, wakuhlonela oko wahamba, xa usapho lwakhe nelomyeni wakhe lithe laxoxa, kwagqitywa ekubeni abuyele emzini wakhe, nalapho ubahlonele wenjenjalo. Nto ebonisa ukuba eli bhinqa alizange lizibone lilikhulu libaluleke ngaphezulu komyeni walo ngenxa yena ephangela, umyeni wakhe engaphangeli. 
Uye wahlala engumntu onentlonipho nembeko maxa onke.  
Oku kungqinwa yile ncoko ingezantsi: 
Sigqibo: O-o! Uqonde ukuba mawubuye wena eli xa mna bendithe andikufuni? 
Nolasti: Ngenditheni xa amawenu ebeye kundilanda? 
Sigqibo: Waqala nini wena ukumamela into ethethwa ngamawethu? 
Uze kuba usazimisele ukwenza into ethandwa nguwe? 
Nolasti: Uyandityhola kanti. Besendiyincamile into yokubuyela apha mna, qha amaJwarha namaCirha aye avana ukuba mandibuye… 
Oku kungentla kungqina into yokuba uNolasti lo akazange naninina abe nentloko enkulu ngenxa yesikhundla akuso emtshatweni wakhe, nangona inguye yedwa ophangelayo kubafazi bakaSibonda.  
Nabo ke abahlobo bakaFuneka befaka uLoni isifuthufuthu ngokuthi bangamyeki ngetyala ade asele, wade naye wayekelela wasela. 
Koloku uFuneka usabambe esaa sicela sikaNdila sokuba makasebenze uLoni, ade abe sisicaka sotywala. 
Apha kule drama umbhali usizobele abalinganiswa abhinqileyo phambili njengabantu abasebenzisa amadoda ukufumana izinto abazifunayo, bengakhathalisi nokuba la madoda bawasebenzisayo atshatile kwaye aneentsapho ahlala nawo. 
Lo mbhali usizobela abalinganiswa uZanele kunye noFuneka njengamabhinqa enza amadoda amaxhoba emalini. 
Ubazobe njengabantu abaxhomekeke kubantu abangamadoda ukuze babe nemali kwaye babe nazo zonke izinto abazifunayo. 
Lo mbhali wale drama akaphelelenga ekusizobeleni aba balinganiswa babhinqileyo njengee“GoldDiggers” njengokuba kusitshiwo esiNgesini, kodwa usibonisa nempembelelo ehamba noko. 
Apha usikrobisa indlela la mabhinqa asetyenziswa ngumntu wesilisa ukubuyisa ikratshi kumntu angavani naye. 
Oku kubonisa kwa indlela abantu besilisa abawasebenzisa ngayo amabhinqa ngendlela ezimdaka, ngoba oku kuhlisa isidima sobubhinqa, kodwa bona abayiboni loo nto ngenxa yokuthanda ukunakekelwa. 
Nanku umzekelo ophilayo apha kweli bali le drama, apho umlinganiswa wesilisa uNdila ephembelela eli bhinqa uFuneka ukuba lizenzele kwixhoba elinguLoni, ngenxa yengxabano abakuyo: 
Funeka: Ukuba ufuna imali utsho ebhatyini mtshana . 
Funeka: Hayi wethu ndiyaqhula. 
Ndila: Uyaqal’ukuthetha. Uyayazi into yokuba ndiphelelwe emsebenzini kwaye ndicinga ukuba uyazazi nezizathu.  
Ndila: Uthando malube nemisebenzi, le mpahla ikule ndlu iyathetha. Ubumnandi balo mcimbi yinto yokuba into yokuthandana kwethu lihlebo lethu (watsho emwola) Look, Funie girl, umdlalo uwuqhelile sondeza uMawonga, izabatha zaziwa nguwe. 
Funeka:Ndakuyibambisa intaka leyo, ndiyithini? 
Ndila: Yixhwithe iintsiba, kuba buyaphela ubuntaka bayo zakuvuthuluka iintsiba. 
Funeka: Ndiyakukhe ndizame mtshana, kodwa makhe lulane uthuli. 
Ndila: Mtshana wam! (Bawolane kwakhona.) 
Kwesi sicatshulwa singentla umphandi uyibonisa gca into yokuba uNdila ukhokela uFuneka ukuba enze ububi bokuxhwitha uLoni ngenxa yekratshi alibamba kuLoni. 
Naye ke uFuneka uyavuma engaphozisanga maseko ngenxa yalo mntu anguye, uhlelinje efuna ukuphila ubomi obungaphezulu kunaye. 
Lo mbhali uthe wakhetha indlela afuna ukubazoba ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo kwincwadi yakhe yedrama, wathi njengoninzi lwababhali 
bedrama abangabantu besilisa, wabazoba njengabantu abangasweli nto abayifunayo, abangenamqolo wokuzimela ngaphandle koncedo lwendoda ebomini babo. 
Ixhaphakile ke le nto kwiincwadi zedrama ezibhalwe ngababhali besini sobulisa, nto le ijongwa lolu phando. 
Lo mbhali uyichane kanye kanye le ntetho ayikhankanye apha ngentla, ngoba le nto ayithethayo ngendlela ababhali besini sobuduna abathi babazobe abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo njengabantu abonobuqhophololo, yile kanye yenziwe ngumbhali wale drama xa wayezoba umlinganiswa uFuneka kunye noZanele. 
Abantu abakhe bayifunda le ncwadana yedrama baya kubona ukuba uJongilanga ubazobe aba balinganiswa bangamabhinqa njengabantu abaqhatha amadoda, de indoda ifikelele kwingcinga zokuba iyathandwa ngala mabhinqa, ize ilandelise ngokuwenzela nantoni na ayifunayo, kungakhathalekisanga nokuba le ndoda itshatile kusini na. 
UZilandu nenkosikazi yakhe basweleka beshiya unyana wabo okuphela kwakhe, uThembile. 
uThembile ukhuliswa nguyisekazi, uZamile onomfazi onguNojenti. 
UZamile noNojenti abanabantwana. 
Ekukhuleni kwakhe uThembile uthatha inkosikazi egama linguNomava. 
Iqala apho imfazwe nodushe. 
UZamile akavumi neenkomo zikaZilandu ukuba uThembile azeke ngazo. 
UThembile akanangxaki malunga nekhazi. 
Mve uThembile ethatha noTat’omncinci wakhe ngokuthatha umfazi, bave bethetha: 
Thembile: Bawokazi, njengoko ndisekhefini emsebenzini wam, ndicinga ukuba ndithi ndiphethukele emsebenzini ndibe ndinento endiyiqabelisayo kwezobudoda. 
Zamile: Phum’ egusheni Dikela omhle ungajikelezi. 
Iingxaki zobudoda zingangoboya benja. 
Thembile: Bawokazi ndifuna ukuba ndiphethuke kukho umtshakazi ojikeleza phakathi kwalo mzi 
Zamile: Watsho kakuhle mfo wam. 
Bendicinga ukutsho zonke ezi ntsuku koko ndisoyika ukuba nxamnye neengcina zakho. 
Ngaba phofu mfo wam umi njani etikini.
Kaloku ukuzeka asikokudlala undize. Kufuneka indoda isebenze ingafekethi ngemali. 
Thembile: Kwelo cala akukho ngxaki tat’omncinci. Imali ikhona.. 
Apha ngentla uThembile uyazibika kutat’omncinci wakhe ngenjongo zakhe zokuthatha umfazi, kwaye uyamqinisekisa ukuba ume kakuhle nangasemalini, ikhazi uza kukwazi ukulibhatala akukho ngxaki. 
Ingxaki iqala apho uThembile athi xa ecela ukuthatha nokuba ngamathobele ambalwa ebuhlanti, ze uZamile angavumi. 
Yive le ncoko iqhubeka: 
Thembile:Kwelo cala akukho ngxaki tat’omncinci. 
Imali ikhona yaye ndicinga ukuba singathatha nokuba mathathu kula mathole asebuhlanti. 
Zamile: Kaloku mfo wam akunakho ukucinga ngala mathole asebuhlanti xa ufuna ukuzeka. 
Ziinkomo zeli khaya ezi asizizo? 
Thembile: Ewe tata andijonganga zona. Ndijonge ukuba sibhenele kuzo xa kucaca ukuba umcimbi uyenyuka malunga nelobola. 
Zamile: Sukufane ucinge ngezi nkomo, Thembile. Loo nto ndiyayithetha andiyinkuntuzi. Iinkomo ezi zezam. 
Thembile: Kanene tat’ omncinci asinguwe na owandibonisa iinkomo ezazithengwe ngubawo esaphila? 
Zamile: Ewe ndim mfo wam, Uyihlo esaphila ndamncedisa ngamathokazi amabini ekuzekeni kwakhe ngenjongo yokuba naye uya kwenjenjalo ekuzekeni kwam. 
Ngelishwa ke iNkosi yakhawuleza yamphuthuma. Ke ezi iinkomo zikolu thango lwam 
azinakho ukuphinda zibizwe ngaye. Qokelela imali wena uze nayo ukuze sikwazi ukuqalisa umncimbi wokukuzekela.
Ndigqibile ke Qwathi. (Atsho aphakame ayimise ngothango echitha amanzi.) 
UZamile akavumanga kwaphela neenkomo zokuncedisana noThembile nangona wayekhe watsho ukuba zikho nezikatata kaThembile phakathi kwazo. 
Kodwa ngoku ume ngxi ukuba uThembile akazokufumana nokuba inye kwiinkomo ezisebuhlanti. 
Kodwa njengamntu uthatha indawo katata kaThembile kuba owakhe utata wasweleka, kodwa ngoku xa uThembile efuna inkxaso yakhe, uzikhupha ngaphandle. 
UNojenti akayithandi tu into yokuzeka kukaThembile. 
Konke oku kuye kubangelwa ngumona. Kuvelwa ukuyokucelwa intombi ebonwe nguThembile, eyibonele ukuyitshata. 
Bathi xa bebuya, bebuya nengxelo, uNojenti akakwazi ukuzibamba ngendlela anomona ngayo ngokutshata kukaThembile.  
KwaZamile kuhleli uZamile, Kholisile noMdendo. Oonozakuzaku beze nengxelo. 
Zamile: Khanitsho nto zikabawo, nihambe njani? 
Mdendo: Sihambe kakuhle kakhulu mkhuluwa khange sisokoliswe tu. 
Zamile: Abanibethanga kakhulu kodwa? 
Kholisile: Hayi mkhuluwa. Bathe kratya nje kancinci ukudlula kuleya yethu iminwe. 
Zamile:Yitsho kaloku. Badlule kangakanani? 
Kholisile: Bengeze iinkomo ezintlanu ezintlanu ezinethole, baza bathi ezintathu kufuneka zihambe ngamanqina. 
Nojenti: (Eburhamla esentla)Rhaa! Ndingatsho nje ukuba yinkosazana le niyizekayo? 
Yakha yakho intombi elotyolwa ngeenkomo ezingakonexabso eliphezulu olo hlobo? 
Mdendo: Naso ke isimanga! Kwakha kwanje phi na? Sathi sixoxa umcimbi wakwaNoni kwaNoni kwangenela umendi singammemanga, kuhle ntoni? 
Zamile: Nojenti! Nojenti! Nojenti! Nceda ulungise izinto zakho phandle siza kukubiza xa sikufuna. 
Nojenti: (Ephuma) Hayi kodwa nizizisulu. Bonke abantu baya kuzihlolela apha kuni iintombi zabo baze bakwazi ukubiza unothanda. 
Kuqala uNojenti ubonisa ubukrwada kunye nongabi nambeko ngokuthi angenelele kwincoko engamfuniyo xeshikweni kuxoxa amadoda ekhaya ngendaba zelobola kaThembile. 
Ekubeni engenantlonipho enjalo, ubonisa ubukrwada ngendlela avela aphoseleke ngayo ephendula ingxoxo ekude kunaye. 
Kwaye uthetha ngendlela erhabaxa ngokungathi uthetha nabahlobo bakhe. 
Kwelinye icala uTeteleza noNontsipho nabo abayithandi into yokuthandana nokuzekana kukaNomava noThembile. 
Bona banomona kuba benqwenela ukuba uNomava athandane, endele kuNtemese unyana kaTeteleza. 
Khabave ke xa bexoxa ngalomba: Teteleza: Mholo ntokazi. Walibala kukonwaba nkazana akuyivanga ingxaki endikuyo? 
Nontsipho: Yiza nazo Teteleza mfazi: Ndizifuna ngoku zingekabethwa yimitha yelanga. 
Phokoza mfazi isifuba sam somile. Andinayo nento entsha endiza kungena ngayo phakathi kwabanye abafazi namhlanje. 
Ayilunganga into yokuya uze phakathi kwamanye amakhosikazi. 
Kufuneka qho kusisa ufike nenqaku elitsha nokuba liyachitha, nokuba likhaya, ayifuni ooNontsipho loo nto. 
Thina sisebenzisa izixhobo esazinikwa nguThixo. ( Atsho esalatha elulwimini) 
Teteleza: Wethu! Andilalanga phezolo ngunyana wam uNtemese. 
Ubusuku bonke uyashwabula ethetha kalusizi mfazi. 
Nontsipho: Uthi nansti intoni na lo mntwana, Teteleza? 
Nontsipho mfazi, uNtemee uliliswa kukubona esaa simoyoywana singuThembile sincokola ngokuzola noNomava, de baqwele ngokuphuzana xa besahlukana. 
Nontsipho: Yhe Teteleza! Uthi uyayiva le nto uyithethayo? 
Ucinga ukuba uNomava angaze abe nento ayithetha nalla mzobololo womnyewu wakwaSifuba? 
Yintoni yna laa nto, into esoloko ithe bhaku iindlebe ngathi ityiwa ngamakhalane. 
Teteleza: Nontsipho! Ikamba labantwana bethu lisezandleni zethu. 
Ukunyaba kwabo kuxhomekeke kuthi. 
Umntwana wam ukhathazekile. Ukuba unalo mfazi icebo libeke etafileni. Musa ukolula intetho ngathi uyahleka. Kubi mfazi. 
Esi sibini siyenze kwacaca gca apha kule ncoko ingentla into yokuba le ndibano kaThembile kunye noNomava abayithandisisi kwaphela kwaye bengayithandisisi nje kufuneka kwenziwe icebo lokuba iqhiwulwe. 
Ngenxa yokubona le meko kaNojenti, uThembile ugqiba ekubeni ayeke ukuphangela kuba engafuni ukushiya uNomava kolunjalo uchuku. 
uNojenti umphatha kakubi uNomava kuba efuna ukuba ahambe. 
Izenzo zempatho mbi kaNojenti zide zimphathe kakubi uNomava, ade afune ukuhamba, le nto kanye ifunwa nguNojenti. Mve uNomava ethetha nomnyeni wakhe ngempatho-mbi kaNojenti: 
Nomava: (Elila) Bhuti Thembile ingathi ndazikhanda ngenyheke elityeni ukuvuma isicelo sakho. 
Umama wakho akafuni nokundibona, kunjalo nje ndinoloyiko lwento eya kuzalwa yile meko ndiyibonayo. 
Bhuti Thembile sithandwa sam ndilusizi ukuba ndithi ndifika kowenu ndithethe ngomzali wakho kuwe, kodwa ke nawe uyabona ukuba kufanelekile ndenze njalo. 
Thembile: Kunjalo mfazi. Umama uyawuchitha mpela lo mzi. 
Kodwa yonke le nto intsha, ifikisene nokuzeka oku kwam. 
Besaxoxa njalo nanku uNojenti engena nobukrwada bakhe: 
Nojenti: Nkqonkqo – nkqo. Yintoni emzini wam ndabona sendinamaxhwele? 
Yintoni ebangela ukuba ningavuki Thembile nale ntlubuntlubu yomntwana ongenambeko? 
Wena, ngaphandle kobudenge obu bakho wakha wambona umtshakazi elala kude kuphume ilanga? 
Ndifuna ukucoca indlu yam ngoku phumani phandle. 
Nomava: Tyhini mama! Kudala ndiyibona le nto yakho. 
Uthi masiphume ngeli xesha? Kutheni le nto ungakwaziyo ukuyiquma inkohlakalo yakho? 
Nojenti: Ndaza ndasiva isimanga sokukhonkothwa ngumtshakazi okracakraca. 
Yintoni le ndiyiziselwe emzini wam? 
Ndodle, ndondle inkedama kanti ndizilolela izembe. 
Sokuze ndizokulawulwa emzini wam. 
Nditsho ndithi phumani nakuzibonela ukuba maniyephi na. 
Nomava: Utsho phantsi mama. Mna andiyi ndawo. 
Ukuba uyandigxotha kufuneka uthumele oonozakuzaku ekhaya baye kuxela ukuba babengandiceleli mzi. 
Ukuba leyo iyakoyisa yitsho kwakwabo nozakuzaku bandigoduse qha ke. 
Thembile: Mama yeka le nto uyenzayo. Umona awunakamva. 
Nojenti: Thula wena. Uzibona ubudoda ngoku. 
Wakha waphendula kum kakade ngokuya wawungekazeki? 
Thembile: Wawungangcungcuthekisa mna ndeda. 
Andinakuthula kuba umntwana lo wabantu uze ngam apha, ke andinakubukela ephekwa esophulwa. 
Nojenti: Ndokhe ndibone ukuba nakulala phi na namhlanje. 
Watsho ephosa iingubo zabo nokhuko phandle. 
Xa kuxoxwa, kulungiswa uchuku lukaNojenti kuvuka uthuli ngenxa yokuthukwa kukaMdendo nguNojenti. 
UMdendo uqhwaba uNojenti ngempama. 
UZamile ubetha uMdendo ngenduku ambulale enqandela uNonjenti. 
uKholisile uqobongela uThembile ukuba bangaxeli ukuba nguZamile obulele uMdendo koko bathi ujuleke wawa, wasweleka. 
Impatheko-mbi kaNomava iyenyukela. uNomava ufumana umntwana bamthiye igama elinguMava. 
UNontsipho noTeteleza beza necebo lokubulala uThembile kuNojenti naye alamkele. 
UZamile ubulawa kukusela utywala obunetyhefu obebulungiselelwe uThembile. 
UNojenti ukruneka isinqe xa esukela endlwini ukuya kuphazamisa uZamile angaseli utywala obunetyhefu. 
UNojenti uyayichaza ityhefu ukuba uyifumene kuNontsipho noTeteleza abamelwane bakhe. 
Bayakhanyela ooNontsipho noTeteleza. 
Isibhedlela simnika isitulo esinamavili uNojenti kuba kucaca ukuba akanakho ukuphinda ahambe ngeenyawo zakhe. 
UNojenti ucela uxolo “ Ndixoleleni” kuNovanya, Thembile, Nomava nakuwo onke amaQwathi ngokuwuvunduza awuchithachithe umzi ngochuku nomona. .  
Ndaba nomona kukuzeka kukaThembile, ndimmonela ngayo yonke into eniyibonayo kulo mzi. 
Ndamtshutshisa ndimngcungcuthekamisa nomfazi wakhe ndicinga ukuba uya kukruquka ahambe koko wanyamezela. 
Ubhuti uMdendo wabulaliswa ndim kuba indoda yam yayinqanda mna emva kokuba ndimthukile. 
Indoda yam yabulawa ndim kuba ndandingbafuni abantu bomzi wam apha kulo mzi. 
Ityhefu eyabulalaumyeni wam ndandiyinikwe nguTeteleza noNontsipho. 
Namhlanje andikwazi kuhamba ndilusana. Ndixoleleni nonke. 
Ndicela uxolo Nomava. Uze uncede undigcine mntwana wam ndikubonile ukunyamezelakwakho. 
Yonke into elapha kulo mzi endandikumonela ngayo, namhlanje ndiyinika wena noThembile. 
Elo lifa ulinikwe nguThixa ngenxa yokunyamezela kwakho.
UNojenti ude wazibona iziphumo zezenzo zakhe wabona ukuba ulenzile udushe olukhulu nobubi obungaphaya kokuqonda. 
Ngoku ucela uxolo kubo bonke abo athe wabona ngoba uyabona ukuba uqol’uphandle ngoku. 
Uyazivuma zonke izono zakhe, kwaye uyavuma ngoku into yokuba zonke izenzo zakhe besikhokelwa lumona. 
Zonke izinto zakhe uzinikela kuThembile noNomava. 
Bonke bayamxolela. uNonjenti UKholisile uxhela inkabi yenkomo ukubulela uThixo nezinyanya ngokuphinda abuyisele uxolo nobunye kumzi wakwaSifuba. 
Nomava: Musa ukulila mama, sula iinyembezi. 
Mna noThembile sakuxolela kudala, sokuze sikulahle. 
Novanya: Nam ndimxolele kuba siyafana. 
Naye ungumhlolokazi kodwa yena ungcono kuba nguye ozibeke kuloo ndawo. 
Nojenti: NguNontsipho noTeteleza zinkosi zam. Owu! Nandenza zihlobo zam zabumini. 
Akhale kwakhona, Ndixoleleni. Ndixoleleni. 
Kholisile: (Ebhekisa kuThembile) Mfo wam umvile unyoko ezisola ecela uxolo kananjalo. 
Le nto yenzekileyo asikokuthanda kwamntu. 
Yintando kaThixo afuna ngayo ukuzibonakalisa ubukhulu bakhe. 
Uze uncede ungabi nanqala kunyoko amile ngezinto abazenza nabazithetha kuwe. 
Ndiyaphinda ndithi uze ungabanqali abazali bakho. 
Ngabazali bakho aba kuba bakondlile bakukhulisa wada waba yile ndoda uyiyo. 
Yonke le nto yenzekileyo uze ungayibambi… 
Ukuhlamba eli lishwa lokuchithakala komzi, ngomso ndifuna kuhlatywe laa nkabi yenkomo imnyama yam sitye sonke nelali ize kungqina xa sibulela uThixo ngokuphinda avuselele uxolo nobunye phakathi kosapho lwakwaSifuba.  
Nanko ke uNojenti ezisola ngezenzo zakhe zokungcola. 
Ngelaka nethamsanqa, wone abantu abanobuntu kunye noekibuThixo, abakwaziyo ukuxola xa bebona ukuba umntu ebelahlekile. 
Bona ooThembile nooKholisile abenzi le nto yayisenziwa nguNojenti yokuvalela abantu ngaphandle engafuni nokuba bona, bona bayalamkela uxolo lwakhe ngentliziyo ezikhululekileyo ngoba bayaqonda ukuba umona yinto apha enobungozi, kwaye etshabalalisayo. 
Makuthenjwe ke ukuba uNojenti usifundile isifunde sakhe, kwaye uyaqonda ngoku into yokuba, umona alwakhi. 
Ukuba luyalandeleka kakuhle olu phando, kuya kukhumbuleka ukuba pha ekuqaleni kwintshayelelo bekukhankanyiwe ukuba, eli icandelo lijonga indlela ababhali besini sobuduna abathi bazibhalo ngalo izibhalo zabo zedrama kunye nendlela ababazoba ngayo abalinganiswa babo abangamabhinqa. 
Unobangela wokuba oku kukhankanywe kwakhona kungenxa yokuthungelana kweli bali u-‘Ndixoleleni’ kunye neliya lithi, ‘Inene Nasi Isibhozo’. 
Xa sijonga eli ibali le drama, kuye kubonakale ngokucacileyo ukufana phakathi kwawo kunye neliya likaMtingane. 
Omakaqapheleke kukuba bobabini aba babhali babhale ezi ncwadi zedrama ngabantu besilisa, kwaye indlela ababazoba ngayo abalinganiswa babo ababhinqileyo ifana nkcakasa. 
Kwa umxholo wala mabali mabini uyafana. 
Yiyo loo nto umphandi ezikhethe zombini ezi ncwadi ukubonisa into yokuba ababhali besilisa babazoba ngokufanayo abalinganiswa abangamabhiqa. 
Nakweli bali umba obalaseleyo bubugqwirha nokukhohlakala kwamabhinqa, anamona kwaye aqhutywa kukungcola kwizenzo zabo. 
Oku sikubona kwiintshukumo zomlinganiswa obhinqileyo uNonjenti. 
Kodwa ke olu phando luza kungena nzulu koku, ze luveze banzi oku kuthethwa ngako, kujongwe aba balinganiswa bazotywe ngokufanayo kwelinye ibali ebeselikhankanyiwe. 
Umlinganiswa oyintloko kweli bali kungatshiwo ukuba nguMasukude. 
Uthe akuswelekelwa ngumyeni wakhe uNjinge, waye washiyeka nonyana wakhe uVuma, kwaze kwathi kokuhamba ixesha, wafikelela kwelokuba unyana wakhe uVuma makazekelwe umfazi ngoba ke kaloku yena ufuna umntu oza kujongana nekhaya, ancedisane naye kwimisebenzi yaphakathi ekhayeni ngoba yena uyaguga, kwaye naye uVuma uye esiba mdala. 
Kodwa ukubuya kukaThemba eKapa kwazimosha zonke iinzame zikaMasukude ngokuba kaloku bekungasokuze kukwazi ukuzekelwe uVuma, abe umkhuluwa wakhe yena engekazekelwa. 
Elo ke lisiko lakwaXhosa, ngoko ke bekungekho ndlela yokuba uMasukude aphikisane naloo nto, ngoba isiko aliphikiswa liyahlonelwa. 
UMasukude wabonakala kwasekuqaleni ukuba uzakuba yingxaki kulo mzi, kuba kuhleliinje kukhalwa ngesimilo sakhe, nendlela angakwazi ngayo ukuziphatha. 
Yiyo lo nto abaninawa nabakhuluwa omnyeni wakhe ongasekhoyo baqonda izinto zomzi kabhuti wabo bazithathele kuba, hayi bayiyekele kuMasukude ongevayo oko mntwana ongaqeqeshekanga. 
Mve omnye wabo eyicacisa le nto: Mfolo: (KuLolo) Khawume kuhle (KuMasukude) Uyabona Masukude kukwaNjinge ekhay’apha. 
Lo ngumzi waseMakhwalweni. Okoko kwabhubha uNjinge, lomzi waba ngundaba-mlonyeni phakathi kwezivondoviya zochuku ezikhoyo kule lali. 
Namhlanje ulwa noMadlamini ngento engekhoyo. Nisakuba nilanyulwe, usuka uye kubaqhiwulela ethafeni. 
Nalapho usokoyiswa, ufunza uVuma ukuba aye kubetha ooninamncinci. 
Nantsi into emandikuphe yona: Kusekho uNjinge, besiyichitha imini sonwabile ekhay’apha, simke kungekabikho kukrwentsa-krwentsana; kodwa ngoku sibetha emva kwezindlu ngenxa yesimilo sakho osiphethe ngezandla. 
Kanti ke, khumbula ukuba indoda yakho iyazibona zonke ezi zinto zingamasikizi uzenzayo. Thina ke bakowayo asinakukukhalala kuphele kuba sakuba sikhalala yona. Nanku uLolo, umninawe kaNjinge, oliliso lalo mzi. 
Ukuba kukho into ekuxakileyo okanye ongayithandiyo, yibike kuye nibonisane ngayo nobabini. 
Andifuni kuphinda ndithethe ngolu hloboo kuwe. Xa ndize ekhaya apha, ndingavuya ndize umzimba wam ukhululekile, ndifike wonke wonke umntu onwabile, nam ndibuye ndimke kusahlekwa. 
Qweba isimilo ke njengawo onke amakhosikazi andilekileyo. 
Esi similo sikaMasukude sobubi sibonwe kwakude kudala, seqhanqalaze nje ekuhambeni kwencwadi, esenza ububi, ukwenza oko sekukudala wacelwa ukuba aqeqeshe isimilo sakhe. 
Siyabona apha exelelwa ukuba uLolo uzakuba liliso losemzini wakhe, aze athi ancedisane naye kwizigqibo ekufuneka ezenzile phakathi kwekhaya kuba uNjinge engesakhoyo. 
Kodwa yena uMasukude ufuna ukuba ngumfazi noyihloko emzini wakhe, hayi le nto yokuba kufuneka agqibe kubantu basemzini wakhe xa efuna ukuthatha isigqibo kwinto afuna ukuyenza. 
Ingxwabangxwaba paya yaqala ekubeni uLolo, umninawa kaNjinge, abe kanti ujongene nalo mzi, nto ethetha ukuba nguye oza kuthi enze izigqibo zeli khaya, nto apha angayithanga kwaphela uMasukude ngoba ke kaloku, lo mzi ngowakhe, ngoke ke nguye ekumele ukuba abe yintloko. 
Ekubeni uMasukude exelele uLolo ngenjongo zakhe zokuba kuzekelwe uVuma kuqala kunoThemba, uLolo uye wabiza amanye amadoda akwaNjinge ukuba kuxowe lo mba. 
Kule ngxoxo uMasukude ugxothiwe ngelithi, bona abasoze baxoxe nomfazi. 
Kaloku ingcingane yesini sobukhomokazi isixelela ukuba amadoda awababoni ebalulekile amabhinqa kwaye awafuni ukuwabandakanya kwizinto ezibalulekileyo zekhaya, ngelithi ngumsebenzi wobudoda lowo ngaphandleni xa esekhitshini epheka, apho indawo yabo ikhona, yiyo loo nto la madoda engakhange avume ukuba kuxoxwe phambi kukaMasukude nje. 
Iva la madoda akwaNjinge, ebhekisa kuMasukude: 
UMfolo: Kuhle, ndingakuxholi, usemile njalo, ngaba lityala eli okanye sihlangene ngomcimbi wekhaya, apha kulo mzi namhlanje? 
ULolo: Sihlanene ngomcimbi wekhaya. 
UMfolo: Ngaba imicimbi yomzi apha siyixoxa kunye nabafazi? 
ULolo: Asiyilungisi nabafazi. 
UMfolo: Lo ke umfazi uza kwaneka umcimbi womzi emadodeni, uza kusanekela ngabuni? 
UMfolo: Wethu, mus’ undiyilozela. Asinguwe na iliso lalo mzi akubhubha umkhuluwa wakho? 
UMazwazwa: Unyanisile umkhuluwa lo. Usisi unokubizwa sithi xa kukh’ into esifuna ukuyiqonda. 
UMfolo: (Ekhomba uLolo) khangela ndiyakunyola ngoku. Xa axoxayo ke amadoda, aphikisana de anyolane.
Uthi ke wena uMasukude makanyolane noyisezala kunye nabakhuluwa bakhe apha? 
Tyhini, bafondini, Ngooban’aba baza  kubhenguzelwa ngeelokhwe? 
(kuMasukude) Masukude, thatha i-emele uyokukha amanzi, upheke, sakukubiza xa sikufuna. 
Umzizi: Ngokwenyaniso epheleleyo, asimelwe kukuphikisana noMasukude xa sixoxa. 
Buyimpazama ubukho bakhe. Kambe nakuthi kuyimpazamo ukukrazula xa sithetha kukho umntu obhinqileyo; kaloku bakhathazeka msinya yintetho eqatha nerhabaxa. 
Ezi ntetho zivela kula madoda athetha apha ngentla, zingaphikiswa mpela ngamabhinqa alwela ukulingana phakathi kwamadoda namabhinqa.
Ngoba kaloku la madoda athetha ukuba abafazi abanawo amandla okuxoxa izinto ezibalulekileyo kwaye ezinzima. 
Nto apha ekhatywayo ngala mabhinqa, ngoba afuna ukubonisa amadoda into yokuba nawo anako ukumelana neengxoko zekhaya, yiyo loo nto zifuna ukubandakanywa xa kusenziwa iingxoxo ezilolu hlobo. 
Yiyo loo nto ingakhange ingene kamnandi kuMasukude into yokuba izinto zomzi wakhe zixoxwe ngaphandle kwakhe. 
Ibe ibubomi bonyana wakhe wokuqala nowokugqibela lo kuxoxwa ngaye. 
Noko ngebemvumele ukuba ahlale amamele nokuba ke abamvumelanga ukuba ahlomle. 
Umxholo weli bali kungatshiwo ukuba kukubaluleka kokuhlonipha nokuthobela isiko ngoba ingxaki iqale xa uMasukude efuna ukutshintsha isiko ukuze izinto zenzeke ngolwakhe uhlobo. 
Xa siqwalasela eli bali liyidrama, sibona ukuba lo mfazi uMasukude ulwanayo yonke into ekuthiwa yindoda, kwakunye nawo wonke umntu ongumfazi. 
Kodwa ikakhulu ulwa namadoda asemzini wakhe ngoba ngawo ame endleleni yakhe yokuba unyana wakhe uVuma azekelwe kuqala kunetshipa elinguThemba. 
Umbhali apha kwelibali ubhalile ngezenzo zalo mlinganiswa, ngoba lo mlinganiswa kaMasukude ngumlinganiswa apha obalasele kubantu abangamadoda apho indoda ithi yenza nantoni na ukuze le nto ayifunayo yenzeke ngoluhlobo afuna ukuba yenzeke ngayo, ingakumbi kwizinto ezidibanise nezinto zamasiko. 
Ngoko ke umbhali ube nesizathu sokuba lo mlinganiswa amzobe ibe ngumntu obhinqileyo. 
Kwaye umbhali akaphosanga ukusizobela indlela lo mlinganiswa aziphatha ngayo phakathi kwabanye abantu ukubonisa ukuba akoyiki nto kunye namntu. 
Akanantanga tu uMasukude kwisimilo sakhe. 
Masikhe sibone lo mlinganiswa xa esenza ungxwaba-ngxwaba nomnye umfazi apha ekuhlaleni. 
Madlamini: Wenzeni na bethu ade abethwe kangaka? 
MaSukude: Asiyondawo yakho leyo! Asiyondawo yakho leyo! 
Madlamini: Ukubuza kunetyala na sisi? 
MaSukude: Ndithi asiyiyondawo yakho leyo! Asinguye mntwanakho lo. 
Madlamini: Nango ke umhlola bantu basemaZizini! Ndone phi ke ngo- 
MaSukude: Sukapha gagwazanandini! Ucinga ukuba kungokuya nanilimisa uVuma laa ntsimi yakwakho? 
Ezi zinto zenza umntwana isicaka sazo! Ezi zinto zithanda ukulawula! 
Madlamini: (Efutheka) Uphambene! 
MaSukude: Kuphambene wena ntondini. Ezi zinto zilima ngeenkomo zam. Ezi nto zivuyela umhlolokazi 
Apha ngentla umbhali uyasibonisa isimilo sikaMaSukude ukuba sinjani. 
Ukrwada, kwaye akanaso isimilo, ingathi akatshatanga, nokuba umyeni wakhe akasekho. 
Ude athi uyagezelwa ngenxa engumhlolokazi kodwa nguye ogeza agqithisele. 
Xa ugeza oluhlobo kubantu bangaphandle, kubethiselaphi kubantu ahlala nabo. 
Ukungalingani ngokwesini apha kweli bali sikubona kucace gca kuqala pha kula meko apho amadoda akwaNjinge angavumi ukuxoxa udaba lokuzeka 
kukaVuma phambi koMasukude kodwa nguye umama kaVuma, kwaye ngumzi wakhe lo baxoxa ngawo. 
Uthe xa uLolo exelela la madoda ngolu daba, impendulo yabo yabonisa ngoku- 
pheleleyo ukuba bona abasoze bazibandakanye namfazi xa kusiziwa kwizinto zekhaya, ngoba kaloku bona abafazi abababoni njengabantu abakwazi 
ukuxoxa nokubonisana ngezinto ezibaluleke olu hlobo okungathi abanangqondo yokucinga. 
Yiva impendulo yala madoda xa aphendula ubukho bukaMasukude engxoxweni: 
ULolo: Sihlangane ngomcimbi wekhaya. 
UMfolo:Ngaba imicimbi yomzi apha siyixoxa kunye nabafazi? 
ULolo: Asiyilungisi nabafazi. 
UMfolo: Lo ke umfazi uza kwaneka umcimbi womzi emadodeni, uza kusanekela ngabuni? 
ULolo: Kaloku, njengomnikazimzi- 
UMfolo:Wethu, mus’ukundiyilozela. Asinguwe na iliso lalo mzi akubhubha umkhuluwa wakho? 
Ukuba la madoda ebemhlonipha uMasukude, emjonga nje ngomntu onakho ukumelana nezinto zomzi wakhe, ngeyingekho ingxaki. 
Bona bambona njengomfazi ongasoze akwazi ukuzenzela izigqibo zomzi wakhe kuba engumfazi, yiyo loo nto bathi babeka uLolo njengeliso lekhaya emzini kaMasukude. 
UMasukude sesenza amayelenqe okubulala uLolo kunye noThemba ukuze imfuno zakhe zifezeke kungenxa yale mpatho yala madoda. 
Awazange amnika ithuba lokuba azihoyele izinto zomzi wakhe kuba benale ngcingane yokuba amabhinqa akumelanga abe nomzi ongowabo, kwaye amabhinqa awanaso isakhono sokujongana nomzi wonke opheleleyo kuba kaloku umsebenzi webhinqa kuphelele kuphela ekunakekeleni indoda yakhe, ukucoca njalo njalo. 
UMasukude wazifumana kwindawo apho wayefuna ukubonisa abantu ukuba umfazi angenza nantoni azixelele ukuba uza kuyenza, nangona yena wathi wayenza ngendlela engekho semthethweni kuba kaloku izenzo zakhe zabangela ukuba kubekho izidumbu ezininzi, ukuquka esonyana wakhe, nto le engakhange aqonde ukuba inothi yenzeke, ngenxa yokutyhalwa ngasemva yingcinezelo yamadoda. 
Uphononongo lwezinto zenkcubeko kweli candela liza kube lijonge amaxesha akudala namaxesha angoku. 
Kweli candela umphandi unqwenela ukuphonononga impembelelo yenkcubeko yakwaXhosa kubalinganiswa abangamabhinqa. 
Eli candela liza kujongana nezinto zamasiko akwaXhosa, ukungalingani ngokwsini nangokwezikhundla ekhayeni, ingakumbi emtshatweni.
Kwindlela esikhuliswa ngayo thina bantu baMnyama, sikhule siyazi ukuba izinto zekhaya zijongwa ngutata lowo wekhaya. 
Izigqibo ezibalulekiyo ezibandakanya izinto zamasiko nezithethe zosapho zihoywa ngutata wekhaya. 
Kodwa ngenxa yokutshintsha kwamaxesha, inguqu koko iyabonakala. 
Xa sijonge kwikhaya lwakwa Njinge, kuInene Nasi Isibhozo kaMtingane, siyayibona ingxwaba-ngxwaba yongquzulwano phakathi kwabantu bosapho xa kuxoxwa izinto zamasika nezithethe akwaXhosa, umzekelo, 
UMasukude ufuna ukuba unyana wakhe uVuma azeke kuqala kunoThemba, umkhuluwa wakhe. 
Qaphela ukuba isiko lakwaXhosa lithi unyana omdala nguye ozeka kuqala. 
Nalu ke olu ngquzulwano kwinkcubeko kunye namaxesha esimanje-manje. 
Ayikho indoda enokuyeka umfazi enze izigqibo zekhaya, kodwa amadoda osapho asekhona, nokuba umyeni wakhe sele wasandulelayo. 
Kodwa amabhinqa angoku angakuphikisa oko. Kaloku amaxesha ahlukile. 
Iindlela zokwenza izinto azisafani nezi zakude kudala. 
Amabhinqa ngoku ayakwazi ukuzenzela izigqibo, kwaye ame kwizigqibo zawo nokuba kukho ukungavisisani phakathi kwawo nabantu besilisa. 
Ndiyacinga ukuba yilento ebezama ukuyizoba umbhali xa wayebumba umlinganiswa uMasukude, kodwa ke yena wabe ebhalela phantsi kwexesha lakudala, hayi ela ngoku. 
Yiva uMasukude ethetha noLolo: UMasukude: Apha ekhaya akukho mntu.
ULolo: Ewe UMasukude: Kungekho mntu nje, nam sendimdala. 
UMasukude: Iintanga zam azisasebenzi ngolu hlobo ndisebenza ngalo. 
ULolo: Ewe ngenene unyanisile 
UMasukude: Ndifuna ke bhuti kubekho umntu ondincedisayo apha ekhaya. 
UMasukude: Ndifuna ke uVuma azeke. (Kuyathuleka) 
ULolo: Mh, hayi ndiyakuva. (Kuphinda kuyathuleka) Phofu, kutheni kuza kuqala uVuma, echo nje uThemba? 
UMasukude: UThemba uyafika, asimazi nokuba uza kuhlala na. 
ULolo: Unyanisile, kodwa masikhe sikhangele iinjongo zabo bobabini kuqala. 
UMasukude: Sikhangel’iinjango kanjani na? 
ULolo: Sijong’izinto abazicingayo. 
UMasukude: Ngeli xa nisakhangel’ iingcinga, mna ndiza kuncediswa ngubani? 
ULolo: Loo nto ayinakuthatha ixesha. 
UMasukude: Ukub’ uThemba ufun’ukuzeka? 
ULolo: Kuya kuba kulungile kaloku. 
UMasukude: O, ufuna kuqale uThemba? 
ULolo: Kuqala omdala kakade 
UMasukude: UVuma aze azithathe phi yena iinkomo zokulobola? 
ULolo: Beziya kuvelaphi kuThemba? 
UMasukude: (Ubambelela emadolweni) Tyhini! Tyhini! Bhuti, ezi nkomo ufuna ziphelele kuThemba? 
Efutha, Inene, nasi isibhozo! Akunakuze kuzekelwe itshiph’elagqiba ishumi leminyaka eKapa, ekh’uVuma umnt obelima egcine nezi nkomo… 
ULolo: Kuhle ngomsindo, akulunganga sense izinto sisemsindweni. 
UMasukude: (Emnyola) Umsindo ntoni? Umsindo wantoni? Ndikunqanda la maqhinga angakanana nje!
Bhetel’ izint zenzelwe emsindweni kunokuba zenzelw’ emaqhingeni. 
Apha ngentla siyambona umlinganiswa uMasukude ezama ukunyanzelisa ukuba kutshate unyana wakhe kuqala, kulityalwe ngesiko kwenziwe le ifunwa nguye. 
Oku kubonisa olu tshintsho lwamaxesha, ngoba ngexesha lakudala, umfazi ebengasoze athetha nabantu basemzini wakhe ngolu hlobo. 
Umbhali ayasibonisa indlela amasiko atyeshelwa ngayo kule mihla, nendlela umgangatho wentlonipho phakathi kwamakhaya uthe wehla ngayo. 
Le ncwadi yedrama ithi “Inene Nasi IsiBhozo” iyayixhasa, iyiqinisekisa ingcamango yokuba amabhinqa anzulu kwaye ngawona anobungozi ekuhlaleni kuphela, obu bungozi bubangela ukuba babonwe njengabantu abanako ukuba ngamagqwirha athakatha abanye abantu, de banikezele 
ngeengcebiso ezingendawo kwaye ezilahlekisayo. 
UMasukude nguye otyholekayo ekwenzeni la msebenzi umdaka obonwa njengokuthakatha nokuphatha gadalala unyana womnyeni wakhe. Yiva le ntetho ingezantsi: 
UMaDlamini: Gqwirandini elingenanceba ngumntwana ongenanina! 
Le ntetho ingentla ibonisa ukuba iintshukumo zika MaSukude zezomntu lo uthakathayo kwaye ungenasizi, kwaye akamkelwa lusapho lwakhe ngenxa yendlela amphatha ngayo lo mfana. 
Oku kucebisa ukuba unentliziyo yobugqwirha, ntliziyo ke ikhokelele ekubeni abulale umntu enganatyala. 
Oku kubonisa ngokucace gca okwekat’ emhloph’ ehlungwini ukuba abantu abazibandakanya kwimisebenzi emdaka engaqondakaliyo bajongeka njengabantu ababandakanyeka kwizinto zobuthakathi.
Le ntetho ilandelayo ibonisa into yokuba eli bhinqa likulungele ukubulala umntu ongenasono: 
UNoayini: (Erhola iqhina) Akunavalo kodwa ngoku? 
UMasukude: (Elithatha) Mfazi, ndiqine ngaphezu kwelitye lenyengane. 
UNoayini: Lifihle ke kweyona ndawo uyiqondayo. 
Olu caphulo lungentla luzoba umlinganiswa uNoayini njengesikhohlakali esiluhlazo phakathi kwabanye abantu. 
Ibonisa into yokuba lo mlinganiswa ubhinqileyo uhlelinje ukulungele ukwenza okubi. 
uNoayini uzotywe nje wangumlinganiswa omdaka, kwaye ongcolileyo, onikeza iingcebiso ezikhohlakeleyo kuMasukude. 
uMaSukude unika uThemba umvubo onetyhefu ukuze umbulale. Iinjongo zakhe kukumnqanda ekubeni atshate phambi konyana wakhe uVuma. 
UMasukude: … Nifuna ukutyela phi? 
UThemba: Hayi silungile apha emlilweni mama, umvubo uyagodolisa 
UMasukude: Kulungile. (Uthatha izitya ngokuziqwalasela. Unika uThemba esi sinento. 
Esinye usinika uVuma) Yityani nihluthe , niye kuzibeka amacala, niphumlele imini yangomso… 
UThemba: Lo mvubo usuke wabulumeza 
Oku kubhalwe ngentla kubonisa indlela uMasukude athe wamfakela yona ityhefu uThemba ekutyeni. 
Ukubonisa ukuba uzimisele kule nto ayenzayo uyaqinisekisa ukuba uThemba uthatha esi sinento emdaka isitya. 
Bobo bugqirhwa kuthethwa ngabo ke obu, uthe wabenza ngendlela apho athe wenza ingathi uyamthanda uThemba, ude amenzele nokutya. 
Ukumfakela ityhefu khange kumonelise uMasukude, wazixelela ukuba uza kubulala nabani na oma endleleni yakhe yokufumana oko akufunayo apha emzini wakhe. 
UMaSukude: Uyabona ke, le komityi ize iphunge uLolo uyeva 
Le yona intetho ibonisa into yokuba uMasukude usebenzisa elinye iqhinga lokubulala umninawa womyeni wakhe. 
Kodwa icebo lakhe liye limjikela ngoba iti le ayikhange iye kulo mntu ebefuna iye kuye, yase yatsho ukumjikela. 
Lo mfazi akaphelelwa kukungcola namayelenqe okwenza okubi ebantwini abamsulwa, akayeki nto ime phambi kwakhe noko afuna ukwenza. 
Ibisele ichatshazelwe indlela apho ababhali abathi babachonge ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo njengezikhohlakali zamagqwirha. 
Nalapha kweli ke ibali ledrama, uMbovane udlalile ngaloo ngcamango xeshikweni ebezoba lo mlinganiswa ubhinqileyo unguNojenti. 
Abababhali besini sobukhomokazi uMtingane kunye noMbovane abohlukanga kakhulu kwindlela ababhala ngayo amabali abo bedrama. 
Kwaye abohlukanga kwindlela abawazoba ngayo amabhinqa kumabali abo. 
Nto le iphendula umbuzo okhe wavela kolu phando, wokuba, ingaba ababhali abasini esifanayo babhala ngokufanayo na. 
Babazoba ababalinganiswa babe ngendlela ethile, njengoko kusenziwa ngabanye ababhali abasini sobuduna. 
Umbhali apha ngentla usivezela into yokuba ababhali besini sobuduna abanavelwano ngamabhinqa xa bebhala la mabali abo, okanye baswela indlela yokubazoba ngendlela ephucukileyo okanye indlela enyusa isidima sabo ekuhlaleni nakwiintsapho zabo. 
Ekufundeni kwethu eli bali ledrama, sibe siqwalalasele umlinganiswa uNojenti, kuyacaca ukuba lo mlinganiswa uneempawo zikaMasukude, pha kulaa drama kaMtingane. 
UNojenti uzotywe njengebhinqa eliqhutywa ngumona kunye nenkohlakalo kwizenzo zakhe. 
Lo mona wakhe uye udale udushe, dushe olo luqanduselwa kukubhubha kwabantu, kanti loo nto ayimnqandi uNojenti kwizenzo zakhe. 
Kuthe xa uNontsipho kunye noTeteleza besiza necebo lukubulala uThembile kuNojenti, naye uNojenti alwamkele, ukubonisa indlela lo mfazi anzulu ngayo, cebo elo lithe lamjikela, laselibulala umyeni wakhe uZamile endaweni kaThembile. 
Kulapho athi aqabuke aqale ukuchaza inyani, azibone ukungcola kwakhe, kuba izenzo zakhe zithe zamjikela zamthathela isithandwa sakhe, ze naye azibone sele ehlala esitulweni, onzakele ezama ukunqanda ingozi, abe umzi wabantu sele kudala ezama ukuwuchitha-chitha ngochuku nangomona. 
(KwaZamile kuhleli uZamile, Kholisile noMdendo. Oonozakuzaku beze negxelo.) 
Zamile: Yitsho kaloku. Badlulle kangakanani? 
Kholisile: Bengeze iinkomo ezintlanu ezinethole, baza bathi ezinthathu kufuneka zihambe ngamanqina. 
Nojenti: (Ebharhamla esentla) Rhaa! Ningatsho nje ukuba yinkosazana le niyizekayo? Yakha yakho intombi elotyolwa ngeenkomo ezingako nexabiso eliphezulu olo hlobo? 
Nojenti: (Ecaleni kwendlu) Yhe bethuna! Kazi nguncanyelweni esiza kumthini na lo! Wakha wakho umcimbi oqalwa ugqitywe ngemini enye? 
Kuyacaca ukuba lo mntwana ebesele ekruqule kokwabo. 
Apha siyayibona le nkohlakalo kaNojenti xa kanye isaqandusela, kwindlela aphendula ngayo akuva ilobola ebhatalelwe uNomava, lowo ukufundayo 
oku uyabona kusasukwa ukuba uNojenti seyazi ukuba akamthandisisi kwaphela uNomava, ngoku engamazi nokumazi. 
Ukanti le nkohlakalo kaNojenti ibisaqala apha ngentla, oyena mntu ebezimisele ukuyijulisa kuye kuNomava, ngenxa yomona nenkohlaka. 
Mve xa ethetha gabalala kumntwana wabantu, ongenasono: 
Nomava: Nkqo-nkqo. 
Zamile: (Evula ucango) Ngena mntwana wam 
Nojenti: Ngubani lo usivusa sizilele? 
Nomava: Mholweni mama. Ndim ndizise into ephungwayo. 
Nojenti: Yintoni ebangela ukuba usivuse silele? Uve ngabani ukuba sifuna ikofu eyenziwe nguwe? 
Ndiqhele ukuyenza ikofu apha ndenzele nalo myeni wakho webhongo. 
Hamba uphume apha nalo mgrwatyili womngxambuluza wekofu yakho. 
Ndiza kuvuka ndizenzele ikofu. 
Nomava: Yhini mama sowuyeka utata aphunge yena. 
Nojenti: Yhoo! Waphendula uNozesazi. Sebekuthwesile abahlebi bale lali, kanti senditshilo. 
Zamile: Hamba mntwana wam, ndiza kumthethisa unyoko lo. 
Nojenti:Kudala ndikuxelela ukuba le nto yokuzeka kukaThembile andiyithandi mna kodwa wena akufuni kuphulaphula. 
Andazi ukuba uza kuva ngawuphi na umfazi xa ungeva mna. Yena uThembile ndiza kumbonisa. Ndiza 
kumngcungcuthekisa nalo mfazi wakhe baphume ngomva kula masango am. Yhini le! Bazenza iinyoka? 
Bafuna ukungena okweenyoka kumzi wam ongaka ukuba mkhulu ndiwakhe ngamagxa am. Soze ndibone sele ndinemingqungu yabantwana abajonge ukuxhamla ilifa lamandla am. 
Umphandi uzama ukubonisa ngokucacileyo ukukhohlakala kwalo mfazi. 
Umbhali wale drama wenze umsebenzi omhle ukumzoba lo mlinganiswa njengesikhohlakali. 
Uziveze zonke iinkalo zebhinqa elikhohlakaleyo. Mboneni uNojenti ethukisa, ethetha amazwi arhabaxa kuNomava phambi komyeni wakhe, engenazo 
neentloni zokuthetha amazwi amdaka ehleli ecaleni komyeni wakhe, ekumele ukuba umhlonele kwaye umhloniphile. 
Yiyo loo nto umphandi eza kuthi, umbhali wenze umsebenzi omhle ukumbumba lo mlinganiswa. 
Kodwa lowo ufundayo makaqaphele ukuba, oku akuthethi ukuba wonke umfazi umphatha olu hlobo umntwana womnye umntu, nokuba akenzanga siphene ngakuye. 
Kodwa singabantu abaphila kweli xesha, masithembe ukuba abantu abanje ngooNojenti abasaphili phantsi kweli langa. 
Zininzi iindlela ababhali bedrama abathi bawabhale ngazo amabali abo edrama, bewabhala ngeenjongo ezahlukileyo. 
Ekubeni umbhali efikele kwisigqibo sokuba uza kubhala ngantoni, uye ayazi ukuba ibali lakhe liza kuba nabalinganiswa abanjani. 
Kuyaqondakala ke nalapha kweli ibali ledrama, uthe umbhali akufikela kwisigqibo sokuba uza kubhala ngantoni, waze wakhetha indlela afuna 
ukubabumba ngayo abalinganiswa bebali lakhe. 
Kweli ke icandelo kuza kutsawla iliso kwindlela lo mbhali athe wazoba abalinganiswa abangamabhinqa njengamaxhoba okuthanda izinto zalo mhlaba. 
Apha umbhali usikrobisa kwelinye icala lamabhinqa, apho amabhinqa axhaphaza abantu besilisa ukuba bafumane konke abakufunayo, ze nabo ngokunjalo baxhatshazwe kwangaba bantu besini sobuduna, phantsi kwezabo iimeko ezixolisa iintliziyo zabo. 
Oku kungqinwa zizenzeko ezilapha kweli bali. 
Siyambona umlinganiswa uZanele eqhatha uLoni emxelela indlela amthanda ngayo, ze alandelise ngokumphendla-phendla efuna ukubona ukuba yintoni na uLoni anokuthi amenzele yona. 
Khawuve uZanele esithi: Zanele: Papa, ukuba ndinokuthi kuwe ndizele neqhiya enamasondo asixhenxe ungathini. 
Mawonga: Nokuba seyiphantsi kwamanzi, kweentaba, nakwinkotyo yehlathi, ndoyiyiphuthaphutha sana ndize nayo. 
Zanele: O, kekhona! Ndikuthanda sendilele. Andazi ukuba bendiya kuthini na ngaphandle kwakho. 
O, papa wa-a-am. (Watsho emanga. Babukana okwamaqalabonana) 
Mawonga: Yintoni sana lwam? Ndikwenzele ntoni? 
Zanele: Igumbi lam lize papa lindenza iintloni ndakufikelwa nguwe. 
Akungendincedi ngedipozithi nje qha kuphela? Andinakuhlazeka ukho kule mpi yepati. 
Mawonga: Ufuna nje idipozithi? 
Zanele: Oku kwayo yodwa papa, ndokubuyisela ungaphelanga unyaka. 
Mawonga: Ndiya kukunika ngomso oku sthandwa, ibiyintoni idipozithi kwabathandana njena ngathi? 
Zanele: Khon’ ungatshongo mnqweno wam wobomi, olungenamisebenzi lufana nexin ehlokomayo. 
O, kofana yam, sthandwa sam sokugqibela! Ndingakwenzela ntoni? 
Mawonga: Hlala nam ngonaphakade (Bawolane)  
La mazwi uZanele uwathetha enganazinjongo zokuthandana naye uLoni, nto nje ufuna le nto ayifunayo. 
Apha lo mlinganiswa ulibhinqa uzixelele ukuba uza kuthetha nantoni na eza kumfumanisa le nto ayifunayo. 
Amabhinqa ke anayo mpela indlela yokucofa amaqhosha endoda, de enze le nto ayifunayo, le nto ke yile siyibonayo apha kuZanele, eyenza kuLoni, ngoba uthe uLoni akuphelelwa yimali nangamacebo, wamlahlela ecaleni. 
Mawonga: Nkqonkqo! Nkqo!(Cwaka) Zanele! Zanele vula! Nkqonkqo! Nkqo! (Cwaka) Tywalakahla-wahla wophula ifestile. 
Zanele: Yintoni ebusuku apha? 
Mawonga: Vula uza-ku-ndiva. Vula, vu-u-ula 
Zanele: Kudala ndakuxelela ukuba funa ndawo yimbi. 
Mawonga: What? Uqhele ukubancuva, ubancuve ubalahle. 
Vula (abethe ucango ngamandla.) 
Funeka: Uyokomela apho. 
Zanele: Mawonga, uhlawula irente apha? Siza kungalali ngenxa yakho? Uyaqala ukwaliwa? 
Mawonga: Ungena phi wena? Zanele, Vula, (Cwaka) Akulalwa tu. 
Imali y-a-m. Enga-aka? Vu-u-la Zanele. 
(Ukhwaze watsha ilizwi wadumba inqindi kukubetha ucango wancama wagoduka emdaka enjalo.) buyabonakala ububi obenziwe nguZanele kuLoni, umxhwithe woma nko waze wamlahlela ngaphandle xa egqibile ngaye. 
Akukhathaliseki noba utshatile kwaye izenzo zakhe zingawophula umtshato kaLoni kunye nomfazi wakhe, kwaye uza kubangela ingxwaba-ngxwaba kusapho lwakhe. 
Into nje ayithandayo yinto yokuba le ebeyifuna uyifumene, kwaye yena wonelisekile. 
Ekuphononongeni ezi ncwadi zedrama zithe zasetyenziswa kwesi sahluko, kubonise uthungelwano kwindlela ababhali besini sobuduna abathi bazibhale ngayo izibhalo zabo zamabali edrama. 
Olu thungelwano luye lwaphendula owona mbuzo umphandi ebenawo, mbuzo lowo uthe wakhokelelo kolu phando kwasekuqaleni. 
Kaloku umphandi wathi waqaphela into yokuba ababhali besini sobuduna banendlela yabo efanayo yokuzoba abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo kwizibhalo zabo zedrama. 
Oku kwabangela ukuba umpandi ayijongisise le ndaba, aqonde ukuba ingaba oku yinyani. 
Eli candelo lelona likungqinileyo ke oko. Sithe sakujonga ezi ncwadi zintathu zedrama ezibhalwe ngababhali abasini sobuduna kwabanokala ukuba kungathiwa ngumntu omnye lo ubhale le midlalo, ngenxa yokuyelelana kwendlela ababhala ngayo nababumba ngayo abalinganiswa babo ababhinqileyo. 
Umzekelo ophilayo ngabalinginiswa uMasukude kaMtingane kunye noNojenti kaMbovane. Aba balinganiswa ungathi babunjwe ngumbhali omnye. 
Bobabini bakhohlakele, banomona kwaye bangcolile, kubo ubomi bomntu abubaleli ntweni, babuthatha ubomi bomntu omsulwa nje ngephanyazo. 
Kweli bali ledrama u-‘Inene nasi isibhozo’ bekuqwalaselwa ikakhulu indlela umbhali athe wabazoba ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo abaphambili. 
Oku ke sikubonile pha kulaa mlinganiswa uMasukude. 
Umbhali umzobile uMasukude njengomlinganiswa okrwada, onomona, okhahlakeleyo kunye nonobugqwirha. 
Ewe umphandi uyavuma into yokuba amabali edrama yimidlalo elungiselelwa ukudlalwa eqongeni, kodwa kaloku le midlalo iyafundwa nasezikolweni naluluNtu jikelele. 
Loo nto ke ngoku iye izale ixhala kulo wenza olu phando, ngoba ukuba wonke umbhali wesini sobuduna ukholise ukuwazoba olu hlobo amabhinqa 
kwizibhalo zabo, ingxaki ikho kwaye inkulu. 
Cinga umntwana ofunda lo mdlalo esikolweni, athi xa egoduka afike ajongisise izenzo zikamama wakhe, abone into angayithandiyo kwizinto 
ezenziwa ngumzali wakhe, agqibe kwelokuba umama wakhe uneempawo zikaMasukude, noba zincinci kanganani na, 
ngoba aba babhali bakholise ukuzoba amabhinqa ngendlela engakholisiyo, ngendlela ebahlisela isidima. 
Esi sidima samabhinqa sesi kudala silwela ngabhinqa iminyaka emininzi, kodwa iincwadi ezinje zigalela amanzi kumsebenzi abawenzayo, ngoba bacula iculo elohlukileyo kweli liculwa ngala mabhinqa. 
Kuqwalaseka okufanayo naxa kujongwe u-‘Ndiyekeni’ kaJongilanga. Indlela lombhali abazobe ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo uFuneka kunye noZanele, uyawuchitha umsebenzi owenziwa ngamabhinqa alwela ukulingana phakathi kwabantu bezini ezahlukileyo. 
Bukho ubunyani kwindlela abaziphatha ngayo, ngoba kunanamhla akho amabhinqa athanda ukwenzelwa izinto ngamadoda, zinto ezo abangazisebenzelanga. 
Kodwa loo nto ayithi ababhali bethu mabathathe loo ntlekela baze badyobhe amabhinqa njengabantu abangenantlonipho ngobomi babo kwaye abangenazintloni, nto abanokuyithatha le ngxaki babhale ngayo, kodwa bangasishiyi isisombulo, ukuze lowo usakhulayo athi xa efunda le midlalo, 
ayazi ukuba angaze afane noZanele noFuneka abaxhwitha oobhuti babantu baze babalahlele ngaphandle xa begqibile ngabo, ngoba bubukhohlakali obo. 
Ukanti kukwanjalo kulaa drama ithi ‘Ndixoleleni.’ 
Sibona indlela umlinganiswa olibhinqa uNojenti azotywe ngayo wafana nkcakasa noMasukude, njengoku besekukhankanyiwe ngentla. 
Le nto ithetha ukuba uninzi lwababhali abasini sobuduna bababona ngokufanayo amabhinqa, ngoba kungathiwa kutheni ke bebazoba phantsi kweziphene ezifanayo. 
Aba babhali abaphelelanga kuphela ekuzobeni aba balinganiswa babhinqileyo njengabantu abapholileyo abangabalulekanga ekuhlaleki, ngokuthi babazobe nje ngezingcoli, kodwa benze umsebenzi omhle ukusebenzisa abalinganiswa besini sobuduna ukucinezela aba balinganiswa. 
Xa sijonge phaya ku- ‘Inene nasi Isibhozo’ siyabona indlela amadoda asemzini kaMasukudu athi amvalele ngaphandle kwizinto ezibandakanya izinto zomzi wakhe ngenxa yokuba elibhinqa. 
Ayiphikiswa indaba yokuba, amabhinqa awakunaxoxa izinto zasebuhlanti, ngoba isiko lwakwaXhosa alikuvumi oko, kodwa loo nto ayithethi ukuba makavaleleke ngaphandle ngoba ekugqibeleni ngumziwakhe lowa, naye uvumelekile ukuhlomla kwizinto ezibandakanya izinto zomzi wakhe. 
Naxa sibuyela umva kulaa ncoko iphakathi kukaFuneka noNdila pha kulaa ncwadi u-‘Ndiyekeni’, uNdila uthuma uFuneka ukuba ahambe ayokuxhwitha uLoni konke anakho, naye uFuneka akaphozisi maseka, uhlohla isihlobo sakhe uZanele kuLoni ngokukhawuleza ukuze amxhwithe ome nko uLoni. 
Apha umbhali usibonisa ukuba amabhinqa zizibhanxa, ayawayeka amadoda awaxhaphaze awathengise kodwa kube kungekho nto iphucukileyo azokuyizuza kuyo yonke loo nto ngaphandle kokuhlisa isidima sabo phakathi kwabantu basekuhlaleni. 
Esi sahluko asohlukanga kuyaphi kwisahluko esiphambi kwaso, kuba nalapha kujongwa indlela ababhali ababazoba ngayo abalinganiswa babo ababhiqileyo. 
Kwisahluko esi phambili umphandi ebejonga indlela ababhali abasini sobuduna abathi babazobe ngayo abablinganiswa babo ababhinqileyo kwizibhalo zabo zedrama. 
Kanti ke kwesi isahluko umphandi ufuna ukuqwalasela indlela umbhali olibhinqa abazoba ngayo abalinganiswa abangamabhinqa kwincwadi yakhe yedrama. 
Unobangela woku, kukuthelekisa ukuba kukho umehluko kusini na phakathi kwendlela ababhali abasini sohlukileyo ababazoba ngayo abalinganiswa babo ababhinqileyo. 
Kumacandelo aphambili umfundi ubonile into yokuba ababhali abasini sobuduna babazoba ngokufanayo aba balingiswa, ngoko ke apha masijonge le yantlukwano. 
Apha ke kuza kusetyenzwa phantsi kweethiyori ezimbini eziza kuthi zingqanyaniswe nencwadi ebhalwe ngumbhali olibhinqa uHlumela Mothlabane, ethi-‘Iinkunzi ezimbini’, 
ezo thiyori zezi: Ingcingane yokungalingani ngesini kunye naleyo ithi, Ingcingane yesini sobukhomokazi. 
Ikakhulu apha umphandi ufuna ukuphonononga indlela amabhinqa acinezalwa ngayo ngabalinganiswa besini sobuduna, noko bakwenzayo ukuzihlangula koko. 
Ngoko ke kuza kuqwalaselwa ubunzima amabhinqa adibana nabo emakhayeni abo, emitshatweni nasemisebenzin ngenxa yesikhundla esiphezulu esinikwa amadoda. 
Lo mbhali usikhokelela kuyo kanye le nto kuza kuthethwa ngayo apha kwesi sahluko xa kuphononongwa le ncwadi ikhethiweyo. 
Eli bali lingoSibonda uSigqibo Mnangwe onabafazi abathathu, uNokhaya, uNofinishi kwakunye noNolasti, lo mfazi wokugqibela uNolasti waba kanti ufundile, efundile nje uyaphangela emakhitshini, kusapho lwabelungu. 
Emgcwabeni kumzi wasemaZangweni kuphakama umhlobo omkhulu walowo ungcwatywayo, uSabelo Ntungo, uphakamela ukuxelela abantu ukuba le nto amadoda ebhubha kangaka nje kungenxa yabafazi babo. 
Kaloku aba bafazi babo bazibona bephucukile kule mihla, kodwa eyabo impucuko iswele ingqikelolo. 
uSabelo namanye amadoda ale lali yaseMachubeni akhala ngento yokuba abafazi babo bababulala mihla le ngesifo sentliziyo. 
Indaba yesini inenxaxheba enkulu kakhulu eyidlala ezimpilweni zabantu, kodwa ke kuyo yonke lonto, ayisebenzeli wonke umntu ngokulinganayo, umbhali uRidgeway (2001:1) ubhala enjenje malunga nalomba: 
Ukongeza kule ngcingane, uKay (2012:76) uthetha athi ngale ngcingane; 
Nto esixelela ukuba ukungalingani ngesini kukungalingani kwamalungelo abantu abasini esohlukileyo. Le ngcingane ibhekisa kuphatho olungalinganiyo phakathi kwabantu abasini sobukhomokazi kunye nabantu besini sobuduna. 
Le ngcingane ibeka ityala lokungalingani kwamadoda namabhinqa kwi nqubo yoqoqosho yobukapitali. Ngokwe sichazi-magama sakwa (oxford 1985:158) siyicacisa oluhlobo le nkqubo: 
Into ethetha ukuba yinkqubo yoqoqosho apho iimali ezinkulu, amashishini kunye nezambhiwa zilawulwa ziziqu okanye amaqela athile, lube uninzi lunga xhamli kobubutyebi. Umbhali uWalby, (1990:4) unaba enjenje ngale ngcinga: amadoda athi asebenzise umthetho ukuza babacinezele. Ngoko ke indima yabo kukulwa oko, ukuze nabo bakwazi ukuba nomthetho ecaleni kwabo. 
La amabhinqa aphantsi kwale ngcingane yesini sobukhomokazio ngalo alwa umagunya wamadoda . 
Athe aqaphela ukuba amadoda anamagunya aphezulu ngamandla kunalawo amabhinqa, kwaye wona amabhinqa awanamalungela alinganayo nala amadoda, ngoko ke, kukho oko kuzokufuneka ukuba kutshintshe. 
Kaloku lento ibonakala phaya emisebenzi ikakhulu phaya kwizikhundla zika rhulumente apho amadoda athi aphathe yonke into, ufumaniseke omama bona banikwa zonke ezazikhundla zisezantsi. 
Olu udidi lwamabhinqa alwa into enye, ukulingana phakathi kwamadoda kunye namabhinqa kwinto yonke. 
Kodwa eyona nto bayiqwalaselayo kukungalingani kwamadoda namabhinqa xakufikwa kwimfundo nase misebenzini uWalby (1990:6) ubhala enjenje: 
Bafuna ukukwazi ukwenza umsebenzi ofonayo nalowo wenziwa ngamadoda, aze abhatalwe imali elinganayo, bafuna ukukwazi ukuba nendlu egamelini labo, hayi phantsi kwegama lendoda, konke abakufunayo yinto yokuba kubekho ulingano phakathi kwamadoda namabhinqa. 
Abantu abahlala bonke ekuhlaleni, bedityaniswa kumthetho omnye, iinkcubeko ezifanayo nendlela yokuphila enye. 
Le nkcazelo ingentla isixelela ngabantu abahlala kunye kwingingqi enye abenza into ekuthiyi yiSociety ngokwasesi Ngesini. 
Oku kwenzeka xa indoda okanye ibhinqa lifuna ukwabelana ngesondo nomnye umntu ngaphandle kwesivumelwano. 
Lento ivame kakhulu phaya emaphandleni, kodwa ke nalapha ezidolophini ixhaphakile kakhulu. 
Umntu akunyanzeleka ukuba ade abe uyabelana nomnye ngesondo, zininzi ndlela zokuxaphaza umntu ngokwesondo eziquka ukumbambha-bambha kwindawo ezifihlakeleyo eziquka amabele nezinye indawo. 
Inkcubeko ngumba onobunzulu nobuzaza, ngokunxulumene nokwahluka apha naphaya kwezizwe, ingakumbi ezimnyama. 
Loo nto iphembelela ukwahluka ngokunxulumene nemiba ngemiba ephathelele kwezentlalo. 
Uhlanga ngalunye lunenkcubeko yalo, nto ethi izinto abathi bazenze, ziye zohluke kolunye uhlanga, ngokuxhomekeke ekubeni, hlanga luni olo. 
UHofstede uyasixelela apha ngentla into yokuba inkcubeko yinto apha ekuthiwa ifundwe, kweye ifundisw. Umntu akade azalwe nayo. 
Ixhomekeke kwindlela apho umntu athi akhuliswe ngayo, nempembelelo leyo yenawo akhuliselwe kuyo. 
Ukuxhatshazwa komntu, ingakumbi ibhinqa, kuxa umntu athi enze ubodlobongela komnye umntu ngenjongo zokumvisa kabuhlungu. 
Obubudlobongela akunyanzelisi ukuba ibekukumbetha, oku kwenzeka nangamazwi athi awaphose komnye umntu, ngonjongo yokuhlisa isidima sakhe, indlela azibona nendlela aziphatha ngayo phakathi kwabantu. 
Amaxhoba okukuxhatshazwa aye angayazi abakuwenze ukuzikhupha kule meko kuba beziva bengenamandla ngenxa yokusoloko bejongelwe phantsi 
Uyasixelela ukuba esi senzo sibi, kwaye siye simkhathaze ngempela lowo ulixhoba, ngoba oku kuye kuphazamisane nobomi bakhe, indlela azibona ngayo, kunye nendlela athi aziphathe ngayo phakathi kwabantu, ngenxa yokuba lixhoba lengcinezelo. 
Ukuze lowo uphandayo athi afike kwindawo ajolise ukufika kuyo kolu phando kuye kwafuneka kusetyenziswe isikrweqe sohlalutyo lomongo. 
Oku kuthetha ukuba umphandi kuye kwanyanzeleka ukuba afunde izibhalo zabanye ababhali abathe babhala ngalo mba mnye. 
Kuye kwafuneka aziqhelanise neengcamanngo zabanye ababhali phambi kokuba afikele kwisigqibo sokuba uza kuza kweliphi na icala kuphando lwakhe. 
Akwazi ukufikela kwisigqibo sokuba uyangqinelana na kanye uyaphikisana nabanye ababhali. 
Kwaye ukuze akwazi ukuqinisekisa ukuba akaphandanga ngendlela ebekusele kuphandwe ngayo. 
Umphandi ulubona olu phando lubalulekile ngoba luchaphazela udaba oludlwengula umxhelo, daba olu esiphila phantsi kwalo mihla le. 
Olu daba luthetha ngomba wokungalingani kwabantu abasini esahlukileyo nendlela apho elowo efuna ukuzibona esesikhundleni esiphezulu kunomnye. 
Iminyaka emininzi abantu besini sobuduna kudala bezibona besesikhundleni esiphezulu kunabo besini. sobukhomokazi, nto leyo iliwa ngamabhinqa, ngoba nabo bayazibona ukub banazo izakhona zokuba kwisikhundla esilinganayo namadoda, nangaphezulu ukutsho. 
Apha kolu phando kuza kuthi kuboniswe ukuba indlela esathi sadalwa ngayo ayiyo kuphela indlela eza kuthi isigqibele indlela esiphila ngayo. 
Kumabali edrama amane athe axoxwa kolu phando siwabonile amabhinqa ecinezelwa kwaye ephathwa kakubi ngamadoda, ukanti siwabonile amanye amabhinqa nawo axhaphaza amanye amabhinqa. 
Nawe ke mfundi iba namehlo avulekileyo uqwalasele indlela apha abantu abasini esahlukileyo abathi baphathane ngayo. 
Uqaphele ukuba amabhinqa awaziyo aphili phantsi kwengcinezelo, ngoba ngelinye ixesha umntu lo uphila phantsi kwengcinezelo, akayiqondi nalo nto, de yolathwe nomnye umntu, ube wona umonakalo seyenzekile. 
Ukuba wena apha ebomini bakho uyaqonda ukuba uphantsi kocinezelo lo mntu othandana naye, ophangela naye okanye ofunda naye, zama ukuba uphume kolo manyano, nokuba ulibhinqa okanye uyindoda. 
Kaloku namabhinqa anaso isakhona sokucinezela amadoda, ingakumbi emitshatweni. 
Umfazi ayiphathe kakubi indoda yakhe caba indoda ayino kwazi ukwenza nto ngaphandle kokuba icele imvume emfazini, nje ngokuba sibonile pha kwibali lethu u-Iinkunzi ezimbini isenziwa nguSibonda lo nto emfazini wakhe uNolasti. 
Yinto apha le eyimoshayo imitshato, nayo nayiphi na indibano phakathi kwabantu ababini, ngoba kaloku omnye umntu ngoku uzokoyika ukuphila ubomi bakhe, kufuneka aphilele omnye umntu ngenxa yoloyika analo. 
Kweli candelo uphando luza kungena nzulu kwingcingane yesini sobukhomokazi, ingcingane yokungalingani ngokwesini kunye nengcingane ejongene nesidima esiphakamileyo nesinamagunya, esinikwa isini sobudoda. 
Apha kuza kuphononongwa ukuba zintoni ezi ngcingane, zaqala njani, ziqalwa ngubani, ngenjongo ezithini, kwaye ngoku zaziqalwa aba bebezibhexesha ezi ngcamango babeneminqweno ethini. 
Zizo zonke ke iinkalo ekuza kuthi kuxhentswe phezu kwazo xa kuthethwa ngezi ngcingane zidweliswe ngentla. 
Ingcingane yesini sobukhomokazi yingqokelela yentshukumo nengcingane ezijoliselwe ekubeni kubekwe phambili udaba lokungabikho kulingana phakathi kwamabhinqa kunye namadoda. 
Yingcingane apha ejolise ekulweni ingcinezelo kumabhinqa, ecinezelwa ngamadoda. Le ngcingane yesikhomokazi yabekwa bucala ukuze ibhinqa libe namalungelo alinganayo nalowo amadoda, ukuze amabhinqa abonakale ngokulinganayo kumehlo abantu base kuhlaleni ingakumbi kwizinto ezifana nezepolitiki, ukuba ngumnini ndlu kwakunye nezinto ezichaphazela imisebenzi nezemithetho. 
Oku kuyacaciswa nguBillington, kuKramarae noTreichler, (1985:158) xa esithi ngoku bhekiseli koku kubhalwe ngentla: 
Le ngcingane yaqala kumazwe aseNtshona ngomnyaka we-Nkulungwane yeshumi elinesihlanu. Njengokuba iminyaka ihamba nje le ngcingane iye ikhula kwaye imane iqhubeleka phambili. 
Le ngcingane ikhokelelwa ngamabhinqa anenjongo ezohlukileyo ngento afuna ukuyifeza ekubeni athi ayiqala le ndibano yawo yokulwela amalungelo awo obubhinqa. 
Le ngcingane yesikhomokazi ngoyena nobangela weli phulo lale nguqu igqibeleleyo phakathi kwamadoda nabafazi. 
Ukanti le ngcingane iyayibhentsisa inyani yokuba intlalo yonke jikelele iphethwe ngamadoda, lawo athi acinezele amabhinqa ngendlela ezahlukeneyo. 
Bayaphuhla besithi amabhinqa abonwa njengezinto nje, lo ngumkhuba ovamileyo othandwa ngamadoda, ngenxa yoku amabhinqa athe acinezelwa 
ngendlela engaginyisi mathe, kwaye amadoda athe axhamla kakhulu kule ngcinezelo yabafazi. 
Le ngcingane noko sele inempandla kuba kaloku kudala ikhona. 
Yathi ke yaqala kumazwe asentshona aquka iMelika kunye neYurophu, oko kungqinwa ngamazwi kaButler (1990; 
Apha kula mazwi angentla iyaphuhla eyokuba amanye amaphulo ayejongene kunye nodlame ngakwabantu ababhinqileyo kunye nokugcina ucwangco 
kudaba olu malunga nokulingani ngokwesini. 
Amanye kwelinye icala amakhosikazi ambalwa ayengahleki nenye xa kufikwa emadodeni, kuba kaloku babesebenzisa le ngcingane njengesixhobo 
sokuxhasa amaphulo alwa imicimbhi efana nokuxhatshazwa kwamabhinqa ngokwe- sondo, udlame kunye nodlwengulo olwalugquba ngela xesha. 
Into icace gca okwekat’emhlophe ehlungwini ukuba abantu ababhinqileyo kudala bephantsi konyawo lomntu oyindoda, kuba kaloku le ngcingane 
ineminyaka engaphaya kwamashumi amahlanu yasekwayo. 
Kwa ukusekwa kwayo ibonisa ukuba amabhinqa afikelela ekubeni adikiwe, ekwadikiwe nokuba zizigculelo zabantu abangamadoda kuyo yonke imicimbi. 
Ukanti nakwimiba yesondo, ubani uya kuthi afumanise ukuba ijikeleze okanye ithe yangqonga, kwaye yenziwa yafanela iimfuno zomntu oyindoda, 
kodwa ezomntu ongumama iimfuno zesondo azinikwa ngqalelo ncam. 
Le nto ide yabetheleleka kwabanye abantu besisini sesikhomokazi, kuba uzibona ebophelelekile ukuba anelise umntu oyindoda ngokwesondo, kodwa 
abe kwelakhe icala engazinanzanga ezakhe iimfuno zesondo, oko kungqinwa nguWalby (1990:3) xa esithi: 
Yiyo ke loo nto ngamanye amaxesha amanye amabhinqa engazi ngaphambili xa ethe axhatshazwa ngokwesondo, kuba kaloku bacinga ukuba 
sisinyanzelo into yokuba anelise umntu oyindoda ngokwesondo. 
Nakwinkcubeko yesiXhosa kuthi xa kuyalwa umendi kuthiwe kufuneka ahlonele kwaye ayithande indoda yakhe, kodwa soze uwave amazwi anjalo abhekiselele endodeni. 
Kwelinye icala ixhaphake kakhulu into yokubona udlame, izixholo-xholo kunye nodushe zigquba kwimimandla eyahlukileyo, ngokwale 37 
ngcingane, ithi oyena nobangela wodushe, udlame kunye nezi zehlo zokuxhatshazwa kwabantu ngokwesondo, ziindawo esihlala kuzo, oko kukuthi yindlela abantu abakhuliswa ngayo. 
La mazwi athethwa nguHughes (2002:78) anggqina oku kungentla: 
Le nto ibonakala kwaphaya ezikolweni xa umntwana ongumfana ethe wanengxabano nomntwana oyintombazana, uye ufumanise ukuba uza kufuna ukusa isandla kuqala, kuba kaloku umsindo wakhe umkhokhelela kwelo. 
NakwaXhosa ikhona intetho ethi “Umqolo wesidenge wolulwa ngentonga, into ephuhlisa ukuba ukusonjululwa kwengxaki ngodlame nezixholoxholo, yinto ekhuthazwayo kwindawo ezahlukileyo. 
Naxa ubani ejongile, uya kuthi ufumanise into yokuba abona bantu babandakanyeka kwiziganeko zodlame ngabantu abangamadoda. 
Le ngcingane iphinde isixelele ukuba le nto ayipheleli phaya ekuhlaleni, kuba kaloku nezinto zonxibelelwano, 
nezonwabisayo uya kuthi ufumanise ukuba ngoku nazo sele zinalo igalelelo elingummangaliso ekuphembheleni ekubeni abantu babandakanyeke 
kwiziganeko zodlame. 
Kukho imiboniso bhanya-bhanya koomabonakude, miboniso leyo ithi ikhuthaze olu dlame, kuba kaloku uya kuthi uphuma phandle, ubone nabaya abantwana bemane ukukhabana, belinganisa yonke laa nto bayibone koomabonakude uMaccanell (1991:15) ecaphula uBrownmiller ubhala enjenje: 
Kule miboniso bhanya-bhanya xa usilwa, ubendlongo-ndlongo uye ubonwe uligorha, ubone ngamanye amaxesha lomntu ubandakanyeka kwezi zixholo-xholo uyadunyiswa. 
Kwilizwe lonke jikelele imiba kunye nemicimbi ithe yaphathwa ngamadoda, abantu aba bhinqileyo bengabonakali tu. 38 
Umbhali uHearn (1992: 56) ubhala enjenje: Le nto ithetha ukuba ininzi inguqu ekufuneka yenzekile, apho woke ubani uya kuthi axhamle ngokulinganayo nabemi belizwe lonke. 
Le ngcingane akuba ichasene namadoda, koko eyona nto ichasene nayo yimithetho yezopolitiki kunye namaziko asekuhlaleni akhuthaza ukungalingani kwamadoda namabhinqa kwiinkalo zonke. 
Ukanti ke usemninzi umsebenzi ekufuneka wenziwe kuba abantu ababhinqileyo basengamaxhoba okuxhatshazwa kwiindawo ezahlukeneyo, kuquka 
emisebenzini, bayabethwa emizini nezinga lamabhinqa adlwengulwayo alikehli. 
Amabhinqa alwela ukungalingani phakathi kwamadoda namabhinqa. 
Kaloku la mabhinqa ngalawo alwela inkululeko kwinto yonke. 
Nalena ingcinga ayiyo enye yengcinga ezisakhasayo, sele kukudala yasungulwa, umbhali uRuffcon (1999: 23) utyatyadula athi ngalo mba: 
Omnye wabantu abathi baxhamla kule ngcingane ngunkosikazi uWollstonecraft (1759-1799), owathi wabhala isingqinisiso okanye inyaniso malunga 
namalungelo oomama esithi oomama kufuneka befundisiwe njengamadoda ukuze nabo bakhule ngokwempatho, bakwazi ukuzimela. 
Nale ke ingcingane eyona njongo yayo kukuvula loo masango athe avalelwa amabhinqa ekuhlaleni. 
Yona le ngcingane ithi amabhinqa asengamakhoboka kwaye kuyanyanzeleka ukuba kuguqulwe imithetha ekhoyo ukuze nabo bazibone beyinxalenye 
yentlalo, baqukwe kwizigqibo ezimalunga nentlalo. 
Ngoko kwabo inkululeko kwinto yonke yeyona nto ibalulekileyo ukogqitha izinto zonke, kuba xa amabhinqa ekhululekile, amathuba angcono aya kuthi avele. 
Kwelinye icala amabhinqa aziva oku ngathi inkululeko yabo ibalibazisile, kuba kaloku ukuba babeyifumene kwakudala, ilizwe ngelikwelinye 
ibanga elingaphezulu kuneli. 
Umbhali uHeilmann (2004:56) uthi xa ebhala amadoda namabhinqa afana namaphiko entaka amabini, elinye iphiko libhinqa, elinye iphiko yindoda, ngoko ke xa elinye iphiko liqhwalela, intaka ayinako ukubhabhela kwawona majuku-juku aphezu, kodwa ukuba amaphiko ayasebenzisana, intaka ayinako kwa ukunqwandwa sisibhaka-bhaka. 
Into ethetha ukuba ukuba amadoda namabhinqa ayenikwe amathuba alinganayo, ilizwe ngelikwelona banga liphezulu kakhulu ngoku. 
Amakhosikazi ngabantu ekudala bayilwela inkululeko yabo, umzekelo xa siphosa amehlo apha ekhaya, eMzantsi Afrika, kwimibutho yezepolitiki, umbutho i-African National Congress wathi ngomnyaka we-1931 wamkela umbutho i-Bantu Womens Legue njengesebe lawo lamakhosikazi. 
Kwangaphambhili, umbutho i-ANC wawu- ngawamkeli amakhosikazi ukuba abe yinxalenye okanye abe ngamalungu ombutho. 
UMama uCharlotte Mxeke wathi waba ngumongameli wokuqala walo mbutho. Zininzi ke izizathu ezibangela ukuba amabhinqa angaqukwa okanye angayifumani kakuhle inkululeko. 
Okokuqala xa kuyilwa imithetho yelizwe, uya kuthi ufumanise ukuba ambalwa amabhinqa akhoyo, ukuba akhona. 
Nakwilizwe lonke jikelele mnye okanye mabini amabhinqa angoomongameli kuloo mazwe athile. 
Le ke ingcingane ibeka ityala kurhulumente, ukuba abaqukwa bona kwimicimbhi yelizwe, umbhali uHearn (1992: 85) ubhala enjenje: 
Kaloku iphuhlile into yokuba amabhinqa angabonakali okanye athande ukunqongophala kwizikhundla ezithile eburhulumenteni. 
Ukanti esi simbo sokunga- bonakali kwabantu ababhinqileyo kwimicimbhi emalunga nowiso mthetho asiyonto exhaphakileyo kweloMzantsi Afrika 
kuphela, kodwa yingxaki echaphazela ilizwe lonke jikelele. 
Ngoko ngale ndlela amabhinqa anaso isikhalazo sokuba imithetho nendlela ekusingathwa ngayo imicimbi yasekuhlaleni ayifikeleli kwiimfuno zabo. 
Kungoko besithi le mibutho imele bona kufuneka iqinisekise ukuba iza nezisombululo kwiingxaki zabo. 
Ngokwale ngcinga, bathi kufuneka ilungelo lomntu lokuzimela likhuselwe, kwaye urhulumente kufuneka afake isandla ekuphuhliseni abantu ababhinqileyo, kuba kaloku baziva besemva ngenxa yokuba bayawavinjwa amathuba. 
Uyatsho uMurray apha ukuba wonke umntu obhinqileyo unelungelo lokuthi aphile ngaloo ndlela yakhe afuna ukuphila ngayo. 
Kodwa ke sele ibonakala kwezi ntsuku into yokubona umntu obhinqileyo ezizamela isonka sakhe, ephila ubomi ngale ndlela ayifunayo. 
Ngoko le ngcingane igxininisa ekubeni amabhinqa kufuneka akhululeke, ngokomthetho, ngokwezimali afumane imfundo engundoqo ukuze nabo bakwazi ukuba ngabantu abazimeleyo, bangaxhomekeki emivuzweni yabanye abantu. 
Ukanti enye into ebalulekileyo apha siyabona ukuba le ngcingane ithi amakhosikazi makaqukwe kwimicimbhi yowiso-mthetho kunye neminye imicimbi yaseburhulumenteni, njengoko inani labantu ababhinqileyo lithande ukungabikho xa kufikwa kwizikhundla eziphezulu eburhulumenteni. 
Le ngcingane yathi yagqabhuka kwizimvo zomfundi okanye umfundisi wefilosofi ogama linguKarl Max, kuba izimvo ezininzi zale ngcingane zisuka kule nkonde. 
Le nkonde yathi yaqulunqa imithetho emalunga nenkqubo yama kapitali inkqubo yoqoqosho apho imali ezinkulu, amashishini kunye nezmbhiwa zilawulwa ziziqu okanye amaqela athile, lube uninzi lungaxhamli kobu butyebi. 
Wathi ke le mithetho wayibhala kumsebenzi wakhe oxabiseke kakhulu. 
Ngokwale ngcingane abafazi bathe basetyenziswa ngamadoda kwimizi yemveliso, kodwa bona babe bengaxhamli kwaphela. 
Le nto ibibonakala kakhulu phaya emasimini apho amadoda ebesebenzisa abafazi kwiintsimi zabo ukuvelisa imveliso ethile, kodwa ufumane ukuba ababhatalwa, okanye babhatalwa kancinci. 
Ngoko ke le ngcingane ibeka ityala kwinqubo yoqoqosho kunye nendlela zemveliso eziphethwe ngamadoda, abe esebenzisa amabhinqa nzima. 
Ukanti kwakule mihla iyaphawuleka into yokuba ambalwa amabhinqa anamashishini, amashishini amaninzi athe aphathwa ngabanu abangamadoda. 
Kwelinye icala apha kule mizi yemveliso, amabhinqa aye acalucalulwa kuba kaloku kwalapha emivuzweni, uye ufumanise ngelinye ixesha ukuba umntu obhinqileyo, noyindoda benza umsebenzi ofanayo, kodwa xa kufikwa emivuzweni ubone ukuba lo uyindoda ufumana imali okanye umvuzo othe xhaxhe kunalo ulibhinqa. 
Le nto ayenzeki kubi engawenzi kakuhle umsebenzi wakhe, kodwa kuba engumntu obhinqileyo. 
Lilonke le ngcingane ithi imbangi yokuba amabhinqa abhatalwe kancinci, anikwe imisebenzi ethile embalwa ziziphumo zenkqubo yamakapitali. 
Le ngcingane iphuhla isithi, abafazi bajongelwe phantsi, ngaphezulu koko abasebenzi basebenzisa amabhinqa nzima, kodwa ekugqibeleni yonke le nto abaqeshi babe beyenzela ukuba baxhamle kakhulu. 
Ukanti kwelinye icala le ngcingane iyatsho ukuba inkqubo yama- Kapitali, ithi yenze amayelenqe okukhupha abantu abanezakhono emisebenzini, ukuze bazokukwazi ukusebenzisa abo bangenazakhona, injongo yabo ikukwenyusa ingeniso yabo.
Amabhinqa kudala avinjwa amathuba emfundo, ngoko ke nabo baya bandakanyeka kakhulu kwesi senzo sokusetyenziswa kwabantu abangenazakhono zifanelekiyo. 
Kule mihla sele kungcono kuba abantu banamalungelo, kodwa ke abantu abathatha inxaxheba kwinkqubo yamaKapitali banala ngcinga yokuba abantu abangafundanga abawazi amalungelo abo, yiyo ke loo nto abaninzi kubo baye babone umhlaba owehlayo, baxhaphaze, besebenzisa nzima abantu ababhinqileyo. 
Ngamanye ama- xesha abantu abasebenzela amaKapitali ngabantu abasuka kumakhaya angathathi ntweni. 
Abantu abathwaxwe kakhulu yindlala, ngoko abaqeshi bayayayazi ukuba umntu obhinqileyo akasoze ayeke abantwana balale bengatyanga, ngoko baya kwamkelwa nokuba yintoni eza nomqeshi etafileni. 
Kwelinye icala abantu ababhinqileyo basebenza kule mizi mveliso ixesha elide, kodwa ufumanise ukuba akanyuselwa umvuzo tu. 
Ixabiso lemali liyehla minyaka le, yonke into ethengiswayo iyenyuka. 
Loo nto ithetha ukuba baye besokola endaweni yokuba impilo zabo ziphuhle. 
Le ngcingane kwelinye icala ilwa ukuxhatshazwa kwabantu ababhinqileyo ngokwe- sondo. 
Phaya kudala ibike yavama kakhulu into yokuba isiphathamandla okanye iziphathamandla ezithile, zifune ukwabelana ngesondo nomntu obhinqileyo, ukuze abe uyaqashwa kuloo ndwawo. 
Ngamanye amaxesha abaphathi okanye abantu abakwizi- khundla eziphezulu bebesithi baxhaphaze abantu ababhinqileyo ngokwesondo. 
Abantu ababhinqileyo babengayi ngaphambili, okanye bebengayi kumagosa ezoluleka ukuya kubika le ngxaki, kuba kaloku babeyazi ukuba bangaphalelwa ngumsebenzi. 
Ukuphelelwa ngumsbenzi kukuphelelwa sisonka. 
Le ngxaki isenzeka kwezinye iindawo nakule mihla. 
Ukuxhatshazwa ngokwesondo kuziintlobo ezininzi kakhulu, ngamanye amaxesha umntu obhinqileyo uyaxhatshazwa ngokwesondo, 
Kodwa yena abe engayazi ukuba izenzo ezithile ziphantsi koluhlu lokuxhatshazwa ngokwesondo uMacKinnon, (1979:67) ubhala ngokuxhatshazwa ngesondo enjenje: 
Kukho abantu abangenalwazi lokuba kwa into yokubamba okanye ukucofa kuphantsi kokuhlukunyezwa ngokwesondo. 
Abanye abaqeshi banala ngcinga yokuba kuba umntu ekuqeshile, uzakuphatha ungowakhe. 
Ngoko ke le ingcingane ijonge kakhulu impatho embi yabantu ababhinqileyo kwiindawo abasebenza kuzo. 
Ukungalingani ngenxa kokungabi sisini esinye kubangela iyantlukwano eninzi phakathi kwabantu. 
Kukho isini esibonwa sibalulekile kunesinye. Eso sini seso sobuduna. 
Amadoda awafaniswa namabhinqa. Amadoda wona abonwa esemgangathweni ophezulu kunamabhinqa. 
Loo nto ke ibangela ingxwaba-ngxwaba ngoba ayingeni kamnandi kubantu abasisini sobukhomokazi. 
Kodwa ngenxa yodidi lolu phando siza kukhe siphonononge ukungalingani ngokwesini kubantu abathandanayo. 
Ukungalingani ngokwesini kubantu abathandanayo okanye abatshatileyo kuya kuphucuka njengokuba iminyaka iya ihamba. 
Kodwa kuninzi lwabantu abathe bamanyana ngeqhina lomtshato, ulawulo emtshatweni wabo luwela kwicala lamadoda. 
Amadoda namabhinqa indlela abaziphatha ngayo ijongwa ngokubhekisele kwisini sabo. 
Umntu obhinqileyo kunendlela ekulindeleke ukuba aziphathe ngayo, ngenxa yesini sakhe sobubhinqa, nangokunjalo kumadoda. 
Kodwa kuyenzeka ukuba zininzi izinto abagxekwa ngazo amabhinqa, kwaye izinto ekungalindelakanga ukuba bazenze zininzi zihla ngomgca, kodwa xa kubhekisele kumadoda, zimbalwa kakhulu izinto abakhuzwa ngazo. 
Indlela esikhuliswa ngayo iye ibangele ukuba siyibone le yantlukwano phakathi kwabantu abasini esahlukileyo njengento eyamnkelekileyo. 
Kusakhulwa nje, umntwana oyintombazana unxityiswa iimpahla ezohlukileyo kulowo uyinkwenkwe, udlaliswa ngezinto ezohlukileyo kwezo kudlaliswa ngazo amakhwenkwe, nemisebenzi yaphakathi kwekhaya abathi bayenziswe abantwana besini esohlukileyo ayifani. 
Le yantlukwano yinto apha esiyaziswa siseziintsana, de sikhule nayo, ide ibe yinto eqhelekileyo. 
Yiyo loo nto kunzima ukuyiphelisa indlela amabhinqa aphathwa ngayo ngokubhekisele kwindlela amadoda aphathwa nahlonitshwa ngayo. 
Emitshatweni, abafazi balindeleke ukuba babeke izifundo zabo nempangelo ecaleni, nayo yonke enye into ukuze babhekise lonke ixesha labo ekukhuliseni abantwana lomzuzu abayeni babo bephangela . 
Kodwa bakho abafazi abathi bazimisele ukuzenza zonke. Bazimisele kwinto yokuba bafunde, baphangele bekhulisa abantwana babo ngokuba abafuni kuxhomekeka kwaphela emadodeni abo. 
Kuyafumaniseka ukuba, nokuba bakho abafazi abaphangelayo, babeke ukutya etafileni, bangenise imali endlini rhoqo ngenyanga, loo nto ayithethi ukuba imisebenzi yabo yendlu iza kubhekiselwa endodeni, nokuba yona ihlala endlwini ayiphangeli. 
Le nto ibonakala naphaya enkolweni, phaya ezibhalweni ezingcwele incwadi kaPetrosi (1 Peter 3:1-7) ityhila la mazwi: 
“ Ngokunjalo, nina bafazi, wathobeleni awenu amadoda, ukuze kuthi, nokuba kukho kuwo angalivayo ilizwi, athi ngehambo yabafazi, lingekho ilizwi, azuzeke”. 
Abantu abaninzi kwindawo ezahlukeneyo ehlabathini bathe bawaqonda ngendlela eyahlukileyo lamazwi, baphinda bawaxhaphaza kuba lonto ithe yadala ukungalingani phakathi kwamadoda nabafazi. 
Kwelinye icwecwe lakhe u (Florence) utyatyadula enjenje: 
Kubonaka kwalapha kulamazwi angasesentla okokuba abantu bathe bathatha imfundiso zebhayibhile bazisebenzisa njengesixhobo sokucinezela amabhinqa. 
Nangona ucinezelo lwabafazi ngamadoda abo luye lunqumama nje, alukanyamalali kwaphela. 
Ukungalingani kona kusekhona. Olu phatho nokungalingani lubalasele kakhulu ezilalini apho umfazi engavumelekanga kwaphela ukuba aphangele, kwaye into yokuba nomfazi ofundileyo ayinto apha ixatyisiswe kakhulu. 
Umfazi ofundileyo ubonwa njengomfazi oyingxaki ngokuba uza kufuna kuviwe ngaye ngenxa yale mfundo yakhe, kanti kaloku izigqibo zekhaya kulindeleke ukuba zenziwe yindoda. 
Kaloku lento iqalwa kwaphaya ebuncincini, kuba kaloku abantwana bakhuliswa ngendlela apho kufuneka amabhinqa kufuneka esoloko ethobela amadoda, uKambarami (2006) ubhala enjenje: 
Yiyo le nto amadoda ezibona ebalulekile nje kunamabhinqa, ngokuba wona azibona enomsebenzi obaluleke ukogqitha lowo womfazi. 
Yiyo loo nto kusithiwa amadoda ziintloko zekhaya, ngenxa yale mpatho anawo kubafazi nawo onke amanye amabhinqa. 
Amadoda ayawuthanda lo mgangatho abekwa kuwo ungaphaya kunalowo wamabhinqa. 
Uphando lusixelela ukuba amadoda awayithandi into yokuba aqhube iimoto ezinye nezo ziqhutywa ngamabhinqa, awathandi ukuba amabhinqa akwazi ukuzithengela izindlu ngokwabo, okanye laa ngcamango yekhaya elinentloko elibhinqa, kube kungekho ndoda.  
Amadoda awayiginyi ncam indaba yokuba nomsebenzi ofanayo nebhiqa, ingakumbi ukuba nomphathi obhinqileyo, ngoba behlelinje bafuna ibe ngabo abakwizikhundla eziphezulu. 
Kodwa izinto zatshintsha,kulo mnyaka wama-2013 ibhinqa liyakwazi ukwenza nantoni elizimisle ukuyenza, nayo nantoni na enokuthi yenziwe ngamadoda. 
Angazithengela indlu nokuba Ibiza eliphi na ixabiso. 
Olona tshintsho lukhulu lolu lokuba amabhinqa akwazi ukuzala kunganyanzelekanga ukuba abe kanti atshitile okanye ayathandana. 
Zikho iindlela zokukhulelwa kunganyanzelekanga ukuba kudibane umfazi nendoda, ngenxa yethekunoloji esinayo namhlanje. 
Loo nto iyasihlisa isidima samadoda, ngoba mihla le ayabona ukuba abafazi awasabadingi ngolwa hlobo ayebadinga ngalo. 
Amabhinqa ayakwazi ukuzimela azikhulisele abantwana abo, azimele nemizi yawo ngaphandle koncedo lwendoda, olu utshintsho luye lwabalasela ukususela ngomnyaka we-1970 ngokuya le ngcingane yayisakhula. 
Kwantlandlolo phaya embalini amadoda athe angozwi-lakhe kuyo yonke into. Le nto ithetha ukuthi zonke izigqibo, nokuba zimayelana nantoni na, bezisoloko zithathwa ngamadoda. 
Abantu ababhinqileyo babengenayo inxaxheba abayithathayo ekuthatheni izigqibo. 
Kaloku phaya kudala, phofu ke nakule mihla isenzeka loo nto. 
Umntu obhinqileyo ebengenayo imvume yokuba aphendule okanye aphikise izigqibo ezithathwe ngumntu oyindoda. Isicacisi magama sakwa-Oxford) siyicacisa olu hlobo le ngcingane: 
Le ngcaciso ingentla iyayiphuhlisa eyokuba yinkqubo apho athi amadoda aphathe izikhundla eziphambhili nezibalulekileyo. 
Inani labo kwizikhundla zeenkokheli kweze- politiki lonyuke kakhulu ukogqitha amabhinqa, ikwangabo abantu abaphatha imicimbi emalunga nezesimilo kunye nokuziphatha. 
Xa kufikwa kwimicimbi yosapho ikwangabo oozwilakhe, kaloku kule nkqubo amadoda anamagunya angaphezulu kunamabhinqa kunye nabantwana.
