Le nkqubo yinkqubo ethi ibavalele ngaphandle abantu aba- bhinqileyo kuba le nto ithetha ukuba amathuba abo okuba babe negalelo kwinkqubela yelizwe nasekuphuculeni intlalontle yoluNtu, mancinci kakhulu. 
Kwelinye icala umhlaba nempucuko yoluNtu zombini ezi zinto ngezikwibakala eliphezulu ngoku ukuba amabhinqa namadoa ayenikwe amathuba alinganayo kuba loo nto ithetha ukuba ngekukudala kusetyenziswana, izandla ezibini zenza umsebenzi oncomekayo ngesantya esilatyuzayo kakhulu kunesinye. 
Akukho mntu unokutsho gca ukuba le nkqubo isukaphi kanye kanye, kuba kaloku kwilizwe lonke jikele le nkqubo iyafumaneka, ungaya kwilizwekazi iYurophu uza kuyifumana, uye kwilizwekazi iMelika, naphaya ikwakhona, uphinde uphumele nakwilizwekazi i-Afrika, nalapha uza kufika ikhona igquba. 
Yinkqubo ekudala ikhona, uLerner (2004: 3), ubhala enjenje malunga nembali yale nkqubo: 
Apha ngentla iyaphuhla eyokuba le nkqubo ayiyonto idaliweyo, koko yinkqubo enzulu equka izinto ezininzi kakhulu ezenziwe ngumntu. 
Izinto ezibe negalelo ukuyila le nkqubo ziquka ubunjani bendawo, indalo, amasiko nenkcubeko kuye nezinye izinto ezifumanekayoyoluntu.
Umbhali apha ude ayikwekwe le nkqubo esithi sisifo esiyingozi kakhulu kuluNtu lonke. 
Kaloku isifo yinto engamhlalisi kakuhle umntu ngamanye amaxesha siza nokufa kunye nonxunguphalo eluntwini. 
Xa esithi sisifo ubonisa indlela enobungozi ngayo le nkqubo eluntwini, kuba uyatsho umbhali uthi esi sifo sihlukumeza umzimba wendoda kwelinye icala sibe silimaza nomoya welizwe. 
Umbhali xa esithi sihlukumeza umoya wesizwe uzama ukusibonisa ukuba abantu abonwabanga ncakasana yile nkqubo kuba inegalelo futhi itsalela kwicala elinye, icala lamadoda. 
Uyaphuhla umbhali esithi amadoda amaninzi akacingi tu ngale nkqubo futhi akayinanzi, abayazi isukaphi kwaye kutheni isagcinakele nje. 
Loo nto ithetha ukuba le nkqubo yinkqubo esenamandla kwaye yindebe ekudliwa ngayo kwizizwe eziliqela. 
Le nto ikwaphuhlisa ukuba abantu abangamadoda abayiboni iyingxaki le nto yokuba abantu ababhinqileyo besoloko bephantsi kwenyawo zabo. 
Yiyo ke le nto abantu ababhinqileyo bezama ngandlela zonke ukuzama ukuphelisa le nkqubo yokulawulwa ngamadoda, kuba kaloku bayabona ukuba ibavalela amathuba. 
Zibe liqela izinto ezikhokhelele ekubeni abantu ababhinqileyo bacinizeleke ngendlela ezahlukeneyo. 
Xa sinokubalula, ziquka izinto ezifana namasiko, inkcubeko, imfundo kunye nezinye izizathu. 
Xa kuqwalwasela amasiko, izithethe, inkcubeko kunye netlalo yoluNtu apha kwilizwekazi iAfrika, kuthe kwaqapheleka ukuba amabhinqa athe ane- galelo kakhulu ekuphuhliseni intlalo, kuba ngabo abantu ababesithi basebenze ubusuku nemini befundisa abantwana ngenkcubeko kunye neendlela zokuphila, oku kungqinwa nguTaiwo (2010: 230) xa esithi: 
Kula mazwi alapha ngentla kucace gca okwekat’emhlophe ehlungwini ukuba abantu ababhinqileyo bayidlalile kakhulu indima ekulondolozeni inkcubeko kunye nendlela yokuphila kwilizwekazi iAfrika. 
UTaiwo (2010) uthi bebefundisa abantwana indlela yokuthetha, befundiswa ilwimi zesiNtu, amasiko kunye nemixhentso. 
Mandulo phaya ibiyindima kamakhulu ukubalisa iintsomi ebalisela abazukulwana. 
Esi senzo besisenzeka emva kokuba imisebenzi yonke yekhaya igqityiwe. 
Injongo ibikukubafundisa okulungileyo nokungalunganga ngokubalisa ezi ntsomi. 
Nangona ibingathiwa paha imfundiso yentsomi leyo, abantwana bebekwazi ukuyifund’ivaliwe kuba kaloku bebewabona amaqhinga kaDyakalashe emfaka ezingozini ngamaxesha amaninzi. 
Kuyababonakala ukuba isegazini kwaye idaliwe into yokuba oomama bakwazi ukuqoqosha besiza nocwangco kusapho kunye nasekuhlaleni. 
Kwaphaya entlandlolo intsebenziswano phakathi kwamadoda namabhinqa ithe yabonakala, kuba umama ebedlala eyakhe indima ekufundiseni abantwana kunye notata adlale eyakhe indima ekufundiseni abantwana ngeyakhe indlela. 
Ukanti ke bambi ababhali bayayidiza eyokuba ukufika kwenkqubo yamaKomanisi kulapho yathi yaqatsela inkqubo yokungalingani phakathi kwamadoda namabhinqa, la mazwi angqinwa nguClair (1994:19): 
Le nkqubo yamaKomanisi yathi yadala utshintsho oluninzi kwilizwekazi iAfrika, inyanzela abemi balo ukuba benze inguqu malunga nendlela abaphila ubomi ngayo. 
Umzekelo abantu belizwekazi i-Afrika babephila ngokuthi bazilimele imifino neziqhamo, kwelinye icala umntu ebefuya imfuyo. 
Kude kubekho intetho ekhoyo esiXhoseni ethi ubuhle bendoda zinkomo. 
Nto leyo ithetha ukuba, ngelaa xesha lakudala ukuba ubu ngumntu onemfuyo, ubungumntu ome kakhulu epokothweni. 
Kodwa le nkqubo yaseNtshona yayiguqula yonke le nto, kwanyanzeleka abantu basebenze ngoku, Abantu bafudukela ezidolophini, ngecebo lokubeka isonka etafileni. 
Kuye kwavela apha ke oku kucinizelwa kwabantu ababhinqileyo. 
Kaloku usapho yinto ebaluleke kakhulu emntwini, ngoko ke yonke into umntu uyifunda ekhaya. 
Abantwana bakhuliswa beyazi kwaye ibethelelwa kwingqondwana zabo into yokuba akulinganwa ngokwesini nokokuba kwenzeka ntonina. 
Le nto ibonakala kakhulu phaya emaphandleni, ezilalini ukutsho. Umzekelo umntana uthi eselula afundiswe ukuba kufuneka lungaze lusokole usapho lwakhe ekhona, loo nto ithetha ukuba kufuneka ebeke isonka etafileni xa lifikile ilixa. 
Kwelinye icala abantwana abangama ntombazana bayaqeqeshwa ibethelelwa ezingqondweni zabo eyokuba kufuneka bathobeke kwaye babamamele abantu abangamadoda, bayithathele kubo yonke imicimbi efuna ukwenziwa ekhayeni u(Kambarami 2006): 
Amasiko nenkolo zithe ekuhambheni kwexesha zangumntya nethunga kuba kaloku akhona amasiko athe athatha amanyaniswa kunye nemfundiso zenkolo. 
Amasiko nezithethe nje zizodwa bezinemithetho emininzi ethi icinezele abantu ababhinqileyo. La mazwi angqinwa ngu (Marimbha, 2006): 
Ngokwamasiko amaninzi ikakhulu kwi lizwekazi I-Afrika, amasiko ayahlonitshwa kakhulu. 
Kodwa uninzi lwezimfundiso aziwuhloniphi umngangatho wamabhinqa. Umzekelo kwingingqi eziliqela yamkeleki into youba umntu oyinqodwa abe nenani elininzi lwe zinqanda mathe, yaye lomntu uye ahlonitshwe nguye wonke umntu, kwaye uybonwa njengomntu owenza into entle, uye anokwe iwonga. 
Kodwa lento za isenziwa ngumntu obhinqileyo, ithathwa njengehlazo nenyala. Wonke umntu ohlala kulondawo uye ambone umntu obhinqileyo onezinqanda mathe eziliqela njengomntu omdaka, ongazithandiyo. 
Lomntu uye anikwe amagama angaginyeki ncam. (UKambarami, 2006) ubhala enjenje: 
Enye into ebenegalelo elikhulu kakhulu ekukhuthazeni le nkqubo yokungalingani kwamabhinqa kunye namadoda, yinkolo. 
Kaloku inkolo sisixhobo esisetyenziswayo kwilizwe jikelele ukugcina ucwangco nokuqinisekisa ukuba wonke umntu uphila ngendlela efanelekileyo. 
Kaloku ziliqela iinkolo ezifumanekayo elizweni jikelele. 
UDarvishpour (2003: 2) ude adize ukuba inkolo yamaSilamsi ithande ukuba nochatha apha ekucinezeleni abantu ababhinqileyo, ukuveza oko ngokuthi 
Umbhali uthi kumazwe aseNtshona ukungalingani kwamadoda namabhinqa yinto ejongwa ngokwee mpawu zokuzalwa, inkangeleko ukutsho. Uthi ngokwenkolo yama Silamsi, ilelinye ibali indaba yokungalingani. 
AmaMuslim akholelwa ekubeni umntu obhinqileyo unamandla angummangaliso, kwaye ngabantu abayingozi kakhulu eluNtwini. 
Inkqubo ezimayelana nesini ezifana nesithembu, ukucalu-calulwa ngokwesini, zezinye zezinto ezisetyenziswayo ukuqinisekisa ukuba la mandla omntu obhinqileyo akabi yingozi eluNtwini. 
Zonke ezi nkcukacha zityhilwe ngumbhali apha ziyafumaneka kwincwadi engcwele esetyenziswa ngamaMuslim, ethi ukubizwa yi Quran (4:38). 
Kwelinye icala nayo inkolo yamaKrestu enabalandeli abaliqela jikelele elizweni, inayo imithetho ethi ikhuthaze ukuphathwa kwemicimbhi ngabantu ababhinqileyo. 
Le nto iqapheleka phaya xa kujongwa kwizikhundla zobunkokheli, uninzi lwabantu abaphaya kwezaa zikhundla ziphezulu, ngabantu abangamadoda. 
Zonke izigqibo ezibalulekileyo zithathwa ngamadoda. 
Inkolo yamaKrestu iyayibethelela iyigxininisa into yokuba abantu ababhinqileyo kufuneka bephantsi kwamagunya nolawulo labantu abangamadoda. 
Okokuqala umntu obhinqileyo uba phantsi kolawulo lukayise, emveni koko abe phantsi kolawulo lomnyeni wakhe. 
Ukanti kwabaseKorinte (11: 3) kufumaneka la mazwi: Kodwa ke ndithanda ukuba nazi, ukuba intloko yomntu wonke oyindoda nguKristu, intloko ke yomfazi yindoda, intloko ke kaKristu nguThixo. 
Nangona ilizwe nje liqhubela phambhili, kuninzi okufuneka kwenziwe ekuphelisa ukucinezelwa kwabantu ababhinqileyo ngamadoda. 
Lento inako ukwenzeka, abantu ukuba banokufundiswa ngamalungelo abo kungatsho nook kubengcono. 
Enye into enegalelo elikhulu apha ekucinezelweni kwabantu ababhinqileyo kukuswela ulwazi, kuba kaloku abantu basaphila ngezamfundiso zokhokho, mfundiso ezo zithi zibacinezele abantu ababhinqileyo, lonto ayithethi ukuba makulahlwe amasiko, into ekunayo makuzanywe ukunyenyiswa nje eminye imithetho ethi ihlise ngaphwzulu ithobe isidima sabantu ababhinqileyo. 
Kwelinye icala kubalulekile ukuba abantu bangasebenzisi inkolo nje ngesixhobo sokucinezela abantu ababhinqileyo, kuba kaloku ngokomthetheo inkolo bekufaneleke ukuba ibengunobongela wocwango nomanyanisa abantu. 
Kuba ayikho inkolo ethi makucinezelwe abantu ababhinqileyo. 
Kwelinye icala akhona amaziko kunye namaqumrhu azamayo kangangoko ukukhuthaza ukulingana phakathi kwesini sobuduna nobukhomokazi. 
Umzekelo kwi- nkolo yobuBahai (The Bahai Faith) ingungumthetho into yokuba amadoda kunye nabafazi kuyanyanzeleka ukuba mabalingane, kukho incwadi enamazwi amandi 
Apha kula mazwi angentla siyacaciselwa ukuba uluntu lufana nentaka enemphiko ezimbhini. Elinye uphiko ngamadoda ukanti olunye uphiko ngabantu ababhinqileyo. 
Ngoko ke ukuba olunye uphiko luyaqhwalela, intake ayikwazi ukubhabhela kwawona majuku juku aphezulu. 
Lo nto iphuhlisa into yokuba ilizwe ngoku ngelikowona mgangatho xa kujongwa ku phuhliso ukuba abantu ababhinqileyo banikwa okanye babenikwe amathuba alinganayo kunye nawabantu abangamadoda. 
Lentetha indithathe indikhumbhuze isaci salapha kwaxhosa eithi izandla ziya hlambhana. 
Esisicatshulwa siye siphinde siqhubekeke goluhlobo (Fathea’zam 1963:74): 
Izinto zidalwe zasisini esibini, ilizwe lomntu, ilizwe lwezilwanyana kunye nelizwe lwemifino kunye neziqhamo. 
Ude acaphule athi kwilizwe lwemifino kukho isini sobuduna kunye nesini sobukhomokazi, kodwa nangona kunjano, zona ziphathana kakuhle kwaye zinamalungelo alinganayo. 
Lento iphuhlisa into yokuba umntu akazalwanga enalangqondo yokucinezela omnye umntu, into ekunayo yonke lento iye ifundiswe ekuhlaleni 
Nangona imisebenzi yabantu ababinqileyo nemisebenzi yabantu abangamadoda yohlukile, kuanyazeleka ukuba wonke umntu aphathwe ngendlela efanayo kwaye wonke umntu afumane amalungelo alinganayo nawabanye abantu. 
Kuyafuneka abantu bafundiswe ukuba italente zabantu ababhinqileyo azange zaba kumgangatho ophantsi kunezo zabantu abangamadoda, koko ziyalingana. 
Kaloku phaya ntlandlolo amabhinqa akazange anikwe okanye afumane amathuba alinganayo nawa madoda, yiyo ke lonto ngamanye amaxesha ibonakala ngathi abant ababhinqileyo abaphuhlanga ngokwenene xa bethelekiswa namadoda. 
Yiyo ke lento nabo abantu ababhinqileyo kufunekwa besoloko benikwa amathuba, ukuze nabo baphuhle ngokwaneleyo, ngalondlela ilizwe lakuthi liphakamele kowona mgangatho uphakamileyo kakhulu.  
Njengokuba umphandi ebeseqengqelezile kwicandelo elingentla, wachaza ngeethiyori eziza kusetyenziswa xa kuhlalutywa kolu phando, kubalulekile ukuba kugqithelwe kwiincwadi ezithe zakhethwa ngobuchule, eziza kuthi zixhase oku kuthethwa zeza thiyori zichongiweyo. 
Kumacandelo aphambili kucangcathiwe kakhulu kuchazwa ukuba yintoni ingcingane yesini sobukhomakazi nengcingane yokungalingani ngokwesini. 
Ngoko ke apha kuza kuqwalaselwa indlela abalinganiswa abayintloko abangamabhinqa bezi ncwadi zedrama, abathi bazotywe ngayo, ngendlela ephantsi nengabaniki sidima sixhomileyo, kunye nefuthe lezi ngcingane kubalinganiswa abaziintloko kumabali edrama achongiweyo kunye nengcingane yokungalingani ngokwesini kubalinganiswa abayintloko nabanye abalinganiswa abangamadoda kwezi ncwadi zintathu zingezi: 
“Ndixoleleni”, “Inene Nasi Isibhozo” kunye “noNdiyekeni.” 
Apha kweli candelo kuza kuqwalaselwa kakhulu indlela abalinganiswa abangamabhinqa, abaziintloko kula mabali mathathu achongiweyo, abathi bazotywe njengamaxhoba, abantu abangamagqwirha, abantu ekulindeleke ukuba babeka kuqala isiko nezithethe zabo phambi kwayo yonke enye into, kunye nendlela abo bangamaxhoba okuthanda izinto zalapha emhlabeni, ukubala ezimbalwa. 
Oko konke siza kukubona apha kula mabali akhethiweyo, athi angene nzulu ngoku kungentla. 
Esi sibini siyayichasa le ntetho ilapha ngentla, bazama ukusicacisela into yokuba amabhinqa axhatshazwayo aye ayithethelele imeko yabo kwaye bayamkele kuba becinga ukuba akukho bomi bungcono kunobu babuphilayo. 
Kubalulekile ke ukuqonda into yokuba zininzi okweentwala zehagu indlela apho amabhinqa athi enziwe amaxhoba.Enziwa amaxhoba okuthukwa, amaxhoba okubethwa, okucinezelwa njalo njalo.
Jonga oku kusenzeka kuNolasti apha kule ncwadi kaMothlabane. 
Sigqibo: Uligagu kangaka nje kanti ukwakhala kangaka?
Yithi cwaka! 
Akuziva ukuba ungxolela abantu? 
Itsho induku)Siphi isimilo Nolasti? 
Ngubani isilingo? 
Nolasti: (Ekhala njalo) Andithanga usisilingo mna. 
Yhini Sigqibo ungathini ukundibulala xa ungasandifuni? 
(Afumane ithuba lokutaka phandle, abaleke azimele ebumnyameni. 
Abe selefika uGcisa athathe uSigqibo aphuma naye) 
Apha ngentla siyambona uSigqibo, umyeni kaNolasti uhlukumeza umfazi wakhe, embetha ngenduku ngenxa yokuba bephikisana ngento, uSigqibo uziva eneguynya lokumxelela uNolasti into amakayenze nokuba yintoni na, kwaye kuba uNolasti engumfazi wakhe, kunyanzelekile ukuba enjenjalo. 
Nako ke uSigqibo esenza uNolasti ixhoba lakhe lokumthuka naninina ethanda, kwaye ukwamenza nexhoba lakhe lenduku. 
Kubalulekile ukuba ingulowo azazi ukuba ukwimeko apho axhatshazwa khona kusini na. 
Yiyo loo nto elicandelo liza kujonga nzulu kwindlela apho amabhinqa azotywa ngayo ngabaxhaphazi nabaxhatshazwa. 
Kula mabali akhethiweyo edrama kuza kujongwa izinto ezahlukileyo amabhinqa athi azibone ekuzo. 
Amabhinqa azotywa njengabantu abakhohlakeleyo, abathakathayo, athanda imali nezinto zalapha emhlabeni nabangcolileyo. 
Zinto ezo abathi bafakwe ngamadoda kuzo. 
Umzekelo ophilayo woku siwbona pha kule ncwadi kaJongilanga, xa uNdila esubatha uFuneka ukuba azame indlela yokuxhwitha uLoni ngako konke anako, kuba nje efuna ukumfundisa isifundo. 
Bave bethungelana ngalo mba: 
Ndila: …Look, Funie girl, umdlalo uwuqhelile sondenza uMawonga, izabatha zaziwa nguwe. 
Funeka: Ndikuyibambisa intaka leyo, ndiyithini? 
Ndila: Yixhwithe iintsiba, kuba buyaphela ubuntaka bayo zakuvuthuluka iintsiba. 
Funeka: Ndiyakukhe ndizame mtshame, kodwa makhe lulale uthuli. 
Ndila: Mtshana wam! (Bawolane kwakhona.) 
Nako ke oko bekuthethwa ngentla, nanko uNdila ethethathethana noFuneka ukuba enze isenzo sokuxhithwa uLoni. 
Kodwa umbhali xa ebazoba aba balinganiswa babhinqileyo, ubazoba njengabantu abangalunganga, abe engayikhankanyi indaba yokuba baqhutywa 
ngabantu besini sobuduna. 
Ubazoba okungathi ngabantu abazenzelayo konke oku. 
UFuneka ebezihlelele endlwini yakhe phambi kokuba kufike uNdila nalo mboniso, nto ebonisa ukuba nguNdila oziqalele uFuneka ezihlelele. 
Eyona nto kuza kuthi kuqwalaselwe kuyo kwesi sahluko yileyo yokuxhatshazwa kwamabhinqa ngabantu besilisa, nonobangela wokuba ababhali besini sobuduna abathi baphikelele ukubazoba ngale ndlela, noko bazama ukukuphuhlisa kwizibhalo zabo. 
Umphandi uzama ukukrobisa indlela apho abababhali besini sobuduna abathi babazobe ngayo abalinganiswa abangamabhinqa kumabali abo, kuvezwa nale ngcinezelo bathi bayizobe ngokubhekisele kumabhinqa, kaloku khumbula ukuba injongo apha kukuphonononga ukuba, ingaba abababhali besini sobuduna babhala ngokufanayo na nababhali ababhinqileyo, kwaye ingaba kanti oku kuphenjelelwa sisini sabo sobuduna kusini na. 
Abalinganiswa abangamabhinqa kwiincwadi zedrama zababhali besini sobuduna bamela indlela yokuphucula ezoqoqosho ngendlela zokuthi bacwangciselwe imitshato nangokuqhathwa ngendlela ekumele baphile ngayo. 
Ayiphelelanga apho, indima yabo iye iphinde ibe kukuphucula ubomi babo bangamadoda mihla le, kube kungekho kuphucuka kobabo ubomi. 
Umbhali uMiller (1991:467) naye uyanaba kolu daba xa esithi: 
Ngentla apha umbhali usivezela izinto amabhinqa athi ajongane nazo empilweni yawo mihla nezolo. 
Uyatsho umbhali ukuba amabhinqa aphila ubomi obubambekileyo, singade sithi baphila ubomi bentshontsho, apho kunzima nokuzenzela ezabo izigqibo ngezinto ezibandakanya ubomi babo. 
Ude athi lo mbhali, nokuba lowo ubhinqileyo unemibuzo anayo kwinto afuna ukuyiqonda kufuneka alinde de afike ekhaya, ayokubuza indoda yakhe. 
Ude asebenzise igama elithi, “Commanded” into esibonisa ukuba bona baphila ubomi ababuzotyelweyo, ngoba kaloku xa kukho imiyalelo yendlela yokuphila nokwenza izinto, yinto apha ethetha ukuba awukwazi ukwenza nantoni na ofuna ukuyenza, ubomi bakho bucwangcisiwe phambi kwakho, okufuneka ukwenzile kukuyolela imiyalelo leyo. 
Yiyo loo nto umphandi eveza ukuba, amabhinqa aphila ubomi bentshontsho, ingakumbi la endileyo, kubo ukwenda kukuzilahla, bahlelinje benziwa isigculelo, ngoba bathiwa ngxi ngomsebenzi bengenabathetheleli.
Umphandi uye wanecham lokuthi ahlale nebhinqa elisele likhulile noko, elingena nkcakasa kule ngcaciso ilapha ngentla. 
Eli bhinqa lendile, kwaye lihlala nomyeni walo kunye nabantwana abathathu abasafundayo. 
Bobabini eli bhinqa kunye nomyeni walo bayaphangela, ibhinqa lingumongikazi umyeni yena ngumqhubi. 
Esi sibini siphuma xeshanye emsebenzi, baze bafikisane endlini emveni kwentsimbi yesihlanu. 
Xa umyeni efika endlwini, ufika akhulule iimpahla zomsebenzi, ahlale abukele umabonakude. 
Umfazi yena ukhulula impahla yomsebenzi, alungiselele umyeni wakhe isidlo, akugqiba oko, ahlambe iimpahla yabantwana yesikolo ukuba yimini yokuhlamba impahla yesikolo, akugqiba oko, acoce indlu ngoba abantwana babuye bangcolisa, athi ephuma apho, kufuneka alungise isidlo sasebusuku, engekakugqibi oko, kukho iincwadi zase- caweni ezifuna ukujongwa, zilungiswe, ngoba ukwanguye nonobhala wasecaweni. 
Kuyo yonke le nto, eli bhinqa alinamncedisi, akukho mntu azakumohlulela lo msebenzi phakathi, ukuze afumane ukuphumla. 
Kodwa ke inkcubeko yethu yakwaXhosa isixelela ukuba, umfazi ulindeleke ukuba azenze zonke ezi zinto nangaphezulu xa endile, ngumsebenzi wakhe njengomfazi. 
Uthi umbhali wamaqhalo xa ekungqina oku kungentla: 
Okokuba ubawo usadla ubom ngekuthethwa ezinye namhlanje,ukwenda ngamanyala.” 
Ikakhulu kuza kube kujongwe indlela abathi babazobe ngayo njengabantu ababi, abanobungozi kwaye abangathembakaliyo. 
Uthi xa umfundi efunda eli balana ledrama abone indlela umbhali abazobe ngayo abalinganiswa bakhe abangamabhinqa. 
Iimpawu eziphambili azivezayo lo mbhali zezokuba la mabhinqa anobugqwirha obugqithileyo, kwaye angenza nantonina ukuze oko bakufumanayo kwenzeke ngendlela yabo. 
Kweli candelo ke umphandi uza kuthi anabe banzi ngale ndlela lo mbhali athi abazobe ngayo abalinganiswa bakhe abangamabhinqa nje ngamagqwirha akhohlakeleyo angenza nantoni na, nqu ukubulala oku, ukuze bafumane indlela yabo. 
Oku kuza kubonwa apha phambilana kolu phando, xa kuphonongwa indlela abalinganiswa uMasukude noNoayini abazotywe ngayo njengabakhohlakali. 
UNjinge wabhujelwa yinkosikazi yakhe isamzalela umntwana omnye ogama linguThemba. 
Emva koko uphinde wazeka, wazeka uMasukude. NakuMasukude ufumene inkwenkwe enye, egama linguVuma, kwaba kuphela. 
Omabini la makhwenkwe akhule phantsi kukaMasukude ada amadala. 
Ngenxa yempatho egadalala kaMasukude ubalekile uThemba waya kutshipa eKapa. 
Emva kwethuba elide uThemba etshipile, uNjinge ungenwe bubulwelwe wada wabhubha. 
Ukubhubha kukaNjinge kubangele ukuba umninawe wakhe, uLolo, abe mde kakhulu kwaNjinge ngenjongo yokuncedisana noMasukude kwizinto ngezinto 
ezifuna igxalaba lendoda phakathi komzi. 
Oko kukhathala kukaLolo kumenze uMasukude akabi nagunya lokuziphatha ngokuthe poqo emzini wakhe. 
Ukuzama ukukhupha uLolo phakathi kwamasango omzi wakhe, kuye kwafuneka axoze mphini wumbi. 
UMasukude ngokwenkcubeko yesiXhosa akanalo igunya lokuphatha emzini wakhe nangona ebhujelwe yindoda, kuloko inguLolo ophethe izinto zeli khaya. 
Uthe akubona oku uMasukude, wacebisa ukuba kuzekelwe uVuma, unyana wakhe, ngenjongo yokuthathela kuye ulawulo lwendlu yakhe, mve uMasukude kwincwadi kaMtingane 
Hayi Bhuti akukho nto imbi… 
Apha ekhaya akukho mntu, kungekho mntu nje nam sendimdala. Iintanga zam azisasebenzi ngolu hlobo ndisebenza ngalo. 
Ndifuna ke bhuti kubekho umntu ondincedisayo apha ekhaya. Ndifna ke uVuma azeke. 
Kwesi sicatshulwa singentla kuyabonakala ukuba uMasukude wayeneqhinga aqamele ngalo. 
Nangona ebonakala njengomntu ocebisa into entle, wayezazi into aqamele ngayo. 
Kuthe xa kukweso sithuba, oyena nyana mkhulu kaNjinge, uThemba, owayeseleminyaka esixhenxe etshipile eKapa, wabonwa egaleleka kowabo. 
Le nto yenze amadoda akavuma ukuba kuzekelwe uVuma kuqala engekazeki uThemba, oyena nyana mkhulu. 
Le meko iye yenza ithanda elikhulu kulo mzi, UMasukude uqondile ukuba azinakuphumelela iinjongo zakhe, akayi kuba namagunya ngokupheleleyo emzini wakhe ukuba kuzeke uThemba. 
Ufune icebo lokuthintela uThemba angazeki. 
Uthe akutshelwa ziziceku uMasukude wagqiba kwelokuba amgqithis’amafu uThemba, ecinga ukuba isenzo sakhe siza kuthi simkhulule kule ngxubakaxaka azibona ekuyo, oko kungqinwa ngamazwi athe wawabhekisa akufumanisa ukuba kubanjwe imbizo emzini wakhe malunga nale nyewe, mazwi athi: …kodwa, inene nasi isibhozo! 
Uyakuzeka loo Themba wabo mna ndifile, 
Eneneni oku kufa athetha ngako uMasukude wayesazi ukuba kuza kwenzeka, hayi kuye kuba wayesele enalo icebo analo, mve ecetyiswa nguNo-ayini esithi: …nawe ke susa ilitye endleleni ukhangele ukuba wophinda ukhubeke na, 
Eli litye athetha ngalo uNo-ayini nguThemba, kwaye oku kususwa kwakhe endleleni kukubulawa kwakhe, bave xa bedibana: 
No-ayini: kahle kaloku akufuneki sihleli sihamba kunye. 
Thatha le mpahla ibe ngakuwe. 
Masukude: unyanisile yizise apha 
No-ayini (erhola iqhina), akunavalo kodwa ngoku? 
Masukude (elithatha), mfazi ndiqine ngaphezu kwelitye lenyengane. 
Iqhina alinikwa nguNo-ayini uMasukude ucinge okokuba liza kumsombululela ingxaki abe ezibona ekuyo, 
kanti uwuphosile umhlola, lelo qhina kanye eliye lambhijela kanobom kwiingxaki ezingaphezulu kunaleyo ebecinga okokuba yeyona ngxaki. 
Ukufa kukaThemba akuzanga nasisombululo kuMasukude. 
Inkcazo kagqira ngokufa kukaThemba yenze ingqondo kaMasukude yabethabethana, wanovalo. 
Uzame indlela yokumqanda uLolo angazisasazi ezi ndaba zikagqirha. 
Indlela ayifumeneyo ibe kukumdlisa ngeti ayinike umntwana ukuba ayokunika uLolo lowo 
Masukude: uyayibo le komityi? 
Inomgca onjani, uyabona ke le komityi ize iphunge uLolo, uyeva? 
Olu gxininiso lukaMasukude lwenze uloyiko olummandla kuNosisa, kuphele kubhidana iikomityi, kwaqhawuk’uNobathana, kwabhubha uVuma endaweni kaLolo.
Ukufa kukaVuma nokoyika ukubanjwa kwamphambanisa uMasukude. Zonke ezi zenzo zalo mlinganiswa uyintloko uMasukude zibangelwe kukufuna ukuphuncuka ekuphathweni ngamadoda asemzini wakhe. 
Ufune ukwenza into ethandwa nguye emzini wakhe, kodwa ke labe isiko lakwaXhosa lingamvumeli.  
Le ncwadi yedrama ikhethwe ngeenjongo zokukhankanya indlela ababhali besini sobuduna abathi babazobe ngayo abalinganiswa abangamabhinqa kwiincwadi zabo. 
Oku kubhalwe apha ngentla kuye kwenze kuthi qatha amazwi ombhali uAdeleke 
Lo mbhali ulibeka elubala udaba lokuba uphatho lwabantu besilisa kwizibhalo zedrama xa eqhubeka esithi, 
African Literarure is a male created, male-oriented, chauvinistic art. 
Apha ngentla siyambona uAdeleke ethetha ngendlela ababhali abasisini sobudoda abathi babazobe nanjani na abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo, ngenjongo zokuhlisa isidima sabo, baze banyuse eso sobuduna. 
Ude athi lo mbhali bade basebenzise izixhobo ezifana nokuzoba aba balinganiswa ngendlela ezingeyiyo ezixhaphakileyo ke phofu, 
ezifana nokuzoba abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo, njengamagqwirha, izikhohlakali, abantu abanomona, njalo njalo. 
Xa sijonge eli bali likaMtingane, ziyabonakala ezi mpawu zikhankanywe ngulo mbhali, kulo mlinganiswa unguMasukude. 
Ubuxelegu bokungakwazi ukuziphatha bamwisa phantsi ehlazweni uMawonga Loni. 
UJongilanga lo ungumbali wale drama usizoba qaqambileyo isiwo somntu okholwa butywala nangabasetyhini. 
Ibali livulwa esikolweni, eNobutho Higher Primary, kungena uMnu. Maziko isandla senqununu eOfisini kaMnu. 
Loni, inqununu yesikolo. uMaziko ufaka isikhalazo ngomnye weetitshala zesikolo oxhaphaza utywala ngexesha lesikolo. 
Mve uMaziko xa eyofaka isikhalazo:  
Maziko: Nkqo Nkqo, Chief andihleli kodwa kukho isikhwebu endifuna ukukuchubela sona. 
Kudala ndikuxelela ngoNdila lo ukuba umsebenzi wakho omhle uwufuthanisela ngomzondo. 
Uyabona ngoku, sisandul’ ukungena isikolo uzulalele ukuthi gqi kukaLiziwe. Akakho klasini ngoku. 
Undila umthume umqabulo esirhoxweni. 
Inene uza kubon’ imihlola. 
Esi sikhwebu uMaziko athi ufuna ukusichubela uLoni, sesi sokunxila kukaNdila ngexesha lesikolo.
Besaxoxa oko, gqi umntwana odla ngokuthunywa utywala ngutitshala uNdila, babe kanti bayabufumana ubungqina ngolo hlobo. 
Bona oku kusenzeka: 
Maziko: Nankuya uLiziwe esiza Chief. 
Loni: Yiza naye mfondini 
Maziko: Nantsi ke Chief, le tasi ithe qhu nje iyabalisa 
Loni: Liziwe uvelaphi? Yitasi kabani le? (Cwaka) 
Ndithi uvelaphi? 
Liziwe: Uxolo mfundisi. 
Loni: uxolo lwantoni? Khawuthi ndibone le tasi. Yintoni le? Liziwe: Yintoni le? 
Liziwe: Butywala mfundisi. 
Loni: Bobukabani? 
Liziwe: Bobukatitshala 
Loni:Utitshala ubani? 
Liziwe: Utitshala uNdila. 
Nanko ke unqagram wokubhaqwa kwezimbo zikaNdila zokuthuma umntwana utywala ngxesha lesikolo. 
Ukuvela koko kubangela uNqununu Loni abize intlanganiso yekomiti, ngenjongo yokugxothisa uNdila ebutitshaleni, 
kwaye wabe uyaphumelela ngoba kule ntlanganiso kwagqitywa ekubeni uNdila agxothwe esikolweni. 
Ukugxothwa kukaNdila kwadala ububi obuninzi obathi balandela uLoni. 
uNdila waye waza necebo lokuba abahlobo bakhe uZanele noFuneka bampompe uLoni, abe linxila, ze bamxhwithe yonke imali yakhe. 
Elo cebo ke lasebenza, uLoni waba linxila, wayeka nokuya esikolweni, waba linxila lelokishi elilahlekiswa nguZanele. 
Masiqale sibona apho uMawonga wathi waphenjelelwa ukuba asele utywala: 
Kuxutywe zihanjiswe iziselo. 
Uthe xa enikwa uMawonga wala) 
Funeka: Look Wonga boy, yiba yindoda . 
Sonke asithathi kulo mthi kodwa le yimini eyodwa.(Thatha uthamo) Kuyadlalwa qha ke. 
Mawonga: Ndiyakuxelela ukuba andithathi. 
Zanele: Sukuzikhathaza bhuti wam unikwa iappetizer nje. 
Ezi zixhobo zizinto ezingundoqo okanye ezona zidlala indima enkulu kubomi bomntu. 
Into ethetha ukuthi impilo yomntu ayikwazi ukuphelela ngaphandle kwezizinto. 
Ezizixhobo zizixhobo ezithi zimncedise umntu akuba abeyinxalenye yentlalo. 
Xasinobalula singathetha ngabazali, izikolo, abahlobo nazo zonke ezinye izinto ezithi zimncede umntu zikhulise ukuze naye azive eyinxalenye 
yentlalo yoluntu. 
Kodwa eyona yona ibalulekileyo lusapho, kuba kaloku umntu okanye umntwana uchitha ixesha elininzi ehleli nosapho, yonke okanye into eninzi uyifunda apha ekhayeni, oko kukuthi ngabo ababumbha isimilo somntwana kuba uncanca zonke iimfundiso zekhaya, imfundiso zenkolo, amasiko kunye nazo zonke izinto ezifumaneka apha ekhayeni. 
Umbhali kwelinye ikhasi lakhe ubhale wenjenje 
Kuyabonaka ke apha kula mazwi angentla ukuba ubomi bomntu abusoze bubenentsingiselo ngaphandle kokuba umntu afundiswe indlela yokuphila, 
kwaye lendlela kufuneka ihlohlwe kusetyenziswa ezizixhobo. 
Esinye isixhobo esibaluleke kakhulu sisikolo, kuba kaloku umntwana uthi xa ephuma ekhayayeni abheke esikolweni emvakoko. 
Kulapho ke achitha ixesha nabanye abantwana kunye nabefundisi ntsapho efundiswa indlela yokuphila, (Saldana 2013:1)ubhala enjenje ngezikolo: 
Nalapha kuyacaca ukuba nazo izikolo zinegalelo elikhulu ekufundiseni ukungalingani phakathi kwamadoda namabhinqa kuba kaloku uninzi lwezinto umntwana azifundayo uzithatha phaya esikolweni.  
Le yenye yeengcingane ekudadala zikhona, ngolwimi lwesiNgesi ibizwa ngokuba yi”Feminism”. 
Umbhali uHooks (2000:1) uyicacisa oluhlobo le ngcingane:  
Nto leyo ethetha ukuba eyona njongo yeli phulo kukususa neengcambhu umkhuba wokuxhatshazwa, ukubhukulwa kunye noku calu-calulwa ngokwesini 
kwabantu ababhinqileyo. 
Kaloku umntu obhinqileyo uzibone sele ephantsi kwenyawo zomntu wesini sobuduna, ukanti zininzi izizathu ezikhokhelele ekubeni amadoda acinge ukuba wona angaphezulu kwabantu besini sobukhomokazi. 
Enye yezizathu ezikhokhelele kulo mkhuba yinkangeleko yabantu ababhinqileyo, umzekelo ngokwamandla, ukukhulelwa, ukuncancisa usana kunye nezinye impawu. 
Le nto iyangqinwa nguFreedom (2001:13) kulamazwi akhe athi: 
Yiyo ke le nto nakule mihla kuqapheleka into yokuba abona bantu baninzi kweze politiki ngabantu besini sobuduna, kuba kaloku uninzi lwabantu besini sobuduna babene ngcinga ethi umntu obhinqileyo akakwazi ukwenza izigqibo ezinefuthe nezizaba negalelo ekuphuculeni impilo yoluntu. 
Ukanti kwelinye icala uBillington, ecaphula uKramarae noTrichler (1985:158) uthetha enjenje ngale ngcingane: 
Le ngcingane ivezwe ngasentla isibonisa indlela apho kungenziwa iinzame zokuchitha nokuphelisa ukungalingani phakathi kwamabhinqa kunye namadoda. 
Siphinda sive into yokuba, ingcingane yesini sobukhomokazi yingqokelela yeentshukumo eziqoliselwe ekubeni kubekwe phambili udaba 
lukingabikho kulingana phakathi kwamabhinqa kunye namadoda. 
Ijolise ekulweni ingcinezelo kumabhinqa , ecinezelwa ngamadoda kwakunye namanye amabhinqa. 
Ukuxhasa lamazwi angasentla umbhali uHughes, (2002:3) uthe wakungqina oku ngala mazwi: 
Uyibeke yacaca umbhali kula ncwadi yakhe ukuba wonke umntu uyalingana kwa sesizalweni, ngoko ke wonke ubani kufuneka efumene impatho efanayo nelinganayo. 
Isidima esinikwa isini sobudoda esiphakamileyo nesinamagunya. 
Le ngcingane ijongene nendlela abantu abangamadoda athi anikwe amagunya aphezulu kunalawo abantu abangamabhinqa. 
Lengcingane ngoko lwimi lwase mzini yaziwa ngokuba yisingathi, ngokubhekisele koku kungentla, le ngcingane ijongane nabantu abangamadoda abathi banikwe amagunya aphezulu kunalawo abantu abangamabhinqa. 
Le yindlela ebeka amadoda phambili xa kufuneka kugcwaliswe izikhundla kwezopoliko, ulawulo kwimicimbi yezezindlu, negunya loku lawula abafazi kunye nabantwana babo. 
Ndenza isiqinisekiso sokuba olu phando nalo msebenzi ujongene nendlela apho abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo abathi bazotywa ngayo kwincwadi zedrama ngokubhekisele kwisini sabo sabosobufazi, wenziwe ndim. 
Apho ndisokusebenziso aphando lwabanye ababhali, ndizokucaphula ukuba ndisebenzisa amagama omnye umbhali. 
Ndithanda ukudlulisa umbulelo ongazenzisiyo kuGqirha ngenkxaso yakhe kulo msebenzi wam nokuthi ahlale endikhuthaza ukuba ndenze ngcono nokuba sekucaca ukuba kukude ekugqibeni, othu nokuba sethathe ikhefu, aqinisekise ukuba uynxulubelana nam maxa onke uqinisekisa ukuba lonke uncedo endilufunayo ndiyalufumana. 
Eli phepha lithiywe “Ukuzotywa kwabalinganiswa ababhinqileyo, abazintloko kwidrama zolwimi lwesiXhosa, bezotywa ngababhali besini sobuduna nesini sobukhomokazi liza kube lijongene nendlela apho ababhali abasini esohlukileyo, abathi babazobe ngayo abalinganiswa abayintloko, abangamabhinqa kwizibhalo zabo zedrama zelwimi lwesiXhosa. 
Apha kuzobe kujongwe ingakumbi ababhali abasini sobuduna, ngenjongo yokuveza umba wokuba ababhali besini sobukhomokazi babazoba abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo nje ngabantu abangenamiqolo okuzimela ngaphandle kokuba kubekho indoda obomini babo. 
Aba babhali babazoba abalinganiswa ababhiqileyo phansti kwala ngcamango yokuba, apho umntu obhinqileyo ekumela afumaneke khona kusezimbizeni apho baphekela usapho lwabo rhoqo, ekucoceni umzi nasekukhuliseni abantwana, hayi enye into engaphaya koko. 
Ngoko ke eli phepha libhalwe ngenjongo yokuphelisa oku dodobalisa loo ngcamango. 
Baninzi kea bantu abaphikisana nale ndlela yaphotho lwamabhinqa ngamadoda abo, nangamanye amadoda nje jikilele, eli phepha lizobe lingqinelana nolo ninzi lwabantu abathi loo mpatho mbi yamabhinqa mayiphele, kuvezwe imeko yokuba kukho ulingano phakathi kwamabhinqa kunye nabantu abasini sobukhomakazi. 
Intethetha ukuba eli phepha lizakuti ligqithele lijonge kwaye liveze indlela apho kungati kuekho ulingwano phathi kwezini zimbini, nendlela apho uwonke wonke angakwazi ukuphila ngentlonipho omnye komnye kungekho zimpatho mbi, okanye sini sinesikhundla esiphakamileyo kunesinye. 
Olu phando luza kube lujongene nendlela apho ababhali abasini sobuduna kwakunye nabo babhinqileyo abathi babazobe ngayo abalinganiswa abayintloko abangamabhinqa kwiincwadi zabo zedrama zolwimi lwesiXhosa. 
Phambi kokuba umphandi aqhubekeke nolu phando, umfundi makaqale aqonde ukuba yintoni idrama,udidi olu luzakube luphononongwa apha kolu phando. 
Xa kuthethwa ngedrama kuthethwa ngolunye udidi lokubhala, ngumdlalo omfutshane odlalwa eqongeni. 
Apha umbhali unesithuba sokuba abhale nangontoni na afuna ukubhala ngayo, akunyanzelekanga ukuba ibe yinto esekhe yenzeka. 
Umbhali wedrama athu akhuphe izimvo zakhe ngokwenza kuLuntu jikelel, okuthetha ukuba,, uyakwazi noku bhala ngezinto azibona zisenzeka, kodwa ke athi afane iziqholo ezithi zibangele ibali lakhe libe mnandi, kwaye liyondelelane. 
Yiyo lo nto, azukuthi umamele umdlalo weqonga kunomathotholo, uqonde ukuba, le uyivayo ayifani ne nto enokuthi yenzeke naphina, kodwa ibe ingena kamnandi ezindlebeni zakho. 
Luninzi ke udidi lweedrama, kukho iidrama ezihlekisayo, zikho ezibonakalisa intlekele, zibe zikho nezinemfundiso. 
Ngokwakwisichazi magama Britannica (2014), sibhala sithi xa sicacisa ukuba yintoni idrama: 
Nto le ke egxininisa oku besendikuthethile ngentla, xa bendisithi, iidrama siqulathe iintlekele, okuhlekisayo okanye okufundisayo, kube kulungiseelwe ukuboniswa eqongeni. 
Kumabali amaninzi, ingakumbi udidi lwedrama kunye nenoveli, ababhali bathanda kakhulu ukuzoba amabhinqa njengabantu abaxhomekeke emadodeni ngokutsho kuka Stralton (1990), ukutsho, abafazi abakwazi kuzimela emizini yabo kungekho ndoda, ngoba kaloku ukuze ibhinqa libonakale ngokupheleleyo kufuneka kubekho indoda phakathi kwekhaya. 
Uqhubekeka athi lo kaStralton (1990) into ecebisa ukuba ukuze ibhinqa lihlonipheke phakathi kwamanye amabhinqa, kufuneka libe kanti litshatile kwaye linabantwana. 
Kwinkcubeko yabantu abaMnyama,ingakumbi xa sijongene naleyo yakwaXhosa kukho indlela apho umntwana oyintombazana athi akhuliswe ngayo. 
Umntwana oyintombozana ukhuliswa esazi ukuba kukho izinto ezilindeleke ukuba ezenzile phakathi kwekhaya. 
Le yimfundiso ayifundiswa ngumama wakhe(okanye naliphi na ibhinqa elimkhulisileyo),mama lowo wakhe awathi wayincanca kowakhe umama le mfundiso. 
Umntwana oyintombazana uthi ebuya esikolweni kufuneke ukuba angene emsebenzini wasekhaya, aqinisekise ukuba indlu icociwe, ukuba unoobhuti, kufuneka aqinisekise ukuba bazakubuya ukutya kubalindile, kwaye impahla yabo yesikolo icocekile kusini na. 
Lo ngumsebenzi wemihla ngemihla womntwana oyintombazana phakathi kwekhaya. 
Xa kujongwe inxaxheba ethi idlalwe ngumntwana oyinkwenkwe phakathi kwekhaya kuye kubonakale iyantlukwano enkulu ngokubhekisele kwizinto alindeleke ukuba azenze phakathi kwekhaya. 
Ngenxa yamaxesha esiphila kuwo izinto nto zakuthi zatshintsha. 
Ayikho into yokuba umntwana oyinkwenkwe uza kubuya esikolweni ajongane nemfuyo, ngoba kaloku ngoku kuhlaliwa ezidolophini, apho indaba yemfuyo iyinto ebaliswayo, hayi ephilwayo. 
Nto ethetha ukuba lo mntwana uyinkwenkwe ubuya esikolweni, atye, angene ilokishi. 
Yinto ke le eqheleke kakhulu kumakhaya amaninzi, ayinto inyusa umbilini. 
Xa sijonge kwinkcubeko, apha kuthethwa ngendlela abantu abathile abathi bazenze ngayo izinto ezithile ngenxa yenkcubeko yabo. 
Kwaye ezi zinto bazenza, ngendlela engasoze iphikiswe nangoobani na ngoba yindlela abayaziyo kwaye abayiqhelileyo yokuphila. 
Oku kungentla kungqinwa ngala mazwi angezantsi ayethethwe kwiNkomfa ayayiseMexico ethetha ngeePolisi zenkcubeko (Mexico, 1982): 
Esi sithethi sasithetha la mazwi, sayibeka yee gca okwekat’emhlop’ehlungwini into yokuba inkcubeko yethu isizobela indlela ekulindeleke ukuba siphile ngayo, kwaye iyinkxalenye yolwakhiwo lwentlalo yethu. 
Sithe xa sigqithela sizama ukucacisa uthungelwano phakathi kwenkcubeko neyantlukwano ngesini sathi: 
Yiyo loo nto kwinkcubeko yethu yakwaXhosa siyazi ukuba umsebenzi womntwana oyintombazana awusoze ufane nalowo oyinkwenkwe. 
Kananjalo kwinkcubeko yakwaXhosa umntwana oyintombazana uzazi esemtsha izinto ezilindelekileyo kuye, ingqeqesho enjalo uyifumana eselula, kulungiselelwa indlela aza kuthi aziphathe ngayo maxa ekhula. 
Le ngqeqesho akuphikiswana nayo ngoba yindlela ekuthi kubunjwe ngayo umntwana. 
Ngokunjalo xa kubhekiselelwe kumntwana oyinkwenkwe. 
Ukuba kukho umntwana omncinci kowabo oyintombazana, lowo uyinkwenkwe, ngumsebenzi wakhe ukuqinisekisa ukuba akukho bubi buya kuze buchaphazele usisi wakhe omncinci ngokuba yena umsebenzi wakhe njengobhuti kukumkhusela. 
Le ngqeqesho ke yile kukhulwa ngayo. 
Yiyo loo nto namhlanje kuza kuthiwa, umsebenzi katata endlwini kukukhusela usapho lwakhe, ukubakhathalela, ukubondla, ukanti indima yebhinqa ekhayeni kukuqinisekisa ukuba abantwana bacociwe, indlu icociwe kwaye izinto zekhaya zenziwe. 
Le ngqeqesho ke ithe yazala ingcambu ezininzi ezithe zakhokela kwindlela yokuphila kubantu abaMnyama jikelele, kodwa ke iyantlukwano 
ixhomekeke kwinkcubeko leyo yalowo. 
Yiyo ke loo nto siza kuthi siyijonge syihl’amahlongwane kolu phando, nakumabali ethu edrama. 
Kula mabali kuye kuboniswe ingcamango yokuba indaba yokuba umfazi abe nemfundo, aphangele kwaye enze izigqibo zekhaya ayinto ibalulekileyo 
ngoba umsebenzi womfazi usekhitshini apho kufuneka eqinisekisile ukuba indoda yakhe ikhathalelwe, ukutya kukhona etafileni, kwaye indlu icociwe. 
Iincwadi eziza kuthi zishukuxwe banzi kolu phando zezi: ‘Inene Nasi Isibhozo’(2011), ‘Ndixoleleni’(1995), ‘
Ndiyekeni’(1975) kunye no-‘Iinkunzi Ezimbini’ (1994) 
Oku kuthethwe ngako ngentla siyakubona pha kulaa drama yombhali ithi Iinkunzi ezimbini Mothlabane (1994:8) kwincoko phakathi kwabalinganiswa ababini uNolasti nomnyeni wakhe uSibonda: 
Sibonda: Kanene akukho nto niyenzayo ngaphandle kokuthetha nina bafazi. Iphi ikofu Nolasti? Ndidiniwe… 
Nolasti: Ndidiniwe oku kwam ubonanje. 
Ubungenakuyenza ngokwakho nanhlanje ikofu? (Ahleke kancinci) 
Sibonda: Uthi mandenze ikofu? Uyaziva kakuhle le nto uyithethayo? 
Sibonda: …Akundivanga ukuba ndithe iza nekofu. ( Angasukumi uNolasti, abe emthe ntsho. Aye kuye ngomsindo uSibonda. 
Nolasti: (Edlula kuSibonda emthyilizela) Ndizidinelwe mna andinaxesha lale nto uyithethayo… 
Ndiyaphangela mna ngomso ndisaya kuphumla ekoyini. 
Asale embombozela uSibonda 
Sibonda: Yeyiphi ke ngoku le? Kutheni ingathi uya ethath’unyawo mihla le nje lo mfazi?... 
Andisenakufuna nekofu le kodwa ndithi ndinomfazi. …Kutheni ingathi ndiseza kuyicel’ivuthiwe nje into yomfazi wasesikolweni? 
Apha ngentla umbhali wale drama usibonisa umba apho inkcubeko nendlela umntu oyindoda aqeqeshwe ngayo, noko akulindeleyo kumfazi wakhe. 
Akukhathaliseki nokuba ngumfazi ophangelayo, umnyeni uthi alindele ukuba umfazi wakhe enze imisebenzi yakhe yekhaya nokuba sele ediniwe evela emsebenzini. 
uSibonda lo akafuni ukuphikisana namfazi, ufuna ukuba lo mfazi enze konke oko akuthethayo ngelo xesha athi makakwenze ngalo. 
Xa uNolasti engavumi ngenxa yokudinwa, uSibonda ukusulela oko kwinto yokuba uNolasti efundile, ngoko ke umbona njengomntu ofuna ukuziphatha kuba enesikolo. 
Kodwa akunjalo, uNolasti udiniwe ngoba nguye yedwa ophangelayo kweli khaya kwaye uphangela iyure ezinde. 
Indlela abafazi abaphathwa ngayo kule mihla siphila kuyo inayo iyantlukwano kwindlela ababephathwa ngayo mandulo. 
Kodwa le yantlukwano incinci ngoba kunamhlanje nje indima yomfazi iqulunqwa ngabantu basekuhlaleni kunye nabo bomzi wakhe. 
Ngenxa yokuba engumfazi kunyanzelekile ukuba enze izinto nokuba akavumelani nazo. 
Kweli xesha siphila kulo kukho iimeko apho iba ngumfazi yedwa ophangelayo emzini wakhe, kodwa ufumanise ukuba nokuba sekunjalo, intloko yekhaya iza kuba ngumnyeni ngoba nguye indoda yekhaya, nangona kungekho mali ayingenisayo, ngenxa yendlela izinto ezazingayo mandulo, njengokuba bekuse kukhankanyiwe ngentla. 
Uqhabalake wathi omnye umbhali xa ethetha ngentloko yekhaya elibhinqa; 
Ngoko ke le nto iphinde ixake ngokuba kunamhla, ayikho into ethi yenziwe ngamadoda, apho amabhinqa angakwaziyo ukuyenza. 
Awukho umsebenzi ekunokuthiwa ngowamadoda kuphela kule mihla siphila kuyo, ngoba amabhinqa azikhulula kulaa ngcamango yakude kudala yokuba into abayikwaziyo kukuba baphelele ekhitshini nasekuzaleni abantwana kuphela. 
Ngoko ke yintoni unobangela wakuba amabhinqa angakwazi ukunikwa amagunya okuba abe yintloko yekhaya esesikweni? 
Ukuba konke oko kwenziwa ngumntu wesini sobuduna nabo bayakwazi ukukwenza, nangaphezulu, lo mbuzo usalengalenga kunanamhla. 
Le nto ibonakalisa ucinezelo lwamabhinqa ngamadoda emitshatweni, nangaphandle kwemitshato. 
Inkcubeko yethu ithi ilukhuthaze olu cinezelo kubantu ababhinqileyo, kuba uthi umntu obhinqileyo akutshata, athiywe igama elitsha kweli khaya lakhe litsha. 
Esi senzo asimchaphazeli nganto lo uyindoda, akubikho gama litsha alinikwayo. 
Ifani nayo iyajika kufuneka uthathe ifani yakulo myeni. 
Olu cinizelo aluphelelanga emadodeni kuphela, namanye amabhinqa ayakwazi ukuwacinezela amanye amabhnqa. 
Loo nto ibonakala kakuhle kwakule ncwadi kaMothlabane (1994:7) xa uNolasti engangqinelani nabanye abafazi bakaSibonda ngendlela ekulindeleke ukuba baphathwe ngumnyeni wabo, bave xa besithi: 
Nokhaya: Hayi wethu akukho xesha lakuphumla ayeza la macentsa, kuza kubanjani xa esifikela sithe dudlu apha sonke? 
Phumla wena ukuba uyafuna usiyeke thina sisebbenze. 
Nolasti: Yekani oku kumphatha okwesithixo uSigqibo! 
Nini aba baziphathisa kakubi ngoku kumoyika kangaka. 
Unani yena le nto engenakuze akhe azenzele nto? Khaniphumle torho nidiniwe, niyayixikixa nempilo yenu ngale nto yokusoloko nisebenza ngexhala. 
Nofinishi: Uyaphazama ke kuloo ndawo Sisi. 
Akaphethwanga okwesithixo uyise kaMandla kulo mnyanti, kwaye asisebenzi ngexhala. Andazi ukuba ufundile nje uthini ukungakwazi umahluko 
phakathi kokoyika umntu nokumhlonela. 
Simhlonele thina uJwarha kuba uyitshonti yeli khaya. Thina sonke apha… 
Nolasti: … Yintoni ngoku ityhonti?... 
Nofinishi: Awukwazi nokuhlonipha kodwa uthi ungumfazi! Itshonti yintloko, yile nto ke ayiyo uyise kaMandla apha kuthi. 
Uyasondla, uyasinxiba, usikhusele, u… 
Nolasti: Pheza apho ke sendilazi ngentloko elo culo. Ngelishwa ke apha kum alizi nanto intsha kuba ndiyakwazi ukuzenzela zonke ezi zinto zenziwa yityha- uthi yintoni na kanene? 
Mna ndiyazisebenzela… 
Ngokwale ngcamango ingentla kuyacaca ukuba amabhinqa nawo anayo indima ayidlalayo ekucinezeleni amanye amabhinqa. 
Kudala amabhinqa azenza iinzame zokuthi azikhulule kule mbandezelo yocinzelelo. 
Kodwa oko kuzikhulula akuzange kwaba lula. Oko kuzikhulula kwabo nokulwela amalungelo abo ekuhlaleni, emisebenzini nakwizinto zomthetho kwaqalwa ngamabhinqa aseMelika ngomnyaka we-1970, bejolise ekulweni ingcinezelo yamabhinqa ngamadoda, kwakunye nolingano phakathi kwabantu abasini esohlukileyo ngoba babona ukuba ukuze bafumane intlonipho ekuhlaleni naselizweni liphela, kuza kufuneka ukuba balwe lento yokuba amadoda enikwa isidima esiphezulu kwaye esiphakamileyo nesinamagunya, ngaphezulu kwamabhinqa. 
Ngoko ke olu phando luza kube liphicotha indlela apho ababhali abangamadoda nabo babhinqileyo boncwadi lwedrama abathi babazobe ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo,  ngokubhekisele kulwazi lwethu esinalo ngempatho yabafazi ekuhlaleni, kwakunye nokungalingani kwabantu abasini esahlukileyo, ukuze sibone ukuba le mpatho iphilwa ngamabhinqa mihla le, iyafana na nale iphilwa ngabalinganiswa bemidlalo yedrama ezincwadini ezikhethiweyo zolwimi lwesiXhosa. 
Xa sijonge kwezi ncwadi zedrama eziza kuthi zisetyenziswe kolu phando, kukho izinto ezithungelanayo kuzo. 
Incwadi yokuqala kaMbovane ethi : Ndixoleleni, apha umbhali umzobe umlinganiswa wakhe oyintloko olibhinqa njengomntu onomona, ongayimameliyo imiyalelo yomnyeni, kwaye ongenayo intlonipho kubantu abadala base mzini wakhe lo endele kuwo. 
Sigqithe sijonge incwadi yedrama elandelayo uNdiyekeni kaJongilanga, apha umbhali uzobe abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo ngendlela ezahlukileyo, kodwa abona balinganiswa baphambili ngamabhinqa amabini awazobe njengabantu abalandela imali yamadoda apho ingakhona, umbhali ubazoba nje ngabantu abahlala endlini yabo bacinge amaqhinga okutya imali yamadoda, nendlela apho banokuthi bafumane amadoda azothi abathengele izinto, bengazisebenzelanga ngokwabo. 
Sithi sisajonge apho, siye sigqithele kwindlela yena umbhali uMtingane, wencwadi ethi, Inene nasi isibhozo, athi abazoba ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo, sibe sijonge kumlinganiswa ophambili, uMasukude. 
Apha umbhali usizobele lo mlinganiswa wakhe uphambili nje ngebhinqa elinzulu ekucingeni, uhlelinje ucinga ukwenza ububi kubanye abantu xa bengahambelisani nalento ayifunaye befuna ukuma endleleni yakhe. 
Akaphelelanga aph lo mbhali, lo mbhali umzobe uMasukude nje ngomntu okhahlakeleyo, ongcolileyo kwaye othakathaya. 
Konke oku siye sikubone kwizenzo zikaMasukude apha ebalini xa abantu basemzini wakhe bengasivumi isicelo sakhe sokuba kuzeke unyana wakhe uVuma kuqala kunoThemba. 
UMasukude akafuni ukuyivuma le nto ngoba ebesele ezixelele ukuba ubomi bakhe buyakuba ngcono kakhulu ukuba unyana wakhe angazeka kuqala, ngoba lo nto ithetha ukuba uzakuba nawo amagunya okulawula umzi wakhe, ekebeni waswelekelwa ngumnyeni, ngoba okwa ngoku, ngabaninawa nabakhuluwa bomnyeni wakhe abawulayo. 
Lo nto iyamhlupha kakhulu uMasukede, de afikelele kwicebo 
lokubasusa bonke abo bathi bazame ukuma endleleni yakhe, engayazi ukuba ngokwenza oko uzinqikela ilitye elinoxhwangu. 
Jonga yena umbhali wesini sobukhomokazi indlela athi abazobe ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo kweyakhe idrama. uMothlabane(1994) uyibhalile idrama ethi: 
Iinkunzi ezimbini, apha umlinganiswa wakhe oyintloko inguNolasti, owendele kuSibonda, phofu ibe inguye oyintloko yekhaya ngoba nguye aphangelayo, nguye oza nemali endlini, ikwanguye nobeka ukutya etafileni. 
Kodwa kuba inkcubeko yakwaXhosa isithi indoda yintloko yekhaya, uNolasti akanalo igunya lokwenza izigqibo zekhaya kuba elibhinqa. 
Njengoko kutshiwo ukuba kuza kujongwa iidrama zolwimi lwesiXhosa, umphandi ufuna ukujonga ukuba ingaba ababhali baphenjelelwa sisini sabo kusini na xa bebumba abalinganiswa bezibhalo zabo. 
Kwaye ingaba babhala oku bakubhaliyo kuba befuna ukuphuhlisa inkcubeko yakwaXhosa. Konke oku kuzothi kuvele ekuhambeni kolu phando. 
Umphandi uthe phambi kokuba aqalise olu phando, wakhankanya ukuba kukho ingxaki kwindlela amabali ethu edrama esiXhosa athi abhalwe ngayo. 
Kuye kwabonakala ukuba umxholo wala mabali uyafana ukuba awuyelelenanga. 
Umphandi ubonile ukuba ababhali bathetha into enye, kwaye bethetha into enye nje, umphandi akangqinelani nabo. 
Oku kungangqinelani kuye kuzalwe kukutshintsha kwamaxesha. 
Ezi zinto aba babhali bezi ncwadi zedrama babhala ngazo zizinto ezazisenzeka kude kudala. 
Ngenxa yokutshintsha kwamaxesha, akukho mntu ulindeleleke ukuba aphile ngale ndlela ezi ncwadi zisikhokelela ngayo. 
Ukubonisa oku kungangqinelani, umphandi uza kuthi abonise kwaye akhankaye impembelelo yotshintsha kwamaxesha ethi ibonakale kwindlela ababhali abathi babhale ngayo. 
Nto ethatha ukuba, umphandi uzakuthi athelekise indlela ababhali bakutsha abathi bawukhankanye ngayo lo mba wokungalingani ngokwesini, nokucinezelwa kwamabhinqa ngabantu besini sobuduna, kwakunye ngamanye amabhinqa. 
Injongo yoku kukubonakalisa iyantlukwano phakathi kwabababhali balamaxesha ohlukileyo. 
Ingxaki ebonakeleyo yeyokuba, ababhali beedrama zolwimi lwesiXhosa bacebisa ukuba, umntu wesini sobuduna ungcono kunalowo wesini sobukhomokazi. 
Xa ndisithi ababhali, ndibala ooMbekeni, Ntloko, Mbovane, noJongilanga, nje ukuqwalasela abambalwa. 
Ungcono ngandlela yini inokuba uyazibuza mfundi. Ungcono ngendlela yokuba unamandla kwaye unamagunya ngaphezulu kwalowo ubhinqileyo. 
Ngulo wesini sobuduna onalo ilungelo lokuxelela lowo ulibhinqa izinto ekulindeleke ukuba azenze ukuba batshatile, nokuba sijonge abantu abazalanayo, abalekelenayo, okanye abazalana ngomanyano lomtshato. 
Izibhalo zinempembelelo engummandla kwindlela abantu abathi baphile ngayo, ngokunjalo nomabonakude ngamanye amaxesha nosasazo kunomathotholo. 
Ukukhathazeka komphandi kuvele ekubeni athe wakufunda iincwadi eziliqela zedrama wabona ukuba aba babhali bonke bathetha into enye. 
Nto le ingathi yakufundwa ze ilandelwa, izakuthi isiphathele iingxaki kwindawo esihlala kuzo. 
Ngxaki le ekwakuphilwa phantsi kwayo kude kudala, apho amabhinqa ayexhatshazwa, ephila phantsi kwengcinezelo ngenxa yempatho mbi yabantu besini sesiduna kunye namanye amabhinqa. 
Ngoko ke ukuba oko kubhalwayo kwiidrama zethu zesiXhosa akutshintshwa siza kuzibona sisengxakini kwakhona. 
Ezincwadi zithetha into enye ethi, ukuba ulibhinqa, izinto zekhaya azizokuxoxwa nawe, ngoko ke, leyo yinto apha ebandakanya amadoda ekhaya, hayi amabhinqa. 
Ukuba ulibhinqa, kukho izinto ekulindeleke ukuba uzenzile, kwaye ayizinto apha ezixoxisayo ngoba zibonwa njengezinto ezathi zadalelwa amabhinqa. 
Izinto ezifana nokucoca ikhaya, ukuqinisekisa ukuba mihla le isidlo sekhaya silungile. 
Akubalulekanga ke nokuba ungumntu apha ophangelayo, indima ekufuneka uyidlalile emtshatweni wakho ayitshintshi. 
Nanku umzekelo ebesekhankanyiwe ngentla kwenye yencwadi eziza kuthi sijongwe yombhali Mothlabane (1994), ethi Iinkunzi ezimbini. 
Phaya umbhali usizobele umlinganiswa onguNolasti otshatele kuSibonda, Sibonda lowo usisithembu ngoba unobafazi ababini ngaphandleni kukoNolasti. 
Apha phakathi kwelibali liyidrama, siyambona uNolasti ediniwe evela emsebenzini, nanku umnyeni wakhe emngxamela esithi ulinde into ephungwayo, akakhathaliseki nto kukudinwa kukaNolasti yena ufuna nje into ephungwayo emfazini wakhe, kodwa ubayekile bona abababini abanye abafazi  bakhe, uleqa lo udiniweyo uvela ukuyokuphangela, ephangelela uSibonda nabafazi bakhe ababini kunye nanbantwana babo phezu koko. 
Ezi ncwadi zedrama ziphinde zibeke elubala ingcamango yokuba amabhinqa la ngabantu apha abanenkohlakalo kwaye abahleli nje balandelana namadoda kuba befuna imali yawo. 
Oku kukhohlakala sikubona pha kulaa Drama kaMbovane (1995) ethi Ndixoleleni, xa ezoba umlinganiswa uNojenti, umphandi engangenanga lukhulu ebalini, lo mlinganiswa uthe wenza izinto ezibuhlungu kwaye ezimdaka kunyana omnyeni wakhe ngenxa yomona. 
Ze umba wamabhinqa alandela amadoda ngenxa yemali siyibone nkcakasa kulaa drama kaJongilnga (1975). 
Kuninzi ke okuthethwa ngaba babhali, kodwa ke lo uphandayo akafuni ukungenna nzulu lingekafiki ixesha lokwenza oko, ngoba kaloku umfundi kufuneka efunde de ayokufikelela esiphelweni. 
Lo msebenzi uza kwahlulwa ngokwezahluko ezintlanu. 
Kwisahluko sokuqala: kuza kube kutshayelelwa oko kuza kube kuphethwe kolu phando, kujongwe: iinjongo zolu phando, indlela uphando oluza kuqulunqwa ngalo, ingxaki yophando kwakunye nengcaciso magama. 
Isahluko sesibini: sijongene neethiyori ezikhethiweyo eziza kuthi zisetyenziswe ukuphuhlisa le ngcamango yokungalingani kwabantu besini esohlukileyo. ithiyori yesini sobukhomokazi kunye nethiyori yokungalingani ngesini. 
Kuza kuqwalaselwa indlela apho ezi thiyori zithi zilawule indlela abantu abathi baphathwe ngayo, ingakumbi ucinezelo phakathi kwamabhinqa kunye namadoda, nocinezelo lwamabhinqa kwamanye amabhinqa.  
Isahluko sesithathu: siza kujongana nophononongo lweencwadi zedrama ezikhethiweyo ekulindeleke ukuba zixhase ezi ngcingane ziza kube ziphononongwa kolu phando. 
Apha kuza kuqwalaselwa indlela abalinganiswa abayintloko abangamabhinqa bezi ncwadi zedrama abazotywe ngayo. 
Apha kwesi sahluko kuzokuqwalaselwa kwincwadi ezintathu ezibhalwe ngababhali besini sobuduna, beqamelele kwiithiyori zokungalingani ngokwesini, kunye naleyo inika abantu besilisa isikhundla esiphezulu kunabo babhinqileyo. 
Injongo apha kukuphonononga ukuba, ingaba abababhali babhala ngokufanayo na, kwaye ingaba kanti oku kuphenjelelwa sisini sabo sobuduna. 
Isahluko sesine: apha kuzakuqwalaselwa ingakumbi kumbhali olibhinqa, kube kujongwe indlela yena athe wabazoba ngayo abalinganiswa abangamabhinqa. 
Injongo yesi isahluko kukujonga ukuba ingaba lo mbhali unayo iyantlukwano kwindlela ababhali besini sobuduna ababazoba ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo kwezabo izibhalo, kweye sijonge unobangela woko.
Apha kuzakujongwa ikakhulu kula thiyori yokunikwa abantu besini sobuduna amagunya angaphaya kunalawo anikwa amabhinqa. 
Incwadi ezakuphononongwa apha yile: 
Isahluko sesihlanu: sona siza kuqukumbela konke okulapha kolu phando. Kwesi sahluko kuza kube kujoliswe nasekucebiseni uluntu ngeemeko zoxinzelelo phakathi kwabantu abasini esohlukileyo. 
Apha kuza kujoliswa ekuvuleni amehlo abantu ngezinto ezenzekayo apha elizweni mihla le, ngokubhekisele kumalungelo amabhinqa, impatho-mbi 
yamabhinqa ngamadoda nangamanye amabhinqa, kunye nendlela apho lowo uzibone ekule meko anokuthi azikhuphe kuyo.  
UPitso Mosimane noThulani Thuswa bebhiyozela impumelelo yeMamelodi Sundowns eminyakeni eyadlulayo.

uThulani Thuswa – obekade esisithethi seMamelodi Sundowns kwiminyaka egqithileyo. 
Iingxelo zithi uThuswa ulandulele eli emva kokubandakanye engozini yemoto ebehamba ngayo endleleni ephakathi kweMarlboro neSandton ngentseni 
yanamhlanje (iCawe).
Amagosa ezendlela eGoli aqinisekisile ukuba ngokwenene kwehle ingozi yemoto eluhlobo lweMercedes Benz kuhola wendlela uM1 ngentsimbi 
yesixhenxe ekuseni.
Emva koko amazwi ovelwano angene egxalathelana macala onke. 
Abantu abaziwayo abaquka uPitso Mosimane, uDenis Onyango noHlompo Kekana – bakhawuleze bafika kwindawo yesehlo emva kokuva ngengozi eyehlele 
uThuswa obehlonitshiwa kakhulu ngabalandeli beSundowns nabaninzi kumajelo eendaba.

Emva kokushiya kwakhe iSundowns ngo-2019, uThuswa wasungula inkampani yakhe entsha ekuthiwa yiTyler Masons Management.
“Sifuna ukuvakalisa ubuhlungu kukushiywa kwethu nguBhuti wethu, uThulani Thuswa. 
Ebesisibane sehlabathi futhi ebengumntu obelungile” Itshilo ingxelo ekhutshwe lusapho kusasa namhlanje.

akwenzekanga kwanto.

UKaizer Motaung Junior, uyise uKaizer Motaung noStuart Baxter – umqeqeshi omtsha weKaizer Chiefs.
Emva kweeveki eziliqela kusenziwa amaqashiso ngomntu oza kuqeqesha iKaizer Chiefs, namhlanje kwaziswe uMnu. 
Stuart Baxter njengomqeqeshi wayo. UBaxter ufika ezithendeni zikaGavin Hunt – oye wagxothwa ngenxa yokungaqhubi kakuhle kweqela emidlalweni

UChris Nguta ngusozoso waseNgqushwa oyintshatsheli yoMzantsi Afrika.
Inye imini, yile yanamhlanje! Amadoda azizigantsontso aza kukhuphisana kube nzima kukhuphiswano loosozoso (Bodybuilding) KwaZulu-Natal. 
Oosozoso abaphuma kumaphondo onke waseMzantsi Afrika baza kudibana phaya kwitumente eququzelelwe nguMnu. 
Mduduzi Green – okwangusozoso ophambili elizweni lonke. 
IMpuma Koloni iza kumelwa yintshatsheli yoMzantsi Afrika ebeke ithemba layo kuyo – uChris “General” Nguta. 
Itumente iza kuqala ngale ntsasa ngentsimbi yethoba iyophela ngentsimbi yesithathu emalanga.
“Yitumente yokuqala le ndiyakuyo eququzelelwe ngamadoda angoosozoso. 
Zange yenzeka lo nto kwi-Afrika yonke. Bayifumene inkxaso, kangangokuba usozoso ophume phambili zonke izigaba uza kugoduka nekhulu lamawaka erandi (R100 000). 
Ndiya KwaZulu-Natal ngeliyokunika iinkxaso – kodwa kwelinye icala, ikwa yitumente yokuqala ukusukela oko ilizwe lahlaselwa yiKhorona,” utshilo uNguta.
Umgangatho uza kuba phezulu kakhulu. 
Indoda nganye kufuneka ikhwele eqongeni iyazi into eza kuyenza. 
Likhona ixhala kuGeneral kuba ixesha lilide bengasakhweli eqongeni ngenxa yeKhorona – kodwa uthi kuza kudlana iintsimbi.
“Amalungiselelo wam ahambe kakuhle ngoba ndaqala ukuzilolonga ekuqaleni konyaka. 
Abaxhasi bam nabaphathi bendawo endizilolongela kuyo bazamile ukundincedisa kakhulu. 
Likhona lona ixhala apha kum kuba ndigqibele kudala ukukhwela eqongeni. 
Andizazi ke ngoku iinduku abaqule ngazo abanye abantu endiza kukhuphisana nabo phaya. 
Zezo zinto qha endizoyikayo – kodwa ke ndizilungiselele kakhulu. Kodwa ndingatsho ndithi ndikulungele ukuya edabini KwaZulu. 
Owam umkhonto untlangothimbini,” utshilo uNguta.
Abhengeziwe amagama wabadlali beBarcelona abeza eMzantsi Afrika
Itumente yomnyazi iqaqambisa amantombazama ezikolweni -
Umdlalo womnyazi ufumene ufunqu ongumangaliso emva kokuphehlelelwa kwetumente entsha eza kudlalwa zizikolo kwilizwe lonke. 
Le tumente entsha exhaswa nguDStv iza kudlalwa ngabantwana bezikolo abaneminyaka ephakathi kweshumi elinesithandathu ukuya kwabaneshumi elinethoba leminyaka. 
Phantsi kwale tumente entsha ekuthiwa yiDStv Schools Netball Challenge, izikolo zamabanga aphantsi ziza kuqala ukukhuphisana ezithilini, 
kulandele imidlalo yamaphondo kugqibele ekazwelonke eza kukhupha iintshatsheli. 
Eli livelatanci likaMultiChoice lifika kakuhle eyifake phantsi kwekhwapha lakhe yonke imidlalo yezikolo eMzantsi Afrika.
Okuhle ngale tumente kukuba abantwana beelali nabeedolophi baza kufumana amathuba alinganayo okubonwa besebancinane. 
“Umsebenzi wethu kukukhulisa italente nokwakha izakhono eza kuthi zihlale ixesha elide. 
Itumente yezikolo inika amantombazana ithuba elihle lokuziqaqambisa ukuze abonwe ngabacholacholi betalente. 
Siyaziqhenya ngegalelo esilenzileyo ebholeni ekhatywayo nasembhoxweni. 
Ngoku lithuba lokuba sifunqule umnyazi,” litshilo igosa likaMultiChoice, uJoe Heshu. 
Konke oku kwenzeka ngethuba elihle uMzantsi Afrika uqala amalungiselelo weNdebe yeHlabathi yomnyazi eza kubanjelwa eKapa ngonyaka ka-2023. 
Abadlali baza kufumana ithuba lokubonwa ngabaqeqeshi beqela lesizwe.
“Silisebe sivuya kakhulu xa uMultiChoice noNetball SA besizisa itumente enje ngale. 
Emva kokuzuza amalungelelo wokusingatha iNdebe yeHlabathi, singuRhulumente sifuna ukubona okulilifa kuxhanyulwa ngamantombazana ayakuthi 
athathe ibhola yomnyazi ayibeke kwelinye inqanaba,” utshilo uNksz. 
Nocawe Mafu, isekela-mphathiswa weZemidlalo kuzwelonke. 
Abaqeqeshi bezikolo namagosa emidlalo aza kuphatha imidlalo onke aza kufumana uqeqesho olusemgangathweni ophezulu. 
Izikolo ezifuna ukudlala kwiDStv Shcools Netball Challenge kufuneka zibhalise apha: www.saschoolsnetball.co.za

Amanqindi abuyela eMonti emva kwexesha elide enqabile
Emva kokuhlehliswa kwinyanga ephelileyo, itumente yamanqindi eququzelelwa yinkampani yabathelekisi, iXaba Boxing Promotions, iqhubela 
phambili ngoLwesihlanu kule veki eMonti. Abalandeli bamanqindi eBuffalo City – eyona ndawo esaphala phambili ngokuthanda amanqindi – baza 
kufumana inyhweba yokubukela imilo eyohlukeneyo ephakathi kweembethimanqindi eziphambili eMzantsi Afrika. 
Oku kwenzeka emva kwetumente yamanqindi ebiququzelelwe yiRumble Boxing Promotions kwiiveki ezidlulileyo eGqeberha. 
Umlo okulindeleke utsale umdla wabantu abaninzi uphakathi kwegqala, umakadenetha, uNkosinathi Joyi oza kudibana etshatshalazeni netyendyana 
elisaze ngobuso ezweni ekuthiwa ngu-Ayanda Ndulani.
La madoda aza kukhuphisana ngentshinga ye-IBO Miniflyweight emlweni onemijikelo elishumi elinanye. 
UJoyi, 37, obeke wasecicini lokuphulukana nentshinga ye-IBO kwiminyaka egqithileyo, kunyanzelekile aphumelele ngoLwesihlanu, e-International Convention Centre. 
Phantsi kwegama layo le ndedeba yaseMdantsane inamashumi amathathu anesithandathu emilo, ibethwe kahlanu, yadlala ntanganye kwakanye – eminye iyiphumelele yonke. 
UNhlanhla Tyirha noJoey Canoy baza kujijisana kube mdaka iisali emlweni wentshinga engenamntu yeWBA Lightfly emlweni onemijikelo elishumi elinanye.
UTyirha, onekamva eliqaqambileyo, uthembise abalandeli bakhe ngokwenza ezibukwayo kuFacebook emlweni wale veki. 
Imilo ayilwileyo uTyirha yonke uyiphumelele. 
Udibana noCanoy, 27, oyindoda enamava kakhulu ekhe yazigxama kubantu abafana noNkosinathi Joyi noHekkie Budler. 
Nangona kunjalo, uTyirha uthe kuzawubizwa igama lakhe emva komlo. 
Omnye umlo uphakathi kukaNwabisile Cholani noSiphamandla Baleni. 
Ezi mbethimanqindi ziza kulwela intshinga yeSA Jnr Flyweight emlweni onemijikelo elishumi elinanye. 
Zombini ezi mbethimanqindi zinethuba zisemanqindini kwaye zinethuba lokuzenzela imbali.

Umasipala uzimiselele ukuvuselela umbhoxo eNgquza.
UMnu. Ndiphiwe Mhlakaza ngumhlohli waseMqikela S.S.S. kodwa ukwanguye nomthandi wombhoxo.
Umbhoxo ufile kwiindawo zaseNgquza. Oku kubhenceke ngethuba uMultiChoice enika iMqikela S.S.S. ibala lemidlalo entlobontlo kwinyanga ephelileyo. 
Imidlalo efana nebhola ekhatywayo, umnyazi, intenetya neminye inayo indawo – kodwa wona umbhoxo awunayo indawo. 
Lo nto iwubeke emngciphekweni wokubhanga umbhoxo eNgquza ngoba zonke iilali azinawo amabala. 
Umdla embhoxweni ugcinwe zizikolo – kodwa kunzima ngenxa yamabala angekhoyo. UMnu.Ndiphiwe Mhlakaza, ongumhlohli eMqikela, uxelele I’solezwe lesiXhosa ukuba isikolo sakhe besifudula sihamba phambili embhoxweni – kodwa akusekho njalo ngoba akukho zindawo zokudlalela.
“Kule sekethe yethu yaseMalangeni, akukho nanye ilali enebala lombhoxo kwezingaphaya kwamashumi amabini,” utshilo uMhlakaza.
“Umdla ukhona ebantwini. Zikhona iintwana ezikhe ziziqeqeshe kuba zithanda umbhoxo. 
Ziyadlala kwitumente kaMasipala ngoba umbhoxo uyabandakanywa nawo xa iqhutywa. 
Thina bantu esazi izikolo ezinabantwana abadlala umbhoxo, siye sibadibanise ukuze badlale kula tumente kasodolophi. 
Amaqela walapha ayedlala eMthatha – kodwa ayisenzeki lo nto ngoba akukho mabala okudlalela,” utshilo uMhlakaza. 
Isithethi sikaMasipala, Umnu. Zamuxolo Mathwasa, uvumile ukuba ngokwenene awekho amabala eNgquza – 
Kodwa akhona amatileyile awenzayo umasipala ukuze abekhona.
“Umbhoxo ubukade udlalwa ezikolweni, ungekho ezilalini. 
Yilo nto ebangele angabikho amabala. 
Kodwa xa siqhuba imidlalo kamasipala, umbhoxo siyawufaka. Umbhoxo besiwudlalisa eNgqungqushe okanye eMqikela S.S.S. – apho uMultiChoice akhe khona ibala. 
Umasipala unephulo lokwakha amabala emidlalo entlobontlobo. Mabini agqityezelwayo. 
Ngamabala alungiselelwe yonke imidlalo. Sizama ukufumana umhlaba ezinkosini ukuze sikwazi ukuphucula amabala wombhoxo. 
Siyathetha nazo izikolo, sifuna ukuncedisana nazo ngale nto yamabala wombhoxo. 
Sifuna ukubuyisela umbhoxo ukuze ube ngumdlalo odlalwayo nawo,” uvale ngaloo mazwi uMathwasa.
UHollywoodbets utyale izigidi zerandi kwiNational Women’s League! 
UNksz. Sandisiwe Bhengu weHollywoodbets, uGqirha Danny Jordaan weSafa no-Ian Plaatjies weSABC entlanganisweni ebiseGoli ekuqaleni kweveki. 
Ibhola ekhatywayo yamantombazana ayisoze ifane neyeminyaka edlulileyo. 
Ekuqaleni kwale veki, iSouth African Football Association (Safa), ibhengeze iHollywoodbets njengomxhasi omtsha weSafa National Women’s League. 
AbakwaHollywoodbets batyale imali engaphaya kwezigidi esithathu zerandi (R3-million) eziza kuphucula ibhola ekhatywayo yamantombazana eMzantsi Afrika. 
Sekulithuba elide amanenekazi eyidlala ibhola eMzantsi Afrika ngaphandle yenkxaso yamaqumrhu azimeleyo – kodwa izinto ziguqukile ngoku.
Kwiminyaka edlulileyo, aBanyana Banyana benze inkqubela emangalisayo nebonakele ngokuphulela indebe yeCOSAFA bephindaphinda nokuya kwiNdebe yeHlabathi okokuqala ngo-2019. 
Ezo zinto zanyanzele iSafa ukuba isungule iNational Women’s League eza kwaziwa ngokuba yiHollywoodbets Super League ukusukela ngoku ukuya phambili. 
Iintshatsheli zalo unyaka ziza kuzuza indebe ehamba nezigidi ezibini zonke zerandi (R2-million) okokuqala. 
Lona iqela elibambe indawo yesibini liza kufumana isigidi serandi (R1-million).
Imali engaka iza kuqinisa ukhuphiswano iphucule nobomi babadlali ngoba baza kufumana ubugcwabalalana bemali ethe chatha kunangaphambili. 
“Utyalomali luza kuqinisa amaqela luncedise kakhulu nakuphuhliso lomdlalo wamanenekazi. 
Kuyasivuyisa kakhulu ukubambisana noHollywoodbets,” utshilo uMongameli weSafa, uGqirha Danny Jordaan kwindibano ebiseGoli. 
Umanejala wezorhwebo kwaHollywoodbets, uNksz. Sandisiwe Bhengu, uthethe wenjenje:
“Apha eMzantsi Afrika sinetalente eleleyo. Sinethemba lokubona ukusebenzisana kwethu neSafa kuza kuyiphucula ibhola ekhatywayo yamantombazana. 
Uphuhliso lwemidlalo yinto ebalulekileyo kuthi kwaHollywoodbets.” 
Ukusasazwa ngqo kwemidlalo yeNational Women’s League lijelo losasazo loluntu, iSABC, kubenalo igalelo ekutsaleni umdla weenkampani ezifana noHollywoodbets. 
“Sibulela iSABC ngokuphakamisa imidlalo yeWomen’s League eyakuqina xa ibukelwa ngabantu abaninzi,” utshilo uMnu. Tebogo Motlanthe, ingqonyela yeSafa.
Ilizwe lothuswe kukubhubha kukaThulani Thuswa obesisithethi seMamelodi Sundowns.
Andisenguye umqeqeshi weChippa United, utsho uVladislav Heric.
UHeric Vladislav, obengumqeqeshi weChippa United, ugxothiwe emva kokubethwa kwayo yiBloemfontein Celtic emdlalweni weDStv Premiership izolo. 
Iqela lebhola ekhatywayo laseMpuma Koloni elidlala kwiPSL, iChippa United, likhangela umqeqeshi omtsha emva kokuba likhombe emnyango uVladislav Heric. 
Ukugxothwa kukaHeric kulandela emva kokuba iChippa United ibethwe yiBloemfontein Celtic ngamagowuli amabini kwelinye (2-1) emdlalweni weDStv 
Premiership obubanjelwe eSisa Dukashe Stadium izolo ngorhatya. 
“Yinyaniso leyo, andisenguye umqeqeshi weChippa United,” utshilo uHeric, ethetha neli phephandaba. 
Le ndedeba yaseSerbia kwinyanga iqeshwe kwinyanga nguMnu. 
Siviwe Mpengesi emva kokuba engazange akwazi ukuqesha uLuc Aymael – owayetyholwa ngobuhlanga ngethuba esengumqeqeshi eTanzania.
Phantsi kukaVladislav Heric – iChippa United iqhothozile kwicala lokuqokelela amanqaku ngokubetha amaqela afana neKaizer Chiefs 
neStellenbosch – kodwa bekungonelanga. 
Umqeqeshi ugxothwa iChippa ishiyekelwe yimidlalo emibini kuphela nasemva kokubethwa yiTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila kwiNedbank Cup. 
Ihleli kwindawo yeshumi elinesihlanu entla kweBlack Leopards esemsileni. 
Ukuba ayikwazanga ukuliphepha izembe, iChippa iza kufumana ithuba lokulwela indawo kwiDStv Premiership ngokudlala namaqela adlala kwiGladAfrica Championship. 
Igama likaLehlohonolo Seema.
IPirates izenzele umsebenzi onzima kwiCAF Confederation Cup - 
UVincent Pule we-Orlando Pirates noMarouane Hadhoudi weRaja Casablanca emdlalweni weCAF Confederation Cup obubanjelwe e-Orlando Pirates.
Xa kudlalwa umlenze wesibini weCAF Confederation Cup, yona i-Orlando Pirates iza kufana neqalelayo ngoba ayikwazanga ukukhusela igowuli kowayo. 
Konke oku kwenzeke emva kokuba iPirates ibambene ngegowuli elinye macala (1-1) neRaja Casablanca emdlalweni obubanjelwe e-Orlando Stadium emalanga namhlanje. 
Ukufumana kwayo igowuli iCasablanca emdlalweni oseMzantsi Afrika kuyinike amandla ngoba uxinizelelo lakuba kwiPirates xa kusiyiwa emdlalweni olandelayo eMorocco kwiveki ezayo. 
Umdlalo iwuqale kakuhle kakhulu iBucs ngoba yiyo ebihlasela. Unozinti weCasablanca, uAnas Zniti, wenze umsebenzi oncomekayo kwangoko emdlalweni ngethuba evala ibhola ebikhatywe nguWayde Jooste.
Emva koko, uDeon Hotto uzame ukukhaba ekude – kodwa ibhola yakhe iphume ecaleni. 
Itsazise igazi kuqala iBucs ngegowuli elifakwe nguVincent Pule – ofumene ibhola elungisiweyo nguDeon Hotto. 
Emva kokuya kwixesha lokuphumla ihamba phambili, bekulindeleke iPirates ivale emva okanye yongeze elinye igowuli. 
Ayikwazanga ukwenza nanye kwezo zimbini izinto. 
UBen Malango woyise amadoda amabini ebhokisini wafaka igowulu kwangoko kwisigaba sesibini. 
Imcaphukisile kakhulu lo nto uJosef Zinnbauer – ovezwe ethivini elahla phantsi izipeksi zakhe ebezisesandleni. 
Umdlalo weRaja uye wafunquka emva koko, kufanele ngoba ifumene eyona nto ebiyizela futhi isazi kakuhle ukuba iza kulwela ukungabethwa eMorocco.
Ukungena kwabadlali abafana noThembinkosi Lorch, uThabang Monare noPaseka Mako akwenzanga mahluko ngoba iPirates ayikwazanga ukugqobhoza emva kwiRaja Casablanca. 
Kubekho ithemba xeshikweni uDeon Hotto efumana ithuba endaweni entle sekuza kuphela umdlalo. 
Akakwazanga ukukhabela unozinti ngoba ebegadiwe kwabe kungekho mdlali okufutshane kuye obenomnikela ibhola. Kube njalo nakuMako ozamileyo 
ukukhabela ezipalini – ngelishwa lakhe, uZniti ebethe qwa. 
Kunyanzelekile iPirates iphumelele kwiveki ezayo xa idibana neCasablanca emdlalweni wesibini ukuze ikwazi ukuya phambili kwiCAF Confederation Cup.
Pirates: Sandilands, Nyauza, Hlatshwayo, Jooste, Sam, Motshwari, Ndlovu, Pule, Hotto, Mabaso, Makaringe.
Amalalela: Ofori, Monare, Zungu, Mntambo, Lorch, Dlamini, Mako, Maela, Mhango.
Raja Casablanca: Zniti, Madkou, Jbira, Haddad, Hadhoudi, Arjoune, El Wari, Ngoma, Benhalib, Rahimi, Rahimi, Malango.
Amalalela: Bouamir, Boutayeb, Soukhane, Achchakir, Zrida, Makahasi, Nanah, Noah, Habti.

Le ngcingane imemelela ukuba makubekho inguqu egqibeleleyo ekulungisweni kwentlalo apho ulawulo lwamadoda kwinto yonke kufuneka lushenxisiwe. 
Kaloku le ngcingane ayohlukani nengcingane yesikhomokazi kuba ingunozala wale ngcingane. 
Le nyanga ikwayinyanga yokuqhayisa ngesinxibo sethu sesintu, ukutya kwethu kwanomculo wethu.
KWIINTSUKU ezintathu uThambi Manganya sele ehambe ngeenyawo zakhe umgama weekhilomitha ezilikhulu elinamashumi amabini ananye (121km).
Lo mgama wezi khilomitha (121km) ukumlinganiselo wokusuka eBika eGcuwa usiya eMonti okanye ukusuka kuCofimvaba ukuya eDutywa.
UThami Manganya ukuhambo lwe-800km ukusuka eRhawutini ukuya eDutywa.
UManganya (26), wakuGamgam eDutywa, ukuhambo lweentsuku ezingamashumi amabini kwiikhilomitha ezingamakhulu asibhozo (800km) ukusuka eRhawutini ukuya eDutywa ngeenjongo zokonyusa ingxowamali yokunceda izikolo kwakunye nezemidlalo kwiilali zaseMpuma Koloni.
UManganya, ophumelele isidanga sakhe kwizifundo zobudlelwane kwezehlabathi kwakunye nezeendaba (International Relations and Media Studies) eWits kunyaka ophelileyo, uthi ujolise ekurhwebesheni imali ekwiR1.28 million ukunceda abafundi basemaphandleni kweli phondo.
Ngosuku uzimisele ukuhamba umgama weekhilomitha ezingamashumi amane anesibini (42km), umgama okumlinganiselo wokusuka eColosa (eDutywa) ukuya edolophini eGcuwa.

NgokweCandelo 16 lalo mthetho (Section 16), ubani angajongana notshutshiso xa eveza esidlangalaleni umfanekiso webele lomntu obhinqileyo, welomntu oguquke ngokwesini (transgender) kwanelomntu ozelwe nezini ezinxaxhileyo (intersex).
Eli Candelo 16 lalo mthetho likwathi “nokuba akaziwa okanye uyaziwa (ngegama) lo mntu ovezwe kumboniso/kumfanekiso”, lowo usasaze lo mfanekiso/mboniso angajongana notshutshiso.
Kwakhona eli Candelo 16 lithi ubani angajongana notshutshiso xa enobonwa enomfanekiso okanye umboniso wamalungu angasese (nude) womnye umntu ngaphandle kwemvume yakhe.
ICandelo 14 lalo mthetho lithi ubani angajongana notshutshiso enokuhambisa umyalezo onelizwi okanye umboniso obeka emngciphekweni omnye umntu okanye abanye abantu angagwetywa iminyaka enokufikelela kwemithathu okanye umdliwo 
(okanye zombini – umdliwo nesigwebo) xa efunyenwe enetyala yinkundla yomthetho.
Lo mthetho ngokweCandelo 11 udiza ukuba ubani angagwetywa iminyaka enokufikelela kwishumi elinesihlanu okanye umdliwo (okanye zombini – umdliwo nesigwebo) xa enokufunyaniswa enetyala lokuba nePassword (iinkcukacha zokuvula) okanye ikhowudi yokuvula ifowuni okanye ikhompyutha yomntu ngaphandle kwemvume yalo mntu.
Ubani xa enomfanekiso okanye umboniso wakhe (webele, welungu langasese) awubone ukomnye umntu okanye abantu ngaphandle kwemvume yakhe, angabika oko kumagosa ezomthetho.

Oku kuthethwe nguMercy Cwayi oyiNtloko kwi-On Eagles Wings Multi-Purpose Centre yaseJeffreys Bay kulandela iimfundiso azifunde kwingxoxo 
ebiququzelelwe yiPOWA (People Opposing Women Abuse) ngokusebenzisana nenkampani eyenza iti iJoko.
Le ngxoxo ijolise ekufundiseni amaxhoba odushe olujoliswe kwisini ukuba ohlukane nokuthula cwaka ngoxhatshazo lwawo.
Kwingxoxo evangwe ngeti ebibanjelwe kwityalike iPCG eJeffreys Bay, amalungu oluntu kula mmandla aye afumana ithuba lokufunda ngeengxaki zoxhatshazo ajongene nazo bekwaphendla neendlela zokuqubisana noko.
UMercy Cwayi, iNtloko kwi-On Eagles Wings Multi-Purpose Centre kwanoKate Mocheki, iNtloko yeeProjekthi kwiPOWA.
UCwayi uthi kwezi ngxoxo ufunde ukuba amakhosikazi kufuneka ahlale eneenombolo zikaxakeka zokuwanceda ngomhla wengxaki.
“[Sikwafunde] ukuba amakhosikazi makabenebhegi kaxakeka eneempahla nezinto zokuhlamba nokuthambisa ehlala icwalile, ukuze imeko yoxhatshazo bayishiye ngokukhawuleza. 
Sikwafundiswe ukuba masixelele uluntu ukuba amaxhoba odushe olujoliswe kwisini makakholelwe futhi nokuba amadoda ahlonitshiweyo ngokwezemfundo kwanokuphumelela kwawo ngokwempangelo angangabo abaphembeleli bodushe olujoliswe kwisini,” utshilo uCwayi.
Kusenjalo, kwakwezi ngxoxo ezivangwe ngeti, eMthatha kuye kwabanjwa iingxoxo malunga nombandela wokuthwalwa kwamantombazana ngaphandle kwemvuwe yawo.
Ngokusebenzisana nePOWA neMthatha Women’s Support Centre bathe babamba ezi ngxoxo, bekwagxile kumbandela wokuthwala.
Amakhosikazi aseMthatha exoxa ngemiba edla wona.
INtloko yeMthatha Women’s Support Centre, uKoliwe Nongauza, uthe: 
“Ngamanye amaxesha abazali [bavuma ukuba kuthwalwe abantwana babo] ngenxa yendlala kuba bebona ukuba abanakumelana nendlela eyiyo yokukhulisa umntwana wabo oyintombazana.”
“Kumaxesha amaninzi, le ndoda ixhwile le ntombazana okanye lo mfazi iye imkhulelise ngokukhawuleza, ukuze athibazeke ukubuyela ekhayeni,” 
Utshilo uNongauza, ekwathi basebenzisana namapolisa ukuqubisana nalo mbandela.
UKate Mocheki, iNtloko yeeProjekthi kwiPOWA, uthi eyona njongo iphambili yabo kukuqinisa amazwi adlamkileyo kuluntu ukuze kuphele ukuthula cwaka kwimiba yodushe olujoliswe kwisini.

“[Iikota ezintathu kwezo zine] 75% yohambo ndilugqibile. Siza kuba seDutywa ngomhla weshumi elinesibhozo”.
UManganya, wakuGamgam eDutywa, ukuhambo lweentsuku ezingamashumi amabini kwiikhilomitha ezingamakhulu asibhozo (800km) ukusuka eRhawutini ukuya eDutywa ngeenjongo zokonyusa ingxowamali yokunceda izikolo kwakunye nezemidlalo kwiilali zaseMpuma Koloni.
Eli qhawe, neliphumelele isidanga salo kwizifundo zobudlelwane kwezehlabathi kwakunye nezeendaba (International Relations and Media Studies) eWits kunyaka ophelileyo, lijolise ekurhwebesheni imali ekwi-R1.28 million ukunceda abafundi basemaphandleni kweli phondo.
Iinjongo zakhe kolu hambo, ngokwezemfundo, kukunyusa ingxowamali yokuthenga iikhompyutha ezingamashumi amahlanu kwizikolo ezilishumi zaseMpuma Koloni ukuze abafundi basemaphandleni babenolwazi kwezobuchwepheshe. 
Ukwajolise ekuthengeni iikhalityuleyitha ezingama-500, oobhaka abangama-500, iipere zezihlangu ezingama-250, iiphedzi (sanitary pads) kumantombazana aliwaka (1 000), iDatha kwanemali yokufaka isicelo seyunivesithi kubafundi bakaGrade 12 abangama-500.
Ngokwezemidlalo, uManganya ufuna ukurhwebesha iR200 000 yokuncedisa kwizixhobo zebhola ekhatywayo, umnyazi, iqakamba, umbhoxo namanqindi ukunciphisa ukusetyenziswa gwenxa kweziyobisi.
“Ukuqukwa kwezixhobo zokulolongela amanqindi (boxing gym), asiyonto yezemidlalo nje, kodwa yindlela (yokufundisa) ukuzikhusela. 
Amakhosikazi nabantwana, ngabona bantu bangamaxhoba odushe olujoliswe kwisini noxhatshazo. 
Ngokwale ndawo yokuzilolongela amanqindi, baza kuqeqeshelwa ukuzikhusela xa ubomi babo buphantsi kwesigrogriso,” utshilo uManganya kwimbalelwano.
Ebalisela I’solezwe lesiXhosa uManganya uthi emva kokujonga imeko abajongene nayo abafundi basezilalini, uhleli phantsi wacinga icebo. 
“Ndibone ukuba yintoni endingathi ndiyenze ukwenza umahluko, ndagqiba ngokuthabatha olu hambo,” utshilo uManganya.
Kodwa uManganya uthi uyayicela nangakumbi inkxaso ngokwezimali kolu hambo.

Njengabaqulunqi bebali nabUkuvela kwengxaki yempilo engekhonye ngaxeshanye kumntu omnye.

Intengiselwano okanye umsebenzi owenziwa ngaphandle kokuhlangana kwabantu
Isenzo okanye umgaqo-nkqubo wokunciphisa ukwanda okanye ukunwenwa kwentlekele yendalo, isifo esosulelayo, okanye enye into eyingozi
Into eshiyekele kwimiphezulu yeendawo (efana neendonga, imigangatho). Kungenzeka ukuba ihleli nje ngokungancamathelanga, njengothuli nje oluqhelekileyo, okanye kunokwenzeka ukuba incamathele ngenxa yokuhlangana neekhemikhali.
Iqela leentsholongwane elibangela isigulo esisukela kumkhuhlane nje oqhelekileyo ukuya kutsho kwizifo ezimandundu kakhulu, ezifana neMiddle 
East Respiratory Syndrome (i-MERS-CoV) kunye neSevere Acute Respiratory Syndrome (i-SARS-CoV). 
Intsholongwane i-novel coronavirus ekungekudala ifunyanisiwe inikwe igama lokuba yi-SARS-CoV-2 kwaye ibangela iCOVID-19.
Igama lesifo esibangelwa yintsholongwane i-novel coronavirus, iSARS-CoV-2, nesisishunqulelo se-“Coronavirus Disease 2019.”
Uvavanyo lokufumanisa isifo yiyo nayiphi na indlela esetyenziswa ukuqokelela ulwazi lwezonyango ngenjongo yokwenza isigqibo sezonyango (ukutsho oko, ukuqinisekiswa kobukho besifo).
Indlela yodluliselo yesifo esosulelayo nebandakanya amathontsana amakhulwana anxulumene nokuphefumla, ahamba umgama omfutshane (ngaphantsi kwe-6 feet) naveliswa xa uthimla, ukhohlela, okanye uthetha.
Ukwenyuka, amaxa amaninzi ngequbuliso, kwenani labantu abosuleleke sisifo ngaphezulu koko kulindelekileyo ngokwesiqhelo kuluntu olukulo ndawo.
Isalathiso esibonisa isifo, esaziwa ngokuba yi-epidemic curve, yitshathi yeenkcukacha-manani esetyenziswa kwinzululwazi ngezifo ukubona ixesha lokuqala kokuqhamka kwesifo.
Uphando malunga nendlela izifo ezenzeka nezinwena ngayo kwiindawo zabantu zokuhlala.
Isebe lezonyango elifunda ngendlela ezenzeka ngayo izifo nezinwena ngayo kwiindawo zabantu zokuhlala.
