Igalelo letolofiya eNgqushwa Igalelo letolofiya eNgqushwa
Itolofiya sisiqhamo esityalwa ngamafama aqikelelwa kumakhulu alithoba eMzantsi Afrika, kodwa uNozukisile Yali noAsive Yali bayikha kumahlathi aseNgqushwa bayithengise.
La makhosikazi athi enza imali ethi incedise iintsapho zawo ngokuthengisa itolofiya, kwaye enza oku elandela ekhondweni labazali babo.
“Kudala yathengiswa itolofiya izihlelele endle. 
Abazali bethu babesenza ngolu hlobo senza ngalo, bezivunela endle baze kuyithengisa apha ecaleni kohola wendlela uN2,” kucacisa uNozukisile.
Umyinge webhakethi elibunzima buziilitha ezintlanu bawuthengisa ngeshumi leeponti kwabo bagqitha ngale ndlela.
”Xa imini iqhube kakuhle senza imali ekwikhulu leerandi nangaphezulu, bakho ke nabo bathenga amagaqa, lona silibiza iiponti ezimbini,” kutsho uNozukusile.
Rhoqo kuqala unyaka, iindlela eziphambili zeMpuma Koloni eziquka uN2 noN6 zihonjiswa ngamakhosikazi athengisa esi siqhamo sinqabileyo.
“Sivuka ngentseni siye kuvuna emahlathini, sibuye nemithwalo, siyosule size kuyibeka apha, eli xesha enyakeni iyatyeka noko,” utsho uNozukisile.
Ingeniso yeTolofiya icacile kumakhaya wala makhosikazi aseNgqushwa, kwaye iguqula ubomi.
“Kuba izikolo zivulwe kade, sikwazile ukuthenga izinto zokunxiba zesikolo, ngoku siqokelela imali yeejezi zasebusika zabantwana besikolo. 
Khumbula asithengi ukuze sithengise, sikha ehlathini,” kucacisa uAsive Yali.
Uthi ngenxa yengeniso abayenza apha bayakwazi ukuthenga ukutya emakhayeni rhoqo xa bebuya kuthengisa.
“Into efunekayo kukukhuthala nokuzinikela kuwe qha, itolofiya ikhona ehlathini ikulindile, asikho ke isizathu sokuba kulanjwe, ingakumbi ngeli xesha isekhoyo ehlathini,” utsho uAsive.
Bathi nangona izihlelele endle le tolofiya, zikho iingxaki abathi badibane nazo xa bezingela imithi yayo.
“Amanye amafama anomona kaloku, la mahlathi asezifameni zawo, ngoku sikhe sigxothwe okanye sileqwe kusithwa sinyathela ingca necingo,” utsho uAsive.
Batyhola urhulumente ngokungaliqapheli olu hlobo lwabo loshishino nangona linegalelo elihle ekuhlaleni.
“Sicela izixhobo zokuvuna le tolofiya kurhulumente. 
Izixhobo zokuthutha, izixhobo zokuzikhusela, siyahlatywa ngamanye amaxesha xa sivuna,” kucacisa uAsive.
Amafama asakhulayo kweli anolwazi oluncinci kakhulu ngokutyala itolofiya logama linyukayo inani leemveliso zayo kwihlabathi.
Umthi wetolofiya uthanda ukuzimela enzulwini yehlathi phakathi kwemithi enameva. 
Igaqa layo likhula kwibhlayi elibambelele kwisikhondo somthi wetolofiya.
Iivenkile ezifana noWoolworths, Pick ’n Pay noCheckers ziyayithengisa itolofiya.
Imveliso yayo iyayenza ibhiya, iwayini kwakunye nezinto zokuthambisa ulusu kumahomba.
Xa iqhuba kakuhle itolofiya ithengisa amashumi asixhenxe amawaka eerandi (R70 000) itoni kweli loMzantsi Afrika. 
Ingxelo ekhutshwe ngabakwaAgricultural Research Council (ARC) ithi amafama weli avukelwa ngumdla kwitolofiya. 
Oku kungenxa yenguqu eyenzeka kwimozulu kwihlabathi nembalela. 
Ingcali eyenze olu phando uHermanus Fouche uthi amafama atshintsha iimveliso zawo ngenxa yembalela, avelisa itolofiya.
“ENtshona Koloni kukho umfama obekade evelisa idriwa, ngoku ngenxa yokubethwa kukuguquka kwemozulu nembalela, uthathe isigqibo sokutyala itolofiya, kulula ukuyikhulisa, kodwa ithatha ixesha,” kutsho uFouche.
Le ngxelo yeARC ithi zikumakhulu alithoba iifama ezivelisa itolofiya kuMzantsi Afrika, kumyinge womhlaba oziihektare ezingamawaka amane namakhulu amahlanu. 
Xa kuvunwa amafama adinga abasebenzi abakumawaka asixhenxe namakhulu amahlanu ukuze kuvunwe ngempumelelo.
Iindawo ezahlukeneyo zoMzantsi Afrika zivuna ngamaxesha ahlukeneyo, iMpuma Koloni ivuna itolofiya kwiinyanga zokuqala zonyaka, logama iindawo ezikumantla elizwe zivuna kwiinyanga zokuphela konyaka. 
Ihektare enye yetolofiya ivelisa iitoni ezingamashumi amabini ukuya kumashumi amathathu. 
Ngolwazi oluthe vetshe amafama angakhangela ulwazi kwiSouth African Cactus Pear Growers Association (SACPGA).
ULangaliyakhanya Mboniswa waseMagemfaneni eCacadu, uyayonwabela ingxolo engafunwayo ngabaninzi eyenziwa ngamaKwalikwini kwifama yakhe. 
Lo mfama uzibalule ngokufuya ezi ntaka sele zinqabile ukufuywa ngabantu abaninzi bekhala ngezizathu ezahlukeneyo.
“Iinkunzi zilishumi elinesihlanu, iimazi zingamashumi amane anesihlanu, amantshontsho aneenyanga ezintathu ngamashumi amathathu anesixhenxe logama aneenyanga ezimbini ilishumi elinesihlanu,” ngoncumo kucacisa uMboniswa.
Ikhaya lakwaMboniswa likwenye yeengxingwa zeefama ezindala kwiilali zaseMtsheko ezazisebenza kwakwiminyaka yoo1890 zivelisa zikwathengisa imifuno, umbona neziqhamo.
“AmaKwalikwini sikhulele kuwo apha ekhaya, abazali babe wafuyile, nathi ke salandela ekhondweni ngenxa yokuwathanda,” utsho uMboniswa. 
Ngenxa yemvula, amaqanda abolile kwaye ebefukamile ngelo xesha amaKwalikwini akhe.
“Ngamaqanda aphaya kumashumi alithoba anesithandathu athe aboliswa yimvula enetha ingayeki apha. 
Ayasuka efukwini lawo kukho amanzi okanye enye into engeneleleyo, ndilahlekelwe,” kucacisa uMboniswa.
Ngokukhula komsebenzi wakhe wokuvelisa amaKwalikwini, uMboniswa uneenjongo ezibanzi.
“Ndijonge ukuthengisela iivenkile ezinkulu zokutya, ndithengisele abantu. 
Ndingavuya ukuba ndingafumana ithuba lokuwathumela kumazwe angaphandle,” utsho.
Uthi akanqweneli ukuba ngumfama okhulayo ixesha elide, koko unqwenela ukugqitha kwelinye inqanaba abe ngumfama ophume izandla.
”Ayathanda kakhulu ukutya uhlaza, lo nto yenza ukuba avelise amaqanda aphilileyo. 
Ayathengiswa ke nangaliphi ixesha enyakeni xa umntu efuna amaKwalikwini,” kutsho uMboniswa.

Isenzo sokuzibekela bucala kwabanye abantu okanye uzikhwarantine ngokwakho. Nakuba kunjalo, ukubekelwa bucala (ukuphepha ukuhlangana nabanye abantu xa umntu egula) nokukhwarantinwa. 
Ukuphepha ukuhlangana nabanye abantu emva kokuba kungenzeka ukuba mhlawumbi ubukhe wadibana nomntu owosulelekileyo, kodwa ube ungaguli, azithethi into efanayo.

Ukubonisa iimpawu zesifo.
Nabuphi na ubungqina besifo obukhoyo.
Imisebenzi ebhalwayo edyunivesithi isethwa ukuze ibe nemiyalelo ethe ngqo kunye nebanzi.
Ukuyiqonda le miyalelo linqanaba lokuqala kwinkqubo yokubhala.
Ngokuqhelekileyo imiyalelo iquka imiba efana nomxholo okanye isihloko, ekumele kugqaliselwe kuko kunye nezinto eziyimida, zikhankanywe zonke kwingxelo yemiyalelo.
Le vidiyo inikeza ngolwazi lokuhlalutya lo ngxelo ukuze ukwazi ukucwangcisa ukubhala kwakho ngokukuko.
Inqanaba lokuqala kukukhangela amagama abalulekileyo kwingxelo yemiyalelo.
Okokuqala, khangela amagama okwenza akuxelela okumele ukwenze, njengezenzi.
Nanku umzekelo: Xoxa uze uthelekise amagama athi unxibelelwano phakathi komntu nomnye (interpersonal) kunye nonxibelelwano lomntu naye yena siqu (intrapersonal).
Amagama okwenza afana nokuthi chaza kunye nokuthi thelekisa. 
Ngoko ke kufuneka unikeze ulwazi malunga nezi ntlobo zimbini zonxibelelwano UZE ubonise izinto ezifana ngazo kwanezo zahluke ngazo.
Qaphela ukuba kunokwenzeka ukuba ingxelo yemiyalelo ingacaci ngokuphandle, umzekelo, yakha kunye nokuthi phendula umbuzo wophando ofanelekileyo.
Oku kukushiya ukwazi ukukhetha okuthile okumele ugqalisele kuko kumsebenzi wakho wokubhala. 
Kule meko, unokuba nalo ufifi ngomxholo obanzi wokubhala kwakho, umzekelo unxibelelwano,kodwa kuyacetyiswa ukuba ubonisane nomhlohli wakho okanye lowo wongamele umsebenzi wakho ukufumanisa ukuba yintoni kanye oza kubhala ngayo.
Okwesibini, khangela amagama esihloko okanye umxholo, ngokuqhelekileyo izibizo.
Amagama omxholo ngala athi unxibelelwano lomntu nomnye kunye naye yena buqu. 
La magama omxholo abonisa isihloko, umzekelo, njengecandelwana lomxholo omkhulu ofana nonxibelelwano, kwaye ngamagama angundoqo oza kuwasebenzisa xa ukhangela ulwazi kwixesha elizayo.
Ngamanye amaxesha kunokungabi lula ukwazi ukuba ugqaliso lomsebenzi wakho kufuneka lube mxinwa okanye lube banzi kangakanani na. 
Ukuba ngaba kunjalo, nceda ubonisane nomhlohli wakho okanye lowo wongamele umsebenzi wakho.
Wakuba ugqibile ngoko ekumele ugqalisele kuko, unokuqhubeka nokuqulunqa ingxelo yethisisi yakho. 
Esi sisivakalisi esinye esichaza owona myalezo ungundoqo womsebenzi wakho wokubhala.
Okwesithathu, kufuneka kananjalo uthathele ingqalelo izinto eziyimida okanye isikowuphi somsebenzi wokubhala. 
Ezi zinto ziya kwehluka kwiimeko ezahlukeneyo.
Izinto eziyimida zinokuquka ubude bombhalo, amaxesha amaninzi buchazwa kumlinganiselo wenani lamagama.
Ugqaliso lomsebenzi nalo lunokuba nemida olunayo, umzekelo, ukuqwalasela banzi isihloko ngokwemeko yaseMzantsi Afrika, okanye ukubhala malunga nesini esithile, okanye ukuphanda ngethuba lexesha elithile, umzekelo 2000 – 2010.
Ukuthathela ingqalelo ezi zinto ziyimida kuya kwenza ukuba ukwazi ukuqonda ngcono ngombhalo oza kuwuvelisa.
Kananjalo ukuzazi izinto eziyimida kubalulekile xa ukhangela ulwazi.
Eminye imisebenzi yokubhala iya kuhamba nommiselo wokumakisha okanye irubrikhi.
Irubrikhi sisixhobo esibalulekileyo xa uhlalutya umsebenzi nanjengoko ikunika umfanekiso obanzi woko kulindelekileyo kuwe kwaye ibonisa ukuba aza kunikwa njani amanqaku.
Unokuyisebenzisa ukuchonga izinto eziyimfuneko ezibalulekileyo kumbhalo wakho.
Xa ingekho irubrikhi, qwalasela ulwazi olukhoyo ukufumana izikhokelo okanye izinto ezifunekayo kumsebenzi.
Ukuba ngaba ungumfundi osele enaso isidanga sokuqala, uyacetyiswa ukuba uyithathele ingqalelo irubrikhi esetyenziswa liziko lakho. 
Kuyakuba luncedo kuwo nawuphi na umsebenzi wokubhala ukuwuhlalutya ngokugqibeleleyo umsebenzi.
Nokuba ngaba uchonga amagama abalulekileyo kwingxelo yemiyalelo, okanye uqulunqa ngokwakho eyakho ingxelo yethisisi, thathela ingqalelo oko kumele ugqalisele kuko, izinto eziyimida kunye nezinto ezifunekayo kumsebenzi.
Ukubhala kwezemfundo kufuneka kucwangciswe ngononophelo. Umbhalo wezemfundo oza kuwuvelisa ungumboniso wothungelwano olubanzi lwezinto eziyinyani, iingxoxo, izigqibo kunye neziphetho, zonke zihlanganisiwe ukuphendula umbuzo othile wophando.
Nangona nje kungekho ndlela inye “eyeyona” yokucwangcisa ukubhala kwakho, le vidiyo ikunika iingcebiso ezimbalwa malunga nendlela yokuqalisa le nkqubo.
Wakuba ukugqibile ukuhlalutya umsebenzi, kubalulekile ukuba uvuse kwaye ucwangcise iingcinga zakho ngaphambi kokuba uqalise ukukhangela ulwazi.
Imephu yokucinga kwengqondo, kunye nemibuzo inokuba luncedo kwesi sigaba sokuqala socwangciso.
Imephu yokucinga kwengqondo yindlela engumfanekiso yokubonisa iingcinga zakho.
Le ndlela isebenza ngokukuko ekuboniseni ubudlelwane phakathi kwezihloko ezingaphantsi kwezinye,kwaye inika umfanekiso omkhulu ngomsebenzi.
Ukuzoba imephu yokucinga kwengqondo, thatha iphepha elibhalwanga nto, uze embindini wephepha elo ubhale/uzobe umbono ofuna ukuwuphuhlisa.
Emva koko bhala izihlokwana ezinxulumeneyo zijikeleze isihloko esi sikhulu uze uzidibanise ngemigca.
Qhubeka nokongeza izihlokwana ezikumanqanaba angezantsi njengoko ubona kufanelekile ukukunceda ekwenzeni isakhiwo seengcinga zakho.
Ukubuza imibuzo lelinye iqhinga lokwenza isicwangciso elinokukunceda ukufumanisa oko ukwaziyo nekufuneka ukuba ukufumanise malunga nesihloko esithile.
Ukuba ngaba isihloko somsebenzi simalunga nempembelelo yeepateni zokulala kwindlela oqhuba ngayo kwizifundo, le mibuzo ilandelayo ingakunika isikhokelo esibalulekileyo kwindlela ocwangcisa ngayo:
1. Yintoni iipateni zokulala?
2. Zihlanganiswa njani ngokwamaqela okanye zahlulwa njani iipateni zokulala?
3. Kutheni kukho iipateni zokulala nje?
4. Ingaba lwakhe lwenziwa uphando ngeepateni zokulala kunye nendlela ekuqhutywa ngayo kwizifundo?
Imephu yokucinga kwengqondo kunye nemibuzo yokuqala ingakukhokhelela kukukhangela kwakho ulwazi olufanelekileyo.
Ukufunda imithombo yolwazi lwezemfundo ethembakeleyo kubalulekile.
Njengokuba ufunda nje, qhubeka nokuyilungisa kwanokumane uyitshintsha imephu yokucinga kwengqondo yakho. 
Kunokwenzeka ukuba ushiyelele amacandelo abalulekileyo okanye wafaka ulwazi olungafanelekanga, umzekelo.
Ngokuye ufunda ngakumbi ngesihloko sakho, unokumane uvelelwa yimibuzo kunye neempendulo ezintsha.
Wakuba uyilungisile wayitshintsha-tshintsha imephu yokucinga kwengqondo yakho kunye neempendulo, unokuba nolwazi olwaneleyo ngoku lokwenza ithebhule yeziqulatho yokuqala.
‘Ithebhule yeziqulatho’ sisikhokelo esibhaliweyo umbhalo wakho oza kusekelwa phezu kwaso.
Kubhalo lwezemfundo, icandelo lokuqala lethebhule yeziqulatho maxa onke iba yintshayelelo, lize icandelo lokugqibela ibe, sisiphetho.
Ezinye izihloko kunye nezihlokwana zidwelisa amacandelo awohlukeneyo omxholo. 
Kananjalo esi sikhokelo sikunceda ekubeni ukwazi ukucinga ngonxulumano phakathi kwamacandelo kunye nendlela yolandelelwano ofuna ukuwadwelisa ngayo.
Ithebhule yeziqulatho asiyonto engenakutshintshwa, kwaye ngokuye ufunda ngakumbi futhi uvelelwa zezinye iingcinga ungakwazi ukuyitshintsha.
Ukusetyenziswa kweemephu zokucinga kwengqondo, imibuzo kunye nethebhule yeziqulatho kuya kukunceda ukucwangciseni ngokukuko kwangaphambili, ngalo ndlela ke kuncede ukuthintela ukungawenzi kakuhle umsebenzi.
Kunokwenzeka ukuba usebenzisa u-Google xa ukhangela ulwazi.
IiWebhusayithi ezifana no-Wikipedia, iiblogi kunye namaphephandaba amaxesha amaninzi iba yeyona mithombo yokuqala oyifumanayo.
Nakuba kunjalo, edyunivesithi, kufuneka uqinisekise ukuba ulwazi olusebenzisayo luthembakele. Le vidiyo iza kukubonisa apho kumele ukhangele khona ulwazi olufanelekileyo kuzo zonke iibhokisi.
U-Google unokuthelekiswa nomntu owaziwayo ekuhlaleni – wonke umntu umenyiwe kwitheko. 
Akukhathaliseki nokuba ungubani, xa nje unebali ongalibalisayo, wamkelekile ukuba ungangenelela.
Izinto zinokuba sisiphithi-phithi kancinci... 
Makhe ndisibonise esi sikweko ngokukhangela ku-Google isihloko malunga “nokufudumala elizweni jikelele”.
Uyalibona ukuba liphezulu kangakanani inani leziphumo ezifunyenwe ngu-Google? 
Iziphumo ziquka iinkcazelo ezivela kwiiwebhusayithi ezaziwayo ezifana no-Wikipedia.
U-Wikipedia sisibonelelo solwazi esivulekileyo kwaye nabani na angafaka okanye atshintshe oko kuqulethwe kuye, akanakuthenjwa.
Ngaphambi kokuba usebenzise nawuphi na umthombo owufumana ku-Google, kufuneka ujongisise kakhulu.
Ingaba usemthethweni? Ingaba uthembakele? 
Ingaba ufanelekile?
Oku kuya kuthatha ixesha lakho elininzi.
Ingxaki ngemithombo efunyenwe ku-Google, kukuba inokuba nezinto ezibhalwe zaziinyani kodwa ezingachanekanga.
Kwimeko yezemfundo, endaweni yoko kufuneka ukhangele kwiindawo ezinolwazi lwezemfundo ezifana ne-Google Scholar okanye i-Academic Search Premier.
Ukuba ngaba siqhubeka nesikweko sethu, i-Google Scholar ingathelekiswa nomntu okhetha kakhulu nowenza iindibano ezincinci, nezingenabantu baninzi – kungenwa ngesimemo kuphela. Zonke iindwendwe ziyakhethwa.
Iindawo zokukhangela ulwazi lwezemfundo nazo zenza ngokunjalo. Yonke imithombo eziyifakayo ihloliwe ngabanye abalingane. 
Oku kuthetha ukuba imibhalo okanye iincwadi zivunyiwe liqela leengcali, ukuqinisekisa ukuba ulwazi lusemthethweni, luthembakele kwaye luyakholeleka.
Xa ubhala usithi “ukufudumala elizweni jikelele” ku-Google Scholar, ufumana iziphumo ezimbalwa kunezo uzifumana ku-Google kwaye ulwazi lulungele ukusetyenziswa kwimeko yezemfundo.
Ngoko ke, xa ufuna ukwazi ukuba umboniso bhanyabhanya uqala xesha nini na, sebenzisa u-Google. Kodwa xa ufuna ulwazi oza kulusebenzisa kumbhalo wakho wezemfundo, u-Google akayiyo eyona ndawo ifanelekileyo yokufumana imithombo.
Ukusebenzisa indawo yokukhangela ulwazi lwezemfundo efana no-Google Scholar kokona kufanelekileyo.
Ungaluthemba ulwazi olufumanayo kuba lukhethiwe lwaze lwahluzwa ngendlela eyiyo.
Kutheni uza kuchitha ixesha lakho ku-Google xa indawo yokukhangela ulwazi lwezemfundo yona efana no-Google Scholar ingakwazi ukukuthatha ikuse ngqo kwimithombo ethembakeleyo.
Kwimo yokubhala kwezemfundo, oko ukubhalayo, kunye nokuba ukubhala njani, kubalulekile.
Ukubhala kwezemfundo asiyonto inye, eyimfumba eyenziwe ngokungafaniyo,koko kuyohlukana ngokwendlela eziqhelekileyo ezilandelwayo kwizifundo ezahlukeneyo kunye nangokoko kukhethwa ngumbhali othile ngamnye.
Nakuba kunjalo kukho izinto eziliqela ezamkelekileyo ngokuqhelekileyo njengeempawu zokubhala kwezemfundo.
Ividiyo ijongana ngokufutshane nokuba sesikweni, ukungaqhutywa luluvo kunye nokuchaneka.
Kukubhala kwezemfundo, kufuneka ukhethe iindlela ezisesikweni phakathi kweendidi ezahlukeneyo zolwimi
Umzekelo: xa into ivakala, kungcono ukubhala ukuba yamkelekile,
Ize ithi into xa ixhomisa amehlo, endaweni yoko ubhale ukuba ngumba obalulekileyo.
Kuya kufuneka ukuba ukuphephe ukusebenzisa izifinyezo koko amagama uwabhale ngokupheleleyo.
Kulumkele ukusebenzisa izimelabizo zomntu wokuqala kunye nezomntu wesibini rhoqo.
Oku kuya kukunceda ukuba ukwazi ukusoloko usebenzisa ithoni engaqhutywa luluvo kunye nengabhekisi mntwini umzekelo ukuthi Ngokwamkelekileyo akuqhutywa luluvo kunokuthi Mandivume.
Kubhalo lwezemfumdo, zamkelekile izifinyezo okanye izishunqulelo kodwa kufuneka uzisebenzise ngendlela echanekileyo.
Ukuba ngaba usebenzisa igama lenkampani okanye amagama ezobugcisa ngokuthe gqolo, ungasisebenzisa isifinyezo okanye isishunqulelo.
Kufuneka ulibhale igama ngokupheleleyo xa ulisebenzisa okokuqala, uze unikeze isifinyezo okanye isishunqulelo ngqo emva kwalo.
Ukusuka kwisihlandlo sesibini ukuya phambili, sebenzisa kuphela isifinyezo okanye isishunqulelo.
Xa ufuna ukubhala inani, bhala ngamagama ukusuka kwisinye ukuya kwishumi. Emva koko, sebenzisa amanani.
Xa uqala isivakalisi ngenani, kufuneka ulibhale ngokupheleleyo ngamagama.
Kananjalo xa ubhala inani elikhulu, shiya isithuba rhoqo phakathi kwegijithi yesithathu ukusuka ngasekunene. 
Oku kwenza kubelula ukulifunda.
Kananjalo kufuneka uqinisekise ukuba lonke igama olibhalayo ulipela ngokuchanekileyo.
Sebenzisa isincedisi sokujonga upelo esifumaneka kwi-word processor yakho. 
Kulula ukusisebenzisa kwaye side sibonise naxa izithuba phakathi kwamagama kunye neziphumlisi zingasetyenziswanga ngokuchanekileyo.
Ngokucofa kwimpazamo nganye, ungakwazi ukukhetha okunye okuchanekileyo. 
Khumbula ukuba isincedisi sokujonga upelo asingekhe sikwazi ukubona iimpazamo kumagama okwenyani.
Nangona likhona igama elithi igqwirha, lisetyenziswe ngendlela engachanekanga apha. 
Imisebenzi yesincedisi sokujonga upelo inokwenziwa ukuba ilungele iimfuno zakho. 
Sebenzisa uncedo lwe-word processor yakho ukufunda ngakumbi.
Ukubhala kakuhle kwezemfundo kuya kuqinisekisa ukuba uthatha inxaxheba ngempumelelo kwincoko yezemfundo. 
Okukhulu kukuba lowo ufunda umbhalo wakho uyakukwazi ukuziqonda ngokungcono iimbono zakho. Kufuneka uziqhelanise.
Khumbula, zibalulekile iimbono ezivakaliswa ngabanye abakwezemfundo ekuziphuculeni.
Ewe, oko ukubhalayo kubalulekile, kodwa ukuba ukubhala njani nako kubalulekile.
Izincoko zahlulwa zibe yimihlathi kuba umbhalo omnye omde kunganzima kuye nawuphi na umntu ofundayo ukuwulandela.
Oku kwahlulwa kufuneka kube nentsingiselo.
Umhlathi liqela lezivakalisi eziphuhlisa isihloko okanye imbono enye.
Imihlathi kananjalo kufuneka ilandelelane ngendlela evakalayo.
Isihloko somnye umhlathi kufuneka silandele ukusuka kwisihloko somhlathi wokugqibela kwaye kufuneka sikhokelele kwisihloko somhlathi olandelayo.
Imbono engundoqo yomhlathi ngamnye ngokuqhelekileyo ichazwa ngesivakalisi esinye – isivakalisi esingundoqo okanye esisihloko.
Ngokuqhelekileyo esi sivakalisi sifumaneka ekuqaleni komhlathi kwaye siqulatha amagama abalulekileyo angundoqo.
Okunye okulapho kumhlathi kunaba malunga nesivakalisi esisihloko ngoko kubizwa ngokuba zizivakalisi ezixhasayo. Ezi zivakalisi zifanelekileyo zixhasayo ziqulethe ubungqina, 
Imizekelo okanye iinkcukacha ezixhasa isivakalisi esisihloko ukuzama ukuphuhlisa ngokupheleleyo imbono engundoqo yomhlathi.
Umhlathi uphela ngesivakalisi esiqukumbelayo nesishwankathela umhlathi lowo.
Ngoko ke, uyayichaza ngamagama alula, uze ubonise ubunyani bayo, emva koko uqinisekise oko ukubhalileyo ngesishwankathelo esifutshane.
Ukusebenzisa iibhulorho zezivakalisi okanye izixhobo zokudibanisa ngobuchule kwizivakalisi naphakathi kwezivakalisi ezahlukeneyo zomhlathi kunganceda ukwenza ukuhlangana kombhalo wakho.
Ukuhlangana kombhalo kuthetha ukuba umfundi uyakwazi ukukuqonda ngokulula nangokucacileyo oko uzama ukukutsho.
Izixhobo zokuphinda okutshiwoyo kunye namagama azi-sign-post zizixhobo zokudibanisa ezibini kwezininzi onokuzisebenzisa.
Isixhobo sokuphinda okutshiwoyo kuxa kuphindwa ibinzana, kodwa hayi ngamagama afana ngqo.
Kwizivakalisi ezibini ezixhomekeke kwisixhobo sokuphinda okutshiwoyo uyabona ukuba kufana nebhulorho enceda umfundi ukusuka kwesinye isivakalisi ukuya kwesinye.
Amagama azi-sign-post anceda umfundi ukuba akwazi ukulandela. 
Anceda‘ngolandelelwano’ lomhlathi, nanjengoko edibanisa iimbono okanye izivakalisi.
Jonga kumhlathi. Ngokuqaphelekayo wakha ugxininiso.
Kwindawo yokuqala kwaye okwesibini unceda ukuhlela ulwazi ngokwamaqela amabini.
Nangakumbi uxelela umfundi ukuba kukho ulwazi olungaphezulu oluzayo 
Kwaye Ukuphetha luphawu lokuba esi sisiphelo somhlathi.
Imihlathi ebhalwe kakuhle ibalulekile kubhalo lwezemfundo.
Oku kuthetha ukuba kufuneka uthi gqolo nokuluthathela ingqalelo ulwakhiwo lwemihlathi ukunceda lowo ufundayo ukuba akwazi ukuqonda kwaye ngethemba lokuba avumelane nombhalo wakho.
Kule vidiyo sigxininisa kwiinxenye ezimbini ezibalulekileyo zolwakhiwo olukhulu lobhalo lwezemfundo, ukutsho oko intshayelelo kunye nesiphetho
Emva kokuba ukucwangcisile ukubhala kwakho, kufuneka ukuba ube nolwandlalo lombhalo wakho, kwakunye namanqaku angundoqo engxoxo.
Intshayelelo nesiphetho ziinxenye ezincinci zombhalo omkhulu ezinomsebenzi wokuvula iziqulatho ezingundoqo, kwakunye nokuvala ekugqibeleni.
Intshayelelo ibonisa isiqalo esihle ngelixa isiphetho ikukugqiba ngendlela eyomeleleyo.
Intshayelelo kunye nesiphetho sombhalo wakho akufuneki ukuba zibe ngaphezulu kwe-10 ukuya kwi-15% yombhalo wakho uwonke, kwaye la macandelo mabini kufuneka aphantse ukuba bulingana ngokobude.
Xa kuchazwa ngokulula, injongo yentshayelelo kukuchaza ukuba kutheni kubhalwe umbhalo kwanokuba uza kwakhiwa njani,ngelixa isiphetho kufuneka sichaze ngokuphandle ukubaluleka koko kuthe kwafunyaniswa.
Intshayelelo yindawo yokuqala yengxoxo yakho. 
Kufuneka ubonise ukuba uyasiqonda isihloko ngokuba udandalazise iinyaniso zezemfundo.
Indlela eyiyo yokwenza oku kukunikeza isandulela okanye ulwazi olufutshane lwangaphambili, nolukhokhelela ekuchongweni kwengxelo yengxaki,ethi yona ikhokelele kumboniso wangaphambili wamanqaku angundoqo engxoxo.
Ngoko ke silandela indlela efana kanye nefaneli – sisebenza ukusuka kwindawo ebanzi ukuya kuleyo ithe ngqo.
Kufuneka ubonise ukuba uyasiqonda isihloko ngokunikeza iinyaniso ngokwezemfundo.
Kwisandulela kufuneka unike ulwazi olufutshane lwangaphambili ngomxholo wakho. Oku kunika lowo ufundayo ubungqina bokuba uyawuqonda umxholo kwanokuba uyakwazi ukuyibona ingxaki ethe ngqo ekumele kujongwane nayo. 
Kwingxelo yengxaki, kulapho umntu anika inkcazelo ecacileyo yoko kufanele ukuba kuphandwe kumsebenzi.
Ngokuqhelekileyo ingxelo yengxaki ilandelwa yingxelo yethisisi;ezi zombini zinxulumene kakhulu.
Ingxelo yethisisi inokuchazwa njengecebiso lakho lokuqala lesisombululo kwingxelo yengxaki.
Kwinxenye yokugqibela yentshayelelo kuvezwa amanqaku angundoqo esiqu sombhalo omkhuluyenza ukuba umfundi afumane ingqiqo ngesakhiwo sakho ngokupheleleyo; ngamanye amazwi, ibonisa oko uza kuxoxa ngako ngenjongo yokubonisa ubunyani bengxelo yethisisi yakho, kananjalo nendlela yolandelelwano xa unika ingxoxo yakho.
Isiphetho siyafana nentshayelelo, koko apha uza kubhekisa koko kwenziweyo kwisincoko.
Kuba ngumbono omhle amaxesha amaninzi ukubuyela kwingxelo yakho yengxaki, uze ubonise ngokucacileyo ukuba ingaba ithisisi yakho ibichanekile, okanye ungathanda ukuyilungisa njani na ukuze ufumane impendulo yengxaki.
Kubalulekile kakhulu ukuziqondisisa izinto ezifanayo phakathi kwamanqanaba okuqala kunye nawokugqibela omsebenzi wezemfundo.
Ngoko ke kufuneka uphinde uchaze ingxelo yengxaki kunye neyethisisi kwakhona,ushwankathele amanqaku angundoqo engxoxo,uze ubonise ngokucace phandle ukuba umba obuphandwa ukhokelele njani na kwisiphetho.
Kulo mhlathi wokugqibela ubonisa ukubaluleka koko uthe wakufumanisa ngokuphendula imibuzo ethi “ngoko ke?” okanye “yintoni elandelayo?” 
Khumbula, isiphetho sibhalwa ngokwexesha elidlulileyo.
Ukushwankathela, intshayelelo ngamagqabantshintshi avakalayo, nayinyani yoko kuza kuxoxwa ngako kumsebenzi, kutheni uza kuxoxa malunga nako, kwanokuba bobuphi ubunyani ofuna ukububonisa.
Isiphetho sinxulumene ngendlela engenakwehlulwa kunye nentshayelelo kwaye lilinge lakho lokugqibela lokunikeza ubungqina malunga nokuqonda kwakho kunye nobuchule malunga nomxholo, kwakunye nokubaluleka kophando lwakho. 
Ngenene uluvo lokuqala nolokugqibela lomfundi malunga nombhalo wakho lubalulekile.
Amaxesha amaninzi eyona njongo iphambili yokubhala kwezemfundo kukubonisa ubunyani bomba othile okanye ukusombulula ingxaki ngokusebenzisa iinyani ezixhaswa kokuthile.
Ukuphumeza oku, kufuneka ucwangcise ngokucokisekileyo ulwakhiwo lwengxoxo yombhalo wakho.
Le vidiyo inikeza intshayelelo yolwakhiwo lwengxoxo olusisiseko ukuya kolona lukwinqanaba eliphezulu.
Makhe sisebenzise iziphumo zokulala kwindlela oqhuba ngayo kwezemfundo njengesihloko.
Abaphandi abaninzi bapapashe amanqaku ezemfundo ukungqina ukuba bukhona ubudlelwane phakathi kokulala kunye nendlela oqhuba ngayo kwezemfundo.
Jonga eminye yale mithombo yolwazi:
Ingxoxo esisiseko kaGilbert noWeaver kukuba ukulala ngokwaneleyo kunceda ukusebenza kwenkumbulo.
UChiang kunye nabanye abaphandi bangqina ukuba ukulala kukwanceda kwiinkqubo zokufunda.
Ngoko ke kunokugqitywa ngelithi kuyadingeka ukuba abafundi balale ukuze baqhube kakuhle edyunivesithi.
Ukusetyenziswa kolwazi kumxholo wakho othe ngqo, nako kubalulekile.
Elinye inyathelo eliphambili kunokufikelela nje kwisiphetho, iyakuba kukubonisa kulowo ufunda umbhalo wakho ukuba yintoni na intsingiselo. 
Kule meko, isenokuba abafundi kufuneka baqinisekise ukuba balala ngokwaneleyo.
Ukuhlola ukubangaba unengxoxo kwesisiseko, ungaqalisa ngentsingiselo yakho uze ke usebenze ngokubuya umva uzibuza imibuzo ethile.
Okokuqala, abafundi kufuneka ukuba balale ngokwaneleyo. Ngoba?
Okwesibini, kuba kudingeka ukuba ulale ukuze uqhube kakuhle kwezemfundo. Ingaba bukhona ubungqina?
Ewe, uGilbert noWeaver babonisa ukuba ngokwenyani kunceda ekusebenzeni kwenkumbulo kanti uChiang et al. ubonisa ukuba ngokwenyani kunceda ekufundeni, futhi zombini inkumbulo nokufunda zizinto ezidingekayo kwindlela oqhuba ngayo kwezemfundo.
Qaphela ukuba ingxoxo yakho kufuneka icace. Kuwe kunokukhangeleka ngokungathi uchaza into ecacileyo, kodwa khumbula: oko kukhangeleka ngokungathi kucacile, kunokwenzeka ukuba akucacanga kulowo ufundayo.
Naxa abantu bejongene neenyaniso ezifana ngqo, kuyenzeka ukuba bafikelele kwiziphetho ezahlukeneyo. Iziphetho ezahlukeneyo ke zona, zinokukhokelela kwiindlela ezahlukeneyo zokusetyenziswa kolwazi.
Luxanduva lwakho ukwenza ukuba indlela ocinga ngayo icace kangangoko ukuze lowo ufunda umbhalo wakho akwazi ukuvumelana neziphetho zakho.
Sebenzisa ulwazi oluvela kwimithombo yolwazi lwezemfundo njengeentetho zakho, chaza ngokucacileyo isiphetho esivakalayo ofikelele kuso ngokusebenzisa olu lwazi, uze wenze kucace kulowo ufunda umbhalo wakho ukuba ithini na intsingiselo yolu lwazi.
Nangona nje ingxoxo esisiseko isebenza ekuboniseni ubunyani bomba okanye ukusombulula ingxaki, kunokwenzeka ukuba lowo ufundayo angavumelani neziphetho zakho, ngenxa yokuba enezinye iinyani ezingaphezulu, okanye kuba iinyani yena ezichaza ngendlela eyahlukileyo.
Ukulungiselela oku kunokwenzeka, unokwenza ukuba ingxoxo yakho yomelele ngokusebenzisa ulwakhiwo lwengxoxo olukwinqanaba eliphezulu nangakumbi.
Kwingxoxo ekwinqanaba eliphezulu indlela yolandelwano evakalayo ilandela ipateni efanayo njengaleyo yengxoxo esisiseko, kodwa umbhali ubona kwangaphambili ukuba omnye umntu kunokwenzeka ukuba abenengxoxo ephikisayo.
Ngoko ke, kulwakhiwo lwengxoxo olukwinqanaba eliphezulu iingxoxo eziphikisayo ezinokubakho ziyaphakanyiswa aze umbhali ajongane nazo ngokuthi abonise ukuba azichanekanga okanye ngokuba avume ukuba zinako ukunyaniseka, aze ke asitshintshe kancinci isiphetho okanye intsingiselo ephakanyiswe ekuqaleni.
Ulwandlalo lwengxoxo eyandiswe ngakumbi lunokukhangeleka kanje:
Ukulala kunceda kwinkumbulo kunye nokufunda. 
Ngoko ke, abafundi kufuneka balale ukuze bakwazi ukusebenza.
Nakuba kunjalo, abanye abafundi babanga ngelithi bangakwazi ukuwakhumbula ngokukuko amanqaku emva kokuba befunde ubusuku bonke.
Oku kunokwenziwa kukuxhomekeka kwabo kwinkumbulo yexesha elifutshane.
Ngoko ke, ukuze ukwazi ukugcina oko ukufundileyo ixesha elide, kuyafuneka ukuba ulale.
Okokugqibela, abafundi kufuneka bacwangcise ngokukuko amaxesha okufunda nawokuphumla ukuze bafumane iinzuzo zenkumbulo yexesha elide ezinxulumene nokulala ngokukuko. 
Ngenene, indlela eyakhiwe ngayo ingxoxo iya kuxhomekeka kulwazi olufumanayo, kwakunye nendlela oluchaza ngayo.
Kukho iindlela eziliqela ongalwakha ngalo ulandelelwano lwengxoxo kunye nolwengxoxo ephikisayo  
Xa ubonisa ukuba aqwalaselwe omabini amacala engxoxo, oko kwenza ukuba ingxoxo yakho yomelele. 
Ngokubhekiselele kwimpikiswano, qaphela ukuba esi sakhono  sintshokothileyo nesinemiceli-mngeni asinakufundiswa kwividiyo enye. 
Yinto ekufuneka ukuba umilisele ingqondo kuyo xa ucwangcisa naxa uphonononga ukubhala kwakho.
Ukubhala kwezemfundo kumele kwenze iyunithi evakalayo nenentsingiselo.
Umgangatho uxhomekeka ikakhulu kwindlela omkhokela ngayo lowo ufunda umbhalo wakho apho kumbhalo.
Kufuneka izivakalisi, imihlathi kananjalo namacandelo emibhalo emide uyidibanise ngokucacileyo ukwenza ukuba ukuqhubela phambili kucace.
Injongo kukuba kungabikho kungaqondakali kombhalo wakho.
Ukufunda umbhalo wezemfundo obhalwe kakuhle kufana nohambo oluphawulwe ngeziphawuli zendlela. 
Nanjengoko iziphawuli zendlela zibonisa indawo ekumele ujike kuyo okanye ziqinisekisa umhambi ukuba usendleleni elungileyo ngenene, kananjalo 
nezakhiwo zombhalo zinceda lowo ufundayo.
Izakhiwo zombhalo ziquka izivakalisi ezizihloko, izivakalisi ezixhasayo kunye neziphawuli zentetho.
Le vidiyo igxininisa kwiziphawuli zentetho.
Iziphawuli zentetho zikwaziwa ngokuba zizihlanganisi ezivakalayo, okanye amagama azi-sign-post, owasebenzisa unenjongo yokukhokela lowo ufundayo koko kubhaliweyo.
Indlela elula yokuziqonda iziphawuli zentetho kukwahlula phakathi (i) kweendlela zokuphinda okutshiwoyo, kunye (ii) nezixhobo ezidibanisayo.
Indlela yokuphinda okutshiwoyo kuxa umbhali egxininisa imbono ngokusebenzisa amagama aphinda kwakhona imbono leyo.
Izifanokuthi, izichasi kunye nokuphindwa kwamagama, umzekelo, zinokusetyenziswa njengendlela yokuphinda okutshiwoyo.
Ngokwesiqhelo isixhobo esidibanisayo sibonisa ubudlelwane phakathi kwezivakalisi okanye imihlathi.
Sikubuyisela emva kwizivakalisi ezingaphambili, okanye sijonge phambili kwizivakalisi okanye imihlathi elandelayo. 
Sisebenzisa izixhobo ukuxhasa lowo ufundayo ukuba alandele indlela yokucinga – khumbula, ufuna ukuba abo bafunda umbhalo wakho bakuqonde oko ubaxelela kona futhi kananjalo udinga ukubaqinisekisa ngengxoxo yakho.
Kukho amagama namabinzana adibanisayo awohlukeneyo esinokuwasebenzisa. 
Konke kuxhomekeka kubudlelwane onqwenela ukubuphuhlisa phakathi kwezivakalisi, okanye iinxenye ezahlukeneyo zombhalo.
Ukuba ngaba, umzekelo, ufuna ukubonisa ukulandelelana kwezehlo, uya kusebenzisa amagama adibanisayo afana nokuthi okokuqala, okwesibini, kunye okwesithathu.
Ukubonisa ubudlelwane obuqhelekileyo, uyakuthi, umzekelo, usebenzise amagama afana nokuthi kuba okanye ngenxa yoko.
Ukuthelekisa kunye nokwahlula izehlo, uya kusebenzisa amagama adibanisayo afana nokuthi nangona, ngokuchasene, kunye nakuba kunjalo. 
Khangela kwiphetshana elinikeziweyo xa ufuna isixhobo soncedo esibanzi nekulula ukusisebenzisa.
Nanjengoko ke ngoku uqonda ukuba ziintoni na iziphawuli zentetho, lixesha lokuba uzibone ezi kunye nezinye izakhiwo zombhalo zisetyenzisiwe.
Masisebenzise umhlathi kaLindi njengomzekelo:
Kwisivakalisi sakhe sokuqala uLindi wazisa isihloko esibanzi somhlathi wakhe.
Kungako sibizwa ngokuba sisivakalisi esisihloko. 
Kananjalo usebenzisa isalathiso somthombo ukuxhasa ibango alenzayo.
Apha uLindi ufaka igama elidibanisayo, nto leyo esixelela ukuba sithathe ingqalelo. 
Nanjengoko ikwaligama lokuqala kwisivakalisi, ukufakwa kwalo kukongeza ugxininiso olungakumbi kukubaluleka kolwazi aza kulunikeza.
Ngokufaka eli binzana, uLindi uqinisekisa isihloko. 
Ngoku siyazi ukuba ulwazi lwamkelekile, kuba luvela ngqo kwicandelo lophando lwengqondo.
ULindi uthe ngqo kakhulu kukubhala kwakhe. 
Ngokuthi ngqo kanjalo wenza ukuba kuthembeke. 
Oku kuthetha ukuba abo bafunda umbhalo wakhe baya kukuthemba oko akuthethayo, nanjengoko engenzi iintetho ezikrokrelekayo nezingacacanga.
Apha uLindi usebenzisa igama elidibanisayo; libizwa ngokuba sisimelabizo soqwalaselo. Ngokwenza oku, uphepha uphinda-phindo olungadingekiyo kwaye siyaqonda ukuba usaxoxa futhi echaza uphando alucaphulileyo.
Ngokusebenzisa eli gama lidibanisayo, uLindi uxelela abo bafunda umbhalo wakhe ukuba baqwalasele, kuba uza kunika izizathu zokuba kutheni oko kungundoqo okufunyaniswe kuphando kubaluleke kangaka.
Zombini lelinye igama elidibanisayo. ULindi usebenzisa eli gama ukugxininisa ukuba intlanganisela yezakhono zokufunda nenkumbulo ibalulekile.
ULindi usebenzisa esi sixhobo sokudibanisa ukucacisa imiba, ukuze aqinisekise ukuba sazi ngokuthe ngqo ukuba ulwazi olukwizivakalisi ezibini ezingaphambili lufaneleke njani kwisihloko somhlathi.
Ngoku uchazela abo bafunda umbhalo wakhe ngokuthe ngqo ukuba uphando alukhankanyileyo lufanelekile kwisihloko somhlathi wakhe.

2. Chonga izinto ezifanayo kunye nezahlukileyo phakathi kwemithombo yakho yolwazi. Unokuthathela ingqalelo izinto ezifana nomahluko kumxholo, imihla yopapasho, iindlela zophando, kunye noluntu olusetyenziswe kuphononongo.

Nazi ezinye izikhokelo ezisebenzisekayo zokuchaza into ngamanye amazwi:

2. Phanda: Chonga iindawo zombhalo wakho ongaziqondiyo uze ukhangele ngokuzimisela intsingiselo yokwenene yomyalezo odlulisiweyo.

Nakuba kunjalo, lo ngxoxo ayisebenzi apha. 
Ukusetyenziswa kwezivakalisi ezibini endaweni yesinye kwenza ukuba kubelula ukusilandela,
Kunye nokufakwa kweekhoma kwahlula iinxenye zesivakalisi ukuze icace intsingiselo. 
Ngumbono omhle ukuba izivakalisi zakho uzifundele ngaphandle ngokuvakalayo ukuze ujonge indlela ezakhiwe ngayo.
Okwesibini, kufuneka uzilumkele iintetha ezibanzi nezingacacanga ngqo. 
Umzekelo, ukusetyenziswa kwegama elithi ‘amaninzi’ xa usithi ‘Iimakethe zezimali kumazwe amaninzi’ akucaci kwaphela.
Endaweni yoko kufuneka ulicacise igama ‘amaninzi’ ngokubhekisa kwiiMakethe zezimali kumazwe amaninzi afana ne-UK, i-USA, neTshayina...
Okwesithathu, kufuneka usebenzise isigama kunye neenkcazelo ezibhekisa ngqo kumxholo xa ukwazi. 
Qaphela ukuba ibinza elinye linokuba neentsingiselo ezahlukeneyo kwimixholo eyahlukileyo. 
Thatha igama elithi ‘ukohlwaya’ njengomzekelo. 
Eli gama linokusetyenziswa njengesenzi okanye isibizo.
Kwimeko yezemfundo, ukohlwaya njengesenzi kunokubhekisa kukusetyenziswa kwesohlwayo ukulungisa ukungathobeli okuthile.
Njengesibizo, icandelo lokufunda linokubhekisa kwisebe lolwazi ngokwesiqhelo elifundwa edyunivesithi. 
Ngoko ke, qiniseka ukuba amagama uwasebenzisa ngendlela echanelekileyo kuwo wonke umbhalo wakho kwaye maxa onke uzifake izalathiso zemithombo zombhalo ukwenza ukuxhasa.
Okokugqibela, ukusebenzisa ulwimi ngendlela eyiyo ngokweelwimi kunganegalelo kumbhalo ocacileyo nochanekileyo.
Ukusebenzisa ulwimi ngendlela engeyiyo kuyayisusa ingqwalaselo koko kuqulathiweyo kuze kwakhe imbono engentlanga malunga nawe, wena mbhali. 
Oku kunokwenza ukuba lowo ufundayo aphelelwe kukukuthemba oko kuqulethwe ngumsebenzi wakho.
Ngokubhala ulwimi ngendlela eyiyo ngokweelwimi uya kwazi ukuqhelana nemithetho kunye nemimiselo yolwimi obhala ngalo.
Musa ukuphela amandla, kanye nabo baphume izandla abasebenzisi bolwimi kusafuneka ukuba bamane bejonga kwizikhokelo zolwimi, iincwadi zesigama kunye nezichazi-magama.
Masishwankathele. Ukubhala ngokucacileyo nangokuchanekileyo kufuneka ukuba: uthathele ingqalelo indlela yokwakha izivakalisi; uzilumkele iintetho ezibanzi nezingacacanga; uwazi amagama kunye neenkcazelo ezikwicandelo lakho lokufunda uze uwasebenzise ngendlela efanayo; futhi uqinisekise ukuba usebenzisa ulwimi ngendlela eyiyo ngokweelwimi. 
Landela ezi zikhokelo ukuziphuhlisa njengombhali kunye nokuphucula umgangatho womsebenzi wakho obhaliweyo. 
Khangela kwiphetshana elinikeziweyo ukufumana iingcebiso nemizekelo engaphezulu. 
Kwividiyo engaphambili, ubukele intshayelelo malunga nenyathelo nenyathelo lokuchaza izalathiso zemithombo (referencing).
Le vidiyo iphononongo izalathiso zemithombo zombhalo ize ibonise ukuba zahluka njani iintlobo ezikhethiweyo zokuchaza izalathiso zemithombo. 
Kananjalo uza kufunda banzi malunga nokufomatha izingeniso ezimbalwa kuluhlu lwezalathiso zemithombo.
Noko ngoku uyazi ukuba kufuneka maxa onke uyichaze imithombo yolwazi oyisebenzisileyo kukubhala kwakho kwezemfundo.
Indlela okubhala ngayo oku kuchazwa kwemithombo, kuxhomekeka kuhlobo lwakho olumiselweyo lokuchaza izalathiso zemithombo.
Kukho iintlobo ezininzi zokuchaza izalathiso zemithombo kwihlabathi jikelele.
Iintlobo ezidumileyo ziquka iHarvard, uhlobo lwe-American Psychological Association, olwaziwa njenge-APA, kwakunye neendlela zemibhalo emincinci esemazantsi ezisetyenziswa ziingcali zoMthetho.
Uhlobo ngalunye luneefomula okanye iinkqubo zalo zezalathiso zemithombo zombhalo kunye nezingeniso kuluhlu lwezalathiso zemithombo. 
Ngaphambi kokuba siqwalasele indlela ezinye zezi ntlobo ezahluka ngazo, makhe siphinde sishwankathele malunga nezalathiso zemithombo zombhalo (ezikwaziwa njengezicaphulo).
Xa usebenzisa intetho eyenziwe ngomnye umbhali, ufaka isalathiso somthombo sombhalo kwisivakalisi. 
Le yindlela efinyeziweyo yoko kufakwa kuluhlu lwezalathiso zemithombo.
Injongo yesalathiso somthombo sombhalo kukunika lowo ufundayo ubungqina bomthombo wolwazi lwakho, ungakhange ufake zonke iinkcukacha zomthombo lowo kumbhalo wakho.
Isalathiso somthombo sombhalo ungasibeka ekuqaleni okanye embindini wesivakalisi. 
Kwezi meko ifani yombhali ngokwesiqhelo iba yinxalenye yesivakalisi.
Isalathiso somthombo sombhalo sinokubekwa ekupheleni kwesivakalisi, ngaphambi kwesingxi. 
Kule meko ifani yombhali iba ngaphakathi kwizibiyeli. 
Kufuneka uyithathele ingqalelo ngononophelo indawo ezibekwa kuyo izalathiso zemithombo zombhalo.
Xa ifani yombhali iyinxalenye yesivakalisi sakho, ukhokhelisa phambili umbhali lize elakho ‘ilizwi’ lithathe indawo engasemva.
Xa isalathiso somthombo sombhalo sifakwe ekugqibeleni, wakha isithuba selakho ilizwi. 
Khangela le mizekelo mibini:
NgokukaHealy (2011:17) izigulana zidinga ukwazi ukuba zingazithemba kwaye zixhomekeke kwiingcali zonakekelo lwempilo ngokubhekiselele 
kukujongana neengxaki zazo. 
Kwesi sivakalisi, umfundi uchaza nje ngawakhe amazwi intetho kaHealy. 
Nanjengoko izigulana ziziva zibuthathaka kwaye zingomelelanga, zidinga ukwazi ukuba zingazithemba kwaye zixhomekeke kwiingcali zonakekelo 
lwempilo ngokubhekiselele kukujongana neengxaki zazo (Healy, 2011:17). 
Kumzekelo wesibini, umfundi uthetha ngobuthathaka bezigulana ukongeza kwintetho kaHealy. 
Oku kubonisa indlela umbhali ahlanganise ngayo ukuqonda kwakhe kunye nolwazi lombhali.
Kubalulekile ukuba kubekho isingeniso kuluhlu lwezalathiso zemithombo ngesalathiso somthombo ngasinye sombhalo. 
Nanjengoko uHealy engomnye wemithombo yolwazi esetyenziswe ngumfundi, zonke iinkcukacha zalo mthombo wolwazi kufuneka zifakwe kuluhlu lwezalathiso zemithombo.
Uhlobo ngalunye lokuchaza izalathiso zemithombo linezazo izikhokelo ngokubhekiselele kwizalathiso zombhalo kunye nezingeniso kuluhlu lwezalathiso zemithombo. 
Ngokwesiqhelo ezi zikhokelo ziyafumaneka kwiwebhusayithi yohlobo olo okanye kunoncwadi wesebe lakho lemfundo.
Ngoku siza kuqwalasela izikhokelo zenguqulelo yohlobo lweHarvard kunye nohlobo lwe-APA. 
Ezi zalathiso zemithombo zombhalo zaqulunqwa ngokwenguqulelo yeHarvard. 
Nanjengoko ubona ifakiwe ifani yombhali, unyaka wopapasho kunye nenombolo efanelekileyo yephepha, zaze zohlulwa ngekholon. 
Ngokwenguqulelo yeHarvard, iinombolo zamaphepha kufuneka maxa onke zifakwe kwizalathiso zemithombo zombhalo.
Izalathiso zemithombo zombhalo kuhlobo lwe-APA ziyohluka kancinci. 
Nanjengoko ubona, apho isalathiso sombhalo sifakwe ekuqaleni okanye embindini wesivakalisi, inombolo yephepha iyohlulwa kumbhali kunye nomhla. 
Xa isalathiso somthombo sombhalo sifakwe ekupheleni kwesivakalisi, ulandelelwano lolwazi luyafana nolo lweHarvard, kodwa lukhangeleka njengolwahlukileyo. 
Qaphela iikhoma ezimbini, unobumba u-p, kunye nesingxi.
Ngokohlobo lwe-APA, iinombolo zamaphepha zifakwa kuphela ukuba ngaba ulwazi olusebenzisileyo lukwiphepha elithile kumthombo wolwazi. 
Ukuba ngaba wenza isalathiso somthombo, umzekelo, kwindlela abona ngayo umbhali ngokubanzi kumba othile, ngumbhali kunye nomhla wopapasho kuphela izinto ezidingekayo.
Uluhlu lwezalathiso zemithombo licandelo elibalulekileyo loxwebhu lwezemfundo. 
Xa uqulunqa uluhlu lwezalathiso zemithombo, kufuneka ulandele izikhokelo zohlobo kwaye uthathele ingqalelo inkcazelo nganye encinci.
Olu luluhlu lwezalathiso zemithombo olubhalwe ngokohlobo lweHarvard lokuchaza izalathiso zemithombo -. 
Qaphela ifomathi yesingeniso senqaku lejenali.
Ingaba uyabona ukuba umbhali wesibini nowesithathu bohlulwe nge-ampersand?
Kuze emva koko kulandele unyaka wopapasho kunye nesihloko senqaku lejenali.
Okulandelayo ibe sisihloko sejenali sibhalwe bukekela, umqulu wejenali, inombolo, ikholon kuze ekugqibeleni ibe ziinombolo zamaphepha. 
Qaphela isingxi esisekugqibeleni.
Olu luluhlu lwezalathiso zemithombo olubhalwe ngohlobo lokuchaza izalathizo zemithombo lwe-APA uhlelo lwesi-6 Qaphela ifomathi yesingeniso senqaku lejenali. 
Zombini iintlobo zidwelisa ababhali ngendlela efanayo,
Kodwa jonga izikhewu ezisekuqaleni kuhlobo lwe-APA.
Umhla ukwizibiyeli.
Kulandela isihloko senqaku ize ibe ligama lejenali nalo libhalwe bukekela.
Umqulu kunye neenombolo zamaphepha zikhangeleka zohlukile kancinci – ayikho ikholon.
Ndiqinisekile uyawulandela umfanekiso. 
Kanye nanjengokuba inqaku lejenali linefomathi ethile ngokohlobo lokuchaza izalathiso zemithombo, kunjalo nakwiiwebhusayithi, iividiyo, 
iincwadi kunye namanqaku amaphephandaba, phakathi kokunye. 
Iindaba ezimnandi zezokuba, akudingeki ukuba uzinkqaye ezi fomathi. 
Nokuba ngaba yiHarvard, i-APA okanye naluphi na olunye uhlobo, odinga ukukwenza nje kukusebenzisa izikhokhelo zohlobo oluchongiweyo.
Le vidiyo ikwazisa kumba wentembakalo kwezemfundo.
Sonke sakhe sahlangana namagama athi ‘ukubiwa kwentetho ebhalwe ngomnye umntu (plagiarism)’ kunye ‘nokukopa’. 
Eneneni athetha ukuthini?
Ewe, ukubiwa kwentetho ebhalwe ngomnye umntu kunye nokukopa zizenzo ezingamkelekanga kwaphela. 
Nangona kunjalo ukubiwa kwentetho ebhalwe ngomnye umntu kuyaqhubeka nokuba ngomnye wemiceli-mngeni emikhulu ezijongene nayo iidyunivesithi.
Abahlohli, nangona nje bebalumkekisa abafundi ukuba bangayibi intetho ebhalwe ngomnye umntu, bayasokola ukuwusombulula lo mba.
Ukubiwa kwentetho ebhalwe ngomnye umntu kuyaqhubeka nangona nje abafundi beyazi inkcazelo yokubiwa kwentetho ebhalwe ngomnye umntu futhi bekuqonda ukuba kufanele kungenziwa.
Ngoko ke, le vidiyo inikeza ulwazi lokufundisa malunga nale ngxaki. 
Wakuba unolwazi olubanzi malunga nokuba kuthetha ukuthini na, kungani kusenzeka kwaye ukuthintela njani, ungakwazi ukukhula ube ngumbhali wezemfundo othembakalayo.
Ukuze ube ngumfundi onempumelelo kufuneka uzithathele ingqalelo ekhethekileyo izakhono ezidingekayo ukubhala umbhalo wezemfundo onguwo.
Kufuneka uthathe uxanduva olupheleleyo lokuphucula izakhono zakho zokubhala, kuba ubhalo lwezemfundo ludinga ubugcisa kakhulu.
Lwahluke ngokupheleleyo kulwimi lwemihla ngemihla esilusebenzisa mihla yonke, kwakunye nengxoxo ezingasekelwanga ntweni amaxa amaninzi, 
okanye eziqhelekileyo esizisebenzisa kwiimpilo zethu zemihla ngemihla.
Kufuneka siyitshintshe njani ke ngoko indlela esijongana ngayo nobomi bezemfundo?
Besebenzisa uphando lwabo u-Esra noTuba bachaza ukuba ngokuqhelekileyo abafundi bakopa iintetho zabanye ababhali ngenxa yezi zizathu zithathu:
Amaxesha amaninzi abafundi abanazakhono zizizo zokulawula ixesha labo. 
Abafundi abachithi ixesha elaneleyo bezilungiselela ukwenza umsebenzi, kananjalo beqondisisa imiyalelo. 
Ukufumana imithombo yolwazi efanelekileyo yinkqubo ethatha ixesha elide, qiniseka ukuba uzakhela ixesha elaneleyo lokwenza oku.
Abafundi banobunzima bokufunda nzulu ngendlela ehlaba amadlala. 
Kufuneka ufunde yonke imithombo yolwazi ngendlela oyiqondayo, ukuze ukwazi ukuvavanya nzulu ulwazi ngendlela ehlaba amadlala. 
Xa ungayilandeli ungayiqondi imithombo yolwazi usebungozini bokuba wenze iziphene xa uchaza izalathiso kunye nakumalinge akho okuhlanganisa imithombo yolwazi kumbhalo wakho.
Abafundi banobunzima bokuqonda ukuba kutheni benesalathiso somthombo nje. 
Isizathu sokuchaza izalathiso zemithombo asikuko ukuthobela nje isikhokelo sokunikezwa amanqaku, koko kukunika umsebenzi wakho intembakalo. 
Khumbula, kufuneka ubonise abanye ukuba usebenze ngenkuthalo ukufumana ulwazi lwezinye iingcali, ngendlela yemithombo yolwazi oyisebenzisayo, kwisihloko sakho. 
Akufuneki ucinge ngendlela yokuthintela ukuba intetho yomnye umbhali, koko ucinge ngendlela ongababonisa ngayo abanye ukuba wenze konke okusemandleni akho ukukhusela izimvo zakho.
I-Write-it inikezela ngolwazi kunye nezakhono ezibambekayo zokukuphuhlisa ukuba ube ngumbhali ongcono wezemfundo.
Le vidiyo igxininisa kwintembakalo kwezemfundo, nento ebonwa njengengundoqo kwiimpawu zentsulungeko zombhali wezemfundo. 
Kubalulekile ke ngoko ukuba uyilawule indlela oziphatha ngayo kwezemfundo. 
Imisebenzi idinga ukumiliselwa kwengqondo kunye nolawulo lwexesha. 
Kufuneka uzenzele ixesha lokwenza amalungiselelo, uphando, ukufunda, ukubhala amalinge aliqela ngaphambi kokungenisa oko kukokona kokugqibela. 
Xa kuthethwa ngokufuziselayo, sonke siyaziqeqesha ukuba sibe ngabatoli abaziingcali. 
Olu hlobo ‘lomdlalo’ aludingi ukusetyenziswa komzimba okungako, kodwa liyakudinga ukumiliselwa kwengqondo, ukuziqeqesha ithuba elithile lexesha.
Nangona kunconywa umyinge wamanzi ophezulu kumadama aphambili kwisithili saseChris Hani, amafama werhalinati eMitford ngaseHewu ayakhala.
La mafama akhalela ukutshabalala kwemveliso yawo yerhalinati ethe yatshabalala ngenxa yamanzi nemvula enqabileyo.
Ingxelo yala mafama ithi esi sityalo sixhomekeke ngamandla kwimvula eyaneleyo ethi isakungabikho basebenzise amanzi wedama elikufutshane. 
Usihlalo wokopolotyeni wale fama, uWilliam Fani, uyangqina ukuba ngenene ikhona ingxaki eMitford.
“Sixhomekeke ngamandla kumanzi edama apha, wona asuka emvuleni, xa ingekho imvula eyaneleyo siyalahlekelwa kakhulu. 
Azikhuli ngokwaneleyo iziqhamo zethu,” kutsho uFani.
Uthi intle intsebenziswano phakathi kwabo noMasipala weSithili saseChris Hani ukuzama ukukhulisa le fama yeRhalinati.
“Xa inethe kakuhle imvula apha, ligcwale eli dama sinkcenkceshela kakuhle. 
Xa ligcwele amanzi ahlala iminyaka emibini singenangxaki,” utsho uFani.
Ukanti kunyaka ophelileyo imvula ibintle kwaye nesivuno sabo besisihle, kodwa zibekho iingxaki.
“Kunyaka ophelileyo ingxaki ibe kukuthengiswa kwayo. 
Asikhange sifumane malike yokuthengisa, yahlala apha yade yabola ingahambi irhalinati,” kutsho uFani.
Uthi isisombululo sengxaki yabo kukuba banikwe amanzi aneleyo namathuba okungena kwiimalike eziphambili ehlabathini.
“Sicela ukwenzelwa umpompi othembakeleyo kuba ngoku sixhomekeke kumanzi asuka emvuleni. 
Xa sinompompi sakuhlala sinamanzi logama sikhangela imalike kwelinye icala,” utsho uFani.
Ilizwe laseNdiya lihamba phambili ngokuvelisa iindidi ngeendidi zerhalinati kwihlabathi. 
Ngenxa yoku ela lizwe livelisa, likwathengisa irhalinati iinyanga ezilishumi elinesibini zonyaka.
UMasipala weSithili saseChris Hani ngomnye kwiinkampani ezixhase ukusungulwa nenkqubela yeli phulo lokuveliswa kwerhalinati.
Othethe egameni loMasipala weSithili saseChris Hani, uBulelwa Ganyaza, uthi bayazazi iingxaki zala mafama erhalinati.
“Enye yeengxaki eziphambili eMitford kukunqongophala kwamanzi. 
La fama ixhomekeke ngamandla kumanzi wedama elukufutshane phaya. 
Ngenxa yeemeko eziguqukayo zemozulu awakho amanzi,” kucacisa uGanyaza.
Uhambisa athi bebambisene namafama werhalinati eMitford bakhangela isisombululo sexesha elide.
“Phakathi kwezinye izinto esijonge ukuba zenzeke phaya kukuba kugrunjwe umpompi othembakeleyo ukuzisa amanzi. 
Sikwajonge ukufakela iphiko eliza kudontsa amanzi oneleyo kwisicwangciso sexesha elide,” kutsho uGanyaza.
Ukuvaleka kwemibhobho ebalekisa amanzi okanye imeko yokuhlala namaqondo obushushu kubangela iingxaki kwimveliso yerhalinati.
Izakhamzimba ezifumaneka kwirhalinati zibangela ukucoceka kwesikhumba logama ikwavula iintunja zesikhumba. 
Esi siqhamo siyazama ngamandla aso ukuncedisana nokuthoba amafutha emzimbeni. 
Ukwehla kwamafutha kubangela ukwehla kobunzima kumzimba lowo. 
Irhalinati iqinisa amathambo logama ikwahlupheza amajoni omzimba ukuba alwe ngamandla nezifo ezingena emzimbeni.
Isithili saseChris Hani sineefama ezivelisa iziqhamo eziquka iorenji, amazimba nombona omninzi.
USibongile Mkhwanazi ulisabele ikhwelo lokuba intsangu isetyenziswe njengechiza lokunyanga ngokusemthethweni eMzantsi Afrika. 
Ungumnikazi, ekwangumsunguli wenkampani EyeZulu High Kitchen, evelisa iindidi zemveliso yentsangu.
Uthi konke oku kuqale ngokuba athande ukutya, ekwathanda ukusebenza kwigumbi lokupheka ekhayeni lakhe.
“Umakhulu wam ebengumntu othanda ukupheka kakhulu, ndisoloko ndisecaleni kwakhe, ndiqwalasele iindlela enza ngazo xa epheka ukutya,” kutsho uMkhwanazi.
IEyeZulu High Kitchen ivelisa iimveliso eziquka iziqholo zokutya ezinjenge oyile yokupheka, ioyile yokongeza incasa ekutyeni nezinye.
“Ekhaya bekunkonkxwa ukutya emva kokuba kuvunwe egadini, kugcinwe ixesha elide kumakhulu wam, kodwa umdla wawusoloko usekuphekeni,” utsho uMkhwanazi.
Ukhuliswa ngunina obengenamyeni, yena eyintombi endala. 
Kwamnika ithuba lokufunda nzulu ngokupheka ngendlela ezahlukeneyo.
“Emva kokuqukumbela imfundo ephakamileyo, ndiye ndadibana nabantu abangamaRasta ndaphila impilo enye kunye nabo, ndafunda lukhulu kubo ngentsangu,” kucacisa uMkhwanazi.
Uthi ufunde intlobo entsha yokutya, ukusetyenziswa kwentsangu nezinye eziyinxalenye yesizwe samaRasta.
“Bendisoloko ndiphambili kwiinkqubo zokupheka nokulungiswa kokutya kwamaRasta xa sinendibano yenkonzo yamaRasta,” utsho.
Sele kuyiminyaka engamashumi amabini uMkhwanazi ephila ngokutya kwamaRasta, iintsangu nezinye iimveliso ezihambelana nentsangu.
“Iimveliso zam zonke zentsangu ndizenzela ekhayeni lam, ndizikhulisela intsangu yam ngokwam, ndize ndenze ke le mixube yezi ncindi, 
andinakuyichaza ke ncakasana imixube yam kuba yimfihlelo yeEyeZulu High Kitchen,” kutsho uMkhwanazi.
Isonka sentsangu yenye yeemveliso eziphambili eziveliswa nguMkhwanazi kumsebenzi wakhe wokuzikhulisa kwimveliso yentsangu.
Ethetha ngemveliso yentsangu nokukhuliswa kwayo kweli, uMphathiswa weSebe lezoLimo noPhuhliso lwaMaphandle uNomakhosaza Meth.
“Sijonge ukuyikhulisa kakhulu imveliso yentsangu eMpuma Koloni, singahle siyifakele ibe sisifundo esisemthethweni kwezinye zeeKholeji zeli phondo ingakumbi emaMpondweni,” watsho uMeth.
USibongile Mkhwanazi uthi ukusebenzisa amakhasi onxibelelwano ukuthengisa iimveliso zakhe kuzele amaduna namathokazi, kwaye zikho iimpawu zokukhula kwishishini lakhe. 
“Ndibuzwa rhoqo ngabantu ukuba ndakuyivula nini indawo yokuthengisela iimveliso zam, bendithumelela imiyalezo ngokusebenzisa amakhasi onxibelelwano,” utsho uMkhwanazi.
Intsangu ineendidi ngeendidi ezibizwa ngamagama ahlukeneyo ngokweelwimi zasemzini, kodwa ngeelwimi zesintu linye kuphela igama layo.
“Ndijonge ukubiza abantu beze eEyeZulu High Kitchen nokuba kukanye ngenyanga ukuze bangcamle, bathenge iimveliso zethu, ngolo hlobo lakukhula ishishini lam,” utsho uMkhwanazi.
Intsangu sesinye sesityalo abafikele kuso abantu beli xa bebesuka kumazwe akuMntla noMbindi weAfrika, befikela kwisizwe sabaThwa. 
Eli cuba labaThwa mva liye lawela kwisizwe samaMpondo emva kokoyiswa kwemikhosi yabo ngamabutho amaMpondo.
Imimandla ephambili ukulima intsangu kweli kwamhla mnene, iquka iidolophu zamaMpondo ezifana neSajonisi, Lusikisiki, Libode naseNgqeleni nezinye.
Ibhunga elizibiza ngokuba yiThe Cannabis Development Council of South Africa lithi lilo elijongene ngokusemthethweni nokuphuhliswa kokusetyenziswa kwentsangu ngabantu beli. 
Ukusukela kwinyanga ezayo kuza kubanjwa iinkomfa kumaphondo amathathu kweli, aquka iNtshona Koloni, iRawuti kwakunye nephondo laseKZN kuxoxwa banzi ngentsangu.
Ufunde kumaRasta ngentsangu uSibongile Mkhwanazi
USibongile Mkhwanazi ulisabele ikhwelo lokuba intsangu isetyenziswe nje ngechiza lokunyanga ngokusemthethweni eMzantsi Afrika. 
Ungumnikazi, ekwa ngumsunguli wenkampani EyeZulu High Kitchen, evelisa iindidi zemveliso zentsangu.
Uthi konke oku kuqale ngokuba athande ukutya, ekwathanda ukusebenza kwigumbi lokupheka ekhayeni lakhe. 
”Umakhulu wam ebengumntu othanda ukupheka kakhulu, ndisoloko ndisecaleni kwakhe, ndiqwalasele iindlela enza ngazo xa epheka ukutya,’kutsho uMkhwanazi.
IEyeZulu High Kitchen ivelisa iimveliso eziquka iziqholo zokutya ezinje nge oyile yokupheka, ioyile yokongeza incasa ekutyeni nezinye.
”Ekhaya bekunkonkxwa ukutya emva kokuba kuvunwe egadini, kugcinwe ixesha elide kumakhulu wam, kodwa umdla wawusoloko usekuphekeni,”utsho uMkhwanazi. 
Ukhuliswa ngunina obengenamyeni, yena eyintombi endala kwamnika ithuba lokufunda nzulu ngokupheka ngendlela ezahlukeneyo.
”Emva kokuqukumbela imfundo ephakamileyo, ndiye ndadibana nabantu abangamaRasta ndaphila impilo enye kunye nabo, ndafunda lukhulu kubo ngentsangu,”kucacisa uMkhwanazi. 
Uthi ufunde intle entsha yokutya, ukusetyenziswa kwentsangu nezinye eziyinxalenye yesizwe samaRasta.”Bendisoloko ndiphambili kwinkqubo zokupheka nokulungiswa kokutya kwamaRasta xa sinendibano zenkonzo yamaRasta,”utsho.
Sele kuyiminyaka engamashumi amabini uMkhwanazi ephila ngokutya kwamaRasta, iintsangu nezinye iimveliso ezihambelana nentsangu.
“Iimveliso zam zonke zentsangu ndizenzela ekhayeni lam, ndizikhulisela intsangu yam ngokwam ndize ndenze ke lemixube yezincindi, andinakuyichaza ke ncakasana imixube yam kuba yimfihlelo yeEyeZulu High Kitchen,”kutsho uMkhwanazi.
Isonka sentsangu yenye yemveliso eziphambili eziveliswa nguMkhwanazi kumsebenzi wakhe wokuzikhulisa kwimveliso zentsangu.Ethetha ngemveliso zentsangu nokukhuliswa kwazo kwei uMphathiswa wesebe lezolimo nophuhliso lamaphandle uNomakhosaza Meth.
”Sijonge ukuyikhulisa kakhulu imveliso yentsangu eMpuma Koloni, singahle siyifakele ibesisifundo esisemthethweni kwezinye zeKholeji zeli phondo ingakumbi emaMpondweni,”watsho uMeth.
USibongile Mkhwanazi uthi ukusebenzisa amakhasi onxibelelwano ukuthengisa iimveliso zakhe kuzele amaduna namathokazi, kwaye zikho iimpawu zokukhula kwishishini lakhe. 
“Ndibuzwa rhoqo ngabantu ukuba ndakuyivula nini indawo yokuthengisela iimveliso zam, bendithumelela iiyalezo ngokusebenzisa amakhasi onxibelelwano,”utsho uMkhwanazi.
Intsangu inendidi ngendidi ezibizwa ngamagama ahlukeneyo ngokwelwimi zasemzini, kodwa ngelwimi zesintu linye kuphela igama layo.
”Ndijonge ukubiza abantu beze eEyeZulu High Kitchen nokuba kukanye ngenyanga ukuze bangcamle, bathenge iimveliso zethu, ngolohlobo lakukhula ishishini lam,”utsho uMkhwanazi.
Intsangu lelinye lamafama abafikele kulo abantu beli xa bebesuka kumazwe akuMntla noMbindi weAfrika befikela kwisizwe sabaThwa. 
Elicuba labaThwa mva liye lawela kwisizwe samaMpondo emva kokoyiswa kwemikhosi yabo ngamabutho amaMpondo. 
Imimandla ephambili ukulima intsangu kweli kwamhla mnene iquka idolophu zamaMpondo ezifana neSajonisi, Lusikisiki, Libode naseNgqeleni nezinye.

Omabini amaqela aye emdlalweni ezithembile emva kokuqhuba kakuhle emidlalweni yeDStv Premiership egqithileyo. 
Umdlalo utake iintlantsi zisuka ngoba bekudlala amaqela athanda ukuyibeka phantsi ibhola xa ehlasela esebenzisa isantya esiphezulu.
USiphiwe Tshabalala, obeqala ukudlala kwiqela likaBenni McCarthy, uzibonakalise ngokukhaba ibhola entle edibene nentloko kaLimbikani Mzava – kodwa eye yabanjwa ngunozinti weLeopards, uKing Ndlovu. 
Emva kokusukelana ixesha elide, omabini amaqela aye kwixesha lokuphumla kungekho elikwazileyo ukubhalisa ebhodini nangona amathuba wokufumana amagowuli ebekhona kwisigaba sokuqala somdlalo.
Iqela laseLimpopo, iLidoda Duvha, liqhufuze iqanda ngebhola efakwe nguMohammed Anas – obeluncedo nangethuba iLeopards ibetha iGolden Arrows ngo’2-1 emdlalweni weDStv Premiership obuphakathi evekini.

Iinguqu ezenziwe nguMcCarthy kwisigaba sesibini somdlalo khange zibe nefuthe kwaphela. 
Umdlalo uphele iLeopards ifuma impumelelo eyidlulisele kumjikelo olandelayo weNedbank Cup. 
Emidlalweni edlalwe izolo, iTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila ibethe iSwallows FC ngo’4-3 kumapenela emva kokuba amaqela ebambene ngo’2-2 kwixesha elongezelelweyo.

Ndihlutshwa liphulo nentengiso yomzi odidiyela nothengisa utywala iCastle Milk Stout, ngokusengela phantsi inkolo yesiNtu noxa amathunga 
ekho, ngelithi umisela usuku lweziNyanya! 
Eli phulo alizukunceda ukuvuselela inkcubeko, okulilifa, amasiko nezithethe zamaAfrika nanjengoko bebanga njalo!
Esi senzo siphuhlisa ubuzungul’ ichele obungenantanga ngokusebenzisa inkolo yesiNtu ukuzenzela ingeniso nanjengoko bejolise ekunyuseni iintengiso zabo.
Okona kudanisayo kukuba abantu abafanele ukuba ngabalondolozi bamasiko nezithethe (iinkokheli zemveli) zizibandakanye nephulo lokunyusa iintengiso zikadlomdlayo egameni lenkolo yesiNtu nebezifanele ukuba ngamatshantliziyo atshotsha phambili ekuyikhuseleni koozongul’ichele abayisengela phantsi.
Mhlawumbi ukuze esi simbonono ndisenzayo sicace nakuthathatha, mandiphuhlise ezi ngongoma zilandelayo:
1. Amasiko esiNtu akazozenzo/ misitho elabalabayo, koko yindlela yokuphimisela inkolo yesiNtu.
2. Isiko asibotywala okanye inyama yento exheliweyo, koko lilizwi elithi liphume kubantu bekhaya abanyulu nabamanyeneyo.
3. Utywala basemlungwini bungumgqakhwe kumasiko esiNtu!
4. Inkolo yesiNtu nephinyiselwa phakathi kwezinye izinto ngamasiko nezithethe, ayikho kukhuphiswano lokuba ibe nemisitho ekwikhalenda kuba ezinye iinkolo zanikwa loo nyhweba zizirhulumente ezinefuthe lobukoloniyali.
5. Esintwini akudingeki tywala ukuze kukhunjulwe iziNyanya, kwaye ziyinxenye yobomi bethu bemihla ngemihla!
6. Inkolo yesiNtu ayonkolo yabantu abaqamele ngodlomdlayo. 
Isizwe sinengxaki yolutsha olungene gabhu emphandeni, kodwa kusangcwaliswa umbulalazwe ongudlomdlayo!!
Liyinene elomfo wasemaMpingeni elithi, “Ithafa elingenazingxangxosi lisisigqubu seenyoka”. 
Kwezi nkolo zingaka kweli lizwe nezibanendywala zasemlungwini xa ziqhuba imicimbi yazo yonqulo, bekutheni ze kuchongwe le? 
Impendulo ilele kwela qhalo lomfo wasemaMpingeni. 
Kaloku ezasekhapha izinja zikhumkile!! Yilo nto nemizi edidiyela udlomdlayo isiqabela ngaphandle kwesali isiNtu!!
Ndikhwebela zonke iiKumkani neeNkosi ezizingcayo ngesiNtu, zizibhekelise kula manyal’enyoka izibandakanye nawo iContralesa! 
Nayo iContralesa kuyafuneka izibhence ukuba ingaba isadlala le ndima izigasa ukuba idlala yona, okanye sele iliqonga labantu nje abancwase ukuzalisa izisu zabo – mhlawumbi abanye bengengabo nabo bantwana begazi!
Ukuba iContralesa izimisele nyani ukukhuthaza inkolo yesiNtu, ibanjwe yintoni ngoku? Kutheni ifuna ukuxhathisa ngodlomdlayo ukuze yenze oko? 
Ingaba yintoni egwenxa ngokusebenzisa usuku esele likho nelibekelwe bucala kwikhalenda yesizwe, umhla wama24 kweyoMsintsi nolusuku lokukhumbula amafa esizwe?
Mayixelele (iContralesa) isizwe, ukuba ifunjathiswe ntoni ngulo mzi wotywala iqhubela kubo uluntu, egameni lenkolo!!
Ndiqinisekile ukuba imibutho yamatshantliziyo enkolo yesiNtu ayinakuze ithule oku ngathi akwenzekanga nto, sakugqiba ukubhuntsekwa umnwe wokuphalaza elisweni isiNtu!!
Olu luluvo lukaMonde Ciko (uTshatshu) olitshantliziyo leNkolo yesiNtu!
UMonde Ciko (uTshatshu) olitshantliziyo lenkolo yesiNtu.
INKWENKWE yaseQonce uAxola May (16) ebezibona esiya eYunivesithi emva kokugqiba amabanga wakhe aphezulu, ekwanephupha lokuba ngumdlali wombhoxo.
Kodwa ilanga litshone emini amathemba aphela kuAxola emva kweendaba ezibuhlungu zokuhlaselwa kukungahambi kwegazi ngendlela efanelekileyo emathanjeni akhe omzimba (bone marrow).
Ngokudizwe lusapho lukaAxola, ungumntwana onothando kwaye okhululekileyo obonwabelayo ubom nosapho lwakhe kwakunye noontanga bakhe. 
Ikwanguye nomthandi kwanomdlali webhola yombhoxo.
Esona sisombululo esinokuthi sihlangule uAxola kule ngxaki kwaye afumane obunye ubomi kukuba enziwe utyando lokujongwa kwencindi phakathi emathanjeni.
Ingxaki kuAxola, iqale ngokumane ephuma igazi ezimpumlweni, ulusu lwajika, kwamane kuqaqamba iindlebe kwaye kumane ukuphuma igazi kwiintsini.
Iindaba zokuba uAxolea uhlaselwa sisigulo esibeka ubomi bakhe emngciphekweni, khange zimphathe kakuhle umakhulu wakhe kwakunye nomakazi wakhe nabamkhulisayo emva kokubhubha kukamama kaAxola eseneminyaka emibini kuphela.
“UAxola ebekungxamele ukugqiba esikolweni kwaye aye eyunivesithi. 
Phambi kokuba agule, ebezixelele ngokudlalela iqela lebhola yombhoxo laseKapa iWestern Province Rugby. 
Ebesoloko ejonge kuSiya Kolisi kwaye iliqhawe lakhe,” kutsho usapho.
Ngokokutsho kukaJames Alana onguMlawuli kwiDKMS Africa Country, uthi imeko kaAxola imbi kakhulu kwaye izigulana ezininzi zaseAfrika zisemngciphekweni kakhulu ngenxa yokunqaba kwenani labantu abanikeza ngegazi. 
IDKMS, ibongoza uluntu ekubeni lubhalise ukuze kukhule inani akwazi uAxola afumane umntu anokuchanana ngqo naye ngegazi.
“Ndiyacela ndidomboza kuye nabani na onokunikela ngegazi ancede unyana wam aphile, azotsho akwazi enze konke ebekunqwenela ukwenza ebomini,” woleke ngelo umakazi wakhe.
Ungabatyelela abakwaDKMS xa ufuna ukunceda kumnatha wonxibelelwano.
KULE mpelaveki eNgqushwa kuza kube kudlalwa umdlalo obizwa Ghost of Glenmore.
Lo mdlalo, wabhalwa yindumasi kwimidlalo yeqonga uXabiso Zweni .
UZweni, okwangumdlali nomqondisi walo mdlalo, ukunye noAnele Penny okwadlala kwindawo ephambili kuwo.
UPenny, 40, owaziwa ngendima yakhe kaMqokeleli kwibali loMhlobo Wenene elithi Ithini Na Le Nto?, yinzalelwane yelali yaseWoodlands eNgqushwa – nekulapho iGhost of Glenmore iza kube idlalelwa khona.
Encokolela I’solezwe lesiXhosa, uPenny, obengawuvali umlomo ngokuza kwenzeka ngalo Mgqibelo elalini yakhe, uthi ufumene ithuba loyokubonisa ngesakhono sakhe phambi kwabantu bakokwabo.
“Lo mdlalo uziswa eNgqushwa ngenkxaso enikwe abadlali beqonga ngeli xesha linzima lobhubhane oyiCorona ngabakwa-EPACC,” kutsho uPenny.
“Ndibulela kakhulu kwabakwaECPACC ngendima abayidlalayo kuthi badlali beqonga ngeli xesha libi kangaka. 
Ngoku nditsho ndafumana ithuba lokuba ndiyokubonisa ngesakhono sam phambi kwabantu endizalelwe, ndakhulela phambi kwabo!”
Lo mdlalo udlala ixesha elingangeyure kuphela. Amaxabiso yiR30 kuphela ukungena emnyango.
Ngenxa yemiyalelo nemiqathango yeCorona, uPenny uthi kuza kungena abantu abangamashumi amahlanu kuphela yaye ongenamaski akazokuvunyelwa angene.
” Ngelishwa abangaphantsi kweminyaka eli13 abakwazi ukungena,” kucacisa uPenny.
Lo mdlali weqonga, othande ukuxhaphaka kwilali yakhe ukuze aphuhlise italente yabantwana bendawo yakhe, uthi ukhona omnye umcimbi awuphekayo wabantwana oza kuba kule nyanga izayo obizwa ngoMdlungu Odlekayo.
“Apho ndiphuhlisa khona izakhono zabantwana belali yam kumculo, umxhentso nokulinganisa eqongeni,” kutsho uPenny.
Lithini ke ibali ngesi Siphorho saseGlenmore? Sakuva eWoodlands eNgqushwa kulo Mgqibelo ngentsimbi yesine emva kwemini.
NTWAZANA yaseMdantsane iphumelele ukhuphiswano lweTruTalent Search lonyaka ka2021.
Olu khuphiswano, oluqhutywa sisikhululo seSABC, iTruFM, likhangela italente kusasazo neyooDJ abakwaziyo ukuxuba iingoma ngobuchule.
UHlumela Qabo ophumeleleyo, ebengenele kwicandelo lezosasazo.
Iindaba zokuphumelela kwakhe zibhengezwe liBambela Manejala kwiTruFM, uMasi Mdingane, kwinkqubo iDrive 326 ebhexeshwa nguSlujah Bunu noBabalwa G.
UQabo, uphumelela emva kweeveki eziliqela zokuvan’ amandla noompondo zihlanjiwe kwiqonga losasazo.
Eli nenekazi lohlule uSima Fiyo ebelikhuphisana naye kwiTop 2.

Ukanti ophumelele kwicandelo looDJ nguSinovuyo Chula owaziwa njengoMtizo Da DJ.Halala!!!
Umqeqeshi weGolden Arrows, uMandla Ncikazi, uthi uzingoba isifuba ngomsebenzi omhle owenziwe liqela lakhe ukusukela oko kuthe kwaqala isizini. 
Oku kuthethwe nguNcikazi emva kokuba Abafana Bes’thende benze imbali ngokuphumelela iQ2 Innovation okokuqala kwimbali yebhola ekhatywayo. 
Isibhengezo ngewonga elikhatshwe sisigidi esinesiqingatha serandi (R1.5-million) senziwe yiPSL ngoMvulo, ekuqaleni kwale veki. 
Ngumsebenzi omkhulu lo owenziwe nguNcikazi – othathe iintambo ezishiywa uSteve Komphela owasabela ubizo kwiMamelodi Sundowns emva kokuhamba kukaPitso Mosimane ekuqaleni kwesizini.
Abafana Bes’thende boyise iSundowns ebiqhube kakuhle nayo kwiQ2 Innovation – eyasungulwa kwiminyaka edlulileyo ngelizama ukukhuthaza amaqela adlala kwiPSL. 
“Okubalulekileyo kuko konke kukubulela abadlali bethu nabaqeqeshi ngefuthe labo elithe lasinceda ukuze sikwazi ukuqokelela amanqaku amaninzi ngaphezulu kwamanye amaqela (akhe aphumelela iQI) emidlalweni esixhenxe,” utshilo uNcikazi ngovuyo olukhulu.
“Ngenxa yomfutho senze imbali ngokuba liqela lokuqala KwaZulu-Natal eliphumelele into enjena. 
Ngaphezulu kwalo nto, amanqaku alishumi elinesithandathu esiwazuzileyo nemidlalo esiyiphumeleleyo mininzi ngaphezulu kunamaqela awakhe aphumelela iQ Innovation ngaphezulu. 
Andiqondi ukuba akhona amazwi anokucacisa indlela endizingomva isifuba ngayo ukuba yinxalenye yeGolden Arrows,” Impempe.com, imcaphule ngaloo mazwi uNcikazi. 
Umqeqeshi unethemba lokuba Abafana bes’thende baza kuloleka liwonga abalifumeneyo.
“Endikuthandazelayo ngoku kukuba impumelelo yethu isilole ukuze sihlale sikulambele ukufumana iQ Innovation elandelayo. 
Lo nto singayenza ngokuqokelela amanqaku alishumi elinambini emaqeleni aseLimpopo aza kudlala nathi ebaleni lethu, iSugar Ray Xulu Stadium,” 
utshilo uNcikazi, onexhala kuba amaqela eza kuyijonga ngenye iGolden Arrows ukusukela ngoku. 
“Kufuneka sibambelele kwindlela esenza ngayo izinto ngoba okulindelwe kuthi kukhulu ngoku. 
Kumnandi kodwa ngoba iingqondo zethu beziphilile ngoba besingadlali neqela sibe sijonge indawo elikuyo,” utshilo uNcekazi wabo.
Umqeqeshi weqela lesizwe lamantombazana aselula (Under-17 Women) oMzantsi Afrika, uSimphiwe Dludlu, uzixolise ngelithi kuninzi okufundiweyo liqela lakhe kwindebe yehlabathi. 
ABantwana bachiphize iinyembezi emva kokuvuthululwa yiBrazil ngamagowuli amane kwelinye (4-1) kumdlalo weFifa Under-17 Women’s World Cup ebanjelwe e-Uruguay. 
Kanti kwiveki ephelileyo, uMzantsi Afrika ungonjwe yiJapan kakubi ngamagowuli amathandathu kwelinye (6-1) emdlalweni wesibini kwindebe yehlabathi. 
Ukubethwa koMzantsi Afrika kuthetha ukuthi libuyela ekhaya linenqaku elinye jwi elafumaneka kumdlalo owadlala kuwo ntanganye (0-0) neMexico.
Nakubeni iqela likaDludlu liye kwindebe yehlabathi linethemba lokuya kumjikelo olandelayo – kodwa kuye kwabonakala ukuba umgangatho walo usephantsi. 
Umqeqeshi uthi nangona iqela lakhe libethiwe kwindebe yehlabathi – kodwa libuyela ekhaya kukho into eliyifundileyo. 
“Sizile, sabona saphinda safunda e-Uruguay. Namhlanje sidlale kakuhle kakhulu noxa soyiwe emdlalweni. 
Ikhadi elibomvu esilifumeneyo libenayo indawo yokusichana ngoba kuye kwanyanzeleka ukuba sidlale singaphelelanga. 
Ndiyafuna ukuthi abadlali bawafumene amava,” utshilo uDludlu.
UMphathiswa weziMali uOscar Mabuyane ethetha eBhisho ngoLwesine.
UMphathiswa wezeZimali eMpuma Koloni, uOscar Mabuyane, uthi urhulumente wephondo kufuneka abekele bucala imali yokuxhasa abo bakushishino lwekhabatiso laselokishini nasezilalini, esithi oku sisisombululo kumbandela wokungalingani kwanentswelongqesho.
Ebethetha kwiNdlu yoWiso-Mthetho eBhisho ngoLwesine, kwintetho yakhe yokuqala ngqa yohlahlo lwabiwomali lwaphakathi enyakeni ephondweni.
UMabuyane uthi baza kufaka inkxaso koosomashishini basezilalini naselokishini abafuna ukuxandisa kwanokuphucula amashishini afana nokuhlamba imoto, ukulungisa imoto, ukuchwela, ulwamkelo-zindwendwe kwanabo bathengisa ezitalatweni. 
Yiminyaka evisayo oomama abahlala kufutshane naseBhisho bethengisa amarostile namagwinya kwanejinja eBhisho. 
Aba mama bathengisela amagosa karhulumente ubukhulu becala.
Kwixeshana nje emva kokonyulwa njengoMphathiswa wezeZimali, uPhuhliso loQoqosho, ezoKhenketho kwaneMicimbi yezeNdalo, uMabuyane watyelela aba mama eyokuhlola iimeko abasebenzela phantsi kwazo.
“Sifikile eBhisho, sayibona imeko abasebenza phantsi kwayo oomama abaphekela abasebenzi bakarhulumente, singenelele sasibuyisa isidima sabo.
“Sizofika nakwabanye abathengisa phantsi kweemeko ezifana nezi kulo lonke eli phondo lethu. 
Sibulela uMasipala oMbaxa waseBuffalo City ngokusabela ubizo,” utshilo uMabuyane kwintetho yakhe ngoLwesine.
UMabuyane ukwathe urhulumente eyedwa asoze akwazi ukukhulisa uqoqosho.
“Sizokucengana nazo ezi nkampani kulo mba side sifumanane.

“U-SAB funeka asichazele ukuba ilinywa phi le nto adidiyela ngayo imicimbi yakhe eselwayo. 
Sinawo umhlaba nathi kweli phondo,” kutsho uMabuyane.

Kukhangeleka ngathi kungenzeka into embi eseyithanda ukwenzeka ukuba aBafana Bafana bayoyiswa kukuzibekela indawo kwi-African Cup of Nations kwakhona. 
Intandabuzo ibangelwa yimeko elikuyo iqela lesizwe phambi komdlalo wokugqibela ohlakulela iAfcon ekunyaka ozayo eCameroon. 
UMzantsi Afrika udlale ntanganye ngegowuli elinye macala (1-1) neNigeria emdlalweni obuseFNB Stadium ngoMgqibelo weveki ephelileyo. 
Inqaku elinye elifunyenwe yiSuper Eagles liyingenise galakangqa ngaphakathi kwi-Afcon ka-2019. 
Kanti bona aBafana Bafana kufuneka begqithe kwiLibya ebethe iSeychelles ukuze bakwazi ukuzibekela indawo kwitumente ye-Afrika. 
Linye jwi inqaku elidingwa nguMzantsi Afrika – qha ingxaki yimeko elikuyo ngoku emva kokungakwazi ukubethwa iLibya neSeychelles emidlaleni ekwakufuneka liphumelele kuyo iqela likaStuart Baxter.
Nangona ilizwe ligutyungelwe lunxunguphalo nokulahleka kwethemba ebantwini ngenxa yendlela engancumisiyo abadlala ngayo aBafana Bafana – kodwa indlela abadlali ababini, uPercy Tau noLebo Mothiba, abazimisele ngayo emidlalweni yeqela lesizwe – inika ithemba.
UMothiba ufake igowuli kwiNigeria ngempelaveki egqithileyo. Yena uTau ufake igowuli ngomzuzu wokugqibela emdlalweni weNelson Mandela Challenge ophele ngo’1-1 phakathi koMzantsi Afrika nelizwe laseParaguay ngoLwesibini ebusuku eMoses Mabhida Stadium. 
Njengokuba iqela likaStuart Baxter belidlale umdlalo ophucukile xeshikwenye liqubisene neNigeria – kodwa lisinde ngolambisa kwiParaguay ngenxa yomdlalo walo obungadibenanga ncam. 
Ukutshintshatshintsha kwendlela abadlala ngayo aBafana kuko okubangela abantu balahlekelwe lithemba futhi bangayi nasebaleni xa bedlala.
Njengokuba kukho ukuthandabuza ebantwini – kodwa uPercy Tau uthi uqinisekile ukuba uMzantsi Afrika uza kuya kwi-Afcon. 
Anika ithemba amazwi wakhe ngoba ngoyena mdlali oqaqambileyo kwiBafana Bafana. 
“Ndicinga ukuba siza kuya kwi-Afcon. 
Into efunekayo kukugcina nje indlela esidlala ngayo ndawonye ukuya kunyaka ozayo,” utshilo uTau. 
Ephawula emva kokudlala neParaguay, uTau uthe umdlalo ubunzima ngenxa yegowuli elifakwe kubo kwangoko emdlalweni. 
“Bekunzima ngoba kufakwe igowuli kuthi kwangoko emdlalweni. 
Sizamile ukusebenzisa amacebo wethu – kodwa ingxaki ebesinayo kukuba besingabazi, ibingabadlali abasebenzisa amandla futhi ibhola yabo ibibaleka,” utshilo uTau.
Ukuzithemba enkampini yeqela lesizwe lamantombazana, iBanyana Banyana, kunyukile emva kokuphumelela imidlalo emibini kuGroup B kwiWomen’s Africa Cup of Nations esingathwe lilizwe laseGhana. 
Ilizwe lase-Equatorial Guinea libokoboko macala yinduku yoMzantsi Afrika emva kokuolibetha ngamagoquli asixhenxe kwelinye (7-1) kumdlalo obumhle eCape Coast Sports Stadium ebusuku izolo. 
Impumelelo yabadlali bakaDesiree Ellis kwimidlalo emibini kubabeke phezulu kwiGroup B – kodwa kusafuneka basebenze emdlalweni ozayo ukuze baqinisekise indawo yabo kumjikelo olandelayo.
Abadlali abafake amagowuli weBanyana Banyana nguThembi Kgatlana (ufake amabini), uLinda Motlhalo, uNompumelelo Nyandeni, uJermaine Seoposenwe, uRefiloe Jane no-Amanda Mthandi.
Kuyiwe kwixesha lokuphumla uMzantsi Afrika ubhakuzelise umnatha kabini – kodwa nayo iEquatorial Guinea ikwazile ukufaka elinye lokubika ekhaya. 
Abadlali boMzantsi Afriaka bawulawule umdlalo kwisigaba sokuqala; into nje akhale ngayo kakhulu uDesiree Ellis kukuphisa ngebhola endaweni yokulawula umdlalo ngendlela efanelekileyo. 
Izinto ziye zajika kwisigaba sesibini somdlalo ngoba aBanyana Banyana babuye belume ongezantsi futhi begalela amagowuli ngendlela engenambaliso. 
Umqeqeshi weBanyana Banyana uyivuyele kakhulu impumelelo ezuzwe liqela lakhe – kodwa kwangaxeshanye, uvakalise ukungaxoli yindlela elidlale ngayo kwisigaba sokuqala emdlalweni wayizolo. 
UDesiree uthe indlela abadlali bakhe abayilahle ngayo ibhola akayithandanga kwaye ibe nefuthe kwindlela abadlale ngayo.
“Ngexesha lokuphumla sithethile ngokubaluleka kokwabelana nokugcina ibhola kuthi. 
Sithethile ngokudlala iibhola ezinde – eyona nto ebe lichaphaza elibi emdlalweni wethu kuba ingeyiyo indlela yethu yokudlala. 
Kunyanzelekile siyibethe iZambia ngoba amanqaku amathathu ayakucacisa indlela yethu eya kumjikelo olandelayo. 
Kufuneka siye kuyo ngokuzithemba, sidlale ngendlela yethu ngoba siyazana nayo kakhulu,” utshilo uEllis emva komdlalo.
Isekela likaKapteni, uRefiloe Jane, uthe limchulumancisile igowuli alifakileyo emdlalweni. 
“Ukuba iqela liphumelele, wonke umntu uphumelele. 
Kuyandivuyisa ukuba phakathi kwabadlali abafake amagowuli. 
Leyo yinto endisoloko ndizama ukuyiphucula emdlalweni wam. 
Ukuphumelela kwethu kufunqule ukuzithemba kuthi phambi kokudibana neZambia. 
Umdlalo uza kubanzima ngoba kukho imbali phakathi kwethu nabo (iZambia),” uvale ngaloo mazwi uJane.
Le ngcingane ikhokelelwa ngamabhinqa anenjongo ezohlukileyo ngento afuna ukuyifeza ekubeni athi ayiqala le ndibano yawo yokulwela amalungelo awo obubhinqa. 
Kaloku le ngcingane yathi yavela mhla amakhosikazi athi akruquka kukungabonelwa ntweni ngamadoda. 
Ngamakhulu-khulu eminyaka abantu ababhinqileyo bephantsi kwemphatho embi yamadoda. 
Zingcinga ezifana nale ezizama ukwenza inguqu kwindawo ngendawo. 
Phaya kude kudala nabo abantu ababhinqileyo bazabalaze kwinkalo zonke, abakhange balwele amalungelo abo kuphela, kodwa baye balwela amalungelo omntu wonke. 
Kaloku amabhinqa ngabantu ababecinezeleke ngendlela ezininzi, emisebenzini, ekhaya kunye nakurhulumente wobandlululo apha eMzansi Afrika. 
Kwinkomfa yamakhosikazi uHannah (2010:18) ubhale wenjenje ngale ngcingane: Kubonakala apha ukuba amabhinqa kudala esiwa evuka ezabalazela ukuba nawo mawathathwe njenga bemi belizwe, babe namalungelo kunye namathuba alinganayo nawabanye abantu. 
Apha ngezantsi kuza kuthi kungenwe nzulu kwiindidi ezintathu zale ngcingane yesi khomokazi.  
Amabhinqa alwa isidima namagunya aphezulu athi anikwe amadoda. 
Njengokuba iminyaka ihamba nje le ngcingane iye ikhula kwaye imane iqhubeleka phambili.
Amadoda amathathu awapakanyela  intwazana eneshumi elinesithoba ubudala ngokuyidlwengula ngobusuku obuthile ivela ecaweni, agwetyiwe 
yinkundla yengingqi yamatyala eTsomo ngoLwesine.
Ngokwengxelo ephuma emapoliseni, ixhoba lalivela ecaweni lizihambela lodwa ngethuba ligagana nala madoda mathathu endleleni kuse busuku. 
Oku kwenzeka ngomhla weshumi elinesihlanu kwekaCanzibe  ngo2014 kwilali yaseBhongithole kuHebe-hebana eNgqamakhwe.
Isithethi samapolisa aseGcuwa neendawo ezingqongileyo uKapteni  Jackson Manatha, uthi ixhoba larhuqwa ngala madoda elirhuqela kumzi ongasahlali bantu bafika batshintshiselana ngalo.
Ityala lavulwa kwisikhululo samapolisa eNgqamakhwe ze laphandwa ngamapolisa ajongene namatyala okukhusela abantwana namanina abangamaxhoba okuxhatshazwa aseGcuwa.
