Abahlali baseXolobeni emva kokuphumelela idabi lokuchasana nomgodi enkundleni.
UMphathiswa wezeZimali, uPhuhliso loQoqosho, ezoKhenketho kwaneMicimbi yezeNdalo eMpuma Koloni uOscar Mabuyane, uthi kufuneka ivoti (referendum) kumbandela womgodi ongundabamlonyeni waseXolobeni eMbizana.
UMabuyane uthi le voti inganceda ukufumanisa ezona zimvo zabantu baseXolobeni malunga nalo mgodi.
Oku kuza emva kokuba iNkundla ePhakamileyo yoMntla Rhawuti igwebe ngakwicala labahlali baseXolobeni abachasene nomgodi ngelithi banelungelo lokuthi “hayi” xa bengawufuni umgodi.
NgoLwesine kule veki, indibanisela yabahlali baseXolobeni, ezibiza iAmadiba Crisis Committee, iphumelele kwidabi layo lasenkundleni lokuba ifuna ukunikwa imvume yokuthi “hayi” ekombiweni komgodi eXolobeni.
Kwimbalelwano le komiti ithe: “Olu luloyiso kwidabi labahlali leminyaka engaphaya kweshumi elinesihlanu. 
Kudala sizabalaza. 
Sibhiyozela amaqhawe ethu asishiyayo afana noMadoda Ndovela, Scorpion Dimane, Mthanjelwa Mpotomela Mthwa (“Bhalasheleni”) kwakunye nabanye abaphulukana nemiphefumlo yabo bekhusela umhlaba wookhokho bethu kwabo banyolukele ingeniso yethutyana.
“Sisafuna ubulungisa ngoSikhosiphi ‘Bazooka’ Radebe owagetyengwa kweyoKwindla ngo2016. 
Sifuna iiHawks ezinobuqhophololo zaseMpuma Koloni zithathe idokethe lokubulawa [kukaRadebe] zilinike amagosa awaziyo umsebenzi aqashelwe wona,” itshilo le ndibanisela kwimbalelwano.
UMabuyane uthe: “Ukuze sibone imfuno yokuba umgodi uyafuneka kusini na eXolobeni, kufuneka kwenziwe ivoti – ukuze kubonwe ukuba bathini abantu baphaya ngalo mba.”
“Makwenziwe ivoti phaya ukuze abantu baseXolobeni, ngaphandle kokugrogriswa, bathi ‘asiwufuni umgodi’.
“Makungathathwa abantu abathile abaqokelelwe ngabelungu abathile abangahlali phaya, abaya phaya ngokutyelela besithi baza kuphuhlisa abantu baphaya. 
Yiminyaka ilishumi linesibhozo ngoku (aba bantu bangahlali phaya) bethembisa ukuba baza kuphuhlisa abantu ngezokhenketho,” kutsho uMabuyane.
UMabuyane uthi luninzi uphuhliso obe lunokwenziwa eXolobeni xa lo mgodi ubunokuqhuba.
“Lo mgodi kuthethwa ngawo phaya eXolobeni, ufana nqwa nomgodi wamalahle waseRichards Bay [KwaZulu Natal]. 
Sithi ke ngoku, ngokokubona eRichards Bay, umgodi nezokhenketho uyakwazi ukuqhuba ngaxeshanye.
“Siyasamkela isigwebo senkundla kodwa sithi abantu baseXolobeni, bebonke, mabalinikwe ithuba lokuthetha ngalo mgodi. 
La mgodi uza kunceda abantu ngomsebenzi. La titanium (isimbiwa) singagrunjwa iminyaka eya kumashumi amathathu. 
Luninzi uphuhliso olunokuba khona ukuba nje ubunokuqhuba la mgodi.”
Umqeqeshi weBidvest Wits, uGavin Hunt, uthi iBaroka FC ingayingozi kwiTelkom Knockout. 
Amaqela amane azakube esilwela indawo kumdlalo wamagqibela-kankqoyi weTelkom Knockout xa edibana emabaleni akwiindawo ezahlukeneyo ngempelaveki. 
Njengokuba iKaizer Chiefs iza kududlana okweenkunzi zegusha ne-Orlando Pirates emdlalweni ekulindeleke utak’iintlantsi eMoses Mabhida Stadium ngomso ngentsimbi yesithathu. 
Yona iBidvest Wits, eziintshatsheli ezikhuselayo, idibana neBaroka FC emdlalweni ozakube usePeter Mokaba Stadium ngentsimbi yesithathu emalanga ngeCawe. 
Emva kokuguqisa phantsi iMamelodi Sundowns – iBaroka iya emdlalweni ngeCawe ifuna ukuzenzela imbali ngokuthi iye kwisigaba sokugqibela seTelkom Knockout.
Kwelinye icala, uGavin Hunt ukhangela indlela yokukhusela indebe eyaphunyelelwa liqela lakhe kunyaka ophelileyo elabetha iBloemfontein Celtic ngegowuli elafakwa nguVincent Pule odlalela iPirates kule sizini. 
UHunt unabadlali abasemgangathweni ophezulu kwiWits futhi abanokuyithatha bayibeke endaweni ephezulu – kodwa uyayiqonda ingxaki angagagana nayo phambi kwabalandeli bayo iBaroka. 
“Siza kudibana neqela elikhe lafumana iziphumo ezihle. 
Alingekhe liyithathe indebe yePSL. 
Yiyo lo nto iBaroka iza kubona olu khuphiswano njengethuba lokuphumelela indebe. 
Ndiqinisekile siza kuyibona lo nto kwindlela abadlala ngayo,” utshilo uHunt.
Ukapteni weWits, uThulani Hlatshwayo, uS’fiso Hlanti noBuhle Mkhwanazi, bathathe inxaxheba emidlalweni yeqela lesizwe kwiintsuku ezigqithileyo. 
Abaqeqeshi basoloko bebanexhala xa abadlali babo beye kwiqela lesizwe ngoba babuya bonzakele ngamanye amaxesha abe amaqela enemidlalo ebalulekileyo. 
Nangona kunjalo, uGavin Hunt uxhalatyiswe kukungabikho kukaRobyn Johannes onqunyanyisiweyo ngenxa yamakhadi. 
“Kunyanzelekile sizijule xa sidlala neBaroka. 
Besinabadlali abasuka kwiBafana Bafana ekufuneka sibanyamezela kuba beza kuziqeqesha kube kanye nathi,” utshilo uHunt ethetha neentatheli ekuqaleni kwale veki.
UBrilliant Khuzwayo angadlala okokuqala njengomdlali we-Orlando Pirates emdlalweni weTelkom Knockout namhlanje. 
Oku kuthiwe thsuphe ngumqeqeshi weBucs xeshikweni encokola neentatheli ekuqaleni kwale veki eGoli. 
AmaBhakabhaka aza kuvan’amandla neKaizer Chiefs emdlalweni ojongwe ngamehlo abomvu ngabalandeli bebhola ekhatywayo eMoses Mabhida Stadium ngentsimbi yesithathu emalanga. 
Ngokutsho kukaMilutin “Micho” Sredojevic, unozinti wakhe uphile qete kwaye ukulungele ukudlala. 
Abaqeqeshi bePirates bazibalule njengoongqondongqondo ekufundeni umdlalo; ukudlalisa uKhuzwayo ingasesinye sezixhobo zabo emdlalweni. 
UKhuzwayo watyikitywa yiPirates phambi kokuqala kwesizini emva kweminyaka engumdlali weChiefs – apho wakhala ngokungafumani ithuba lokudlala ngenxa ka-Itumeleng Khune.
Ngelishwa lakhe, wafika kwiPirates wonzakala – lo nto yamnyanzela ukuba alinde ixesha elide phambi kokudlala umdlalo wakhe wokuqala. 
UMicho uthe kungenzeka amqalise ezipalini – kodwa yonke into iya kuxhomekeka emalungiselelweni weqela. 
“Imidlalo emikhulu ifuna kwenziwe izinto ngendlela enomahluko. 
Uyathembisa kakhulu uKhuzwayo xa ezilolonga futhi yonke into ihamba kakuhle. 
Ndingaqinisekisa ukuba ukulungele ukudlala nanini. 
Kodwa into endingeke ndiyitsho kukuba uza kudlala okanye akazukudlala ngoba – lo nto iya kuxhomekeka kumalungiselelo wethu,” utshilo uSredojevic kwiSolezwe.
Ukudlaliswa kwakhe uKhuzwayo namhlanje ingayinto enkulu kakhulu ngoba uzakube edlala neqela asuka kulo, alaziyo naphambi kwabantu bakowabo eThekwini – apho azalelwe khona. 
Amakhosi asantywizisa emva kokubethwa yiPirates ngo’2-1 emdlalweni we-Absa Premier Soccer League obuseFNB Stadium kwinyanga ephelileyo. 
UMicho uxelele iintatheli ukuba iqela lakhe alikafikeleli kumgangatho awufunayo. 
Eli lithuba elihle lokuthi sizibonakalise.abhali sisengxakini enkulu ngokuba indima kaZuko bisele ifikelela enkcochoyini ngoku, kwaye uOndela ebeza kusibonisa amanqam,” kutsho uZitshu.

UMdidiyeli wamabali oMhlobo Wenene, uMnoza Melane, uthi balahlekelwe.
“Sishiyeke sineengcinga ezimnandi ngoOndela, umntu obethobekile nobezimisele. 
Yanga umphefumlo wakhe ungaphumla ngoxolo,” kutsho uMelane.
Omnye woogxa bakaStamper ebalini nobekwangumhlobo osondeleyo, uAnele Penny odlala indima kaMqokeleli, uthi wonakele.
“Ebengumninawa wam uOndela! Zinkulu izinto andenzele zona la mfana!

Abadlali beli bali abaquka uZukiswa Cakucaku (Nolast), Khaya Vuma (Ngxekese), Samkelo Mali (Thubhanana) Nosimo Dikana (Nolufefe), Sithini Mahola (Notiti) noMilisa Mtwa (Khonzeka) kwakunye nabanye, bathi uOndela bengumntu wokubalekela, obengadinwa kukunceda.

Le tumente iya kuphunyelelwa liqela elomeleleyo. 
Kule tumente siphumelele imidlalo emithathu (kuyo yonke) silandela ngasemva kuyo. 
Kwilizwe elincinane njengeCroatia, yimbali eyakuhlala ihleli leyo,” watsho uDalic emva kokubetha iNgilane.
Umhlaba wonke uyavuma ukuba iFrance ziintshatsheli zendebe yehlabathi ka-2018! 
IFrance ibethe iCroatia elwe kwade kwasekugqibeleni ngamagowuli amane kwamabini (4-2) kumdlalo obunika umdla kakhulu eLuzhniki Stadium ebigcwe ithe thwababa ngabalandeli bebhola abakumakhulu asibhozo amawaka ngokuhlwa kwanamhlanje. 
Amagowuli afakwe ngu-Antione Griezmann amabini, nguPaul Pogba noKylian Mbappe – ngawo anike iFrance impumelelo engasoze ilibaleke kumdlalo wokugqibela ovelise amagowuli amathandathu onke. 
Namhlanje kutyhilwe elinye iphepha lembali kaDidier Deschamps ngoba ube ngumqeqeshi wokuqala eFrance ophumelele indebe yehlabathi kabini.
Amaxhwangusha waseCroatia aphume ebaleni ethokombise iintloko emva kokubulawa kwephupha lawo yiFrance namhlanje. 
Nakubeni iCroatia ibiyiyo enamandla emdlalweni – kodwa ibethwe liqela elinobuchule futhi elisebenzileyo. 
IFrance idlale umdlalo ophucukileyo kwisigaba sesibini nakubeni ibinazo iimpazamo ezibambisa amazinyo. 
Enye into ekwazileyo ukuyenza kakuhle iFrance kukufaka amagowuli ngexesha elifanelekileyo. 
Nakubeni iCroatia ikwazile ukufaka amagowuli amabini –  ngelishwa layo, akakwazanga ukuyinceda. 
Igowuli elinike iFrance amandla lelingene ngepenela emva kokuba umdlali weCroatia ebambe ibhola endaweni embi emhlabeni kanozinti.
Isiqingatha sokuqala besinzima – kodwa besilawulwa yiCroatia. 
Iphelile imizuzu elishumi amaqela efundana. 
Izinto zijike ngethuba kusiwiswa uGriezmann kude kufuphi kumhlaba kanozinti. 
UGriezmann utale imbumbulu erhece umdlali weCroatia yahlala emnatheni. 
Iphindisile nayo iCroatia ngegowuli elifakwe ngu-Ivan Perisic kwimizuzu elishumi emva kweleFrance. 
Kwisigaba sesibini, iFrance ibuye yafaka amagowuli amabini atheze amandla wabadlali beCroatia nakubeni bezamile ukutyhala ngesifuba. 
Libe khona ithemba ngethuba uMario Mandzukic efaka igowuli lesibini emva kwempazamo eyenziwe ngunozinti weFrance – uHugo Lloris. 
Ekugqibeleni, umdlalo uphunyelelwe yiFrance ngamagowuli amane kwamabini.

EKAPA: UGWETYWE ubomi ejele unosimokolo owaziwayo waseGugulethu emva kokuba efunyaniswe enetyala lokubulala umfazi wakhe owamdubula amatyeli alishumi elinanye emzimbeni nakahlanu entloko.
UThembile “Morris” Vokozela, 52, waseNY56 eGugulethu ugwetyelwe ukubulala uRegina Vokozela, 42. 
Umzimba kaRegina wafunyanwa ulele tywa phezu kweempahla kwikhaya labo eNY48 kweyoMnga ngo2013.
Uxilongo lwafumanisa ukuba wadutyulwa izihlandlo ezilishumi elinanye emzimbeni nakahlanu entloko ngeentlobo ezimbini zemipu eyahlukeneyo.
Iwisa isigwebo, iJaji yeNkundla ePhakamileyo uDeidre Kusevitsky, uthe izenzo zikaVokozela zohlutha abantwana babo abathathu abaneminyaka ephakathi kwe15 nengama29 ithuba lokuchitha ubomi babo nomama wabo.
Inkundla ifumanise ukuba uRegina wafaka isicelo sokhuseleko ngakuVokozela kwiiveki ezintathu phambi kokuba abhubhe. Ikwafumanise ukuba 
uRegina wamangalela uVokozela emva kokuba wambetha. Wabanjwa waze wakhululwa ngebheyile yeR5 00 kwangalo mini.
Ingxelo yamapolisa ibonakalise ukuba uRegina wabethwa ngenqindi ebusweni, wakhatywa endlebeni, waze wakrwitshwa ithuba elide.
UKusevitsky uthe: “Olo hlaselo lwalulubi kwaye lukhohlakele. Lwenzeka abantwana bebukele kuhlazwa umama wabo. Kwiiveki ezintathu ezilandelayo wabulawa.  
Wabhubhela endlwini yakhe. 
Wena wacoca loo ndawo yobundlobongela, wade wafihla nompu wesibini ongekho mthethweni.”
Umama kaRegina, uGrace Gontsi, uthe uyavuya xa uVokozela egwetywe ubomi ejele nanjengoko wabulala umntwana wakhe wokugqibela obephila. 
“Andinabantwana ngoku ngenxa yakhe. 
URegina ibikukuphela komntwana ebephila. 
Wabulawa ngumntu obefanele ukumkhusela. 
Naye makafele ejele,” utshilo.

Umntu uthi wakuvula isikroxo elokishini okanye elalini, ubone nabanye besenza njalo endaweni yokucinga ngamanye amashishini.
Oku kuthethwe ngoLwesine nguGqirha Thami Mazwai, usomashishini kwanelungu lebhunga labacebisi bakaMongameli kwicandelo lokukhuliswa koshishino lwabantsundu (BEE). 
Ebethetha kwiNgqungquthela yoQoqosho lweeLokishi neeLali ebanjelwe kwihotele i-ICC eMonti.
UMazwai uthi abantu abahlala ezilokishini mabacinge ngeendlela ezohlukeneyo zokwenza ushishino endaweni yokwenza into enye.
UMazwai uthi ukuba abantu basezilokishini nasezilalini bazimisele ukuphucula uqoqosho lweendawo zabo, mabaqale ngokuxabisa iindawo abaphuma kuzo.
“Ngenye imini ndakhe ndancokola nomnye usomashishini esithi liqhuba kakuhle ishishini, ude wane-ofisi edolophini. 
Iqala apho ke ingxaki, utheni i-ofisi ingekho kufuphi neshishini elokishini okanye elalini,” kubuza uMazwai.
UMazwai uthi kubantu abangaphaya kwezigidi ezingamashumi amahlanu anesihlanu baseMzantsi Afrika, izigidi ezingamashumi amabini anesibini kubo bahlala elokishini logama ishumi elinesithoba lihlala ezilalini.
“Kodwa xa uqwalasela imigaqo-nkqubo ephunyezwa ngurhulumente, ufumanisa ukuba iluncedo isikakhulu kwabo basezidolophini,” utshilo uMazwai.
Ethetha kwakule ngqungquthela, uSekela Mongameli David Mabuza uthi lifikile ixesha lokuba urhulumente anike ingqwalasela amashishini 
asezilokishini nasezilalini, hayi nje ngokuthetha koko ngokwenza.
Iphupha lomdlali ophambili eMzantsi Afrika, uPercy Tau, lokudlalela iqela lebhola ekhatywayo laseYurophu lide lafezekiswa namhlanje. 
Oku kuza emva kokuba iMamelodi Sundowns asuka kuyo neBrighton Hove & Albion angumdlali wayo ngoku, zikuqinisekisile ukuya kkwakhe (uPercy Tau) kwiqela laseNgilane. 
Kwiiveki ezidlulileyo, kwavakala iindaba ezithi kukho ukungaboni ngasonye phakathi kukaTau nezikhulu zeSundowns emva kokuba 
zayikhaba imali ekumashumi amahlanu ezigidi zerandi (R50-million) eyabekwa etafileni yiBrighton Hove. 
Abasemfuthweni bathi iSundowns yayincwase ukufumana ingeniso yemali eyileyo phaya kwizigidi ezingamashumi asixhenxe (R70-million). 
Kuthe kwakubonaka ukuba akukho sisombululo, umongameli weDowns, uPatrice Motsepe, wayalela abaphathi beqela lakhe ukuba mamkhulule uTau – obengayanga naseNkampini ekulungiselelwa kuyo isizini entsha – ukuze aye kwiqela laseYurophu.
“UPercy ngumdlali wethu esicinga ukuba unekamva eliqaqambileyo kakhulu ebholeni. 
Italente yakhe asiyithandabuzi emva kokuvotelelwa njengomdlalo wesizini eMzantsi Afrika. 
Sizimisele ukubolekisa ngaye uTau ukuze afumane imidlalo namava kwibhola yaseYurophu. 
Inkqubela yakhe siza kuyibeka esweni ngamaxesha onke,” utshilo umanejala weBrighton, uChris Hughton. 
Kanti kwelinye icala, uTau uthe kuTwitter weDowns: “Ndifuna ukuthatha elithuba ndithi enkosi kwiSudnwons, kubalandeli, kumongameli nakubadlali bonke.”
UPercy Tau (24) ushiya iMamelodi Sundowns emva kokwenza indima ebonakalayo kwezi sizini ezidlulileyo. 
Uyishiya iDowns iliqela eliphokeleyo kwizwekazi le-Afrika yonke emva kokuyinceda ngethuba iphumelela iCaf Champions League, iCaf Super Cup, iindebe ze-Absa Premier Soccer League ezimbini, iNedbank Cup, iTelkom Knockout nezinye. 
Kanti kwisizini ephelileyo ebengomnye wabadlali abafake amagowuli amaninzi kwiPSL. 
Lo mdlali weBafana Bafana ngoyena uthengwe ngemali eninzi kwimbali yelizwe loMzantsi Afrika liqela laseYurophu.
Ngenjikalanga yanamhlanje, iChippa United ibhengeze amagama wabadlali abathathu ebafumene kwi-Orlando Pirates. 
Abo badlali nguBernard Morrison, uThamsanqa Sangweni noThabo Matlaba. 
Kwangaxeshanye, iChippa United iphulukene no-Ayabulela Konqobe, uMdlinzo noSetelele abangachazwanga ukuba bayaphi. 
UKonqobe kuvakele iindaba ezithi uthiwe tshe eNaturena – apho kucingeleka ukuba uza kudlala khona kwisizini entsha noxa kungekabikho siqinisekiso.
“Bonke abadlali esibafumeneyo ngabadlali abakwizinga eliphezulu futhi siqinisekile ukuba baza kuwenza umahluko,” utshilo uSiviwe Mpengesi 
kwingxelo ekutshwe liqela lakhe ngale njikalanga. Abadlali abafikayo baza kuya enkampini – apho kulindeleke ukuba bazixube nabanye abadlali 
abafikayo phakathi kwabo ekukho uDaine Klate osuka kwiBidvest Wits noThabo Ntete obedlalela iMamelodi Sundowns. Kwiveki ephelileyo, iChippa 
United ibiyinxalenye yeMaize Cup ebidlalelwa kwiphondo laseMntla Ntshona – apho ibethwe khona yiFree State Stars ngamapenela.
Umdlali onjengoMorrison uza kuyinceda kwicala lamagowuli iChippa United edlale kakuhle nakwiveki ephelileyo – kodwa engakwazanga ukufaka 
amagowuli. USangweni ubuyela ekhaya emva kokuba izinto zingamhambelanga kakuhle kwiPirates kwisizini egqithileyo aphazanyiswe kuyo 
nakukonzakala. UThabo Matlaba, ngaphandle kwamathandabuzo, ungumdlali osezingeni eliphezulu. 
Uza kuyivala ngokupheleleyo indawo eshiywe nguPaseko Mako othathwe yiPirates kwinyanga ephelileyo.
UMphathiswa wamaPolisa uBheki Cele UMFANEKISO: Phill Magakoe
EKAPA: “SIZA kuthabatha amanyathelo aqatha kumapolisa enza izinto ezingalunganga. 
Asinakuthumela amapolisa ukuba ayokukhusela abantu ababuthathaka ze wona asuke abenze amaxhoba.”
Oku kuthethwe nguMphathiswa wamaPolisa uBheki Cele kwinkomfa yoonondaba, ephendula malunga nezityholo zokudlwengula ezijoliswe kwipolisa 
laseStrand-efunga esithi uza kungenelela ngokwakhe ukuze kuzaliseke ubulungisa.
Ipolisa laseStrand lityholwa ngokudlwengula owasetyhini oneminyaka engama18 okhulelweyo eStrand ngomhla wesine kweyeKhala.
Eli gqiyazana nelingenakuchazwa ngegama, lithi eli polisa lalithatha endlwini yalo laze labeka oogxa balo ababini esikhululweni phambi kokuba liqhube iveni yamapolisa liye kwindawo esecaleni nalapho lamdlwengulela khona.
Kungokunje le nkosazana ikwindawo yokhuseleko nanjengoko isoyikisela ubomi bayo emva kweso siganeko. Uthi wafaka isimangalo kwisikhululo saseLwandle. 
Eli polisa lijongene nokuziphendulela kwiqumrhu lokoluleka izimilo.
Amapolisa akhuphe isibhengezo esithi: “Lo mba (ityala lokudlwengula) uphethwe ngabakwa Independent Police Investigative Directorate (Ipid). 
Iinkcukacha zoluleko azinakubhengezwa nanjengoko ingumba ophakathi kwabaqashi nomqeshwa.”
UCele uthe:  “Sifuna ukuphelisa ukuxhatshazwa kwabesifazana ngamadoda. Akhona amapolisa alungileyo nangalunganga. 
Siza kuthabatha amanyathelo kulawo angalunganga. Ndiza kuzibandakanya kweli tyala.”
Uthe umkomishinala wamapolisa kweli phondo uKhombinkosi Jula kuza kunyanzeleka ukuba asebenze ngokukhawuleza.
Eli bhinqa lithe alikafumani nentuthuzelo.
Echaza okwamehlelayo uthe: “Amapolisa agqogqa indlu aze afumana iziyobisi, athi mandiye esikhululweni. 
Bathatha imali eyayingaphantsi kweBhayibhile. 
Baqhuba iveni yabo sisiya kwisikhululo saseLwandle baze bandicela ukuba ndilinde apho evenini.
Emva kwemizuzu embalwa kwabuya ipolisa elinye laqhuba laya kwisikhululo saseStrand. Landishiya ngaphakathi evenini. 
Labuya lathi lindisindisile ekubanjweni ngoko ke mandihlawule. 
Wathi masabelane ngesondo ndaze ndala. 
Kodwa waqhuba iveni waya kwindawo esecaleni kwisakhiwo esidala waze wandidlwengula.”
Kudibana iinkunzi zebhola ekhatywayo kumdlalo omkhulu ngomso. 
Amakhosi aza kududlana okweenkunzi zegusha neMamelodi Sundowns kumdlalo weShell Helix Ultra Cup ozakube useFNB Stadium ngentsimbi yesithathu emalanga. 
Nakubeni amatkiti omdlalo engakhawulezi nje emakhethe – kodwa abalandeli bebhola bazakube bethe ntsho amehlo koomabonakude xa kudibana amaqela amakhulu kwibhola yelizwe loMzantsi Afrika. 
Esi sisiqendu sokuqala seShell Helix Cup ethathe ithuba kwakubonakala ukuba ayizukubakho iCarling Black Label kulo nyaka ngenxa yendebe yehlabathi ebisingathwe lilizwe laseRussia. 
Omabini la maqela azakube ephethe zonke iziqwayi zawo kumdlalo wangomso – kodwa abalandeli beKaizer Chiefs bafuna ukubona into enye: uKhama Billiat ebetha iDowns.
UBilliat ugaleleke eNaturena ekuqaleni kwale nyanga. 
Ngethuba iChiefs idlala kwiMaize Cup kwiveki ephelileyo, zibonakele iintlantsi zakhe uBulliat. 
Ngomso uzakube edlala okokuqala neSundowns ayidlalele iminyaka emihlanu yonke. 
Le ndedeba yaseZimbabwe ikukhabile ukubaluleka kwakho kumdlalo wangomso ngelithi umdlalo ubaluleke kumntu wonke okwiChiefs. 
Emva kokulambatha kweChiefs iisizini ezintathu zonke – uBilliat kulindeleke enze indima ebalulekileyo xa izama ukubuyisa isidima sayo ebholeni yaseMzantsi Afrika kwisizini eqala kwinyanga ezayo. 
“Ngumdlalo omkhulu ngomso; awukho ngam umdlalo – ungeqela lonke. 
Sizimisele ukuza neziphumo ezincumisayo ukuze sibone ukuba kunxa andawoni namalungiselelo wethu phambi kwesizini entsha. 
Umdlalo uzakuba nzima – kodwa siwulindile. 
Wonke umntu wonwabile futhi sijonge umdlalo wangomso,” utshilo uBilliat ngethuba ethetha neentatheli namhlanje eGoli.
UBilliat uthethe okokuqala ngokuya kwakhe kwiChiefs nangeyona nto emtsalele eNaturena. 
“Kuyandivuyisa ukubonwa yiChiefs njengomdlali ofanele ukuyidlalela. 
Lithuba elihle kakhulu kum eli futhi nayo iChiefs liqela elikhulu. 
Kudala ndakufuna ukudlalela ebaleni eligcwele abalandeli,” utshilo uBilliat.
UBilliat uza kufumana ithuba lokuqhogana noLeonardo Castro owayegil’imikhuba naye emidlalweni ngethuba besadlalela iSundowns bobabini. 
Ngo-2016/17, bobabini noKeagan Dolly – odlalela iqela lebhola ekhatywayo laseFrance – bathiywa igama elithi ‘CBD’. 
“Ngumdlali osezingeni eliphezulu uCastro; ndingatsho ukuba bendikukhumbula ukudlala naye. 
Ndingavuya ukuba singathatha apho sayeka khona. 
Ndiyazi ukuba sikwelinye iqela kwaye nendlela esidlala ngayo ngoku inomahluko – kodwa ndicinga ukuba ikhona into esinokuyenza,” utshilo uBilliat.
UNjengele uPhathekile eqalisa ukwakha indlu yakwaDanstile
UNozibonele Danstile (55) ngomnye wabo bathe bancuma, babulela ngenxa yesikhumbuzo somhla wokuzalwa kukaNelson Mandela, kuba ufumene ikhaya.
“Enkosi bawo uMandela kuba nam nditsho ndangumntu namhlanje, ndinekhaya elanele usapho lwam, andizange ndibenendlu enefenitshala ngaphambili,” enyembezana utshilo uDanstile. 
Oku kwenzeke ngethuba amapolisa eMpuma Koloni ekhokelwe ngumKomishina wawo kwiphondo, uNjengele uLiziwe Ntshinga, enikisa ngendlu kusapho lakwaDanstile eNtabethemba ngaseWhittlesea. 
Othethe egameni lamapolisa eMpuma Koloni uKhapteni Khaya Thonjeni, uthe benza oku njengenxalenye yesikhumbuzo sokuzalwa kukabawo uNelson Mandela.
Uceba wale ndawo uNkululeko Ngcefe uzabalaze ixesha elide esebenzela ukuguqula imeko yentlalo yekhaya lakwaDanstile. 
“Ngumama uNokhaya oze kum endixelela ngemeko yeli khaya, saqalisa ukukhangela amancedo wokuba kuguqulwe imeko yeli khaya, sithethe namapolisa, abezoshishino, uluntu kunye neNtabethemba Taxi Association safumana uncedo,” ucacise watsho uNgcefe.
“Kule ndlu ibinamagumbi amabini kuphela besihlala sibalishumi elinesine, ndim nentombi yam nabazukulwana abalishumi elinesithathu, ibinetha imvula xa kunethayo apha ebusika kubanda oko begula abantwana,” uthethe watsho uDanstile.
Abantu boMzantsi Afrika bathe bhazalala kwiimbombo zone zeli lizwe bekhumbula uMandela ngokwenza izinto eziphucula intlalo yabanye abantu ingakumbi abo bahluphekayo. 
Ilali yaseNtabethemba yasungulwa ngonyaka ka1976 ngabantu besizwe samaQwathi, amaMvulane nabeSuthu ababedudulwa ngurhulumente kaMathanzima eHeshele.
Igama elithi Ntabayethemba lisuka kwintaba ezinze kanye kwinqina layo lelali. 
UVuyelwa Dyasi usisithethi sekomkhulu lamaQwathi.  
“Siyabulela kakhulu ngoncedo kweli khaya kodwa sinqwenela ukuba urhulumente asondele mpela kule ndawo, le ntaba uyibonayo yindawo eyayikade itsala abatyeleli kudala, le mizi izuza ngokuba abantu babekhapha abatyeleli abanyuka kule ntaba besuka kwihlabathi jikelele, sicela ivuselelwe lo nto,” utshilo uDyasi. 
INtabayethemba imile ngokufana twatse nentaba yetafile yaseKapa.
UNtshinga unikise ngale ndlu ephahlwe zizikhulu zamapolisa ephondo eziquka umkhomishina wamapolisa akuKomani uNjengele uPhathekile, iiNkosi noluntu ngokubanzi.
Amapolisa akuKomani ekhokelwe nguNjengene Phathekile angcolise izandla kwasekuqaleni kwalo nyaka kwiphulo lokwakhiwa kwale ndlu.
Amasandawana azimisele ukuvuka ngeKaizer Chiefs emva kokubethwa yiAS Togo-Port ngo’1-0 kumdlalo weCaf Champions League ekuqaleni kwale veki. 
IMamelodi Sundowns iza kuxikixana neChiefs kumdlalo wokuqala weShell Helix Ultra Cup ozakube useFNB Stadium ngentsimbi yesithathu emalanga namhlanje. 
IDowns iza kujonga amalungiselelo wayo kumdlalo wanamhlanje phambi kokuqala kwesizini entsha kwinyanga ezayo. 
Nakubeni iSundowns ingumgqutsu kuGroup C kwimidlalo yeChampions League  – kodwa, u-Anele Ngcongca, uthi lisekhona ithemba lokuguqula izinto kwimidlalo elandelayo. 
Uyithetha lo nto noxa iDowns isakhangela impumelelo yayo yokuqala kulo nyaka kwiChampions League.
“Icango lisavuliwe kuGroup C; lo nto isinika ithemba. 
Ukuba singayibetha iTogo-Port kumdlalo wesibini xa ize kuthi, singanamanqaku amahlanu. 
Asazi kodwa kokwenzeka ntoni phakathi kweWydad neHoroya xa zidlala eMorocco kwiveki ezayo. 
Into efunekayo kuthi kukuphumelela imidlalo – qha,” utshilo uNgcongca ethetha ne-Independent Media kule veki.
Noxa izinto zingayihambeli kakuhle iDowns kwiChampions League kulo nyaka – kodwa kulindeleke ukuba umqeqeshi wayo, uPitso Mosimane, asebenzise abadlali bakhe abafikayo abafana no-Andile Jali nabanye ukuze lithi libuyela kwiChampions League iqela lakhe, libe livavanyiwe yiChiefs.
“Umdlalo wanamhlanje ubalulekile kuthi. Kunyanzelekile sikhuphe umsindo ngokubetha iKaizer Chiefs emva kokubethwa yiTogo-Port. 
Lithuba elihle labadlali abatsha lokuzibinakalisa kubalandeli beDowns.
Umdlalo uzakuba mnandi kumaqela omabini. 
Thina kwiDowns sisoloko sidlalela ukuphumelela. 
Siza kuqinisekisa nangoku ukuba umdlalo siyawuphumelela. 
La maqela azakube edlalela le ndebe okokuqala. Sifuna ibe sithi abayiphakamisa okokuqala,” utshilo uNgcongca.
La maqela aza kuphinda ankankathane kumdlalo wokuqala wePSL kwisizini entsha ngomhla wesine kwinyanga ezayo eLoftus Versfeld Stadium. 
UNgcongca uthi lowo umdlalo uzakube unomahluko kulo wanamhlanje. 
“Umdlalo wePSL unomahluko. 
Abadlali banokuya emdlalweni wanamhlanje belumkele nokonzakala. 
Umdlalo wethu wesizini entsha ubalulekile kwaye kuya nyanzeleka iLoftus Stadium ibe yindawo esiwaxhelela kuyo amaqela,” uvale ngalo mazwi uNgcongca.
Abalandeli bebhola ekhatywayo abasondele kumashumi amahlanu amawaka bafumene umdlalo omnandi futhi babengamangqina ngethuba iMamelodi 
Sundowns iphakamisa njengeentshatsheli okokuqala indebe entsha kraca ekuthiwa yiShell Helix Ultra Cup ngenjikalanga yanamhlanje. 
Amasandawana adlale ibhola entle kakhulu abethe iKaizer Chiefs ngo’2-1 kumdlalo obuseFNB Stadium. 
Impumelelo yeDowns ibalulekile ngoba iza kuhlupheza abadlali bayo phambi kwesizini entsha ekulindeleke ivulwe ngomhla wesine kwinyanga ezayo. 
UJeremy Brockie utsazise igazi kuqala emva kokufumana ibhola ebethe ipali ebikhatywe kakuhle ngu-Anthony Laffor obebapheka ebophula abadlali beChiefs kwizigaba zozibini zomdlalo. 
UThemba Zwane, ongene kwisigaba sesibini somdlalo, ufake ibhola entle ngomzuzu wamashumi alithoba emva kokunikelwa ibhola entle nguGeorge Lebese.
Amakhosi adlale ngaphandle komqeqeshi wawo omtsha, uGiovanni Solinas, osalinde iincwadi zokusebenza kweli lizwe. 
UPatrick Mabedi, olibambela mqeqeshi, uqale mdlalo ngabadlali beChiefs abaqhelekileyo ngaphandle kukaKhama Billiat noMirwa abafike kutshanje eNaturena. 
Kwelinye icala uPitso Mosimane uqale umdlalo ngabadlali abalithoba bonke abangadlalanga ngethuba iqela lakhe libethwa yi-AS Togo-Port ekuqaleni kwale veki. 
Umdlalo wala maqela omabini ubumhle ukusukela kwisiqingatha sokuqala nakubeni iyiChiefs eqale yafumana amathuba engakwazanga ukuwasebenzisa. 
UGustavo Paez akakwazanga ukugqibezela ibhola enqumle phambi kwakhe isuka kuBilliat obeyinkathazo kwiDowns noxa ibimgadile. 
UGaston Sirino ngoyena mdlali obebalasele kwisigaba sokuqala kwiSundowns. 
Kodwa ngelishwa lakhe, akakwazanga ukugqobhoza kwiChiefs emva noxa yena no-Oupa Manyisa noSiphelele Mkhulise bebedlalela emhlabeni weChiefs ubukhulu becala. 
Kuyiwe kwixesha lokuphumla kungekho qela libhalisileyo ebhodini.
Kwisigaba sesibini iDowns ibuye inamandla futhi idlala umdlalo omhle kakhulu oya phambili kunoweChiefs ebekulindeleke yenze ngcono emva kokuphumelela iMaize Cup kwiveki ephelileyo eMntla Ntshona. 
Iinguqu ezenziwe nguMosimane zibe nalo ifuthe ngoba uLebese noZwane ngabona 
badlali abathe benza umahluko emdlalweni. UBrockie uza kulala ubuthongo obehlayo namhlanje emva kokufumana igowuli lakhe lokuqala kwiDowns 
ukusukela oko wafika kuyo ekuqaleni kwalo nyaka. Indlela edlale ngayo iChiefs isafana naleya ibidlala ngayo phantsi kukaSteve Komphela. 
Abadlali beSundowns basebenzise iimpazo azenziwe ngabadlali abafana noDaniel Cardoso no-Eric Mathoho. 
Igowuli lokubika leChiefs lifakwe nguBernard Parker kwixesha elongezelelweyo. 
USolinas unomsebenzi omkhulu wokuqinisekisa ukuba uyabalola abadlali bakhe phambi kokuqala kwesizini entsha.

Nangona ephumelele uSimphiwe Khonco – kodwa uphumelele evile. 
UKhonco uphumelele ngamanqaku emva kweshumi elinambini lemijikelo ebetha uToto Landero welizwe lasePhillipines kumlo obunzima kakhulu eMthatha ngorhatya namhlanje. 
Bekungekho ndlela ingenye, uKhonco ebenyanzelekile ukuba aphumelele ngenxa yabalandeli baseMthatha abavume ingoma ukusukela kumjikelo wokuqala ukuyoqhina kowokugqibela. 
ULandero ngumdlali wamanqindi osebenzayo eqongeni – kodwa kuye kwacaca ukuba uudibene nomntu onamava namhlanje.
Kutake iintlantsi zisuka kumjikelo wokuqala phakathi kukaSimphiwe Khonco noToto Landero obekhusela itayitile ye-IBO Mini Flyweight. 
NguKhonco kodwa oyiphange ngamanqindi amahle indodana yelizwe lasePhillipines.
Ekuhambeni kwexesha kuye kwanyanzeleka ukuba uKhonco akhuphe amandla wakhe wonke ngoba uToto ebesiza phambili engxamile futhi ephosa amanqindi avakalayo. 
Kumjikeloo wesihlanu, umlo obungakacaci ukuba ungaphunyelelwa ngubani ngoba zombini iimbethimanqindi bezisebenza ngokuzimisela futhi ziphanga amanqaku.
Kuye kwafuneka ikona kaKhonco ingxole kuba bekucaca ukuba ize ngamandla imbethimanqindi yasePhillipines. 
UKhonco ebevatha kodwa naye aphose awakhe amanqindi uToto – obenamanqindi akhawulezayo. 
Ukungalwi kukaKhonco isithuba esingaphaya konyaka bekubonakala ngamanye amaxesha ngoba ebengakwazi ukumelana namanqindi akhawulezayo kaToto. 
Kumjikelo wesixhenxe ukwazile ukuhamba umhlaba othe xhaxhe uKhonco emva kokuphanyaza uToto ngamanqindi amahle.
Umjikelo wethuba ubunamandla. 
Ngowona uKhonco akwazileyo ukukhathula kwicala lamanqaku – kodwa kukho into ebegunye ngayo uLandero: kukuphisa xa ethe waxhaphazeka. 
Ebengohlukanga uToto kwiimbethi zasePhillipines ezinamandla futhi ezikhawulezayo. 
Noxa bekubonakala iimpawu zokudinwa maxa wambi – kodwa ebesilwa okwembethimanqindi eze emlweni izilungiselele. 
Ekugqibeleni uKhonco uyikhusele itayitile yakhe ityeli lesithathu. 
Itumente yamanqindi ibiququzelelwe yiLast Born Promotions.
Emva kokuphumelela ngamanqaku, uJonas Matheus, yintshatsheli entsha ye-IBO Bantamweight. 
Lo mfana waseNamibia ubethe uMakazole Tete waseMdantsane kumlo obunemijikelo elishumi elinambini kwiholo ebeligcwele qhu eWalter Sisulu University – eMthatha. 
UTete ubethwe nguMatheus ngayo yonke into. 
Indlela alwe ngayo uTete ayincumisi kwaphela. 
Ebengabonakali njengomntu ozimisele ukuphumelela okanye imbethimanqindi endala. 
Amanqindi wakhe ebesoloko ewagodlile; into ebegunye ngayo kukunyamezela izithonga zikaMatheus obekhawuleza okombane eqongeni.
UMakazole Tete noJonas Matheus (32) akukho nto bayenzileyo kumjikelo wokuqala ngamaphandle kokufundana ngokuphekuzana ngamanqindi angenamandla. Izinto zijike kumjikelo wesibini, indodana yaseNamibia ibonisile ukuba ayizanga zofeketha eMzantsi Afrika. 
Iphengulule uTete idyongwana yakwaMatheus ngamanqindi omeleleyo, imlahla ngapha nangapha – kwade kwabonakala ukuba akanalo iqhinga lokuziphindezela.
Into eye yacaca kukuba uJonas uze kuTete emazi kakuhle indlela alwa ngayo. 
UTete ulwe okomntu odiniweyo phantse kuyo yonke imijekelo. 
Abalandeli bakhe bazamile ukumkhuthaza – kodwa nakubeni kunjalo, indlela asebenze ngayo khange iphucuke. 
UJonas uphumelele umlo ngamanqaku kuyo yonke imijikelo ngoba ebekhuthele futhi oko emgcine ngokumxhola uTete obesoloko esokoneni. 
Le mbethi manqindi yasebumelwaneni iya kukhuthazeka ngakumbi emva kokubetha imbethimanqindi enamava neyaziwayo jikelele kwiqonga lamanqindi. 
UJonas uyintshatsheli emva kokuphumelela itayitile ebingenamntu.
Kwiiveki eziliqela ezidlulileyo, iPremier Soccer League yabhengeza iCape Town Stadium njengendawo ezakuthi kudlalelwe kuyo umdlalo wokugqibela weNedbank Cup. 
Isibhengezo esenziwa yiPSL saqhwatyelwa izandla nguMzantsi Afrika wonke ngoba isixeko saseKapa besingalifumani icham lokusingatha imidlalo ngokufanayo neThekwini, iPolokwane neBhayi ezixhamle amatyeli aliqela.
Yonke lo nto yeenziwa phambi kwemidlalo emibini. 
IMamelodi Sundowns yayiza kudlala neMaritzburg United – kanti yona iKaizer Chiefs yayiza kudlala neFree State Stars. 
Indlela yeDowns yayithande ukucaca kwicala lendebe yePSL – kanti yona iChiefs yayinethemba lokuzixolisa ngeNedbank. 
Wonke umntu wayenethemba lokubona umdlalo omkhulu; ophakathi kweChiefs neSundowns – eKapa. 
Kungenjalo, elinye phakathi kwamaqela amakhulu lidlale nelinye phakathi kwala mabini (Andiwadeleli). 
Wathi ke akujonga indlela athelekiswa ngayo amaqela kwiNedbank – uLunga Adams wabona ngokufanayo nabanye abantu wade wenza isithembiso esikhulu kakhulu. 
Ufana nje nenkukhu esikwe umlomo ngoku, uthe cwaka emva kokuthi ukuba ibala aligcwelanga ngabalandeli bebhola, uza kuhambaze esidlangalaleni abonwe ngabantu.
Zange kwenzeke ngokomnqweno wakhe. 
Abantu abangena ebaleni baphakathi kweshumi neshumi elinesibhozo lamawaka (10 000 – 18 000). 
Inani lalilihle lona – kodwa ke yayingesiso nesiqingatha senani elimumathwa yiCape Town Stadium. 
Into endifuna ukuyithetha kukuba uLunga Adams wonganyelwa yimincili. 
Wena ke Bra’Vuyani “VJ” Joni awukwazi ukuyivumela into embi kangaka yenzeke. 
Uyakuba nesono. 
Ukuba uLunga angayekwa ahambe ze eKapa lo nto iyakuthetha ukuthi kwakuma kwanto ngoba yindoda eyaziwayo futhi ethanda ukubancitha abanye abantu. 
Ndimcelela uxolo kubalandeli bebhola. 
Isithembiso awasenzayo wasenza enethemba lokuba iChiefs neSundowns zakuhlangabezana nomnqweno wakhe ngoba zizo ezinomtsalane ebantwini. 
Makugxekwe iChiefs neSundowns! 
Ukuba uyayekwa uLungas antswayize esidlangalaleni, kwakufuneka umnike ikhefu ngoba ebantwini baza kukhwela phezu kwakhe (Ha ha ha..kufanalekile).
Ndiyacinga ukuba la genge ayihlasela kweza zikroxo zaseLokishini iya kuphuma yonke – kanti kwelinye icala, naba wabashiya belila bakuxhelelwa exhukwana. 
Ndiyacela ke Mhleli weSoccer Laduma nabaphathi bakho, khanimxolele okanye nimxolisele ephepheni uLunga kwiveki ezayo. 
Ndivile ukuba kukho inkampani eseyibeke imali bucaala, ilungiselela umhla omkhulu. 
Ha ha ha…kodwa noxa ndinozisi nje, ndiyarhalela umbona eminciza kwezo zitalato zaseKapa.
Oneshumi elinesibhozo ubanjwe kwikhaya lakhe kwilali yaseBukwini eNgqeleni. 
Ngokwengxelo ephuma kwisithethi samapolisa aseMthatha uKapteni Dineo Koena, amapolisa ebesenza iphulo lawo likagqogqa kula mmandla nalapho bafike kwikhaya lale ntwazana kukho intsangu exabisa amawaka alishumi eerandi (R10 000).
Intwazana kulindeleke ukuba ivele phambi kwenkundla yamatyala eNgqeleni ngoMvulo.
Kusenjalo, ngamagqiyazana amabini, anamashumi amabini anesine ubudala, athe abanjwa ngamapolisa ala mmandla emva kokubhaqwa exabana 
ngentsangu kwilali iTranswilger eLady Grey ngoLwesine.
Inkumanda yamapolisa uBrigadier Xakavu usikhalimele esi senzo, esithi inani lokusetyenziswa kweziyobisi eTranswilger liphezulu ingakumbi lulutsha, esithi oko kufuna ukuqwalaselwa.
INGXABANO evuke emva kokungavisisani ngendlela emayilandelwe ngethuba kuxhelwa ihagu kumzi othile kuMahasana kuGatyana ngoLwesihlanu ikhokelele ekuhlatyweni kwenkwenkwe yabhubha.
Isithethi samapolisa akuGatyana uKapteni Jackson Manatha uthi le nkwenkwe, eneminyaka engamashumi amabini anesihlanu (25), ifike kulo mzi yabe sele ifuna ukukhokela ekuxhelweni kwale hagu.
“Iqale apho ingxabano. [Le nkwenkwe iswelekileyo] ikhuphe imela, ze nale nkwenkwe [ibanjiweyo], eneminyaka elishumi elinesithoba (19), yakhupha eyayo imela, yahlaba le nkwenkwe eneminyaka engamashumi amabini anesihlanu yabhubha,” kutsho uManatha.
UManatha uthi le nkwenkwe, eneminyaka elishumi elinesithoba (19), ibanjiwe emva koko yabekwa ityala lokubulala.
Umrhanelwa kulindeleke ukuba avele phambi kwenkundla kamantyi wakuGatyana ngoMvulo.
IPOLISA elidubule labulala umfazi kumarhe esikhwele, libanjiwe ngoogxa balo kulandela isehlo esimasikizi sokudubula le nkosikazi kwisikolo iVoorpos Primary eCambridge eMonti ngoLwesihlanu.
Ngokwengxelo ephuma kwisithethi samapolisa ephondo uKapteni Khaya Tonjeni eli polisa, elikwibakala lobuConstable, belisebenza kumapolisa aseKidds Beach.
Iingxelo zithi eli polisa lithulule ngeembumbulu kwimoto ebiqhutywa ngunkosikazi walo. 
Iingxelo ezingakhange ziqinisekiswe ngamapolisa zithi, eli polisa likonzakalise indoda ekutyholwa ukuba ibincuma nonkosikazi walo.
UMkomishinala wamapolisa ephondo eNjengele (Lt General) Liziwe Ntshinga uthi siyothusa esi sehlo.
“Sidlulisa amazwi ovelwano kulowo uphulukene nobomi, sikwenza oko ngokugxeka esi sehlo. 
Amalungu ethu makafunde ukuthetha namalungu awo osapho, iinkonzo okanye abazali xa befumana iingxaki kubomi babucala,” utshilo uNtshinga.
Eli polisa lichaphazekileyo liza kuvela enkundleni yaseMonti ngoMvulo ngamatyala okubulala.
IiNkosi zohlanga lwamaKhoi namaSan zimemelela ukuba sibizwe ngoCliffy Brown isikhululo senqwelomoya saseMonti nanjengoko kuxoxwa kuzwelonke malunga noku. 
Ezi Nkosi zithi uCliffy Brown wayelijoni loMkhonto weSizwe elaqeqeshwa nguChris Hani, eyinzalelwane yedolophu yaseMonti.
Okhokele eli gqiza lezi Nkosi uCarman Daniels uthi uBrown liqhawe lesizwe samaKhoi namaSan esazinikela ukulwela inkululeko yeli.
“Wayengumfundi eJohn Basil apha eMonti, waza wayakuzimanya noMkhonto weSizwe esilwela inkululeko, ngoko sinqwenela ukuba anikwe imbeko naye njengabanye abalwele inkululeko, masithiywe ngaye esi sikhululo,” uthethe watsho uDaniel. 
Eli gqiza leeNkosi zamaKhoi namaSan bezizimase umbhiyozo wombutho weeNkosi iContralesa ePhumlani eMonti.
UBrown wabanjwa wavalelwa eThekwini ngenxa yenxaxheba yakhe kwimigushuzo eyahlukeneyo yoMkhonto weSizwe, wabhubhela ezandleni zamapolisa engcinezelo.
“Ngomhla wesithandathu kule yeSilimela sisifakile isiphakamiso sethu sokuba sithiywe ngaye esi sikhululo, sikwamemelela ukuba esaseBhayi sithiywe ngoDavid Stuurman,” utshilo uDaniels.
Uthi banethemba lenkxaso evela kumbutho weeNkosi iContralesa eMonti nakwiMpuma Koloni.
Urhulumente kazwelonke uvule inyoba yokuba uluntu luze ngaphambili namagama ekunokuthiywa ngawo izikhululo zeenqwelomoya eziquka esaseBhayi, Kapa, Monti, Kimberly nezinye. 
“Uluntu lwesizwe samaKhoi namaSan sidlale indima enkulu ukulwela inkululeko yoMzantsi Afrika nanjengabanikazi bokuqala belizwe loMzantsi Afrika,” uthethe watsho uDaniel.
Ukanti usihlalo weContralesa eMonti uNkosi Mthuthuzeli Makinana uthi ukuthiywa kwesi sikhululo ngumcimbi osafuna ingxoxo.
“Kumele ukuba singuContralesa simeme intlanganiso neKumkani ezamaXhosa kunye nezamaKhoi namaSan sixoxe banzi lo mcimbi wokuthiywa kwezi zikhululo,” uthethe watsho uMakinana. 
Kumdlalo wokugqibela kuzakube kukho amaqela amabini, indebe nemizuzu engamashumi alithoba. 
Asithandabuzi ngoba sidlala ngokubambisana thina sonke – yinto esixhathise ngayo leyo. 
Sizimisele ukwenza konke okusemandleni wethu ukuze siphumelele,” utshilo uPogbba.
ICroatia ifuna ukubuyisa izitya ngoba yabethwa yiFrance ngo’98 – unyaka iFrance eyaphinda yathatha ngawo indebe yehlabathi elizweni layo. 
Kwangaxeshanye, iCroatia izakube ifuna iphumelela indebe yehlabathi okokuqala. 
UPogba uthi abazukwenza mpazamo yokubeka iliso [labo] kuLuka Modric yedwa ngoba kukho abanye abadlali abayingozi abafana noMario Mundzukic, u-Ivan Rakitic no-Ivan Perisic. 
“Sinaso isicwangciso sethu salo mdlalo,” uvale ngalo mazwi uPogba.
Nokuba kuphumelela eliphi na ilizwe phakathi kweCroatia neFrance ngentsimbi yesihlanu emalanga eLuzhniki Stadium – kodwa kukho umntu ongasozwe alityalwe ngabalandeli bebhola ekhatywayo kwindebe yehlabathi yalo nyaka. 
Lowo mdlali ngumtshini ozitshintshayo, umavula nokuba kuvaliwe – uLuka Modric. 
Le ndedeba (32) ngumdlali ophume izandla kwibhola ekhatywayo futhi owenze indima enkulu kakhulu kwimimdlalo yelizwe layo eRussia –  apho imizamo yayo iqinisekise ukuba iqela lonke lidlala libambisene, ngokuzimisela okukhulu futhi liyaphumelela ngamaxesha onke. 
Ibingengomsebenzi olula konke konke – kodwa ngoba nguLuka Modric, umdlali weReal Madrid yaseSpain owafumena amava ukusukela kwiitumente adlale kuzo ukusukela ngo-2006 (eGermany) eyalandelwe yebiseBrazil ngo-2014 emva kokungakwazi kweCroatia ukuza eMzantsi Afrika ngo-2010 – izinto ziye zenzeka.
Kwimidlalo emithandathu edlalwe yiCroatia kwindebe yehlabathi ka-2018 eseRussia, uLuka Modric ufumene amawonga amatyeli amathathu, kuloo midlalo ufake amagowuli amabini. 
Lo nto uchaza ngokuthe ngqo indoda ezinikeleyo emsebenzini wayo nesoloko iqinisekisa ukuba ilizwe layo lifumana iziphumo ezincumisayo. 
Omnye wemidlalo awaziqaqambisa kuwo uModric ubuphakathi kwelizwe lakhe ne-Argentina (kwiiveki ezimbalwa ezidlulileyo) ekwakucingwa ukuba iya kuhamba iphakamisele phezulu indebe yehlabathi ngenxa yabadlali abadumileyo eye nabo eRussia abafana noMessi no-Aguero. 
Kuloo mdlalo, uModric wafaka igowuli elihle – zatsho zohlukana izimvo neembono zabantu ngoyena mdlali oyakuthi athathe iwonga eliphambili lomdlali oqaqambileyo kwindebe yehlabathi.
Ayilotyeli lokuqala uModric esiya kwindebe yehlabathi enethemba lokuthatha iCroatia ayibeke endaweni ephezulu – kodwa kulo unyaka, ithemba likhona futhi liqinile kunangaphambili ngoba namhlanje kukokuqala ibandakanyeka kumdlalo wokugqibela kwindebe yehlabathi. 
Ngo-2014, uModric wayengumdlali oselula, kangangokuba wadlala kwimidlalo nje emibini phambi kokubethwa kwelizwe lakhe yiMexico ngo’3-1 lingahambanga mgama omde xa kuthelekiswa nendlela eliqhube ngayo kulo nyaka. 
“Iinkumbulo zam ngokwenzeka eBrazil azimnandanga. 
Zange ndidlale kakuhle. 
Mhlawumbi ndabethwa kukudinwa emva kwesizini eyayinde. 
Ngoku xa ndijonga iitumente endidlale kuzo; ndiye ndibone indlela embi endadlala ngayo kuzo,” ucatshulwe ethetha loo mazwi uModric yiFourFourTwo Magazine.
Ekukhuleni kwakhe, igama lakwaModric lalingadumanga kwaye wakhula nzima ngoba yena nabazali bakhe kwanyanzeleka ukuba bangcucalaze ngenxa yodushe okanye iimfazwe ezazidlakaza iCroatia kwimizamo yayo yokufumana inkululeko. 
Usapho lakwaModric lwafudukela embindini weYurophu kwindawo ekuthiwa yiZadar. 
Kulapho kanye le ndedeba edlalela iqela elikhulu kwihlabathi iReal Madrid nesecicini lokuphumelela indebe yehlabathi eyaqala khona ukukhaba ibhola ezitalatweni. 
“Sasihlala sisoyika – yeyona nto endiyikhumbulayo leyo. 
Kwakusoloko kusitsho izithonga zeziqhushumbisi nezigcayiseli ezintabeni zendawo esasihlala kuyo. 
Ngamanye amaxesha ezo zinto zazisiwela endaweni esasidlala kuyo. 
Ibhola ekhatywayo yeyona nto eyayisilibalisa ekwenzekayo ebomini bethu,” utshilo umqeqeshi weNK Zadar, uTomislav Basic, owayengumqeqeshi 
kaModric eselula kwinqubo kamabonakude kutshanje.
ICroatia lilizwe elincinane, elinabantu abakwizigidi ezine nesiqingatha qha (4.5 million) – kodwa abadlali balo, abaquka uLuka Modric, bazimisele ukulibeka endaweni entle phakathi kwezizwe namhlanje. 
Ukudlala neFrance yinto ezakuba nzima kakhulu kwiCroatia – kodwa ingayifumana impumelelo ukuba ikwazile ukudlala ngendlela yayo yesiqhelo. 
Kutshanje iCroatia ibethe iNgilane ngo’2-1 neRussia ngokulandeleana. 
Ukubetha iNgilane yenye yezinto ezibangele uModric noogxa bakhe babe kwindawo abakuyo namhlanje kuba besithi zange bayithande indlela abajongelwa phantsi ngayo ngamajelo endaba nabantu baseNgilane. 
“Iintatheli zaseNgilane beziyijongela phantsi iCroatia. 
Sazixelela ukuba sakubona ukuba ngoobani abaza kudinwa kuqala.  
Umdlalo sawuphumelela – kodwa kwakufunale ukuba siwusonge kwakwimizuzu engamashumi alithoba,” watsho uModric kwiintatheli emva kokuba ilizwe lakhe libethe iNgilane.
Inkokheli yeEFF uJulius Malema ithetha eDuncan Village eMonti Umfanekiso: Bheki Radebe.
INKOKHELI yeEFF uJulius Malema ukhwele ezehlela kobesakuba nguMongameli weli uJacob Zuma esithi lo mbutho uza kwenza konke okusemandleni ukuqinisekisa ukuba uZuma uyazibhatalela kumatyala obuqhophololo atyatyekwa wona.
UMalema ebethetha nabahlali baseDuncan Village, ngakwiPosi yale lokishi, ngenjikalanga yangoMvulo ngethuba lo mbutho ububambe umsitho wokuhlakulela usuku lwangoMgqibelo eSisa Dukashe Stadium eMdantsane apho uza kube ubhiyozela ukugqiba iminyaka emihlanu wasekwayo.
Yinkungula yamakhulu ngamakhulu wabahlali abathe babuthelana ukuza kumamela uMalema.
UMalema uthi le mali ichithwa ngumbuso ekuhlawuleleni amagqwetha kaZuma, bekufanele ukuba ichithwa ekuphuhliseni ubomi babo bahlelelekileyo.
“UZuma uqalile kwakhona. Bathi uZuma uqesha amagqwetha ngamatyala akhe, futhi [la magqwetha] aza kubhatalwa [ngabemmi beli]. La magqwetha kaZuma atyabula abemmi beli iR150 000 ngosuku.
“Ngoku ke ngoku iEFF ithathe lo mba yawusa enkundleni, kuba asinakubhatalela le ndoda. Le ndoda sisaphulimthetho,” utshilo uMalema.
“Le R150 000, mayize apha eDuncan Village yakhele abantu abahlelekileyo izindlu. 
Sidiniwe nguZuma, onentloko engathi yiButternut.
Asokuze sibhatalele uZuma lonke nje ixesha.
“UZuma sele enepomakazi eNkandla, kodwa usafuna okuninzi kuthi. Mayiphele le nto,” kutsho uMalema.

Abahlali kuvavanyozimvo ngomhlaba eMthatha eMpuma Koloni
NGAMASHUMI alithoba eepesenti abahlali abavakalise ukungamthembi urhulumente kumcimbi wokwabiwa komhlaba ngethuba kuvavanywa izimvo eKomani. 
Uninzi kubo lukhomba iinkqubo ezibonakalayo zikarhulumente besithi zifile ngenxa yobuqhophololo beenkokheli zopolitiko namagosa karhulumente.
UMthuthuzeli Mtshiselwa ngowaseShilow eWhittlesea, le yenye yeendawo ezinamadabi omhlaba acacileyo phantsi kweeNkosi ezahlukeneyo.
 “Asiwathembi la madoda akwarhulumente, mazenziwe iinguqu kweli solotya, kodwa ingenziwa impazamo yokuba babenegunya lokwaba umhlaba, umhlaba mawunikwe iiKumkani neeNkosi zisabele umhlaba wethu,” uthethe watsho uMtshiselwa.
Kwiholo ibizele imi ngeembambo ngabantu abamnyama nabamhlophe, zimbini izimvo ebeziphambili. 
UGqr Pieter Prinsloo ongumnikazi weefama ezintathu eKomani, okwanendawo yokuxhela iinkomo ngesininzi ngosuku ngalunye, yena uthethe wathi.
“Siyayihlonipha le yokuba ngenene kukho imfuneko yokuba umhlaba wabiwe ngokutsha, kodwa kukho umhlaba ovelisa imisebenzi nokutya ngoku sithethayo, nithini ngawo, nifuna umhlaba, niza kutya umhlaba, asiwuxhasi thina umbono wenguqu kweli solotya,”utshilo uPrinsloo.
UNokuzola Ntlemeza waseSterkspuit uthi abanakuphinda bavume ukuqhathwa ziinkokheli zopolitiko ngokuba zithathe umhlaba kwakho, umhlaba mawunikwe iiKumkani.
“Siyaboyika aba tata bakwarhulumente, bahambela phezulu kulo mcimbi womhlaba, sinamava angekho mahle ngabo, mazenziwe zona iinguqu kwisolotya, kodwa umhlaba mawubuyele eziKumkanini zethu, ziwulawule zisabele ngokweeNkosi zethu,” utshilo. 
Igqala lomzabalazo phantsi kombutho wePAC uMpolose Mangqangwana, uxelele loo nginginya ukuba bengumbutho wePAC bakholelwa ukuba olu hlobo uza kuthathwa ngalo umhlaba lungamfaka engxakini urhulumente. 
“Xa usithi uyayihlutha into emntwini uthetha ukuba, uyavuma ukuba ibiyeyakhe, wena uyayithatha ngoku, awuzange ube ngowabelungu umhlaba waseAzania, ngumhlaba wethu lo mawuze kuthi,” utshilo.
Abahlali abe bezimase olu vavanyozimvo eKomani bebephuma kuzo zonke iingqingqi zoMasipala weSithili saseChris Hani. 
IiNkosi eziphuma kumaQwathi eNgcobo naseHewu,kubaThembu baseRhode, kuMandungwane kaNdarhala amaGcina kaMpangele nezinye izizwe.
Abahlali baseGwatyu ngaseKomani bafumene ithuba lokubhentsisa amahlazo angokuthathwa komhlaba wabo ngamagosa aphezulu karhulumente.
UNolizwe Mente utyhola uMphathiswa uGugile Nkwinti ngokubangumzekelo wabo bathatha umhlaba ngobuqhophololo.
“Kwiifama ezisibhozo esixoxa ngazo phaya eGwatyu ngoku, uGugile Nkwinti unayo ifama, ningakulinge nithathe umhlaba ebelungwini kanti nifuna ukwenza obu buqhophololo sinazi ngabo, sishiyeke thina sityiwa yindlala apha, yekani umhlaba kwiiKumkani neeNkosi zisabele ngokuhlala kwethu, nina yenzani nje inguqu kwisolotya nibuye umva, zithembakele iiKumkani neeNkosi kunani,” uthethe watsho uMente.
Kuthe kanti abezi abadlali ababini kwabathathu ekwaqhayiswa ngabo yiChippa United kwiveki ephelileyo. 
IChippa United yakhupha ingxelo ebhaliweyo ethi ityikitye uThamsanqa Sangweni, uBernard Morrison noThabo Matlaba abasuka kwi-Orlando Pirates. 
Ezo ndaba zamkelwa ngovuyo olukhulu ngabalandeli beChippa United – kodwa ekuhambeni kweentsuku, kuye kwacaca okokuba umbandela wabadlali ababini awukagqitywa ncam. 
Iindaba ezivakaleyo emva koko zithi uMatlaba uthe uxolele ukuhlala kwiPirates, alwele indawo yakhe kunokuya kwiChippa United. 
Kwelinye icala, uMorrison uyikhanyele eyokuya kwakhe kwiChippa.
Emva kokuthi cwaka kweChippa nePirates ngalo mba wabadlali ababini ixesha elide, namhlanje kuthe gqi into ethi uMnumzana uSiviwe Mpengesi wathetha naba badlali babini – kangangokuba wade wanika uMorrison imali engamashumi amabini anesine amawaka erandi (R24 000). 
Kuthe kwakucaca okokuba lo mdlali akafuni ukuza kwiChippa, uMpengesi uthe makabuye imali yakhe. 
Nayo iPirates ikhuphe ingcaciso ngokwenzekileyo ngaba badlali ababini.
“Isivumelwano ebesibandakanya uThabo Matlaba asisekho emva kokuba sibambe iingxoxo ngokuya kukaMorrison noThamsanqa Sangweni kwiChippa United. 
Singatsho ukuba kubekhona utshintshiselwano ngemali phakathi kukaMorrison noMnumzana uMpengesi,” itshilo iPirates namhlanje.
UMatlaba akayi kwiChippa kwaye kubonakala ngathi uMorrison uncwase ukuyozama phesheya kolwandle kunokuya kwiqela laseBhayi.
Umphathi weXaba Promotions, u-Ayanda Matiti, uthi konke kume ngommo phambi kwetumente yamanqindi ngomso. 
Zikulungele ukukhwela eqongeni iimbethimanqindi ekulindeleke zixhimfane kwitumente yeXaba Promotions and Events kwitumente ezakuba se-ICC ngentsimbi yesixhenxe ngomso. 
Oku kubhengezwe ngumongameli weXPE, uMnu. Ayanda Matiti, emva koxilongo olwenziwe ngugqirha Zondi kwimbethi manqindi ezisibhozo eziza kulwela intshinga zehlabathi e-Osner Hotel. 
“Zigaleleke ngomvulo zonke iimbethi manqindi zangaphandle.
Ugqirha uzilolongile zonke zikulungele ukukhwela ukulwa ngolwesihlanu,” uMatiti utshilo.
Le ndedeba ithi iyakuba ngumbono omhle ukuba iimbethimanqindi zeli lizwe zingaphumelela zonke kwimilo yentshinga zehlabathi. 
“Iyakuba sisipho esihle kakhulu kuMongameli wokuqala ontshundu utata uNelson Mandela ukuba zinokuphumelela zonke ezi mbethimanqindi zalapha eMzantsi Afrika zilwela,” utshilo uMatiti.
Intshatsheli ye-IBO, uGideon Buthelezi, oyenye yeembethimanqindi eziqabela eqongeni ngomso – ithi iqinisekile ngempumelelo. 
“Ndimbukele uLucus Fernandez yaye ndizibonile iimpazamo zakhe. 
Ndiqinisekile ukuba ndiyika kuyikhusela ngempumelelo intshinga yam,” utshilo uButhelezi.
Umceli mngeni kwintshinga kaButhelezi uLucas Fernandez wase-Argentina uthi akukho mehluko omngako phakathi kwelizwe lakhe noMzantsi Afrika. 
“Akukho mehluko mngako ngokwesimo sezulu kula mazwe mabini. 
Ndikhe ndayibukela imifanekiso bhanya-bhanya yemilo kaButhelezi, noko akayombethimanqindi enobungozi kakhulu. 
Ndiza kuwuphumelela umlo,” utshilo uFernandez.
Imbethimanqindi yasePhilipine, uRene Dacquel, uza kunyathalana ngeentupha noYanga Sigqibo waseZiphunzane kumlo weWBC International enganamntu, ithi inqwenela ukulingqengisa ngophotho eli tyendyana. 
“Ndikhe ndazinika ithuba ndabukela imilo yakhe; uyimbethi manqindi ekhawulezayo. 
Ndifuna ukumngqengqisa ngophotho, kodwa ukuba akwenzeki oko – ndakuzama kangangoko ndinako ukuqokelela amanqaku aza kundiphumelelisa lo mlo,” utshilo uDacquel.
OkaSigqibo ukholelwa kwelokuba ukubamde kwakhe kuDacquel ngesithomo kuza kuwenzela lula umlo. 
“Ndimbukele lo mfana. 
Yimbethimanqindi ethanda ukusebenzisa amandla. 
Into endiqonda ukuba iza kundinceda kukuba mfitshane. 
Ndiza kusebenza ngalo nto,” utshilo uSigqibo.
Eminye imilo yentshinga zehlabathi iquka oka Ntlantla Ngamntwini uqubisana no-Ulises Lara waseMexico kwiWBA international enganamntu; u-Uyanda Nongogo ungquzulana no-Aziz Uliza kumlo we-IBF Youth.

UZONDENI Sobukhwe oyinkosikazi kaNjingalwazi  Robert Mangaliso Sobukhwe, ubhiyozele umhla wokuzalwa kwakhe elele ngandletyananye kwisibhedlele iMidland eRhafu. 
Ingxelo yekhaya lakwaSobukhwe,  ithi le ngwevukazi eminyaka ingamashumi alithoba ananye ingene esibhedlele kwiveki ephelileyo ngenxa yokungabinamandla.

Esona sipho simvuyise kakhulu umama uSobukhwe kukuhanjelwa ngamagqala kaPoqo elandelelana kwikhaya lakhe eRhafu. 
“Kule veki iphelileyo phambi kokuba angene esibhedlele ebehanjelwe ngutata uJohnson Mlambo ehamba nosapho lwakhe, uvuye kakhulu emva koko,” utsho uMilisa.
UJohnson Mlambo uchithe iveki yonke kwikhaya lakwaSobukhwe. 
Lo kaMlambo yenye yamadoda achithe iminyaka engaphezu kweshumi eRoben Island eKapa.

“Lo ngumama wokugqibela esisele naye kubantu abasifundisa ngePAC  ngethuba sivalelwe eRoben Island, ngomnye obe sihambela phaya esixelela izinto eziqhubeka apha ngaphandle kwentolongo,” utshilo uMangqangwana. 
Bengavumi ukuba athethe abantwana bakhe,  umama uSobukhwe ukuphikisile oku. 
“Ngabantwana bakaMangi aba, ngoko ke ngabantwana bam ooMangqangwana aba, andizange ndibenawo umhla wokuzalwa ofana nalo, ndiyabulela kubo bonke, ngento yonke,” uthethe watsho uMam’ uZondeni. 
Uthi ukruqukile zipilisi neenaliti zasesibhedlele.
UMam’ uSobukhwe unikwe enye yeembasa eziphezulu kurhulumente weli ekunye neJaji edla umhlalaphantsi uDikgang Moseneke, oku kusemva kokuba ulutsha lwePAC lanyanzelisa ukuba igama lakhe liqwalaselwe.

Inkokheli yeEFF uJulius Malema ekunye namanye amalungu alo mbutho eSisa Dukashe Stadium eMdantsane UMFANEKISO: ABONGILE GINYA
XA ubani esebenzisa isiyobisi iWhoonga, lo nto ithetha ukuba uyawoyika amanzi – akahlambi – into engafunwayo yiEFF.
“KwiEFF sifuna imbeko nocwangco ukuze silungele ukukhokela urhulumente. 
Amanxila asiwafuni. 
Abo babetyalwe ukuze badungadunge lo mbutho sele sabagxotha. 
Abasatshayi neNyaope, batshaya iWhoonga futhi bayawoyika amanzi (abahlambi),” itshilo inkokeli yeEFF uJulius Malema ethetha nabaxhasi kwanabalandeli balo mbutho eSisa Dukashe Stadium, eMdantsane, ngoMgqibelo.
Ngamawaka ngamawaka eEFF athe abuthelana kweli bala ukuza kubhiyozela iminyaka emihlanu wasekwayo lo mbutho.
UMalema uthi iEFF ngumbutho oza kungena kurhulumente kunyaka ozayo, ethanda engathandi ubani, nokuba zinjani iziphumo zonyulo.
“Singumbutho oza kuba seburhulumenteni, nokuba uthini umntu. 
Nokuba senza urhulumente wenkazathi okanye senza kanjani kodwa siza kube sikurhulumente kunyaka ozayo,” utshilo uMalema.
Uyalele amalungu alo mbutho ukuba asebenze nzima, eqinisekisa ukuba wonke umzi kweli lizwe ufumana ivoti yeEFF.
UMalema ukwakhwele ezehlela kumasipala waseBuffalo City esithi ugcwele abarhwaphilizi kwanamagosa “afuna ukulala namakhosikazi aselula ukuze awaqashe.”
“Ixabiso lokuthenga umbane lixhome kakhulu eBuffalo City kuba lo masipala ufuna ukunyusa ingxowamali yekhabatiso lobuMetro [umasipala ombaxa]. 
Phantsi kweEFF, abantu abarhola indodla baza kufumana umbane namanzi asimahla,” kuthembisa uMalema.
UMongameli weUDM uBantu Holomisa obe zimase lo msitho, uqhwabele izandla iEFF, esithi ukufika kwayo kuyitshintshile ipolitiki yeli.
IBALI elothusayo lokubiwa kwemoto, inabantwana ababini ngaphakathi, liphele ngesenzo esingaqhelekanga sobubele.
Umgulukudu waseMthatha usikwe yimfesana xeshikweni esiba imoto enabantwana ababini ngaphakathi. 
Aba bantwana babini; inkwenkwana eneminyaka elishumi kunye nentombi eneminyaka emithandathu bebesendleleni eya esikolweni nonina oneminyaka engamashumi amahlanu anesine, ngethuba usuku lwabo luthatha inguqu engalindelekanga.
Okokuqala unina utshayise umhambi-nyawo. 
Isithethi samapolisa uDineo Koena uthe: “Eli nina litshayise intombazana eneminyaka elishumi elinesithathu ngecala emveni kwentsimbi yesixhenxe kusasa, kwindlela uR61 ephakathi koMthatha neNgcobo.”
Okwesibini, lithe eli nina lisamokamokana nesimo salo mhambi-nyawo, nelimgilise wophuka umlenze, kwafika indoda engaziwayo yangena kwimoto le, yemka nayo inabantwana ababini ngaphakathi. 
UKoena uthi: “Umrhanelwa uye wabohlisa eDikolina, kwilokishi yaseChris Hani aba bantwana. Wabapha iR20 umntana ngamnye, wabayalela ukuba baye esikolweni.”

UKoena uthe umrhanelwa usagcwele amathafa. 
“Sibongoza nabani na onolwazi aze ngaphambili!” kutsho amapolisa.

ABAFUNDI besikolo iSt Matthews kuQoboqobo bayalelwe ukuba basishiye isikolo kule veki emva kokungeniswa kwenkungula yabafundi esikolweni bekreqwa sisisu kwinto ekholeleka ukuba ibangelwe ngamanzi anentsholongwane.
Iingxelo zithi izolo (ngoLwesibini) abafundi abalikhulu elineshumi(110) bangeniswe kwisibhedlele iSS Gida kuQoboqobo emva kokukhala ngesisu kulandela ukusela isiselo (jusi) esenziwe ngamanzi asuka kumasipala wesithili iAmathole.
Utitshala wesi sikolo uthi la manzi afakwe kumatanki esi sikolo, ehostele nasesikolweni, kulandela ukushokoxeka kwamanzi okusela nokupheka ematankini.
Umfundi oyintombazana oneshumi lesihlanu leminyaka, owenza uGrade 9, uthi uqalwe ngamahlaba esiswini emva koko wasiva simkreqa. 
“Emva koko ndiye ndahlanza ndabe ndihambisa. Ndikhwaze umetroni sabe sele sifunelwa uncedo,” utshilo lo mfundi.
Ngokwengxelo kaRay Tywakadi, uSekela Mlawuli kwiSebe lezeMfundo eMpuma Koloni, abafundi abangamashumi amathandathu anesine, kwabo balikhulu elineshumi, bakhawuleze bakhutshwa esibhedlele logama abanye besashiyeke ngaphakathi benyangwa.
Ubukhulu becala, ngokutsho kukaTywakadi, aba bafundi baphelelwe ngamanzi emzimbeni emva kokuhlanza nokuhambisa.
“Yiyo le nto sithi godukani nibuyele esikolweni ngoMvulo ukuze sivavanye la manzi kwanokutya ukuze sibone oyena nobangela wale ngxaki,” utshilo uTywakadi.
Amagosa esebe lezempilo abesesikolweni ngethuba I’solezwe lifika kwesi sikolo. 
Ambi kula magosa ebenyanga abafundi kumagumbi esikolo logama abanye bebezimase indibano yokugqala umkhombandlela kule ngxaki.
Amawele kaMamTshawe.
AMAWELE kaMamTshawe ayabuya kwakho kulo nyaka, ebuya necwecwe elitsha eliqulethe iingoma ezilishumi elinambini.
Eli cwecwe, elibizwa ‘Sagula’ liphume ngenyanga kaTshazimpuzi kulo nyaka.
Kweli cwecwe lesixhenxe leli qela leMaskandi, kukho iingoma eziquka uSagula, MaNgobese, Zakhala Kamnandi nezinye.
Amawele kaMamTshawe ngabafana ababini bakuCentane – uZama Ntenteni ozobiza uTornado kwakunye noMasibulele Gompo ozibiza uNongoma. 
UTornado noNongoma bazalwa ziintombi zikaMamTshawe, nto ebenza babe ngabazala. 
Bobabini bakhuliswe ngumakhulu wabo uMamTshawe.
“Ingoma ethi Sagula nesikwathiye ngayo eli cwecwe ibalisa ngengoma elubizo kuthi, siyayigulela, siyizalelwe kwaye isegazini kuthi,” kutsho uTornado encokolela I’solezwe.
Amawele kaMamTshawe aziwa ngeengoma ezifana noSongena Nawe, Matsanatsana, Mhla kuphel’ amandla, Imali yegazi nezinye.
UTornado uthi abantu bazozivela kule mbiza intsha bayiphekileyo.
“Silande kwezinye zeengoma zethu. 
Eli cwecwe liphethe iingoma ezohlukeneyo.
“Uyakufumana iingoma zesiGcaleka, ezesiMpondo, ezingolwimi lwesiZulu nomyalezo oya kulutsha,” utshilo.
UTornado, uthi ukuthanda kwabo iMaskandi kwabangelwa kukuthanda umculo woMfaz’ Omnyama nooPhuzikhemisi besebancinane.
Zifumanele eli cwecwe kwiivenkile ezithengisa umculo.

Kapa: Intlungu yokubulawa, kudlwengulwa kwanempatho-gadalala ngakumanina ibibhalwe ebusweni kuninzi lwabasetyhini abathathe inxaxheba kumngcelele ububanjwe kweli leKapa izolo. 
Le mingcelele, nebibanjwe kwiidolophu ezinkulu kweli loMzantsi Afrika ibikhalima impathombi nokubulawa kwabantu basetyhini kuquka nabantwana abaselula ngokweminyaka. 
Kweli leKapa lo mngcelele ubusingise kwiPalamente kazwelonke nalapho amakhulukhulu wamanina anikele ngoxwebhu lwezikhalazo.   
La ngamanina ancame ukwenza iingxaki zawo ngolu suku abhenela ezitalatweni ekhanda ngenqindi phantsi, ngelithi kwanele ngokubulawa kwamanina nentsana zabo.
Ezinye zezi khalazo zamanina kwezo zithiwe thaca, amanina athi awasayi kuyinyamezela impathogadalala ejoliswe kumanina yaye befuna ukuba urhulumente ukuba azame ukwehlisa ezi ziganeko ngakumanina, nalapho badize ukuba bafuna urhulumente azibophelele anike impendulo ngomhla wethoba kule iphezulu.
Lo mngcelele ubuvalele ngaphandle amadoda nanjengoko ubukhokelwa ngabasetyhini kuphela ubuhamba phantsi kwesihloko esithi  Total Shutdown.
“Awona maxhoba kudlwengulo nempathogadalala ngabantu abaphila nokukhubazeka kuba abanawo amandla okuzikhusela” utshilo uMary-Anne Jacobs nonguMququzeleli kulo mngcelele. 
Lo mngcelele ubanjwa ngale nyanga ibekelwe bucala ukuqaphela amalungelo wabantu basetyhini kweli loMzantsi Afrika. 
Kanjalo, lo mngcelele ngoweqela lamanina nabone ukuba zininzi iingxelo zokulahleka kwamanina besazi ngokucacileyo ukuba abasayi kuphinda bahambe ngeenyawo zombini nanjengoko baba ngamaxhoba okudlwengulwa ze babulawe ngokumanyukunyezi nanjengoko bambi kubo baye bantunyekwe ngomlilo. 
Ngethuba la manina ebambe umngcelele, akhankanye amagama amanina nathi abulawa kabuhlungu aquka uAviwe Jamjam, uKarabo Mokoena kwanamanye amaxhoba abulawa kabuhlungu.
Kusenjalo, amanina asaze ngobuso elizweni kumbutho weANC eKapa, nawo ebebambe umngcelele okumila kunje, nalapho ebevakalisa ukucinezelwa kwamanina ngobuhlanga, umgangatho wawo kwanobume besini. 
Lo mngcelele nawo ubusingise kwiPalamente kazwelonke, nalapho amanina akhalazela izinga eliphakamileyo lentswela-ngqesho kwabasetyhini.
“Umhla wokuqala kweyeThupha ubonakalisa inyanga ebekelwe amanina, sikuvile ukubulawa kwamanina oko khange kuhlale kakuhle kuthi,” utshilo uThandi Mahambehlala olilungu lePalamente kumbutho weANC. 
UMahambehlala uthi amanina aselula ngeminyaka kufuneka abumbane yaye kuqinisekiswe ukuba isitshulwa neengcambu impathombi ngakumakhosikazi nentsana zawo.

“Emva kwamalungiselelo wethu, ndingatsho ukuthi ndonwabile kakhulu kunakuqala. 
Ndinamava ngoku; andisenguye umqheliswa ngoku. Abadlali basebenza ngokuzimisela okuphindaphindeneyo kune sizini egqithileyo. 
Abadlali abatsha esibafumeneyo baliqinisile iqela kwaye sinabadlali abathathu kwindawo nganye ebaleni,” utshilo uMcCarthy ngethuba ethetha neentatheli eKapa.
Emva kokuyiphosa kancinci indebe kwisizini yePSL ka-2017/18, uMcCarthy ufuna iqela lakhe lidlalele ukuphumelela kuzo zonke iindebe ezikhoyo. 
“Asifuni ukuza enkundleni yokuziqeqesha singazimiselanga ukuphumelela. 
Sisebenza ngokuzimisela ngoba sifuna impumelelo. 
Sifuna ukuphumelela yonke imidlalo. 
Asizimiselanga ukukhetha imidlalo ethile ngoba asizelanga lo nto apha,” utshilo uMcCarthy.
ICape Town City neSuperSport United zidlala umdlalo wazo wokuqala we-Absa Premier Soccer League ngentsimbi yesithandathu ngorhatya eCape Town Stadium ngoMgqibelo. 
Emva kweziganeko eziliqela zokuphangwa kwamaziko empilo kwingingqi iArea East, ilungu lekomiti kasodolophu elinoxanduva lokuhambisa iinkonzo kula ngingqi uAnda Ntsodo, utyelele elinye lala maziko eKhayelitsha. 
UNtsodo uthi ufuna ukugxininisa ukuba iziganeko zokuphangwa kula maziko azamkelekanga kwaye azizokunyanyezelwa.
UNtsodo uthi “Ndimemelela kubahlali baseKhayelitsha bathathe uxanduva bakhusele la maziko kuba alungiselelwe bona. 
Iziganeko ezinje azinakuliwa ngamapolisa kuphela, kwaye akunakuvalwa amaziko ngenxa yezaphulimthetho”. 
Uthi iofisi yakhe iza kusebenzela ukuzilwa ezi ziganeko.
Ukanti iNtloko kwiCandelo lezeMpilo kwinqwanqwa lophuhliso lweKhayelitsha uNdibongo Mzanywa, uthi kufuneka kuqwalaselwe ngamandla umcimbi wamagosa ezokhuseleko asebenza kula maziko.  
Uthi mawongezwe amagosa ukuba kunyanzelekile.
KUSUKU lwesithathu iqalile iNyanga yamaNina, kufunyanwa imveku esandula kubelekwa ilahlwe kwikhonteyina yokulahla inkukuma kwingingqi yoogobityholo iVlei eSweethome ePhillipi. 
Abasebenzi beprojekthi yokucoca izitalato kula lokishi, bathi bebeqhuba umsebenzi wabo njengesiqhelo ngexa begagana nesi simanga.
UNoluvuyo Sidumo oneminyaka eyi34 ubalisa athi: “Ndithe xa ndisenza umsebenzi wam njengamihla yonke, ndiqokelela inkukuma engekho kwiiplastiki kuba siza kuyifaka ngaphakathi kwikhonteyina, ndibone olu sana lusenenkaba ejingayo lusongelwe ngeqhiya emnyama. 
Ndothukile kakhulu ukubona kwam, ndakhwaza omnye ugxa wam omdala kunam, bendiqale andaqiniseka ukuba ngumntwana kwade kwafika ugxa wam wandibonisa ukuba ngumntwana oyikwekwe.”
USandisiwe Gxulu ongumhlali kula lokishi uthi: “Ibuhlungu le nto kuba baninzi abantu abadinga abantwana, ebe nokumshiya esibhedlele xa engamfuni umntwana.  
Urhulumente wethu uzenzile zonke iindlela zokuba kungakhulelwa umntu ongafuniyo, kucwangciswa mahala, kwaye isisu sikhutshwa mahala, noko akusafanelanga ukuba kusenzeka izinto ezinje.”
USomlomo wamaPolisa ephondweni uKapteni FC Van Wyk, uthi amapolisa avule ityala kwaye kucelwa nabani onolwazi lomntu owenze esi siganeko atsalele amapolisa aseNyanga.
